
-----title
仙游 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1013&endYear=1015')">1013-1015年</a>　不详。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1016&endYear=1016')">1016年</a>　蔡襄偕弟高受教于外祖父卢仁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1017&endYear=1017')">1017年</a>　蔡襄在外祖父家读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1018&endYear=1018')">1018年</a>　蔡襄在外祖父家就读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1019&endYear=1019')">1019年</a>　蔡襄始入乡序就读。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1023&endYear=1023')">1023年</a>　蔡襄得仙游县尉凌景阳赏识，入县学读经书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1024&endYear=1025')">1024-1025年</a>　蔡襄在县学就读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1026&endYear=1026')">1026年</a>　蔡襄由仙游县尉凌景阳荐入郡庠习举业。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1027&endYear=1027')">1027年</a>　蔡襄偕弟高在郡庠就读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1028&endYear=1028')">1028年</a>　蔡襄在郡庠就读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　蔡襄偕弟高从兴化军徒步赴京都参加开封府进士考试。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='bbcb348e834042e59f0eee2eaaffd2a2_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　蔡襄回乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='97128900d5d6401796b6a1e3eb670d30_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("97128900d5d6401796b6a1e3eb670d30");'><span id='97128900d5d6401796b6a1e3eb670d30_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1036')">1034-1036年</a>，23-25岁</div><div id='97128900d5d6401796b6a1e3eb670d30' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　蔡襄从漳州秩满罢归，适弟高登第还乡，阖家荣庆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1035&endYear=1035')">1035年</a>　蔡襄在家事亲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年春</a>　春，蔡襄偕弟高辞亲北上，同赴吏部铨选。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='59a5b3f8d68a41f5ba1beec9d8f02e33_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("59a5b3f8d68a41f5ba1beec9d8f02e33");'><span id='59a5b3f8d68a41f5ba1beec9d8f02e33_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='59a5b3f8d68a41f5ba1beec9d8f02e33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　蔡襄抵家方五日即闻弟高噩耗，不胜哀痛，作《祭弟文》悼之。<div id='poem_1168205' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168205' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168205?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭弟文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168205")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168205_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168205'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168205'>专以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于亡弟开封府太康主簿七郎君山之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168205_comment'></div>吾至家始五日，得汝讣音，以六月七日感疾终于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168205_comment'></div>哀苦号叫，惊迷失次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168205_comment'></div>反覆思虑汝之行，于父母孝谨，于兄弟友悌，于当官涖事公廉无私，事细大莫不尽其心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168205_comment'></div>天鉴孔迩，汝不应不寿而少亡，岂赴告之者谬也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168205_comment'></div>发书寻绎，皆侄彝与蒋生手疏，日月苦疾，终始无一谬者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼，汝其死矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168205_comment'></div>吾闻死而复生者，若秦之谍人、石勒之子是也，犹幸其非望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168205_comment'></div>又涉旬月，无有来问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼，汝不复生矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168205_comment'></div>汝之永诀矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168205_comment'></div>二亲垂老，早暮涕泣，望祭千里之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168205_comment'></div>汝之妻孥，必归江南，旅厝异乡，不独生者悲恸，使死者为有知，衔恨九泉，终古无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168205_comment'></div>吾自五岁与汝从学，及吾年十五，再就乡举，汝时十三，盖亦与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168205_comment'></div>众所指目，期必远到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168205_comment'></div>其后三年，与汝北游京师，吾先得官，为临漳从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168205_comment'></div>及罢归，汝后登第还家，骈首拜庆，乡闾荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168205_comment'></div>吾佐西都留守幕府，汝时选注太康，西来过我，留游久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168205_comment'></div>去年，吾忝对雠，丽名书府，汝以畿县，继来相见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168205_comment'></div>今年夏四月，吾谒告归觐，别汝于国门之外，谁谓此别，为生死之别，呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168205_comment'></div>疾不临药，死不亲歛，殡不拊棺，吾恨如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168205_comment'></div>汝即死，宁无一言以别我乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168205_comment'></div>岂赴告者忍不书也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168205_comment'></div>将疾力而不暇及耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168205_comment'></div>其亦忘我于无言耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168205_comment'></div>吾于汝，爱为兄弟，而学业为朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168205_comment'></div>每聚议通夕，若出入经史记传，浩博贯穿，吾不在汝右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168205_comment'></div>逮根诸理论，吾或有先焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168205_comment'></div>汝有遗文，吾当录次，以传于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168205_comment'></div>汝子犹吾子也，教勖养育，待其成人，扶持汝归，以葬吾土，则吾志足矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168205_comment'></div>吾材与艺，下汝远甚，觊汝光显，以大吾门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168205_comment'></div>今也亡矣，吾力薄而倚重，思此益悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168205_comment'></div>平居议论当世得失，卓然期有发于人者，今岂复能力于是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168205_comment'></div>圣人推天引神，以锡福降殃于善恶，而作民监；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168205_comment'></div>至于善不及福而恶不及殃，学者惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168205_comment'></div>然则贤而夭，孰谓其不寿也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168205_comment'></div>恶而寿，孰谓其不夭也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168205_comment'></div>君子之论人也，在贤与不贤耳，不系其寿且夭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168205_comment'></div>汝之行之学之文，虽不克寿，吾谓之寿也，夫何恨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168205_comment'></div>独手足之念，无所穷极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168205_comment'></div>古有达观之士，一死生而超乎无有，是用决灭情爱，吾不忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168205_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168205_comment'></div>语言嘻嘻，寂而不闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168205_comment'></div>肴浆陈前，不食不饮，魂兮何之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168205_comment'></div>其无知乎，吾徒自苦耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168205_comment'></div>其有知乎，吾知汝之悲与吾均矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168205_comment'></div>伏纸颠倒，不尽所怀，呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168205_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1168205_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fcade486888044ab82bf96f3fc7dbebb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fcade486888044ab82bf96f3fc7dbebb");'><span id='fcade486888044ab82bf96f3fc7dbebb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>，33岁</div><div id='fcade486888044ab82bf96f3fc7dbebb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年1月</a>　蔡襄在家乡营葬弟高并安慰父母。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5e81968b9ac542728c9124dd146270e5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5e81968b9ac542728c9124dd146270e5");'><span id='5e81968b9ac542728c9124dd146270e5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>，33岁</div><div id='5e81968b9ac542728c9124dd146270e5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年3月22日</a>　蔡襄为惠安杨光明撰书《杨公明墓表》<div id='poem_1168172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨公明墓表<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年三月二十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年3月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168172")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168172'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168172'>予友杨公明，景祐元年登进士第，籍名下吏部铨，将补官，辄病，其年某月日终于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168172_comment'></div>其友张平叔用浮屠法火之而归其家，以某年月日葬于皂洋之北山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168172_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168172_comment'></div>人孰不贵，子之禄不逮其身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168172_comment'></div>人孰不寿，子之年止于二十有七，天乎命耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168172_comment'></div>予莫得而悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168172_comment'></div>惟子之志不得伸而利于人者最可悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168172_comment'></div>予幼学于乡序，及长举进士，与公明并研席者数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168172_comment'></div>公明居一室，方床，环列册书，而饮食寝休于其中，早夜读诵不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168172_comment'></div>群居谈噱，终日过耳，若无人笑语者，于是博通经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168172_comment'></div>予观公明而自省，日益脩励，即戏言小失，亦愧公明之知者，予之道获益于公明也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168172_comment'></div>间尝语予曰：「今世取士失其方，而仕者多所矜伐智诈以为材能，位通禄厚，侈心夸欲纵肆，使其风流沾染于下，媮靡败烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168172_comment'></div>我曹傥得志，正当立诚苦节，以代磨世俗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168172_comment'></div>予甚器其言，而未知其为利之博也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168172_comment'></div>自予入官，奔走四方，游京师，观世俗态状，益思其所以语我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168172_comment'></div>呜呼，公明亡矣，予思其言，则矍然检己之所为，使公明且存，其规我者岂少哉，此所以不独为今世惜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168172_comment'></div>公明讳晕，五代祖某，唐末因官入闽，兵乱不还，留居泉州之惠安县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168172_comment'></div>父处士君辅，以善行隐于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168172_comment'></div>妻陈氏，一男尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168172_comment'></div>嗟乎，公明之不显，匪予谁咎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168172_comment'></div>词以纾哀，刻之墓下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168172_comment'></div>后千万年，指此丘曰，贤者之宅，无敢或坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168172_comment'></div>庆历四年三月二十二日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1168172_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c0f391acfe82490abf6057a4e7e0f85d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c0f391acfe82490abf6057a4e7e0f85d");'><span id='c0f391acfe82490abf6057a4e7e0f85d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，34岁</div><div id='c0f391acfe82490abf6057a4e7e0f85d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年2月</a>　蔡襄挈妻孥还乡拜亲。旋复规划在兴化军城南营建新宅。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1a310a5f6ec841139f47a17cbc09bd5e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1a310a5f6ec841139f47a17cbc09bd5e");'><span id='1a310a5f6ec841139f47a17cbc09bd5e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>，37岁</div><div id='1a310a5f6ec841139f47a17cbc09bd5e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年1月</a>　正月，蔡襄因巡列部郡，护送双亲回家乡安居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年3月</a>　三月，蔡襄再还家，作《三月再还家》<div id='poem_249151' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249151' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249151?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三月再还家</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249151")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249151_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249151'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249151'>晓树乡关路，春衣使者轺。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249151'>江眠闻落霰，野饭掇新苗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249151'>入里威棱减，宁亲喜气饶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249151'>勤勤父师教，民病若为消。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249151_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249151'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249151_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7c7b4ae156eb4a3e9dd67edc01cfee39_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7c7b4ae156eb4a3e9dd67edc01cfee39");'><span id='7c7b4ae156eb4a3e9dd67edc01cfee39_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1050')">1048-1050年</a>，37-39岁</div><div id='7c7b4ae156eb4a3e9dd67edc01cfee39' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年10月</a>　十月，蔡襄父琇卒于家，因携眷返乡奔丧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年11月12日</a>　蔡襄作《与答户曹叶君书》答叶任。<div id='poem_1167890' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167890' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167890?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答户曹叶君书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年11月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167890")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167890_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167890'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167890'>十一月十二日，襄顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167890_comment'></div>比闻足下有阃中之忧，方执丧在疚，礼不得吊，又以闻之过时，不果修问，为重惭栗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167890_comment'></div>今奉书，以襄撰次先丈表志，勤勤为谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167890_comment'></div>襄尝以为文者当有典法，言之于今而见者可信，传之于后而闻者无疑，是曰文已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167890_comment'></div>自惟所作不逮前人，故论述功德，以称当世之士大夫者莫敢当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167890_comment'></div>足下以里中之旧，顷以见命，虽复编次事实，第不能赞发贤者之光，而充满孝思之志，用是为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167890_comment'></div>足下过怀谦抑，为意惇厚，殊非望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167890_comment'></div>惶悚惶悚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167890_comment'></div>冬寒，幸饮食自寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167890_comment'></div>蔡襄顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167890_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年12月15日</a>　蔡襄致书谢陈铸。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年12月</a>　十二月，蔡襄接苏舜钦来信慰唁，不日又接到讣告，哀伤不已。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　蔡襄在家守制，作《祭陈比部文》<div id='poem_1168206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭陈比部文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168206")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168206'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168206'>自某行服，退居里门，岁时书问，词意敦勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168206_comment'></div>今君顺化，闻信悽烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168206_comment'></div>襄也法不往吊，言实无文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168206_comment'></div>犹凭薄奠，远感英魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168206_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1168206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年11月</a>　十一月，服除，蔡襄被召赴京复职。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6fd8ac0721cf4096847725e6d4b0b708_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6fd8ac0721cf4096847725e6d4b0b708");'><span id='6fd8ac0721cf4096847725e6d4b0b708_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，45岁</div><div id='6fd8ac0721cf4096847725e6d4b0b708' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　五月中至下旬，蔡襄自泉州返枫亭故家。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c82ee79c329a4bcb8525d6f35488350d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c82ee79c329a4bcb8525d6f35488350d");'><span id='c82ee79c329a4bcb8525d6f35488350d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，45岁</div><div id='c82ee79c329a4bcb8525d6f35488350d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　元月下旬，蔡襄抵家。<br /></div>
-----end

安庆
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='28e721aaf92e4e0aab6337cc19b22bed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("28e721aaf92e4e0aab6337cc19b22bed");'><span id='28e721aaf92e4e0aab6337cc19b22bed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>，18岁</div><div id='28e721aaf92e4e0aab6337cc19b22bed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1029&endYear=1029')">1029年</a>　蔡襄过舒州桐城得梦兆，有诗。作品：《梦中作》<div id='poem_249102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>梦中作<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1029年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249102")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249102_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_249102_0'>① 年十八时入京就进士举，过舒州相城梦中作</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249102'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249102'>白玉楼台第一天，琪花风静彩鸾眠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249102'>谁人得似秦台女，吹彻云箫上紫烟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249102_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249102'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249102_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='753a1301859b43eba99b84db91b00383_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("753a1301859b43eba99b84db91b00383");'><span id='753a1301859b43eba99b84db91b00383_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年春</a>　春，蔡襄赴吏部铨选，受漳州军事判官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9133fb3b19504b0091223c8c95fa6e55_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9133fb3b19504b0091223c8c95fa6e55");'><span id='9133fb3b19504b0091223c8c95fa6e55_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，25岁</div><div id='9133fb3b19504b0091223c8c95fa6e55' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　蔡襄抵京都，待选。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年5月</a>　范仲淹因“越因职言事”贬官，余靖论救之，尹洙请同贬，欧阳修移书责右司谏高若讷，亦先后被黜。蔡襄作长篇组诗《四贤一不肖》讽之。名声大震，契丹使买书归，张于幽州馆。作品：《四贤一不肖五首》<div id='poem_249334' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249334' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249334?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四贤一不肖诗 范希文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249334")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249334_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249334'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249334'>中朝鸾鹤何仪仪，慷慨大体能者谁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249334'>之人起家用儒业，驰骋古今无所遗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249334'>当年得从谏官列，天庭一露胸中奇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249334'>矢身受责甘如荠，沃然华实相葳蕤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249334'>汉文不见贾生久，诏书晓落东南涯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249334'>归来俯首文石陛，尹以京兆天子毗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249334'>名都翼翼郡国首，里区百万多占辞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249334'>豪宗贵倖矜意气，半言主者承其颐。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249334'>昂昂孤立中不倚，传经决讼无牵羁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249334'>老奸黠吏束其手，众口和附歌且怡。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249334'>日朝黄幄迩天问，帝前大画当今宜。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249334'>文陈疏举时密启，此语多秘世莫知。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249334'>传者籍籍十得一，一者已足为良医。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249334'>一麾出守番君国，惜此智虑无所施。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249334'>吾君睿明广视听，四招邦俊隆邦基。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249334'>廷臣谏列复钳口，安得长喙号丹墀。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249334'>昼歌夕寝心如疚，咄哉汝忧非汝为。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249334'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_249334_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249332' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249332' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249332?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四贤一不肖诗 余安道</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249332")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249332_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249332'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249332'>南方之强君子居，卓然安道襟韵孤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249332'>词科判等屡得隽，呀然鼓焰天地垆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249332'>三年待诏处京邑，斗粟不足荣妻孥。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249332'>耳闻心虑朝家事，螭头比奏帝日都。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249332'>校书计课当序进，丽赋集仙来显涂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249332'>诰墨未乾寻已夺，不夺不为君子儒。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249332'>前日希文坐言事，手提敕教东南趋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249332'>希文鲠亮素少与，失势谁复能相扶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249332'>崭然安道生头角，气虹万丈横天衢。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249332'>臣靖胸中有屈语，举嗌不避萧斧诛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249332'>使臣仲淹在庭列，日献陛下之嘉谟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249332'>刺史荣官虽重寄，奈何一郡卷不舒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249332'>言非由位固当罪，随漕扁舟尽室俱。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249332'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_249332", 249332, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>炎陬</span>此去数千里，橐中狼籍惟蠹书。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249332'>高冠长佩丛阙下，千百其群诃尔愚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249332'>吾知万世更万世，凛凛英风激懦夫。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249332_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249332'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_249332_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249331' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249331' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249331?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四贤一不肖诗 尹师鲁</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249331")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249331_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249331'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249331'>君子道合久以成，小人利合久以倾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249331'>世道下衰交以利，遂使周雅称嘤鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249331'>煌煌大都足轩冕，绰有风采为名卿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249331'>高名重位盖当世，退朝归舍宾已盈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249331'>胁肩谄笑不知病，指天报遇如要盟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249331'>一朝势夺德未改，万钧已与毫釐轻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249331'>畏威谀上亦随毁，矧复鼓舌加其评。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249331'>逶迤阴拱质气厚，两豆塞耳心无营。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249331'>呜呼古人不可见，今人可见谁与明。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249331'>章章节义尹师鲁，饬躬佩道为华荣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249331'>希文被罪激人怒，君独欣慕如平生。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249331'>抗书毂下自论劾，惟善与恶宜汇征。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249331'>削官窜逐虽适楚，一语不挂离骚经。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249331'>当年亦有大臣逐，朋邪隐缩无主名。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249331'>希文果若事奸险，何此吉士同其声。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249331'>高谭本欲悟人主，岂独区区交友情。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249331_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249331'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_249331_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249333' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249333' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249333?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四贤一不肖诗 欧阳永叔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249333")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249333_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249333'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249333'>先民至论推天常，补衮扶世为儒方。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249333'>圜冠博带不知本，樗栎安可施青黄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249333'>帝图日盛人世出，今吾永叔诚有望。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249333'>处心学士贵适用，异端莫得窥其墙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249333'>子年五月范京兆，服天子命临鄱阳。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249333'>二贤拜疏赎其罪，势若止沸反扬汤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249333'>敕令百执无越位，谏垣何以敢封囊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249333'>哀来激愤抑复奋，强食不得下喉吭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249333'>位卑无路自闻达，目视云阙高苍茫。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249333'>裁书数幅责司谏，落笔騄骥腾康庄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249333'>刃迎缕析解统要，其间大意可得详。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249333'>书曰希文有本末，学通古今气果刚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249333'>始自理官来秘阁，不五六岁为天章。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249333'>上心倚若左右手，日备顾问邻清光。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249333'>苟尔希文实邪佞，曷不开口论否臧。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249333'>阴观被谴始丑诋，摧枯拉腐奚为彊。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249333'>傥曰希文实贤士，因言被责庸何伤。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249333'>汉杀王章与长倩，当时岂曰诛贤良。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249333'>惟时谏官亦结舌，不曰可谏曰罪当。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249333'>遂今百世览前史，往往心愤涕泗滂。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249333'>斯言感切固已至，读者不得令激昂。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249333'>岂图反我为怨府，袖书乞怜天子傍。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249333'>谪官一邑固分耳，恨不剖腹呈琳琅。<div id='poem_sentence_22_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_249333'>我嗟时辈识君浅，但推藻翰高文场。<div id='poem_sentence_23_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_249333'>斯人满腹有儒术，使之得地能施张。<div id='poem_sentence_24_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_249333'>皇家太平几百载，正当鉴古修纪纲。<div id='poem_sentence_25_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_249333'>贤才进用忠言录，祖述圣德垂无疆。<div id='poem_sentence_26_249333_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_249333'></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_249333_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249335' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249335' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249335?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四贤一不肖诗 高若讷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249335")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249335_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249335'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249335'>人禀天地中和生，气之正者为诚明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249335'>诚明所钟皆贤杰，从容中道无攲倾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249335'>嘉谋谠论范京兆，激奸纠缪扬王庭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249335'>积羽沈舟毁销骨，正人无徒奸者朋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249335'>主知胶固未遐弃，两轓五马犹专城。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249335'>欧阳秘阁官职卑，欲雪忠良无路岐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249335'>累幅长书快幽愤，一责司谏心无疑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249335'>人谓高君如挞市，出见缙绅无面皮。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249335'>高君携书奏天子，游言容色仍怡怡。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249335'>反谓范文谋疏阔，投彼南方诚为宜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249335'>永叔忤意窜西蜀，不免一中谗人机。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249335'>汲黯尝纠公孙诈，弘于上前多谢之。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249335'>上待公孙礼益厚，当时史官犹刺讥。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249335'>司谏不能自引咎，复将己过扬当时。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249335'>四公称贤尔不肖，谗言易入天难欺。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249335'>朝家若有观风使，此语请与风人诗。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249335_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249335'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_249335_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_0_249175'>申命增华衮，遗忠动紫宸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249175'>世风存令子，暮哭有慈亲。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年冬</a>　蔡襄作《送任山归河东》，送任山归太原。<div id='poem_249384' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249384' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a
