ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年11月</a>　十一月初，蔡襄为林冀作《尚书屯田员外郎林君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168176' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168176' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168176?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田员外郎林君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168176")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168176_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168176'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168176'>君讳冀，字希圣，潮州海阳人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168176_comment'></div>曾祖珍、祖知艺，皆以厚行为乡人所慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168176_comment'></div>父洪裔，赠殿中丞，少喜学问，手钞经史传记数千万言，日讲讽自休，以是终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168176_comment'></div>母夫人许氏，封颍川县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168176_comment'></div>君既胜冠，得所藏旧书，益刻厉，考治以为词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168176_comment'></div>大中祥符八年一举中进士第，历辰、惠二州从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168176_comment'></div>以判入高等，乃授大理丞，又迁殿中丞、太常博士，入尚书省为屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168176_comment'></div>历知歙州绩溪及歙二县，治有善迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168176_comment'></div>移同判桂州，以母老还官事归养，不得，请改知梅州，被丧去职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168176_comment'></div>及还朝，复官通判杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168176_comment'></div>宝元元年，三司度支副使段公少连荐君监京师征算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168176_comment'></div>二年十一月戊子疾发且殆，其子从先取股肉杂糜飧以进，祈疾少瘉，卒以其月庚子终于官所，年五十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168176_comment'></div>康定二年十一月初八日，即葬于大墓之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168176_comment'></div>夫人黄氏，封万年县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168176_comment'></div>持躬有法式，处大族，上下无异言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168176_comment'></div>子男从先、从思、从可，皆孝谨力学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168176_comment'></div>女三人，长适进士卢几，次适邵武县尉阮邈，其季始笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168176_comment'></div>孙六人皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168176_comment'></div>君读书不以博记广闻为志，务躬行其所知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168176_comment'></div>平居与众言，开陈理要，或持异论，亦未尝力辨以屈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168176_comment'></div>及莅官当事，前有事势可压以夺人者，君自守益固其直而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168176_comment'></div>在辰州时，五溪夷獠啸聚攻剽，城中益兵以守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168176_comment'></div>君从所分卒，往来督运粮饷，每先期至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168176_comment'></div>事平，诏褒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168176_comment'></div>歙州旧常第民资产，岁敛钱三千万，佣僦舟人挽浙江盐，鬻以牟利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168176_comment'></div>久之，民愈病，或冗散旁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168176_comment'></div>转运使以利病闻，仍表君为歙县，兼总运盐事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168176_comment'></div>君至，更请募人为卒，度材为舟，岁漕益多，而敛不逮下，流者还集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168176_comment'></div>其服劳革弊，举是，馀可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168176_comment'></div>初，君卒，将作监丞黄君瑊以书至洛谓襄曰：「林氏诸孤，哀不能言，将扶持全柩，背淮绝江山，出吴闽数千里，还故乡以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168176_comment'></div>幸而得子之文以铭其先烈，不亦慰诸幽乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168176_comment'></div>襄明道中从官漳州，始遇君郡下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168176_comment'></div>君以某为志于古者，作诗称誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168176_comment'></div>呜呼，今以是铭君墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168176_comment'></div>辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1168176'>求而勿懈者享则既丰，委而不与者畀乃弗充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168176_comment'></div>覃延厥后兮绍德收功，列文幽堂兮以讯无穷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1168176_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年冬</a>　冬，蔡襄为内兄葛宏撰书《葛君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葛君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168177")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168177'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168177'>君讳宏，字文渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168177_comment'></div>先世居广陵，唐末广陵兵起，举族渡江而南，至江阴，遂留家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168177_comment'></div>曾大父讳㣑，以耆德闻于乡邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168177_comment'></div>大父讳详，少尝负知能，谓于时无所用，不若施于吾家以自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168177_comment'></div>乃力于田数十年，累致巨资，益散施以广名称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168177_comment'></div>父惟明，一举进士不中，退而积书数百千卷，戒子孙业之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168177_comment'></div>君始稚，已能去纷侈，从乡党之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168177_comment'></div>既长，记诵通博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168177_comment'></div>由乡举至京师，视等辈之贤己者，咸尽诚礼，屏所挟焉而下之，故与游多闻世之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168177_comment'></div>意气豪举，文章亦甚壮健，不能工偶配皂白，剪磨细碎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168177_comment'></div>以是五试春官辄触罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168177_comment'></div>晚乃寄隐于酒，观少年新学蹑其后，跳取贵盛，一以命决，不挂于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168177_comment'></div>然以己之所学稽本于古人，揣称当世之务甚悉，茍汩焉无闻，孰与发而在人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168177_comment'></div>庆历元年秋，诏选进士，君时以沾疾，犹强力持笔研，属文辞以求贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168177_comment'></div>比归，益疾殆，九月四日终于家，享年五十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168177_comment'></div>以某日葬于青阳乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168177_comment'></div>母夫人承氏与君之父皆年七十馀，而哭其冢子哀甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168177_comment'></div>夫人耿氏躬率礼德，以宜其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168177_comment'></div>子男钧、铸、镗皆向学敦谨，将大其世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168177_comment'></div>二女，长适进士陈贤乂，其季尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168177_comment'></div>君于襄为婚兄弟，求知君之深而宜铭其圹者，襄不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168177_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1168177'>悲乎文渊，学足以辨兴亡之端，而文足以通义理之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168177_comment'></div>卒不克施，其命矣夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1168177_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年1月</a>　一月，蔡襄为莆田陈铸作《陈殿丞送行诗序》<div id='poem_1168053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈殿丞送行诗序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年正月三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168053")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168053'>康定元年，殿中丞陈君铸师回通判福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168053_comment'></div>且去京师，朝之名卿继作歌诗以重其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168053_comment'></div>师回至官之明年，发橐中所得七十二篇，拜走书属襄序其篇首，将刻之石而传于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168053_comment'></div>夫送远之作，必称其事而附为之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168053_comment'></div>师回以文章中甲科，间十六年而为监郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168053_comment'></div>然所治距家才百馀里，奉母夫人官舍，以申孝养之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168053_comment'></div>古之人有以亲故，不择禄而仕者，而师回之禄足以充其养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168053_comment'></div>今之仕者，东西南北或千万里，士大夫得便其家者得相庆幸，而师回又以侍其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168053_comment'></div>然则群公诗之足以劝夫为人子者志乎侈大而远于孝养者，不为空言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168053_comment'></div>若夫闽州之胜，城中三山，山之下，海之潮汐至焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168053_comment'></div>有鱼虾蠃蚌之饶，黄柑丹荔之实，并山又有竹林泉石旷清雅绝之美，可以宴喜而娱游，或杂言之，亦诗人之博兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168053_comment'></div>庆历元年正月三日，著作佐郎、馆阁校勘蔡襄序。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1168053'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1168053_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年春</a>　春，蔡襄作《寄尹师鲁书》，称赞其为文替耿傅辩诬。<div id='poem_1167877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄尹师鲁书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167877")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167877'>襄顿首上师鲁十二兄：去年春，平凉之役，官军失利，师鲁时为经略判官，兵事始末，宜得其详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167877_comment'></div>若耿傅者忠死而毁，尤可哀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167877_comment'></div>初，朝廷褒傅以谏议大夫，而官其五子，于是浮谤兴焉，谓傅迫诸将进军以败，行赏过厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167877_comment'></div>襄窃以谓，诸将多大官，而进退之令，宜有所从出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167877_comment'></div>傅之官微，仅为其部督运粮馈，于势安能制迫诸将哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167877_comment'></div>借使与谋，于其死也，不犹愈于临危茍免、保宠自安者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167877_comment'></div>然谈者籍籍，徒以私智称度，无所据依，莫之辟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167877_comment'></div>及谒告还家，造辞参政晁公，方以西事为念，称叹没者之忠节，因言：耿傅始以书劝诸将勿轻进兵，择利而动，诸将之议不一，遂战而没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167877_comment'></div>襄乃以傅之所以死者明白无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167877_comment'></div>道中作《耿谏议传》，报书一通，寓于欧阳永叔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167877_comment'></div>比襄归京师，则见者多矣，是非或参焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167877_comment'></div>然襄所以云云者，非特弭傅之谤，抑亦为忠义唱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167877_comment'></div>虽群非无愧，况有是焉者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167877_comment'></div>近闻师鲁著《辨诬》、《悯忠》二文，其《辨诬》一篇，为傅发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167877_comment'></div>虽未得其书以观，而推迹其名之所谓，从可知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167877_comment'></div>或曰：「师鲁于耿傅，同事西鄙，相得甚厚，不应作文以辨，盖类夫私与者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167877_comment'></div>襄对曰：「诚而无私，君子之志也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167877_comment'></div>以嫌为避，硁硁者之为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167877_comment'></div>诚而无私也者，不以亲疏置于其间，惟其公而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167877_comment'></div>以其相得之厚，嫌而避之，反乃私也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167877_comment'></div>且疏者不知，而知者不言，则死者之志于何而明哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167877_comment'></div>或者遂解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167877_comment'></div>师鲁居忧河南时，襄为留守从事，始识耿君，其为人材智勇敢，固已推重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167877_comment'></div>若夫道义，则交渐劘之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167877_comment'></div>今者惟义之恤，而死焉不避，襄以是自疚于知耿君之为未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167877_comment'></div>嗟乎，体节殊处，适以招毁！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167877_comment'></div>甚哉，世人莫肯树夫善也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167877_comment'></div>唐安禄山之乱，颜杲卿陷贼，支解中桥，至死骂贼不休，而小说者以杲卿前已向贼，既而悔之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167877_comment'></div>就令杲卿始向而终悔，何为仇贼之坚如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167877_comment'></div>万万无是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167877_comment'></div>杲卿忠烈贯于幽明，而垂之无穷，而好事者忍加诬之，亦何种人也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167877_comment'></div>观古人之遭诬，常为之痛愤，况亲识其人而审其故，得不为之动心也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167877_comment'></div>顷见师鲁为耿君作其先君墓铭，其祖盖亦死国者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167877_comment'></div>今录其传以往，愿增补之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167877_comment'></div>并《辨诬》篇还以为贶，幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167877_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167877_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1167877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　蔡襄上《乞戒励安抚使书》<div id='poem_1167791' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167791' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167791?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞戒励安抚使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（康定二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167791")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167791_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167791'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167791'>朝奉郎、秘书省著作佐郎、充馆阁校勘臣襄谨昧死再拜，上书尊号皇帝陛下：臣伏睹临遣使臣循行郡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167791_comment'></div>臣窃谓人主宅中国，居法宫，而使幽遐异域风谣习尚、冤隐沈抑无一不陈于前者，其道何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167791_comment'></div>托聪明于臣下故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167791_comment'></div>人主知其所托之为难，明赏罚以驭之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167791_comment'></div>赏罚既明，则臣下不敢蔽欺，而聪明无所壅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167791_comment'></div>今天下之俗，至有钜室富家兼并货财，作为奢靡，超踰法制，交通大吏，欺轹愚弱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167791_comment'></div>而贫者父子转流，无养生送死之具，不幸孤独废疾，不得终其天年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167791_comment'></div>州县吏既不能掩遏豪强，矜哀穷厄，而又侵牟渔夺，不识休已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167791_comment'></div>或愚谬昏耄，无所是非，或依倚权势，坏裂公法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167791_comment'></div>其焯然有状可指数也，监刺之官，大率以宽纾含隐为良，即发一奸赃，众辄指目，以是须其自败，乃始纠擿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167791_comment'></div>或有所私虑，垂败之人亦加意覆藏，使得脱去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167791_comment'></div>甚哉，蔽蒙如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167791_comment'></div>监司之设，仅与无同，欲百姓之无害，其可得乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167791_comment'></div>吏之偷茍姑息，寖以成俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167791_comment'></div>顷年遣使安抚诸郡，比其还奏，荐举虽多，而蠹暴不察，是徒取善誉而空厥职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167791_comment'></div>夫收材选能，诚为治之首务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167791_comment'></div>然恶吏不除，穷民不恤，有使之出，不若无出之愈，徒使郡国之民交口而议，曰：是举也，特与被遣之人为荣进梯绠耳，岂有意于吾民哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167791_comment'></div>臣窃见汉武帝遣谒者博士分巡天下，存问孝悌力田、鳏寡孤独，赐帛有差，独行君子遣诣行在，而治苛者奏举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167791_comment'></div>又唐太宗遣杜淹巡关内诸州，出御府金赎贫民男女自卖者还其父母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167791_comment'></div>其后又遣褚遂良等二十二人以六条巡察四方，黜陟官吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167791_comment'></div>臣详观古之遣使，皆务恤穷民，除恶吏，举材能，收滞逸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167791_comment'></div>请令使者所至之郡，存问乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167791_comment'></div>其孝行著闻，及年八十九十以上、鳏寡笃疾，依汉故事，量予布帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167791_comment'></div>即贫无所养，而有男女僦佣于人，偿其馀直而追还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167791_comment'></div>若为僧尼，僧年四十、尼年三十以下，并除其籍而归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167791_comment'></div>更无此等子孙，官给糇粮，责任亲党邻里养之，以没其齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167791_comment'></div>孤独者，戒敕所养之家务全其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167791_comment'></div>冤结无告，使者择吏而治其曲直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167791_comment'></div>力行笃学，衰老沦滞，表之以劝风俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167791_comment'></div>郡县吏治绩可称，条例其状，显褒其尤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167791_comment'></div>贪墨腥闻，即令责讯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167791_comment'></div>材不任职，于其职之相伦者易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167791_comment'></div>或虽洁廉，而违法惨刻，及年七十以上，昏耄而不知退者，咸以名闻，愿一切罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167791_comment'></div>其官吏贪墨，因使擿发，监司之官素所不纠，随而坐之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167791_comment'></div>即使者不纠，异日倾败，事在使者循行已前，并使者坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167791_comment'></div>伏唯陛下垂意生民，而恩泽未大洽于下者，盖督责官吏未尽其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167791_comment'></div>方使者之行，因幸严赐告谕，令其毕力推扬德音以致于下，究悉利害，庶有补于政治，毋徒使郡县供具，吏民遮列道途，迎候往来，重为此纷扰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167791_comment'></div>狂愚之言，愿陛下省览财择，天下幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167791_comment'></div>臣昧死再拜谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1167791_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　蔡襄上《乞罢减降疏》<div id='poem_1167794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢减降疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167794")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167794'>臣伏睹比年以来，盛夏之月陛下亲虑京师系囚，令天下负罪者减降，便从轻典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167794_comment'></div>此盖陛下嗟悯元元重罹禁网，冒炎暑之苦而处狴犴之下，天衷恻然，下宽大之诏，实群生之厚幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167794_comment'></div>臣愚无智虑，不能识天地无垠之施，而窃有惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167794_comment'></div>臣闻古先帝王躬虑狱囚，皆以决疏冤滞，非特专宥过戾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167794_comment'></div>迫隆冬、缘亢旱，则或行之，非一定而不易之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167794_comment'></div>向者国家行之比三年矣，编户之民习蹈前事，咸指时月，轻触宪度，岂非屡行之乃滋而为弊？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167794_comment'></div>夫法者，天下大公之本也，故罪有小大，法有轻重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167794_comment'></div>今所丽者大罪，而所处者轻法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167794_comment'></div>以非其罪邪，虽轻法不得施，安在降其等乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167794_comment'></div>诚当其罪耶，重法尚不足以禁，顾轻之，何以革小人之心而驱之向善哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167794_comment'></div>国家每郊礼必大赦，贷民之罪，固不鲜矣，又仍岁有疏决减降之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167794_comment'></div>臣谓贫弱者多负冤，而富强者多蒙宥，为惠甚小，而其蠹甚大，非有补于治体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167794_comment'></div>伏望陛下参前古之制，拯当今之弊，罢减降之诏，而责天下州郡吏审辨狱情而无久系也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167794_comment'></div>臣职贱而言近，不胜陨越之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167794_comment'></div>臣襄昧死再拜，谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1167794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　蔡襄上《论疏决罪人事疏》<div id='poem_1167795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论疏决罪人事疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167795")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167795'>臣伏闻朝廷疏决罪人有日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167795_comment'></div>臣窃思古之亲虑狱囚，所以申冤隐而出滞淹，非特务宽大而成小惠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167795_comment'></div>近年夏月疏决，例从减放，闾巷之人，谓之「热恩」，指期作过，比比皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167795_comment'></div>夫刑者辅治之本，岂可使民预知而故犯哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167795_comment'></div>然行之且久，恐难即罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167795_comment'></div>伏望陛下临问之时，择其情理最重者特与严断一二事，庶使下民知惧，不敢指恩为罪，乃陛下之深仁也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年10月</a>　十月，蔡襄为岳母承氏撰书《葛处士夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168178' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168178' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168178?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葛处士夫人墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168178")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168178_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168178'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168178'>夫人姓承氏，世为江阴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168178_comment'></div>居其家，以孝谨称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168178_comment'></div>父讳怀与，择其里中人以行闻者而归之，遂嫁为处士葛君惟明之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168178_comment'></div>当夫人之归，葛氏方为大姓，族属亲疏，姑姊娣姒，节时往来，佩簪缨，珥序列，庆贺者甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168178_comment'></div>夫人处其间，自少至壮且老，卒无与忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168178_comment'></div>孝妇于尊章，恭畏自力，姑于其妇，益慰爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168178_comment'></div>故其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168178_comment'></div>虽亲者不敢少慢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168178_comment'></div>而死也，虽疏者哭之亦尽其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168178_comment'></div>享年七十有六，其终于庆历二年八月五日，以十月二十日葬于青阳乡脩德里之原下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168178_comment'></div>生子八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168178_comment'></div>男五人：宏、求皆举进士，不中第，卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168178_comment'></div>定、向勤养不懈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168178_comment'></div>宜上书论边兵利害，得本军司仕参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168178_comment'></div>孙六人，钧最为长，既有子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168178_comment'></div>女三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168178_comment'></div>长适屯田员外郎凌景阳，封丹阳县君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168178_comment'></div>次适进士陈玉，皆先夫人而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168178_comment'></div>季女之婿、著作佐郎、馆阁校勘蔡襄为志其所葬，而又铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1168178'>夫人于家，淑孝则闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168178_comment'></div>既归而宜，法度是勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168178_comment'></div>有子入官，女为士妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168178_comment'></div>冢妇持孙，福祉实多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168178_comment'></div>三月而葬，中礼之常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168178_comment'></div>考卜既吉，冥文以藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1168178_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年11月</a>　十一月，应同年进士陈大素之请，为其父陈光现撰书《赠殿中丞陈府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠殿中丞陈府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168179")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168179'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168179'>府君之先，曾祖讳沆，本魏人，仕后唐，因官江东，为钱吴越王伪署朝散郎、知明州鄞县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168179_comment'></div>卒葬四明山下，子孙始为吴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168179_comment'></div>王父讳镗，声名出吴中，钱氏欲以补阙官起之，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168179_comment'></div>皇考讳处莹，博学，于《周易》、扬雄《太玄》尤推悉其要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168179_comment'></div>钱氏数以礼屈致，冀得为用，亦避不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168179_comment'></div>及钱氏以地归本朝，遂徙居京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168179_comment'></div>府君既长矣，传解经术，尤工楷法，得善书，多手钞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168179_comment'></div>尝梦人有授其蓍者，因专意治《易》，其得要妙，皆诚心潜通，不扳旧书师说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168179_comment'></div>贵游大人或即其居而讯祸福，府君曰：「吾老于《易》，于是求圣人心焉，又以其数度天地万物消长，及天下之所以兴废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168179_comment'></div>人之穷通不足引吾术以證」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168179_comment'></div>愈闭距不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168179_comment'></div>日与诸子考经传疑说，雍然自娱，垂四十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168179_comment'></div>以大中祥符四年八月十四日终，年六十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168179_comment'></div>男三人：长曰见素，终尚书屯田员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168179_comment'></div>曰大素，字仲华，秘书丞、审刑详议官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168179_comment'></div>曰元素，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168179_comment'></div>女二人：长适进士卢冲，次适殿中丞潘轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168179_comment'></div>府君讳光现，字晦之，以子登朝，累赠殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168179_comment'></div>娶吴兴范氏，追封本县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168179_comment'></div>以庆历二年十一月二十七日葬河南缑氏县唐兴乡蒋里，以吴兴太君祔焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168179_comment'></div>仲华于某同年中进士第，先葬，以其世家，来请铭刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168179_comment'></div>铭之言名也，列其先德以及自名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168179_comment'></div>府君之德著，而嗣子继以仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168179_comment'></div>仲华涖官廉平，以材能称于时，将大其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168179_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1168179'>世以善脩而贱贫者，或验于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168179_comment'></div>若府君究《易》之本，行洁而坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168179_comment'></div>其享之厚，孰与夫空富且贵者耶？</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1168179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年11月</a>　十一月，蔡襄撰书《安州孝感县井记》<div id='poem_1168111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安州孝感县井记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历二年十一月十六日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168111")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168111'>欧阳君宗颜始作安州云梦尉，自以事辨治如何，岂下官不足以为哉，乃厉精举职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168111_comment'></div>庆历元年，今资政殿大学士、尚书右丞范公时将其州，表君才能，移孝感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168111_comment'></div>孝感之民负饮旁渎，若岁雨潦溢，汲者罂缶颠道，寒而冰，旱而淤，取远难致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168111_comment'></div>君至，则令其民曰：「吾将井以饮汝，孰与者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168111_comment'></div>百姓奔哗，皆曰：「能是，瘉我病矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168111_comment'></div>相与出雇钱，陶塼治佣以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168111_comment'></div>君为之相所宜地，发之，得泉甘美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168111_comment'></div>其年夏秋不雨，土膏乾燥，他水日索，而泉出愈甘，源来无穷，民益异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168111_comment'></div>又相与砻石乞文，以识其始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168111_comment'></div>古有厮陂渠，教农种，殖货财，或功利饶于人而资于国者，前史书志皆特载而详言之，以法于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168111_comment'></div>以君之智力，使有能知而用之者，尽所谋为，则功利可量哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168111_comment'></div>名氏宜得附书志以显，况复井上铭耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168111_comment'></div>然尉之官微，莫得自效，因井之利而纪之，以永其人之思，且君后果用是以验云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168111_comment'></div>二年十一月十六日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1168111_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　蔡襄作《送杨渥赴西安主簿》，送杨渥赴西安主薄任。作品：《送杨渥赴西安主薄》<div id='poem_249387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送杨渥赴西安主簿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249387")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249387'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249387'>余思去夏还瓯闽，温风赤日争陶蒸。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249387'>舟行夜寄浙江棱，江涛汹涌来相仍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249387'>雷电翕虩蛟螭腾，方床竹簟寒生冰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249387'>上陇西去景色澄，青山两向水一縆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249387'>猿鸟啼叫交酬应，晚樵出雾鱼投罾。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249387'>脱离滓浊跻陵兢，造托微波讯严陵。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249387'>清遐可使贪者惩，山穷水尽乃攀登。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249387'>烂柯岩岫孤崚嶒，幽邃窥瞩崖险凭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249387'>少留观爱喜莫胜，子官其间良足称。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249387'>子材又美神粹凝，万象态度遭披凌。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249387'>吟咏设写踰画缯，当有味者论淄渑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249387'>今予痴仕如秋蝇，飞尘满耳汗浃膺。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249387'>闻子大艑行可乘，骨目森竦神虑兴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249387'>子姑去嗟予未能，送子一念魂九升。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249387_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249387'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_249387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1042&endYear=1042')">1042年</a>　蔡襄作长诗《李山英以疾归田客有言山英移书石守道者因摭取其略作诗以送之》，送李山英归山东。<div id='poem_249359' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249359' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249359?labeling=true' target='_blank'>李山英以疾归田客有言山英移书石守道者因摭取其略作诗以送之</a><span class='authorDate'>（1042年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249359")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249359_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249359'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249359'>吾友守道气刚劲，丑邪扶直出天性。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249359'>意高身贱无所发，胸中事事先后并。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249359'>襄尝畏其大勇果，愿以中直为得正。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249359'>忽闻鲁士李山英，移书告之要力行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249359'>曰今天下最急务，边头战守羌夷横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249359'>异术纷回蠹化原，佞夫欺巧疵邦政。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249359'>生民失职馈敛繁，势若久旱方雩禜。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249359'>安得快雨洗长空，万物萧森蒙大庆。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249359'>古人有以身徇言，前者已僵后者更。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249359'>况值朝廷上宽大，苦谏兼容天子圣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249359'>我疾不幸子可属，或列封章或庭诤。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249359'>勿学得路世俗儿，软语妖歌日酣醟。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249359'>乃知山英落落者，支革虽疲心愈竞。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249359'>予思物理似颠倒，难用智愚准衰盛。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249359'>贤豪既少遇又稀，或老且困壮而病。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249359'>就令贵显亦迍踬，尤触阴机石临阱。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249359'>一思九叹起呼天，何等官曹司是柄。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249359'>由来宰主都冥寞，用舍惟时穷达命。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249359'>山英归去亦何恨，门外无尘春色净。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249359'>回看名宦似浮沤，都把雄心付觞咏。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249359_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249359'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_249359_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄撰书《临安海会寺殿记》<div id='poem_1168112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临安海会寺殿记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年正月十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168112")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168112'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168112'>杭州临安县海会寺，梁大同中始作，号曰「竹林」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168112_comment'></div>及五代贞明之初，钱吴越王又新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168112_comment'></div>王，县人也，少尝往来里中，困甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168112_comment'></div>已而跨有全吴，名贵地大，私念所从来，岂非阴有相我者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168112_comment'></div>且竹林最得山水佳趣，因大治之，益广前制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168112_comment'></div>当是时，吴中浮图居虽百千数，无是伦者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168112_comment'></div>大中祥符间，例易天下寺名，遂锡今额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168112_comment'></div>天禧五年冬十月火，通夕而墟，其徒散去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168112_comment'></div>总持僧有朋顾思惕然，以兴所废为己务，每说于众曰：「吾师之法，或资于塔庙，福报之来，称其所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168112_comment'></div>今殿适谋始，而大家力饶，不能厚施，异时名氏不齿篆载，反索气以后人，其可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168112_comment'></div>于是盛仁俊、张从实先输而唱之，又从而和之数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168112_comment'></div>以圆监元一、盛鋹兼筦度材砻石、塈茨阶级之役，积费钱三千万，行一十年而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168112_comment'></div>既成，列像其下，鼓钟其中，会合邑子而落之，墟者复庀，而散者还集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168112_comment'></div>昔钱王以一国之资基之于前，而有朋以一己之志继之于后，可谓能且勤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168112_comment'></div>庆历三年正月十五日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1168112_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年春</a>　春，蔡襄作《黼扆箴》并《别疏》虽奏状进上。<div id='poem_1168156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168156?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黼扆箴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168156")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1168156_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168156'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168156'>丕显元圣，上奉天时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1168156'>跻俗于礼，任材以宜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1168156'>肃治家政，大隆本支。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1168156'>好问益广，去邪勿迟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1168156'>利急思困，兵连虑危。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1168156'>法令必信，恩赏无私。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1168156'>威福是守，听断不疑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1168156'>太平可致，决所施为。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1168156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1168156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1168156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄作《明谏》奏议。<div id='poem_1168086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明谏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168086")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168086'>为谏之难，非进谏之难，难乎人主听而用之之难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168086_comment'></div>人主之于谏，有甚恶而用之者，其甚悦而怠之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168086_comment'></div>上虽恶谏，迫危亡者或用之也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168086_comment'></div>上虽悦谏，恃治平者或怠之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168086_comment'></div>非谏者之言工于危亡，而失于治平，盖上意之所加者，安危之势异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168086_comment'></div>是故为谏之患，莫先于怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168086_comment'></div>然世之人不究其本，而莫议其失，斯亦惑之甚乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168086_comment'></div>治平之世，人主无大过举，闻谏必深悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168086_comment'></div>然谏者多称前世危亡之事以为监，其言非有今日之明验，上必谓其阔迂而无所考信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168086_comment'></div>佞者得以迹而进其说，由御久安之势，贵乎循故袭常，无烦于更治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168086_comment'></div>于是人主怠心愈加焉，言入而无所是非，真伪浑并，虽外有纳谏之名，而无用之之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168086_comment'></div>忠言日衰而下情滋蔽，患莫先乎此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168086_comment'></div>夫称危亡者，庶乎惧危亡而不至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168086_comment'></div>恃其无有危亡之渐而至也，虽有圣智，不能为已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168086_comment'></div>前世论谏者曰「直谏为下」，以其迂险诞妄，陈指丑恶，易激其怒，不若详善其言使易行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168086_comment'></div>夫迂险诞妄，贤者不由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168086_comment'></div>深言以起怒，非谏者之过，其心岂欲取怒而自抳其所陈哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168086_comment'></div>进谏不能必于用，本乎直而已矣，不逆上之所用舍而枉其志也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168086_comment'></div>纳谏不必皆用，取乎是而已矣，不以其言之婉直而遗其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168086_comment'></div>然则赏谏贤乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168086_comment'></div>曰：与其怠也，宁赏，要之，中则异耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168086_comment'></div>使谏者言常忠也，画常善也，所谓能尽其心而不茍者也，岂志于赏乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168086_comment'></div>而赏之所设，思以辅忠气而开谠论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168086_comment'></div>然妄人随之资言以速进，甚者诡谲而紊政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168086_comment'></div>意茍得焉，喑嘿以自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168086_comment'></div>佞者乘而非之曰：「举天下之好言者均取贵仕耳，孰从而求信夫所谓忠谠者哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168086_comment'></div>于是贤者以进为己累，而寡言则赏焉，欲以劝而适以弭之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168086_comment'></div>故曰：纳谏不必皆用，辨是非则妄言息而忠言进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168086_comment'></div>终谏之说：离怠、戒赏、明用。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1168086_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄作《赏论》奏议。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　三月，仁宗复亲擢欧阳修、余靖、王素三人为谏官，蔡襄作《喜欧阳永叔余安道王仲仪除谏官》贺之。<div id='poem_249264' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249264' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249264?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喜欧阳永叔余安道王仲仪除谏官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249264")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249264_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249264'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249264'>御笔新除三谏官，士民千口尽相欢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249264'>昔时流落丹心在，自古忠贤得路难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249264'>好竭谋猷居帝右，直须风采动朝端。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249264'>人生万事皆尘土，惟是功名永远看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249264_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249264'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249264_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月</a>　四月，欧阳修等以襄诗荐于帝。诏除襄为秘书丞、知谏院，时称“四谏”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年4月</a>　夏四月，诏以夏竦为枢密使，韩琦、范仲淹为副使，蔡襄与欧阳修等交文章论夏竦不宜任枢密使，帝纳之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《论范仲淹、韩琦辞让状》<div id='poem_1167827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论范仲淹韩琦辞让状<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167827")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167827'>臣伏见陕西路招讨使韩琦、范仲淹等各除枢密副使，并以西寇未宁，恳辞恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167827_comment'></div>朝廷再赐手诏，督令赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167827_comment'></div>臣窃料琦等必再有陈论免让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167827_comment'></div>于未决之间，而异同之说有三焉：曰使琦、仲淹皆来也，曰一处乎内、一处乎外也，曰皆留在边也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167827_comment'></div>使之皆来者，此朝廷之本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167827_comment'></div>盖陛下推独断之明，采至公之论，以二人久处边陲，详知本末，致之密宥，思有更变，将以求破贼之计耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167827_comment'></div>然论者之说曰：边臣最苦者，奏报文字或有稽缓，或即裁损，动不如意，所以久无成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167827_comment'></div>今得边臣而任之，细大可知，表里相应也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167827_comment'></div>用兵不胜，由军制未立，无部分统辖之法，若不更变，未见可胜之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167827_comment'></div>今得边臣而任之，可责以更变之术，所以宜一者处乎内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167827_comment'></div>西寇虽已请盟，而戎心不可倚信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167827_comment'></div>琦等素习兵事，上下之情通浃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167827_comment'></div>今尽还朝，新帅郑戬，山川之险易未知，军旅之部伍未练，若贼乘我机便，忽有奔突，必难制御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167827_comment'></div>此所以宜一者留于外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167827_comment'></div>曰皆留在边者，此沮抑之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167827_comment'></div>恶琦、仲淹者若于陛下前百般毁短之，陛下必不信矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167827_comment'></div>若称其材德而言之，陛下不得不疑也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167827_comment'></div>必谓仲淹等威名已著，羌戎甚畏，今将去边，必有侵扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167827_comment'></div>臣谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167827_comment'></div>仲淹作招讨使，羌戎既畏其威名，今在枢府，正议兵谋，其畏必甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167827_comment'></div>若谓关中民情素所倚赖，今既还朝，众失所望，臣又谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167827_comment'></div>昔在陕西，民既倚赖，今在枢府，必陈利病而行之，所赖者愈大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167827_comment'></div>以是校之，情伪甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167827_comment'></div>然或者谓二人孰宜处于内外，臣以物议言之，二臣之忠勇，其心一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167827_comment'></div>若以才谋人望，则仲淹出韩琦之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167827_comment'></div>处内者谋之，而处外者行之，故仲淹宜来，琦当留边，于理甚当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167827_comment'></div>其韩琦、范仲淹，伏乞朝廷不听辞让，各授恩命，上以明陛下任贤之坚意，下以协众庶之公论也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1167827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄复疏请彻底罢免吕夷简。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　五六月间，因灾异连绵，蔡襄、余靖从天人感应论出发，连上《言灾异》奏议四篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《论元昊狂僭之计》等十二篇奏章，表达对西夏元昊请和的看法。<div id='poem_1167743' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167743' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167743?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赵元昊狂僭之计奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167743")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167743'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167743'>赵元昊弃其祖父盟约，妄为狂狡，僭称大号，不臣之迹彰著，朝廷大增边备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167743_comment'></div>议者皆谓，元昊遣人入朝，不从其所请，必寇边郡，以肆狂心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167743_comment'></div>臣切谓不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167743_comment'></div>戎狄之心，见利则动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167743_comment'></div>若元昊欲寇边，当去年未备之时，举众而来，势或难御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167743_comment'></div>于其时尚不入寇，今乃先自狂悖，待我边之皆有御然后入寇，亦有何利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167743_comment'></div>臣窃料元昊本无寇边之心，但张声势，欲求中国岁与货财耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1167743_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《论契丹遣使之意》等七篇奏章，对契丹之居心叵测提出看法。<div id='poem_1167753' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167753' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167753?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论契丹遣使之意奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167753")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167753_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167753'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167753'>契丹举兵征元昊以助中国，仍责以劫略之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167753_comment'></div>或曰：二虏互相疑贰，势不两雄，必有衅隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167753_comment'></div>臣谓契丹与元昊久矣亲好，元昊为中国边患，若与契丹结隙，则腹背受敌，元昊黠贼，岂有如此失策？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167753_comment'></div>假使契丹凌辱百端，元昊亦宁屈而就之，必无目下结隙之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167753_comment'></div>契丹今日之谋，主于自邀通和之功耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1167753_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄再上《乞通和之后早计费用》等六篇奏章。<div id='poem_1167747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞通和之后早计费用奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167747")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167747'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167747'>自赵元昊狂悖以来，朝廷日日发关东兵马，以为边郡守备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167747_comment'></div>然沿边州军，自来只约见在人马刍粟，为一二岁计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167747_comment'></div>今者增兵与马比旧必多数倍，至于馈运刍粟、转辇兵甲、修葺城塞、燕犒给赐之费日以益广，若终一岁而计之，其费用之物大率必倍多于每岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167747_comment'></div>既边兵未有罢期，则其费愈多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167747_comment'></div>臣恐年岁之后，必有议者建白，请赐元昊金帛与之通和者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167747_comment'></div>臣谓此谋非国家长久之计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167747_comment'></div>若元昊削去尊号，臣礼如旧，朝廷但赦其罪，亦不当大与金帛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167747_comment'></div>与之金帛，是为狂悖而得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167747_comment'></div>况元昊岂肯削去称号，何名而赐之金帛、与之通和哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167747_comment'></div>国家遗北虏，其费不少，若更与西虏通和，使北虏窥中国之强弱而启其狡心，非细事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167747_comment'></div>臣谓朝廷将来罢通和之议，莫若早计度减损费用之物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167747_comment'></div>茍费用不减于旧日，则何以持久而制狂虏也？</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1167747_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年7月</a>　七月，蔡襄与欧阳修奏请以范仲淹取代王举正为参知政事，帝纳之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《乞令御史中丞举属官状》<div id='poem_1167826' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167826' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167826?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞令御史中丞举属官状<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167826")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167826_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167826'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167826'>臣闻人主择宰辅，宰辅择长官，长官择寮佐，此至治之要、至简之术也、周命太仆，则曰「慎简乃僚」，汉之公府，令自辟召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167826_comment'></div>唐陆贽作相，奏请诸司长官各择属吏，后因谗谤，辄有变更，陆贽论之详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167826_comment'></div>又高元裕为御史中丞，上言：「御史纲纪之地，官属选用，宜得实才，其不称者，臣请黜之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167826_comment'></div>监察御史杜宣猷、李瑰等并出为府县之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167826_comment'></div>此皆前世专任长官之明验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167826_comment'></div>国朝诸司省监悉非本官，惟御史台职不殊古制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167826_comment'></div>方今台中条制，如台官不称职者，亦许纠举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167826_comment'></div>近年台官，宰辅避嫌，例不中除，多令两制参举，又限资考苛细，多不得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167826_comment'></div>盖由不宽资限，不责长官之弊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167826_comment'></div>近见御史中丞王拱宸奏举杨纮等充台官，朝廷循执旧规，下两制参举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167826_comment'></div>臣谓朝廷既任拱宸为中丞，若实非才，则当别择才者而任之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167826_comment'></div>若才堪其任，则所谓属官，可悉委之，未为过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167826_comment'></div>况拱宸于官属请去不才者，而更择才者，是尽心于朝廷，不避众怨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167826_comment'></div>今御史席平已出润州，若参举之人又得软懦倾险之士，则何以处之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167826_comment'></div>臣故谓莫若专任长官，宽其资限，则责有所归也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167826_comment'></div>臣乞御史台官属，只下御史中丞荐举，宽其资限之格，资深者为御史，卑者为里行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167826_comment'></div>若能称职，亦是官守之常，不必过有升陟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167826_comment'></div>或不称职，可并举者坐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167826_comment'></div>则朝廷有责任之方，风宪有得人之美。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1167826'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1167826_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　九月，赐王素三品服，赐蔡襄、欧阳修、余靖五品服。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年9月</a>　蔡襄复奏执政臣不宜在私第会宾客。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　吕夷简致政，蔡襄复上《乞降吕夷简致仕官秩》<div id='poem_1167732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞降吕夷简致仕官秩奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167732")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167732'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167732'>臣切闻司徒吕夷简致仕，朝廷除太尉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167732_comment'></div>臣切以吕夷简立性奸邪，欺君卖国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167732_comment'></div>出入政府二十年，二虏凌凭，百姓穷困，贤愚失序，赏罚不明，一无功劳，以病罢退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167732_comment'></div>陛下未能诛戮，劝厉后人，岂当滥推恩礼，纵取笑天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167732_comment'></div>其吕夷简麻词乞不赐降下，别令中书详议官秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167732_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167732_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄同欧阳修等劾李淑、梁适奸邪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄书《水迁赋》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄与欧阳修联名上状举荐姚光弼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄作《赠勤师》赠释惠勤。<div id='poem_249428' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249428' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249428?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠勤师</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249428")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249428_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249428'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249428'>勤为浮屠人，形类心不偶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249428'>独负山林栖，远犯风尘走。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249428'>如闻大众居，乃是贤豪薮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249428'>专意学文章，韩编不离手。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249428'>退之所尚者，岂以言深厚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249428'>径驰周孔域，不为杂说诱。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249428'>大凡民之生，虫豸均一丑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249428'>圣人酌中道，君臣与夫妇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249428'>饮食若衣冠，事行而易守。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249428'>不喜释老言，诋斥遭诬负。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249428'>子今读其书，无乃相纷纠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249428'>学本勿学末，何为恤众口。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249428_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249428'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_249428_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《论改科场条例疏》<div id='poem_1167796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论改科场条制疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167796")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167796'>臣伏见隋唐以来，以进士、明经二科取士，迄今以为永制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167796_comment'></div>进士虽通试诗赋策论，其实去留专在诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167796_comment'></div>糊名誊纸，以示至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167796_comment'></div>点抹细碎，条约纤悉，所司奉之，便于考校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167796_comment'></div>明经逐场对义，钞节注疏，计诵字数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167796_comment'></div>至有一字旁写声形类者三两字，如有一中，亦是通义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167796_comment'></div>字犹不识，经旨何从而知，取士之方，一至于此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167796_comment'></div>臣闻有国家者取天下之士，将以治民而经国耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167796_comment'></div>故敦其行，欲以表风俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167796_comment'></div>试其才，欲以济成务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167796_comment'></div>今进士之诗赋、明经之帖义，于治民经国之术了不关及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167796_comment'></div>其间或有长才异节之士，幸而有之，或官而后习，非因设科而得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167796_comment'></div>今有善射者或使之御，其人必自以为不能，世之人亦曰：彼射也，责之以御，强人之所不习，不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167796_comment'></div>而以诗赋、帖义取士，偶与科合者即为中第，一日使之临民谋国，其人必自以为能，而世之人亦习而不怪，兹大可异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167796_comment'></div>或曰：取士在于得人，岂系诗赋策论乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167796_comment'></div>皇甫镈以贤良方正中科，而奸邪过人，岂不专试策乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167796_comment'></div>裴度以进士中第，而功德尤著者，岂不由诗赋而得之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167796_comment'></div>臣窃不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167796_comment'></div>取之以其道，任之以其术，而陷于奸邪，其人自隳也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167796_comment'></div>取之不以其道，任之不以其术，而能功德著闻，其人自立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167796_comment'></div>岂可以自隳与自立之人，而害经久之制乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167796_comment'></div>三代之道，乡举里选，专取德业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167796_comment'></div>汉察孝廉，加之策问，取士有经术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167796_comment'></div>隋唐以来，尽失之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167796_comment'></div>行之既久，难于卒更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167796_comment'></div>今就其所试之业而裁之，以试策为去留进士之术，以大义为去留明经之术，庶几可行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167796_comment'></div>一、天下之州军尽许立学，选择乡里有年德、通经义者补为教授，讲说经书，教授生徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167796_comment'></div>不应举者，三年后乞与助教名目，且令说讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167796_comment'></div>应举之人须经本州学听书，其日限以国子监新立条约为例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167796_comment'></div>一、请试策三道为一场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167796_comment'></div>考校验落外，次试论为一场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167796_comment'></div>又考校验落外，次试诗赋为一场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167796_comment'></div>以三场皆善者为优，或策论诗赋互有所长，则互取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167796_comment'></div>其策仍请一道问经义异同，以观其识；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167796_comment'></div>一道问古今沿革，以观其学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167796_comment'></div>一道问当世之务，以观其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167796_comment'></div>此其大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167796_comment'></div>一、明经只问所习经书异同大义，所对之义只合注疏大意，不须文字尽同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167796_comment'></div>或自有意见，即依注疏解释外，任自陈述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167796_comment'></div>可以明其识虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167796_comment'></div>若以经科文人所习已久，未能变革，即艰其取，而薄其恩，取能对大义者颇优奖之，自然稍有智识之人去彼取此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1167796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《乞责罚医官》奏议。<div id='poem_1167740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞责罚医官奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167740")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167740'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167740'>臣窃见近宝和公主及郓国公主相继夭殇，供药医官已闻下开封府取勘者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167740_comment'></div>臣切知豫王、鄂王薨时，医官亦是取勘，只降一两官，未旬月间寻得牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167740_comment'></div>切虑今来亦只似此行遣，久远不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167740_comment'></div>况近来小儿医官不一二年超升官资，赏赐无数，奏荐异姓恩泽，过于两制臣僚，贱者立贵，贫者立富。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167740_comment'></div>若以生死有命，药饵难工，自来所医疾病尽是当痊愈，此等何故滥受恩赏，恣为侥倖？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167740_comment'></div>若以从来痊愈因药，合受恩赏，今日所医无验，自当伏就刑罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167740_comment'></div>臣窃闻先朝周王薨，其时医官李某杖配广南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167740_comment'></div>陛下一二年间，皇子、皇女继亡六人，尽在此辈数人之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167740_comment'></div>兼臣闻医官各是临病互相推托，不肯及时下药，以致病深，虽有良医，无由措手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167740_comment'></div>其罪至重，比于李某，合更加刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167740_comment'></div>其术至谬，求之今人，不为难得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167740_comment'></div>伏望陛下念祖宗社稷之重，特因此时深行刑罚，庶使后人知惧，药饵尽心，实为久远保育皇嗣之计<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167740_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1167740'>「宝和」下原衍「光」字，又脱「郓国」二字，并据《国朝诸臣奏议》改正。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167740_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167740'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_1167740_0'>⑴ 《蔡忠惠集》卷一五。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷八四，《历代名臣奏议》卷一八七。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1167740_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《论中书吏人刘式之罪》奏议。<div id='poem_1167777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论中书吏人刘式之罪奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167777")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167777'>臣伏见中书提点五房公事、金部员外郎刘式，年满合该例转官、赐紫，入转运资序、知州者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167777_comment'></div>切以刘式本自微贱，因缘入仕，频倚事势，窃弄威权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167777_comment'></div>臣略条一二事，以明刘式奸狡之状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167777_comment'></div>明道初修葺内庭，固无劳效，侥求名目，改转朝官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167777_comment'></div>景祐之间，辄求外补，宰臣留而不遣，侄男特授斋郎，非例推恩，事权愈重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167777_comment'></div>庆历二年，守当官周卞偷窃空字敕黄，伪作祠部，流散诸处，货卖极多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167777_comment'></div>周卞事发之后，刘式与本房堂后官张用和方始陈首举觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167777_comment'></div>及开封府按成之日，惧见录问，别有干连，上下通情，奏请周卞更不录问，直令弃市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167777_comment'></div>岂有中书吏人阴结大臣，诬罔圣聪，回换刑狱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167777_comment'></div>又有守当官荆杞，为婺州客人徐炳进状，乞分家产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167777_comment'></div>荆杞伪作内降劄子，取受炳钱一千馀贯，事将觉发，荆杞杀徐炳父子三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167777_comment'></div>切见天圣中守关人吏马宗寿写造伪敕，下礼部，补苏上达充斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167777_comment'></div>事发，提点五房公事张仁惠有不觉察罪，降之光化军；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167777_comment'></div>堂后官李昭度降授齐州监当；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167777_comment'></div>本房手分并皆除出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167777_comment'></div>去年刘式不觉察周卞、荆杞伪造杀人，其罪甚重，盖缘当政大臣曲为庇护，并只罚赎，仍旧守职，不隔磨勘，依例转官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167777_comment'></div>伏见转运、提点刑狱不觉察部下官吏取受，并降移差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167777_comment'></div>今来人吏才八十员，刘式不觉察，茍免过愆，若更例与优恩，出典大郡，不惟小人侥倖，何以激劝将来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167777_comment'></div>其刘式，伏乞朝廷更不转官，特责降监当，以表朝廷清明，不容憸人干托之私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1167777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄上《请改军法疏》<div id='poem_1167797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请改军法疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167797")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167797'>臣伏见西鄙用兵以来，首尾六年，自刘平、任福、葛怀敏三将覆没，亡者十万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167797_comment'></div>沮损国威，公私空匮，邦赋点差之计，为患日深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167797_comment'></div>今被边之郡，甲兵非不多也，历涉数年，训练非不久也，然而屡战屡败，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167797_comment'></div>臣熟思之，盖军法未立、将谋不专也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167797_comment'></div>所谓军法未立者，今之都部署乃统帅之名，其钤辖、路分都监、都同巡检等，并是佐属裨校，各以宾礼相接。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167797_comment'></div>主帅等威既不尊异，向下官属更无节级相辖之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167797_comment'></div>及至出军，首尾不能相救，号令不能相通，所以多败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167797_comment'></div>所谓将谋不专者，朝廷每有指挥事件，多下逐路，并令钤辖、都监、都同巡检等司共从长商量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167797_comment'></div>大凡兵事，惟大将得以专之，秘计深谋，岂容众议？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167797_comment'></div>乃令僚佐参论短长，至有各出意见，互相诋毁，谋无所主，事无不漏，所以多败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167797_comment'></div>臣窃以军法不立，将谋不专，而胜敌者无有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167797_comment'></div>唐郭子仪、李光弼等以九节度之兵攻安庆绪，而辄败者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167797_comment'></div>子仪、光弼名将也，九帅之师共数十万也，以安庆绪之穷困，岂能御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167797_comment'></div>然而辄败者，盖军无都帅，不相统辖，谋议不同，所以致败也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167797_comment'></div>太宗朝，曹彬、潘美兴兵北举而无成功者何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167797_comment'></div>曹彬、潘美，名将也，三路并入，大举也，然而无成功者，盖监军刘文裕、王诜贪功立异，主将不能夺之，所以无功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167797_comment'></div>以古今事理参之，未有主将不专而能立大功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167797_comment'></div>或曰：今逐路帅臣各得便宜劄子，临事自可处置，何必变更军法乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167797_comment'></div>臣谓若法不素立，威不素行，虽得便宜，岂能使上下必信乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167797_comment'></div>臣请逐路都部署见管兵马人数，列为裨校部曲之差，分为前后左右之属，管兵臣僚官员并乞改换军职使名，依排陈使之类，以所领兵多少为等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167797_comment'></div>大小相乘，节级相辖，如有违犯，并因阶级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167797_comment'></div>所以立威一军，自然选拣精审，以战则胜，以守则坚，此至急之务也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1167797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄作《送许寺丞知古田县》，送许当世出知古田县。<div id='poem_249386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送许寺丞知古田县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249386")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249386'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249386'>大雪拥都门，子行亦良苦。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249386'>予贫乏觞豆，子车谁为祖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249386'>少止听我言，于子不无补。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249386'>于今方用兵，连年戍羌虏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249386'>战死动万计，募人填卒伍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249386'>赐衣靡国帑，走粟填边庾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249386'>平时赋税外，弓刀甲楯弩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249386'>干名应急须，筋皮角毛羽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249386'>前年科巩革，农牛半斤斧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249386'>杀之先冒禁，不杀即鞭楚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249386'>江南供雕翎，是物不栖渚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249386'>十倍买所无，赢利资商贾。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249386'>编纸作战䤴，纫联驱妇女。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249386'>输来不适用，空屋窠虫鼠。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249386'>此类如猬毛，更仆难悉数。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249386'>大凡敛货财，百姓若外府。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249386'>苟可入军须，岂敢怨官取。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249386'>盖患在不均，又索非其土。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249386'>有司失预计，临事才披簿。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249386'>严程弗渝日，落符洒飞雨。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249386'>使者但依违，州家不敢主。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249386'>况复为邑令，暗吟莫伸吐。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249386'>其间或得才，吏手无容舞。<div id='poem_sentence_22_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_249386'>子今佩县章，所领十万户。<div id='poem_sentence_23_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_249386'>志虑固精明，利病前可睹。<div id='poem_sentence_24_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_249386'>姑能务均一，瘵瘼庶苏瘉。<div id='poem_sentence_25_249386_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_249386'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_249386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年冬</a>　冬，蔡襄以双亲年老，乞便郡养亲，诏未许，旨意给假回乡迎双亲来都居住。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e6ddbc37185d45ad9c067fbced34e604_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e6ddbc37185d45ad9c067fbced34e604");'><span id='e6ddbc37185d45ad9c067fbced34e604_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年5月</a>　蔡襄收曾巩所致书札。作品：《上蔡学士书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年6月</a>　蔡襄与余靖等一再上疏谏罢迎舍利和修塔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年8月</a>　诏以蔡襄仍知谏院，进直史馆，同修起居注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　欧阳修罢知谏院，调为河北都转运按察使，蔡襄与孙甫上奏挽留，帝不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄上疏请罢吕公绰纠察在京邢狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄上疏请罢魏兼馆职。<br /><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　保州发生兵变，蔡襄上章力主镇压，并从中吸取教训，改革弊政。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　蔡襄上疏请罢晏殊宰相之职，从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年9月</a>　九月末，蔡襄与孙甫等两次参加苏舜钦邸聚会。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄送王益柔返洛阳，并作《送王胜之西归序》以自规。<div id='poem_1168042' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168042' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168042?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送王胜之西归序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168042")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168042_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168042'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168042'>志于道者，其所以进之之心皆然，而其所以为之或异者，岂明有所蔽与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168042_comment'></div>夫意气广大者善遗俗，而刚介者善仇世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168042_comment'></div>下视世俗，屑屑走趋势利，作仆奴女子态状，羞不可近，反高伉脱去以矫之，往往纵肆，自亦离道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168042_comment'></div>或非之，则曰：「不世人之非而吾非，吾岂势利汩哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168042_comment'></div>虽然，其所以自高者乃甚下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168042_comment'></div>兹有人焉，其心安于仁，而其发适于中，宜力于其间以求至之与否，乃暇与世之人准轻重而度远近，吾未见乎自处之重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168042_comment'></div>今夫衣带食饮群于人者无异焉，幸而是非好恶之明有以过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168042_comment'></div>有过之之明，而不能急岁时以修其性，岂不暗于愚者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168042_comment'></div>愚者无知，莫强其力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168042_comment'></div>知者或隳，何从而作也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168042_comment'></div>予之不明，用是说以省予中者久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168042_comment'></div>于胜之之行，辄进予之自规者，因以告之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168042_comment'></div>谨序。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1168042'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1168042_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄作《送勤上人归吴中》诗送释惠勤回苏州住锡。<div id='poem_249391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送勤上人归吴中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249391")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249391'>吴江水好吴岫灵，吴人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_249391", 249391, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>晰白</span>神气清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249391'>当须比屋皆佳器，奈何傥有名公卿。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249391'>究观是事见藏伏，例学浮图超死生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249391'>遂令才智蓄利泽，若日不下沾四瀛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249391'>勤师内外久著力，文字骨节初老成。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249391'>十年栖迟辇毂下，渊然澹薄无经营。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249391'>惜哉明了足见解，独擘迅翮翻青冥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249391'>残秋忽别东南去，尘土摆落衣裾轻。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_249391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄上《乞选翰林学士不用资序》札子。<div id='poem_1167848' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167848' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167848?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞选翰林学士不用资序劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167848")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167848_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167848'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167848'>臣风闻臣寮上言，为翰林学士员阙，乞求添补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167848_comment'></div>臣窃谓暂减员数，不若精选贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167848_comment'></div>有唐以来，此职最为亲近，朝夕閒宴，与天子论议天下之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167848_comment'></div>如陆贽、李绛皆不世之才，所论者足以开悟人主聪明，赞成天下之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167848_comment'></div>今来只循资序，随例补选，或行迹奸邪，或才识暗懦，中书据名除改，莫敢抑退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167848_comment'></div>况兹一职，动是两府之资，茍不择人，岂陛下选任忠良之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167848_comment'></div>臣欲乞今后翰林学士阙员，中书不得依资差除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167848_comment'></div>伏望出于圣衷选人任用，庶乎奸邪暗懦之人无由滥进。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1167848_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄尝约李之才去西郊涉猎。作品：《城西射弓挺之以病不至简示新诗有唯应欠我渭城歌之句今谨吟一篇以答佳意》<div id='poem_249234' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249234' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249234?labeling=true' target='_blank'>城西射弓挺之以病不至简示新诗有唯应欠我渭城歌之句谨吟一篇以答佳意</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249234")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249234_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249234'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249234'>雪后西郊物外清，官閒乘兴此閒行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249234'>出门疏树无尘色，入内流渠带野声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249234'>近腊酒醪香更酽，得风弓箭力还生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249234'>知君病起心犹壮，独背船窗唱渭城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249234_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249234'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249234_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄上《论民不可不恤，财不可不通》札子。<div id='poem_1167857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论财用劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167857")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167857'>臣伏睹陛下赐三司䌷绢诏书曰：「使敛无暴横而公须足，民无愁痛而国用登」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167857_comment'></div>又闻诏旨，以利触罪者与议轻刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167857_comment'></div>臣伏惟陛下视赤子有父母之慈，临万物有天地之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167857_comment'></div>不缘嗜爱而率敛于下，每因乏匮而资助于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167857_comment'></div>有以见陛下克己恭勤，忧民切至。<div class='inline'
