id='poem_sentence_4_1167857_comment'></div>德音屡降，圣虑弥深，庶官所宜奉行，百姓固当少息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167857_comment'></div>然而残苛之吏未已，供应之家转劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167857_comment'></div>陛下恤黎庶之心翻无实事，海内仰朝廷之令悉是空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167857_comment'></div>首尾乖违，弊病安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167857_comment'></div>臣以贫贱之迹，叨耳目之官，细民疾苦之情，天子未闻之事，俱合陈论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167857_comment'></div>伏自羌贼负恩，天兵致讨，备御之处数千里，更戍之役五六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167857_comment'></div>飞挽刍粮，缮修器械。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167857_comment'></div>于是不时之敛作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167857_comment'></div>无名之赋兴焉，言利之臣出焉，缘奸之吏起焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167857_comment'></div>配取相仍，蠹伤滋甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167857_comment'></div>供军之物，制作多门；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167857_comment'></div>任土之求，有无不一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167857_comment'></div>金谷之职，转迁靡常；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167857_comment'></div>管库之司，给纳是利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167857_comment'></div>前符未至，后条已行，郡县承风，急于星火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167857_comment'></div>虐者先期集事，曲施酷毒之威；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167857_comment'></div>贪者与吏通谋，力恣诛求之害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167857_comment'></div>以欺罔穷愚为智，有作者茍得而必行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167857_comment'></div>以攘夺豪富为公，当权者避嫌而不主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167857_comment'></div>破家流离之苦，十室九空；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167857_comment'></div>呼天苦诉之词，万人一口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167857_comment'></div>原其本末，皆有因缘，挟私雠者有之，为身计者有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167857_comment'></div>只如陕西榷盐，江南议铁，增添酒课，采取铜苗，移东就西，指无为有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167857_comment'></div>或赐章服，或改职名，或与迁官，或承奖诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167857_comment'></div>所以争求目下锱铢之利，不为日后久远之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167857_comment'></div>臣窃谓朝廷推赏不责其实之所致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167857_comment'></div>倍添屋税，鬻卖官田；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167857_comment'></div>刷江淮见镪上供，欠商贾便钱不给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167857_comment'></div>配物于不产之所，严程于可缓之期：如此之类，三司之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167857_comment'></div>借买银绢，豫折田苗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167857_comment'></div>逼抑纳钱，名为劝诱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167857_comment'></div>高下物估，官取赢馀：如此之类，转运司之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167857_comment'></div>贫富不均，奸贪不禁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167857_comment'></div>妄为退剥，故作滞留；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167857_comment'></div>杀牛纳皮，仍科徒罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167857_comment'></div>偿官竭产，更虐亲邻：如此之类，郡县之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167857_comment'></div>触类滋长，不可殚论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167857_comment'></div>汹汹生民，若在风涛之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1167857_comment'></div>嗷嗷四海，偷为旦暮之安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1167857_comment'></div>远近之情若斯，国家之患未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1167857_comment'></div>臣闻民为邦本，本固邦宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1167857_comment'></div>又闻财聚则人散，财散则人聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1167857_comment'></div>是知民不可不恤，财不可不通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1167857_comment'></div>若专奉公家，不究民病，所得则寡，其失则多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1167857_comment'></div>臣非不知吏员军旅之繁，郊庙赐宴之广，北有饵胡之费，西有御寇之须，常赋既不足充，遗利必当悉取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1167857_comment'></div>臣又非敢故兴恤民之论，务黜言利之人，执高古之虚文，遗当世之切务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1167857_comment'></div>所冀言利者上能资于国，下不害于民，饶益既多，孰云不当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1167857_comment'></div>所可痛心者，明知无利，冒怨必行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1167857_comment'></div>幸可宽期，力为督迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1167857_comment'></div>自古剥下无厌而民不乱，诛财无已而国不危者，未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1167857_comment'></div>昔汉武帝远事征伐，算及舟车，四方彫残，大业几废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1167857_comment'></div>以至下哀痛诏，封富民侯，虽仅安全，而刘氏之不亡者如线。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1167857_comment'></div>唐德宗朝，卢杞辈专为刻剥，税椽僦匮，别敛促追，掊虐于民，都下尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1167857_comment'></div>泾兵乘怨，径入长安，驱呼市人，用此藉口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1167857_comment'></div>臣窃思今日之事，兵不得已而用，财不得已而求，然汉唐致危乱之因，种种略施行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1167857_comment'></div>故复寇盗未平，干戈未息，或百姓之心骚动，顾天下之计如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1167857_comment'></div>伏望陛下践诏书之言，推实惠于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1167857_comment'></div>民不胜苦，在精择郡县抚养之人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1167857_comment'></div>利不可遗，在博求钱谷通流之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1167857_comment'></div>所入之赋有常，而所费之数无极，则去太冗而节烦费；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1167857_comment'></div>所得至薄，而敛怨至深，则去小利而存大惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1167857_comment'></div>上下相济，公私两行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1167857_comment'></div>伏惟宗祖不拔之基全付陛下，朝廷更张之事更待何时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1167857_comment'></div>愿陛下申戒大臣，力求众弊，以干家之术而忧国，以恕己之善而及人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1167857_comment'></div>使百姓之心不挠，则天下之计大定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1167857_comment'></div>言先于事，多为迂阔之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1167857_comment'></div>事至而言，无救阽危之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1167857_comment'></div>臣忧深语切，意拙文繁，陛下傥赐详观，于时实有裨补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1167857_comment'></div>臣所言民间疾苦及处事乖方者形之于左。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1167857_comment'></div>臣所闻所见民间疾苦，不敢备载，粗举一二条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1167857_comment'></div>所冀上达宸览，知天下有如此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1167857_comment'></div>其间启请者乞赐施行<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1167857_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1167857'>二句「乖违弊」三字原作「多端其」，据宋本改。</div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1167857_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167857'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_76_1167857_0'>⑴ 《蔡忠惠集》卷二二。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷一○一，《历代名臣奏议》卷二六四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1167857_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　诏以参知政事贾昌朝代晏殊为枢密使，以陈执中为参知政事。蔡襄与孙甫上奏言陈执中刚愎不学，不可任以政，帝发怒，襄等遂不敢言。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　为尚书主客郎中王惟正撰书《尚书主客郎中王君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书主客郎中王君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历四年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168180")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168180'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168180'>君讳惟正，字晦蒙，太原人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168180_comment'></div>曾王父讳袭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168180_comment'></div>王父讳刿，赠大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168180_comment'></div>皇考讳恩，累赠尚书工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168180_comment'></div>皇妣范氏，追封昌乐县太君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168180_comment'></div>胡氏，封永安县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168180_comment'></div>王氏之居太原者为大姓，自君之先，数世无显者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168180_comment'></div>君始举明经，咸平元年中第，选注瀛州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168180_comment'></div>会契丹钞边，河北用兵，择能吏督刍粮，君兼魏、镇、定三州，皆以期办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168180_comment'></div>转运司以状闻于朝，授光化军判官兼通判，用保荐者改光禄寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168180_comment'></div>东封西祀恩，再迁大理寺丞、赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168180_comment'></div>又迁殿中丞、国子博士，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168180_comment'></div>入尚书省，为虞部、金部、司勋三员外、主客郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168180_comment'></div>初知怀安之金水，通判耀州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168180_comment'></div>州将尤涛与君论事不相能，条君十八事不如法者以闻，诏辨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168180_comment'></div>逮狱具，而涛悉以诬服，人益称君廉能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168180_comment'></div>移知绛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168180_comment'></div>岁饥民流，辄发常平仓粟赈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168180_comment'></div>时权臣有不喜吏在州下，风君去之，且得善官，不肯应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168180_comment'></div>其后当丞殿中，抑久不报，君力辨乃迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168180_comment'></div>被工部丧罢归，服除，历知辽、雅、卫、德四州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168180_comment'></div>雅州之俗右鬼神，而巫觋凭依祸福，勒民财以自利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168180_comment'></div>君按祠庙之不在祀典者，投其像于江，彻屋材以补官舍，巫觋为之易业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168180_comment'></div>龙图阁直学士刘公烨表君廉平，可监刺列郡，授荆湖南路提点刑狱，升广南西路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168180_comment'></div>时安南西道节度使、南平王李蕴薨，二子与其叔争立，叛掠宜、钦、邕三州，败戍兵，杀寨主，势以益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168180_comment'></div>朝廷委君与曹克明图之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168180_comment'></div>君训兵走粟，为守御策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168180_comment'></div>作木龙，断钦、廉海路，贼不得进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168180_comment'></div>君度其内争，必一而止，勒兵待之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168180_comment'></div>踰年，一子果杀其弟、叔自立，遣使称藩，交趾平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168180_comment'></div>君应例迁，回让赠王父一官，即评事君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168180_comment'></div>居岭外，闻祖母病，请解使职，幸得便郡以就养，遂知解州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168180_comment'></div>道京师，图上交趾事宜，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168180_comment'></div>至郡十馀日，徙晋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168180_comment'></div>未几，为江东路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168180_comment'></div>丁永安太君忧，还，充三司户部判官，言钱谷利病，多所施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168180_comment'></div>潞州于河东号为繁会，君得之，励精为治，屡辨冤狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168180_comment'></div>入判三司凭由司，出领亳州、密州，最后再为绛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168180_comment'></div>庆历二年七月二十日，终于廨，寿年七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168180_comment'></div>以四年九月二十日葬于某所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168180_comment'></div>夫人韩氏封万年县君，嫔配之宜，治家教子，悉有法度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168180_comment'></div>子五人：长曰敏中，试秘书省校书郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168180_comment'></div>次曰建中，试大理评事、监楚州盐仓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168180_comment'></div>曰执中，未仕而亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168180_comment'></div>曰柔中，辽州辽山尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168180_comment'></div>皆以荫补官，谨而好学，为吏得其家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168180_comment'></div>女适殿中丞长路开，次适颍川陈晟，次适右侍禁陈宗望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168180_comment'></div>孙三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168180_comment'></div>君喜书史，老益不懈，尤通纬象卜筮之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168180_comment'></div>持己以俭，奉官以法，仕五十年而无吏过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168180_comment'></div>将葬，诸孤谋曰：「古人之传于如今者，托于文也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168180_comment'></div>况郎官于令应刻石以载功德，不刻不传，其惟孝思乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168180_comment'></div>建中裒叙其世系官次治迹，走求文于余，为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1168180'>吏治之兴功利，脩科条，奋奇断而不顾者，斯可谓之材矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168180_comment'></div>然不移势要，根人以资己，唯是令善，必昌厥后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1168180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年10月</a>　蔡襄以亲老乞乡郡，旨授右正言知福州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄离京前上《乞与福建路转运使同共相度盐法札子》<div id='poem_1167846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞与福建路转运使同共相度盐法劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167846")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167846'>臣于去年曾上言，为福建路州军盐官中煎卖，每年官中所费甚多，而获利甚少，枉令生民日陷刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167846_comment'></div>臣条件利害，乞许百姓纳钱通煎，及许客人纳钱于本路通贩，可以岁减数万人之狱，及获一两倍之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167846_comment'></div>后蒙朝廷送下三司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167846_comment'></div>寻闻三司送下本路相度，诸州官吏不知本末，多有异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167846_comment'></div>伏乞朝廷连臣所言文字，令臣到福建日，与本路转运使同共商量，分析利害以闻，然后朝廷相度可否施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167846_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月</a>　蔡襄离京前致书《致吴副枢贴》向吴育告别并祝贺升迁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年1月</a>　蔡襄离京前与梅尧臣饯别。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ce25b58f1f1d434194eb635bef7ff8da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ce25b58f1f1d434194eb635bef7ff8da");'><span id='ce25b58f1f1d434194eb635bef7ff8da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1055')">1051-1055年</a>，40-44岁</div><div id='ce25b58f1f1d434194eb635bef7ff8da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月</a>　蔡襄当殿奏救御史唐介。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年10月26日</a>　蔡襄作《山居帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年11月11日</a>　蔡襄作《与彦猷学士》寄唐询。<div id='poem_1167893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与彦猷学士书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年11月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167893")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167893_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167893'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167893'>十一月十一日，襄再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167893_comment'></div>贤弟殿中君虽同年，而未尝接识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167893_comment'></div>至京又不往还，但有见君子多或称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167893_comment'></div>前月十九，当直后殿，辄见其作为，动摇山岳，雷霆之下，挺然不动，遂得春州之行，斯大可叹骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167893_comment'></div>前史所载古人事，岂复能过之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167893_comment'></div>惜其不幸，所论不从，而身窜穷荒，愧恨何极！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167893_comment'></div>近有敕旨，减放三州身丁米，斯圣情哀怜远民之深，故有是举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167893_comment'></div>今岁，都下大寒非常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167893_comment'></div>近登陛，首问圆小茗造作之因，殊称珍好，恐知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167893_comment'></div>两日前堂中下进奏，取江西及福建赴治月日，后逼节，未有闻，不知作何行，当是别有命耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167893_comment'></div>夜寒笔冻，挥洒纵横，愿君侯恕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167893_comment'></div>蔡襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1167893_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄书入京沿途所作诗篇13首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄书御撰《元舅陇西王碑》，并辞李家润笔。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄作《汾阳夫人挽词二首》<div id='poem_249196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249196?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汾阳夫人挽词二首<span class='inlineComment2'>（其夫李留后端懿国甥）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249196")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249196_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249196'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249196'>福偶天家出，贤名戚里推。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249196'>朱颜不待老，万事却成悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249196'>宿露沾新陇，秋风过旧帷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249196'>谁歌均一德，传继召南诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249196'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249196_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249195' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249195' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249195?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249195_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249195'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249195'>借有百年在，都如一梦回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249195'>幻生还复灭，仙去不重来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249195'>乐色閒宵院，衣香秘夜台。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249195'>行人知令淑，哭送侍儿哀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249195_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249195'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249195_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　年初，蔡襄陛进《茶录》二篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年1月18日</a>　蔡襄作《入春帖》致葛公绰言到京近况。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　正月下旬至二月上旬，蔡襄两次与梅尧臣、马遵会饮于京郊，并挥毫作书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年2月</a>　蔡襄撰写《葛氏草堂记》<div id='poem_1168114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168114?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葛氏草堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐四年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168114")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168114_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168114'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168114'>葛君公绰即其居之东园植竹桧果花几万本，又因其高下以为丘池，疏渠行水于其间，冠丘以亭，跨池以梁，作堂其中，可以安处而游息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168114_comment'></div>予尝过之，公绰指而谓予曰：「宅于山，虽有岩壑靓深之趣，然与人远，欲从贤豪游，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168114_comment'></div>至于都城，虽与人近，然俗尘时溷人意，欲自清迈，不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168114_comment'></div>吾不晦于山，不迫于城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168114_comment'></div>堂中储书数百千帙，先生当前，子弟群植，考经义之微，咀文章之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168114_comment'></div>如是者，吾所以学为业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168114_comment'></div>若夫花飞而草长，竹阴而泉鸣，蟹鱼果蔬，俛仰掇拾，登临据倚，醉欢笑歌，此吾所以从宾游也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168114_comment'></div>宾既休矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168114_comment'></div>虫鸟幽幽，树林暝色而烟归，荷芰泛光而月来，此吾之所以閒燕而自适也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168114_comment'></div>若东园之胜，吾专有之，吾无负于斯矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168114_comment'></div>予谓之曰：「子之兄子雅君而下，皆以文艺中科，走官四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168114_comment'></div>子之词业日益新，又将仕矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168114_comment'></div>然则所谓东园者，殆与仕而老归者为谋，子安能专有之而且不负也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168114_comment'></div>皇祐四年二月日记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1168114_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　蔡襄偕梅尧臣、江休复、刘敞诣宋中道家观赏书画。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年春</a>　蔡襄寄茶叶杜衍，杜谢以诗，蔡襄作《和杜相公谢寄茶》奉和。<div id='poem_249207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和杜相公谢寄茶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249207")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249207'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249207'>破春龙焙走新茶，尽是西溪近社芽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249207'>才拆缄封思退傅，为留甘旨减藏家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249207'>鲜明香色凝云液，清彻神情敌露华。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249207'>却笑虚名陆鸿渐，曾无贤相作诗誇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249207'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年4月</a>　蔡襄撰书《延安郡主李氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168186' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168186' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168186?labeling=true' target='_blank'>延安郡主李氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168186")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168186_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168186'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168186'>延安郡主李氏，太宗皇帝之外孙，真宗皇帝之甥，齐国献穆大长公主之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168186_comment'></div>父为镇国军节度使、驸马都尉，赠太师、中书令、尚书令、许国公，谥和文，讳遵勖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168186_comment'></div>大父连州刺史、赠太师讳继昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168186_comment'></div>曾大父枢密使、镇国军节度使、赠太师、中书令、尚书令、陇西郡王，谥元靖，讳崇矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168186_comment'></div>家世勋业，列在国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168186_comment'></div>大中祥符三年十一月主生于永宁第，弥月，献穆公主见主于帝所，帝曰：「女，吾之所出也，且有奇法，异时非才贤不以逑匹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168186_comment'></div>因出缣帛以为庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168186_comment'></div>逮周晬，召至内省，临视除发，以珍宝戏物百馀种赉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168186_comment'></div>甫七岁，即赐冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168186_comment'></div>入谢赐，见皇太子，将拜之，帝曰：「齿同矣，孰为长」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168186_comment'></div>徐推主生月日后皇太子，乃使拜，盖欲以长幼序之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168186_comment'></div>每宴会中，常呼置旁坐，所以恩爱之良厚，非诸王公主女所可拟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168186_comment'></div>天圣五年，封长寿县主，以归今閤门使、忠州防御使钱君晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168186_comment'></div>钱氏自忠懿王举所承袭十有三州之籍上于朝廷，而其人民数十百万不罹兵革之役，以至太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168186_comment'></div>阴施深长，勋美盖世，主家以是通婚姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168186_comment'></div>及主归，而其君舅文僖公以代诰命，参禁密，遂持将相印，其族<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1168186", 1168186, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>植笏</span>而通省户者以百数，门阑厮役，青紫群列，号为贵显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168186_comment'></div>然以主之重，务自损下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168186_comment'></div>主益恭谨持礼，承舅姑，奉祭祀，夙暮不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168186_comment'></div>姻亲娣姒，降屈色词以相接，亲疏有意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168186_comment'></div>于是诸钱内外悉称主贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168186_comment'></div>明道二年，进延安郡封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168186_comment'></div>自和文公薨，主叹曰：「吾独有母存乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168186_comment'></div>孝忧愈至，时物之新者，必先献乃敢用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168186_comment'></div>皇祐三年，献穆捐世，主哀戚甚，却珠金之饰，日夜涕泣思慕，因见癯悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168186_comment'></div>上念先皇帝弟兄无复存者，乃恤其孤，谓主曰：「大长公主岁常资郡主厚甚，今寂寞耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168186_comment'></div>俸钱每月六万，特增至十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168186_comment'></div>是年除夕，主还外舍设奠，盖岁新矣，而母不复见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168186_comment'></div>号恸咽绝，左右更劝，莫能止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168186_comment'></div>夜中气懑胸，比归，疾益，力戒二子自强以立门户，歛葬之用必以约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168186_comment'></div>四年正月四日终，春秋四十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168186_comment'></div>上恻悼，不视垂拱朝一日，命中司宾临吊，赙赠加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168186_comment'></div>以其年四月十日葬河南府洛阳县邙山之原，从先姑之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168186_comment'></div>子三人，曰景初，光禄寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168186_comment'></div>景裕，大理评事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168186_comment'></div>其季早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168186_comment'></div>女适右班殿直赵思复，封寿安县君，先主二年而亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168186_comment'></div>孙男四人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168186_comment'></div>初，父和文公博雅有文，喜与贤士大夫游，献穆又以贤德辅之，著于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168186_comment'></div>主更见积习皆善行，故不以贵势富侈自用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168186_comment'></div>闾阎民有死丧不能给，必资其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168186_comment'></div>隶侍使令，未尝诃谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168186_comment'></div>有嘉宾焉，亲视烹饪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168186_comment'></div>虽其资敏淑，然有所从来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168186_comment'></div>主善书，能为五七言诗，居閒，设烈女图，读书史以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168186_comment'></div>二子就学，日程其所为，又勤解说曰：「吾观持梁策肥者，外虽矜豪，而中空无有，多慢侮人，岂圣人所谓爱亲者不敢恶于人之义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168186_comment'></div>若不为此，吾意安矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168186_comment'></div>故二子知所以为学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168186_comment'></div>防御君能亢其宗，以有声名，主实训有助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168186_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1168186'>猗哉延安，肖于悊亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168186_comment'></div>少所养习，既归有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168186_comment'></div>婉娩令善，率礼而文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168186_comment'></div>唯时贵重，世莫与隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168186_comment'></div>群从祁祁，车服有容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168186_comment'></div>天子惟舅，言朝于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168186_comment'></div>北第高门，爰东其轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168186_comment'></div>父王之孙，母兮帝子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168186_comment'></div>曰予尔思，我适则喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168186_comment'></div>旋于我家，相印簪斧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168186_comment'></div>齐珥则多，君姑娣姒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168186_comment'></div>以承以比，和乐有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168186_comment'></div>孝爱深矣，哀陨其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168186_comment'></div>子学而力，夫以材名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168186_comment'></div>胡不遐考，用观厥成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168186_comment'></div>孰不愿年，曷支其倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168186_comment'></div>惟德之寿，寖久益明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168186_comment'></div>于何其寿，其寿斯铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1168186_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年5月</a>　蔡襄作《祭范侍郎文》祭范仲淹。<div id='poem_1168208' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168208' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168208?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭范侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168208")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168208_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168208'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168208'>谨遣某人以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于故资政侍郎高平公之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168208_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168208_comment'></div>生死聚散，物理之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168208_comment'></div>何公之亡，贤愚涕洟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168208_comment'></div>人幸公年，非有爱私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168208_comment'></div>幸公复用，庶几有利于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168208_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168208_comment'></div>使公且存而复用，终有为乎，其无有也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168208_comment'></div>在天圣中，公当言责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168208_comment'></div>时士大夫，依阿厚嘿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168208_comment'></div>公乃言事，倾动天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168208_comment'></div>触指奸权，开道谏诤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168208_comment'></div>尹京之政，例为宽大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168208_comment'></div>借吏齿牙，光饰眉面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168208_comment'></div>公政清明，卒以毁去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168208_comment'></div>羌种窥边，天兵议讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168208_comment'></div>公云士伍，未可即用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168208_comment'></div>投书叛酋，语之祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168208_comment'></div>逮其款附，终若前料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168208_comment'></div>登于政府，天子问状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168208_comment'></div>公拔根株，扳蹑三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168208_comment'></div>不为目前，茍且之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168208_comment'></div>劝农养士，塞窒侥进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168208_comment'></div>众訾成波，挤落在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168208_comment'></div>至死流离，惟道是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168208_comment'></div>大航楫维，胶于泥沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168208_comment'></div>涉者罔济，临流赍嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168208_comment'></div>公薨之初，众悼以哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168208_comment'></div>市利田宅，子女金犀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168208_comment'></div>厚味入骨，老死营持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168208_comment'></div>公薨之后，独无馀资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168208_comment'></div>君国以忠，亲友以义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168208_comment'></div>进退安危，不易其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168208_comment'></div>立身大节，明白如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168208_comment'></div>襄晚登公门，尝辱知遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168208_comment'></div>公丧在东，欲吊无路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168208_comment'></div>陈酹以文，千古斯慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168208_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1168208_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年6月</a>　蔡襄作《送石昌言知宿州》<div id='poem_249383' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249383' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249383?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送石昌言知宿州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249383")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249383_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249383'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249383'>符离封城古云望，扼控东南地形壮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249383'>飞流金粟走舟车，镇压奸雄宿兵仗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249383'>昌言才思老台阁，声名远出风骚将。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249383'>倦直承明得守符，诏书遣临士民上。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249383'>万家裁制须得宜，譬若楩楠迎大匠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249383'>京师从游日月久，送君酒酣益惆怅。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249383'>人生岂效鸡鹜群，意在糠粱取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_249383", 249383, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>甘养</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249383'>边隅多故方急材，往往稠人拔公相。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249383'>吾侪有策空自奇，皎皎丹衷亦谁亮。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249383'>欲随戎马仅胜衣，强作文章还覆酱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249383'>大都用置系于时，丈夫未死固难量。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249383'>觥巡卷到君勿辞，行看岸下船头放。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249383'>我今联束若愁鹰，注目青云思远飏。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249383'>一麾当复泛隋渠，愿君加数为公酿。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249383_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249383'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_249383_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年6月</a>　蔡襄送杨畋赴广东领兵讨伐智高。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年8月12日</a>　蔡襄作《许处士墓表》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　八、九月，蔡襄奉敕试制诏书二道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年9月</a>　蔡襄迁朝奉郎、起居舍人、知制诰、权同判吏部流内铨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　蔡襄作《举官自代状》，举孙甫代己修起居注。<div id='poem_1167828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举官自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1052年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167828")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167828'>兵部员外郎、秘阁校理孙甫，为学深于经书，属词长于史传，洁廉可以励世，端方可以立朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167828_comment'></div>向自谏垣，求补外吏，历更六任，首尾八年，资序高于辈流，才行信于时俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167828_comment'></div>臣近叨渥命，俾职训词，以甫代臣，实允舆论。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1167828_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年10月</a>　朝廷有除知福州之命，蔡襄以私事辞免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年11月5日</a>　蔡襄致书同乡叶任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年12月</a>　蔡襄奉敕书《孝经》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　蔡襄曾上《请以产钱定重难役户等第》奏折。<div id='poem_1167800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请止以产钱定重难役户等第奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167800")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167800'>臣尝为福建路转运司，见一县之中所差里正衙前，各于逐县有三十年或五七年轮差一次者，有一百贯至十贯皆入十分重难者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167800_comment'></div>请止以产钱多少定其所入重难之等。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1167800_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1052&endYear=1052')">1052年</a>　蔡襄作《纡问帖》，令家人看管好园子。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年2月</a>　蔡襄授权礼部贡举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年春</a>　蔡襄撰《尚书职方郎中谢公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168187' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168187' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168187?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书职方郎中谢公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168187")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168187_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168187'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168187'>君讳某，字某，泉州晋江人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168187_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某，以信义称于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168187_comment'></div>太夫人徐氏，生三子，君为最少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168187_comment'></div>祥符八年举进士，历抚州临川令、漳州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168187_comment'></div>太守受赇贿舞法，君据平无所挠，讼者不之守而之君，州政得不败，守亦善去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168187_comment'></div>改大理寺丞、知龙溪县，县人曰：「是故州从事，持守正，使无害，有恩于我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168187_comment'></div>相与喜，具酒食相过从为庆贺者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168187_comment'></div>至则决滞讼，条刬旧蠹，民以便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168187_comment'></div>徙容州北流县，城郭、仓庾、廨舍、道梁一皆新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168187_comment'></div>就知雷州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168187_comment'></div>州傅海，有蛮夷风，不知学，为葺孔子庙，聚诸子弟，教以儒术，雷人业进士自君始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168187_comment'></div>大豪李郁筑城得古印，立盗契，夺民田百馀家，五十年不能直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168187_comment'></div>有诉于君者，即捕系庭下问状，具伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168187_comment'></div>而郁老当赎，君条其甚恶，不可假卒，致以法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168187_comment'></div>通判福州，画购巨盗，悉诛其党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168187_comment'></div>谏议大夫方公谨言治广州，辟君贰政，廉取番舶输官之利，以招其徕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168187_comment'></div>至罢去，夷人涕泣思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168187_comment'></div>知建州，岁无留狱，长老纪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168187_comment'></div>又知开封府之祥符，治愈精，微有声名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168187_comment'></div>朝廷用荐者言，将任以刑狱钱谷，而君恳求便藩，得海州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168187_comment'></div>会岁旱，有蝗过境，一昔拱穟死，吏民惊叹，以为异政之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168187_comment'></div>皇祐五年正月十四日卒于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168187_comment'></div>其孤护全柩以归，某年某月某日葬某县某里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168187_comment'></div>娶黄氏，故直史馆宗旦从妹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168187_comment'></div>再娶其弟，封永康县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168187_comment'></div>子四人：彦辅，太庙斋郎，先卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168187_comment'></div>仲规，举进士第，越州萧山尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168187_comment'></div>叔矩，未仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168187_comment'></div>季成，太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168187_comment'></div>女八人，适余炳、祝嘏、杨璟、刘鼎臣、黄世永、朱仲、陈大雅、陈箴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168187_comment'></div>君性乐易，无贵贱亲疏，接之皆尽其衷，故人多喜爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168187_comment'></div>数官岭表，不以僻陋自失，所至喜设施，为民赖利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168187_comment'></div>在海州，尝谓其子曰：「谢氏居闽，未有仕者，吾起家州县，自大理丞八迁为尚书职方郎中，赠吾父都官郎中，母长寿县太君，斯亦荣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168187_comment'></div>历官三十九年，无小过失，实吾谨畏然尔，汝曹念之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168187_comment'></div>故其子益循笃学，皆可以大其家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168187_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1168187'>六十九，为已寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168187_comment'></div>位郎官，才未究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168187_comment'></div>政在民，斯不朽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1168187_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年3月22日</a>　蔡襄作《别纸·与曹待制书》与福州曹颖叔。作品：《别纸·与曹侍制书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年5月</a>　蔡襄作《阁下昼眠》<div id='poem_249084' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249084' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249084?labeling=true' target='_blank'>阁下昼眠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249084")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249084_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249084'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249084'>急雨初收宫殿明，红薇花落暑风清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249084'>忽传午正惊残梦，寂寂西轩喜鹊声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249084_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249084'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249084_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　七八月，蔡襄奉敕书真宗《奉神述》上碑，书成进上，仁宗御书“君谟”二字赐之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　蔡襄撰书《内殿承制王君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168188?labeling=true' target='_blank'>内殿承制王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐五年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168188")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168188_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168188'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168188'>王君讳翊，字辅之，两浙都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168188_comment'></div>罢还，皇祐五年五月七日卒于京师，以其年七月二十四日葬于开封府开封县褒亲乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168188_comment'></div>其孤兟哭而杖，授书使者以来请铭，曰：「我先君之先，钱塘人，后迁于汴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168188_comment'></div>少孤家窭，以书艺补官，历七任，终六十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168188_comment'></div>今葬有期，且走公门下日久，固知其所为，幸或铭诸墓，使有闻于后世，公之赐深矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168188_comment'></div>余为次其官族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168188_comment'></div>初授泾州保定主簿，治有称，再调永州司理参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168188_comment'></div>州将曲狱，君曰：「狱辟定法，可妄移哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168188_comment'></div>永边溪洞蛮獠寇境，杀巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168188_comment'></div>君请募敢战五百人自率之，遮阨设伏，饵以羸形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168188_comment'></div>贼果来，击之，败走，入焚其庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168188_comment'></div>以理官不应捕寇，不当其赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168188_comment'></div>除常州无锡尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168188_comment'></div>转运使段少连以材明严察部吏，每行郡县，必载君舟中，语至移日，出界乃遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168188_comment'></div>尉满，君叹曰：「俸微，不能芘吾族」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168188_comment'></div>还都退居，视时物上下，取与出纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168188_comment'></div>居二年，厩有粟马，所与游皆贵近人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168188_comment'></div>久之，陕西用兵讨元昊，君奋曰：「陋矣，吾视此屑屑耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168188_comment'></div>上封章言十事，书奏，即召对延和，又令于资善堂究陈利病，再遣使问所欲为，曰：「臣言可用，幸天子用之，不敢徼利」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168188_comment'></div>夏随为陕西招讨使，荐君智能，授左侍禁、泾州长武寨主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168188_comment'></div>元昊入寇，至渭州，寨民将逃去，君谕之曰：「入保此，吾必能守」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168188_comment'></div>众乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168188_comment'></div>迁西头供奉官、河东麟府路走马承受公事，专置堡寨一十有五，招怀蕃户二万馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168188_comment'></div>每进对，多言时政得失，辄触权要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168188_comment'></div>再迁为承制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168188_comment'></div>三司使叶公清臣任君监在京榷货务，仅十月，计所赢钱二百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168188_comment'></div>三司使移他官，君失所知，求见上言事，愿解局，遂除都巡检使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168188_comment'></div>又上书曰：「臣有通流货财之术，岁可得钱千四百万」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168188_comment'></div>欲道其所以然于上前，再三，不得召，犹曰：「罢归，幸得望殿陛咫尺，尽吐吾术矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168188_comment'></div>比至京师，病且卒，卒不能出其术，悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168188_comment'></div>君娶胡氏，子七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168188_comment'></div>男曰威，三班奉职；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168188_comment'></div>曰兟、兢，举进士，兢中第；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168188_comment'></div>哲、珏皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168188_comment'></div>女，长适前河中河东主簿吕公，次适谢公弼，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168188_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1168188'>材以时，成则资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168188_comment'></div>材艰于用，匪成之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168188_comment'></div>利国有原，动如转圜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168188_comment'></div>曰时与成，惟命惟天。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1168188_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年秋</a>　蔡襄移居铨舍，作《铨舍后轩》<div id='poem_249115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>铨舍后轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249115")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249115'>秋栏疏索水荭花，坐见花边日向斜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249115'>莫问幽人超世诀，即心无累是仙家。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249115'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　蔡襄作《谢杜相公》诗，并以草书寄之。<div id='poem_249413' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249413' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249413?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢杜相公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249413")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249413_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249413'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249413'>谢政闲宫傅，当年老相君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249413'>诗情通造化，笔力作风云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249413'>是则经纶手，施于淡泊文。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249413'>捧窥心感悸，无路候公门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249413_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249413'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249413_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年9月</a>　蔡襄上《启用新乐于郊庙札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年10月</a>　蔡襄撰书《右班殿直监慈湖都铁冶务程君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168189' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168189' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168189?labeling=true' target='_blank'>右班殿直监慈湖都铁冶务程君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168189")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168189_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168189'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168189'>程君居兴国军大冶县，世为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168189_comment'></div>右班殿直讳叔良，字仲卿，尤有善行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168189_comment'></div>其曾祖讳侃，仕伪唐军器副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168189_comment'></div>祖讳满，光政院承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168189_comment'></div>父讳昭，字某，三班奉职，以材智自高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168189_comment'></div>金陵平，浮江而上，至慈湖，依铁山冶以通吴蜀之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168189_comment'></div>积数十年，致钜资，散施周人急难，名誉翕然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168189_comment'></div>君承父兄之旧，少从学，好老氏书，服其慈俭之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168189_comment'></div>所居夏秋潦水环民舍，衣食无所从得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168189_comment'></div>君计其口而食之，疾者饵以药石，死者葬以槥，岁用为常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168189_comment'></div>明道中，江南饥疫，殍殣狼藉道上，诏督郡县开廪以济之，发徒以瘗之，尚莫能周，而君之里间无饥人，无露骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168189_comment'></div>其视人之所苦若出于己，昼夜不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168189_comment'></div>亲戚之贫而归者，随所厚薄而活之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168189_comment'></div>至于资身，自为约薄，不营出入，悉责家奴，时一省视，去其欺己者，以是虽居丰有而甚适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168189_comment'></div>旁居田墅，治园池，植草木，发泉石，在处为亭台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168189_comment'></div>宾亲游行啸歌，一醉洒然，当世名公卿作诗以咏道其善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168189_comment'></div>年五十有六，以疾终，皇祐二年闰十一月六日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168189_comment'></div>将疾，自疏簿目一通，皆治丧事亲族之礼、施用之具，与其葬所若年月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168189_comment'></div>既终，其孤启而行之，无有乏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168189_comment'></div>遂以五年十月二十五日葬于流水里之南冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168189_comment'></div>君两娶郑氏，有子九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168189_comment'></div>男大年，三班奉职，治经史，力世其家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168189_comment'></div>曰龟年、尧年、康年，皆敏饬向学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168189_comment'></div>女五人，长适大理寺丞郭之美，次适开封府太康主簿蔡高，次适卫尉寺丞聂平仲，二人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168189_comment'></div>太康主簿，予亡弟也，以婚姻家，知君最旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168189_comment'></div>有所部官尝以书通客，与之钱，不能塞欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168189_comment'></div>其人后言财利事，得出使南方，犹泄前怒，增君官课铁岁百万，指期必破产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168189_comment'></div>或谕君出其手迹以直其事，君曰：「宁破吾产，勿破吾行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168189_comment'></div>予乃知君终长者，为之序且铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168189_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1168189'>致适于无，以放其身，厥隐于真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168189_comment'></div>捐己之有，利及于人，唯义之伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168189_comment'></div>爱协乡闾，不独其亲，允富其邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168189_comment'></div>生也勿累，没焉不泯，考信于文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1168189_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年11月</a>　蔡襄扈从南郊祭天地，作《亲祀南郊诗》表进，帝有诏答。<div id='poem_249431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲祀南郊诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249431")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249431'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249431'>天畀元统，赤运开祉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249431'>圣祖神宗，海域平砥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249431'>思皇真考，岳封汾祀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249431'>饵系戎胡，包束戈矢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249431'>丕显灵德，光被万里。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249431'>民寿而康，恩及萧苇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249431'>恭惟皇帝，继文之始。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249431'>兢兢日慎，夙夜勤只。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249431'>哀怜困穷，有如在己。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249431'>惟刑是恤，弗繇怒喜。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249431'>躬服俭约，黜弃浮侈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249431'>罔有逸欲，日惟三纪。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249431'>大中则经，兴亡则史。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249431'>阴阳时序，日纬躔轨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249431'>乐律本原，礼法根柢。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249431'>兵韬术数，万微精旨。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249431'>该通变贯，咸烛厥理。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249431'>岁舍壬午，盗发南鄙。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249431'>帝曰汝青，治办行李。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249431'>毋大诛割，定患则已。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249431'>猎猎灵旗，启道径指。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249431'>凶渠踣仆，俘徒授耳。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249431'>岭服既平，勋赏周被。<div id='poem_sentence_22_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_249431'>封殁录孥，门户晔炜。<div id='poem_sentence_23_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_249431'>粤兹明年，农家丰美。<div id='poem_sentence_24_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_249431'>廛庐积腐，庾漕储峙。<div id='poem_sentence_25_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_249431'>帝咨相臣，匪台德尔。<div id='poem_sentence_26_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_249431'>穹昊眷赉，祖考佑俾。<div id='poem_sentence_27_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_249431'>何施不报，将祀郊畤。<div id='poem_sentence_28_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_249431'>号令四下，若建瓴水。<div id='poem_sentence_29_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_249431'>荒服述职，奔走输委。<div id='poem_sentence_30_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_249431'>仲冬丙寅，斋寝以俟。<div id='poem_sentence_31_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_249431'>先时霾晦，飙籁号起。<div id='poem_sentence_32_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_249431'>真意益庄，降鉴伊迩。<div id='poem_sentence_33_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_249431'>夜漏适中，星露云靡。<div id='poem_sentence_34_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_249431'>大辂既驭，清阳出晷。<div id='poem_sentence_35_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_249431'>休光无垠，令容有伟。<div id='poem_sentence_36_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_249431'>爰翊殊庭，奠享仙机。<div id='poem_sentence_37_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_249431'>高灵委蛇，元气旭卉。<div id='poem_sentence_38_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_249431'>阴施自远，大功续似。<div id='poem_sentence_39_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_249431'>拥格纯禧，益厚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_40_249431", 249431, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>丕址</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_40_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_249431'>入宿庙下，月魄初朏。<div id='poem_sentence_41_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_249431'>龙章采藻，瓒爵擎跪。<div id='poem_sentence_42_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_249431'>拜于祢宫，慈颜仅咫。<div id='poem_sentence_43_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_249431'>至诚馨香，甘荐涤瀡。<div id='poem_sentence_44_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_249431'>哀念劬劳，譬瞻岵屺。<div id='poem_sentence_45_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_249431'>濯泪沾圭，将逡复止。<div id='poem_sentence_46_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_249431'>京都之南，崇丘迤逦。<div id='poem_sentence_47_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_249431'>飞螭蹑尘，法乘徐柅。<div id='poem_sentence_48_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_249431'>地环帟幄，霄揭隅雉。<div id='poem_sentence_49_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_249431'>警角飘萧，彀骑连累。<div id='poem_sentence_50_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_249431'>言降言陟，实惟告已。<div id='poem_sentence_51_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_249431'>烛错宵明，坛圪空紫。<div id='poem_sentence_52_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_249431'>交佩陆离，庶旄飒纚。<div id='poem_sentence_53_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_249431'>乐变神格，列周甲癸。<div id='poem_sentence_54_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_249431'>三后咸在，上苍临视。<div id='poem_sentence_55_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_249431'>皇皇富媪，从执笾簋。<div id='poem_sentence_56_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_249431'>七精闪忽，五镇瑰玮。<div id='poem_sentence_57_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_249431'>星官下翔，涛祗腾跱。<div id='poem_sentence_58_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_249431'>等级卑高，食饮嘘哆。<div id='poem_sentence_59_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_249431'>欣歆告言，奏福来底。<div id='poem_sentence_60_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_249431'>更御步辇，夹途军垒。<div id='poem_sentence_61_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_249431'>钲鼓惊轰，跳呼牛鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_62_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_249431'>异域穷陬，黄发稚齿。<div id='poem_sentence_63_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_249431'>动荡成波，欢喧成市。<div id='poem_sentence_64_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_249431'>端闱停午，玉色尚扆。<div id='poem_sentence_65_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_249431'>赦泽春行，幽加蛰蚁。<div id='poem_sentence_66_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_249431'>废滞振拔，垢瑕<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_249431", 249431, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>刷洗</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_67_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_249431'>宽贷赋取，削减逋诡。<div id='poem_sentence_68_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_249431'>皇帝慈孝，下民胥拟。<div id='poem_sentence_69_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_249431'>皇帝恩仁，四国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_249431", 249431, "Clauses/141/Comments/0")'>倾倚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_70_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_249431'>皇帝曰咨，群公卿士。<div id='poem_sentence_71_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_249431'>舜隆联夔，商圮朋嚭。<div id='poem_sentence_72_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_249431'>孰忠予是，孰谗予匪。<div id='poem_sentence_73_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_249431'>入官多门，孰予窒弭。<div id='poem_sentence_74_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_249431'>蓄兵过制，孰予究揣。<div id='poem_sentence_75_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_249431'>百姓窘穷，其患孰弛。<div id='poem_sentence_76_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_249431'>外夷狃骄，其强孰箠。<div id='poem_sentence_77_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_249431'>驱人以法，曾莫如耻。<div id='poem_sentence_78_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_249431'>化民成俗，曾莫如礼。<div id='poem_sentence_79_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_249431'>百官敕业，相予表里。<div id='poem_sentence_80_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_249431'>登任俊良，刬斥奸宄。<div id='poem_sentence_81_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_249431'>天锡帝年，万有亿秭。<div id='poem_sentence_82_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_249431'>天锡圣嗣，诜诜众子。<div id='poem_sentence_83_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_249431'>乾刚不息，章明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_84_249431", 249431, "Clauses/169/Comments/0")'>度揆</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_84_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_249431'>无疆惟民，惟帝其侍。<div id='poem_sentence_85_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_249431'>臣襄咏歌，直道是履。<div id='poem_sentence_86_249431_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_249431'></div><div id='poem_sentence_87_249431_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　蔡襄上《郊湮奏外甥恩泽状》<div id='poem_1167842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167842?labeling=true' target='_blank'>郊禋奏外甥恩泽状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1053年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167842")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167842'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167842'>右，臣叨尘侍从，无补盛明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167842_comment'></div>偶大礼之庆成，广推恩而逮下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167842_comment'></div>臣有亲姊之子戴乂，粗亲师训，未齿仕途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167842_comment'></div>幸属均釐，冀沾初命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167842_comment'></div>兼臣自皇祐年忝两制以来，不曾酌荐异姓恩泽，伏望圣慈许于文资内安排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167842_comment'></div>冒渎宸严，臣无任祈天俟命、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167842_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1167842_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年11月28日</a>　蔡襄作《郊燔帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《亳州永城县庙学记》<div id='poem_1168116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168116?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亳州永城县庙学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（皇祐五年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168116")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168116_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168116'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168116'>孔子之门人，颜渊最为高弟，其称之曰：「有颜回者好学，不迁怒，不贰过」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168116_comment'></div>昔之所以教人，与其所以为学者，类斯道尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168116_comment'></div>孔子没，其书传于后，而学者繇其言以之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168116_comment'></div>顾有不至者，非道之远，盖利汩之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168116_comment'></div>战国以材智相倾，士以儒文其身，而挟其私术趋时向利，独孟轲、荀况颛其所守，而不屈于当时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168116_comment'></div>汉以明经射策，六经之徒自名其家，颛务师说，是非或戾于大中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168116_comment'></div>然决大事尚傅经以正其义，故其治迹文质有可观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168116_comment'></div>由汉以来，世褒孔子，至列王爵而庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168116_comment'></div>郡县奠其春秋，用尊大其道，以劝民学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168116_comment'></div>而取士之路，以配词为进士，以数字为明经，中其选者，相蹑为公相，显荣天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168116_comment'></div>天下承流，其徒以千万数，至不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168116_comment'></div>其师弟子皆以仕进之具相从，幸如博奕，茍入科则禄仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168116_comment'></div>或以孔子之教人者倡于其徒，则为穷师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168116_comment'></div>以颜子之所为学者学之于人，则谓穷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168116_comment'></div>数百年间，虽大贤功业，班班见于史载，而其风化之美，不臻于三代之隆，盖其源流异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168116_comment'></div>亳州永城县孔子庙，居城西隅，庳陋不完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168116_comment'></div>皇祐四年，大理评事杜君谊知县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168116_comment'></div>杜君以孝行闻，而治民有诚信，以谓均赋徭、辨曲直、剔奸弊、兴美利，斯材吏之易能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168116_comment'></div>孰若教民以善道，而使渍于仁义乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168116_comment'></div>明年，出奉泉，迁庙于东南，直汴之阳，作文宣王及兖国公而下十人像，笾簋之数，率据典礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168116_comment'></div>又旁庙设学舍数十区，将以教育人材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168116_comment'></div>于是县人之为学者，各以其力相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168116_comment'></div>冬十二月，庙学成，杜君录其本末以来请文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168116_comment'></div>予谓居其舍者，师若弟子，皆知其所以教人与其所以为学之本，勉而求之，能以是治其心而立其身，所谓进士、明经之术者庸有不能哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168116_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168116_comment'></div>瞻于庙，游于学，以思其道，斯可谓之学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168116_comment'></div>舍是而言学，学斯为利；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168116_comment'></div>学其利乎，斯下也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168116_comment'></div>谨记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1168116'></div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1168116_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1168116'><span class='label'>谨记：</span>原无，据《二百家名贤文粹》补。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1168116_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年12月28日</a>　蔡襄作《砚记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1053&endYear=1053')">1053年</a>　蔡襄常同王洙切磋书艺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年1月</a>　蔡襄作《温成皇后挽词》二首。作品：《温成皇后挽词二首》<div id='poem_249268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>温成皇后挽词二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249268")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249268'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249268'>紫极腾轩曜，青春委蕣颜。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249268'>云軿何处去，金殿几时还。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249268'>仗下编箫咽，陵中夜烛閒。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249268'>六宫哀送返，疑是梦魂间。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249268'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249268_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249267?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年1月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249267'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249267'>翟䌽开新礼，金文易大名。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249267'>真游上仙路，故物感皇情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249267'>月落辞丹禁，春前引素旌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249267'>宫闱鸣挽铎，不是佩环声。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249267'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　蔡襄上《乞罢温成皇后立忌》疏。<div id='poem_1167724' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167724' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167724?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢温成皇后立忌奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167724")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167724_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167724'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167724'>臣伏闻陛下为温成皇后立忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167724_comment'></div>臣切谓圣人制礼，所以明轻重尊卑之节，过与不及，皆曰失礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167724_comment'></div>故太常设官，职在检详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167724_comment'></div>陛下临御天下三十馀年，动遵典法，圣德之盛，明如天日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167724_comment'></div>近者温成皇后薨逝，事不下礼官详检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167724_comment'></div>既以施行，虽有过当，无由追改，乃又立忌，考之于礼，未为适中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167724_comment'></div>伏以孝章、淑德、章怀四后于陛下为伯祖妣、为皇妣，其属之尊如此，向来奉慈，皆不立忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167724_comment'></div>温成皇后生则为妃，后乃追册，于陛下为卑幼之列，不应立忌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167724_comment'></div>伏望圣慈追还敕命，庶乎天下之人知陛下以礼断情，合于中道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167724_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167724_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年2月</a>　蔡襄上《乞不往奉先寺酌献》疏。<div id='poem_1167725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167725?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不往奉先寺酌献奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167725")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167725'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167725'>臣伏睹太常礼院公文，十二日驾幸奉先寺，诣庆基殿酌献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167725_comment'></div>盖陛下孝思之心，不惮所至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167725_comment'></div>然外人唯见向来奉先未尝亲往，今为温成皇后陵庙成就，恐因而谒庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167725_comment'></div>臣窃料陛下圣明，必不为此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167725_comment'></div>臣恐献议之人不思典礼，愿陛下深思熟议，以慰人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167725_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167725_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年春</a>　蔡襄上所摹真宗御制《奉神述》刊本，帝嘉之，特赐襄母卢氏冠帔。作品：《御书碑序》<div id='poem_1168050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御书碑序</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年六月二十四日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168050")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168050'>皇祐五年秋，陛下以真宗皇帝《奉神述》再刻之碑，亲誊篆额，敕臣模写，终篇既成，奏御，蒙赐臣御书一轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168050_comment'></div>臣辄形颂章，上述旨义，又辱奖诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168050_comment'></div>明年春，刊本上之，特赐臣母仁寿郡太君卢氏冠帔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168050_comment'></div>臣历考故事，未有列官侍从而宸毫赐字，不缘名品而象服及亲，独臣恩荣，前无比例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168050_comment'></div>伏惟陛下性资孝诚，覆养万物，精通经谊，游适艺文，矜优高年，原本慈惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168050_comment'></div>每观先帝睿文，若临宗庙，志容必尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168050_comment'></div>亲勒题颜，恭记一十九字，念思勤勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168050_comment'></div>以臣得与翰墨之间，探《春秋》褒劝之法，稽《虞书》谟谋之义，神笔飞动，妙入无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168050_comment'></div>敦尚老老，推及臣亲，日月之光，下烛幽昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168050_comment'></div>盖繇陛下根于仁厚而形于政事，岂愚者之虑所能诵道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168050_comment'></div>窃念臣出入省闼，向馀十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168050_comment'></div>其间居言诤，触贵权，所以护而器使之，悉赖天聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168050_comment'></div>今兹忝冒重叠，莫知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168050_comment'></div>谨摹御书及录奖诏，镌著于石，臣所献诗并亦附见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168050_comment'></div>传之四外，垂之万世，非特微臣之荣遇，抑亦兴朝之盛举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168050_comment'></div>至和元年六月二十四日，朝奉郎、起居舍人、知制诰、权同判吏部流内铨、上骑都尉、赐紫金鱼袋臣蔡襄谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1168050_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年5月</a>　蔡襄为苏舜元撰书《苏才翁墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168184' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168184' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168184?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏才翁墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168184")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168184_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168184'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168184'>苏才翁，讳舜元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168184_comment'></div>其先自汉典属国武葬武功，其后周邳公、隋房公、唐许公、文宪四相世居不迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168184_comment'></div>文宪之后曰传素，避广明乱，西入蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168184_comment'></div>其子振仕蜀为梓州桐山令，生剑州司马寓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168184_comment'></div>司马生赠刑部侍郎讳协，是为曾祖考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168184_comment'></div>其配薛氏追封河东郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168184_comment'></div>刑部生祖考赠太师、尚书令兼中书令讳易简，终礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168184_comment'></div>祖妣崔氏，广平郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168184_comment'></div>礼部生皇考赠工部侍郎讳耆，终尚书工部郎中、直史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168184_comment'></div>娶王氏，金城县太君，太尉文正公之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168184_comment'></div>生三子，皆有才名，而才翁最长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168184_comment'></div>七岁能为歌诗，文正公爱且奇之，奏授同学究出身，调蔡州兴平主簿，移尉越之新昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168184_comment'></div>时诏复唐十一科，而新令门选者不得与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168184_comment'></div>君乞还所有官以应诏，不得报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168184_comment'></div>乃上所著文章，召学士院试，赐进士出身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168184_comment'></div>明道中，主开封之扶沟簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168184_comment'></div>畿内饥甚，君欲发廪以赈之，其令畏缩，辄移病，君即出粟以活饥者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168184_comment'></div>用举任者改大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168184_comment'></div>服工部丧，外除知开封咸平县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168184_comment'></div>咸平聚兵以万计，军中旦阅卒，有厌大校之虐己者，方持弓矢，辄怒骂，众军牵连，一营惊哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168184_comment'></div>君闻之，至其所，众惶泣且诉，君慰劳罢之，因饮射至暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168184_comment'></div>明日，易其军校，而流其唱为惊哗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168184_comment'></div>迁殿中丞，移知眉州眉山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168184_comment'></div>会西夏元昊寇延安，君条上御贼方略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168184_comment'></div>知府事吴公遵路荐其才，除通判□州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168184_comment'></div>贼酋李兴归命，边州系之，而上其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168184_comment'></div>踰时□□下，君因言，其贼来者，宜厚其资，速宠借，以驱□其未至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168184_comment'></div>李兴辈反为囚虏，必已自悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168184_comment'></div>且元昊惨毒，而其偏校虽畏之，其心岂易服从哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168184_comment'></div>若饵以购赏，必相引而至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168184_comment'></div>并陈攻守利害十二事以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168184_comment'></div>以太夫人忧去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168184_comment'></div>寻勾当京东排岸司，改太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168184_comment'></div>三司使王公任君三司勾当公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168184_comment'></div>出为荆南路提点刑狱，未行，易福建路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168184_comment'></div>汀州民王宁殴王先至死，以赇盖覆，得不败，且三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168184_comment'></div>君至，即捕按。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168184_comment'></div>尚书屯田员外郎王稷为部将，治穷其事，发王先尸验其伤，犹然以岁久为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168184_comment'></div>君特奏杀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168184_comment'></div>又迁尚书祠部员外郎，移京西，未几又移河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168184_comment'></div>以弟舜钦谪死湖州，求江吴一郡，得扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168184_comment'></div>未至，改两浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168184_comment'></div>凡四皆为提点刑狱，君益谨职。<div class='inline'
