id='poem_sentence_42_1168184_comment'></div>颜杲卿、真卿之后流寓温州，君索其祖告身、家谍推之，得其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168184_comment'></div>建言近年守臣因贼屈附，抵法诛戳，盖忠义不修，莫为之劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168184_comment'></div>今二颜之裔曰惟孜、似贤，皆为编户民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168184_comment'></div>若录其嗣，显白二颜事，以动天下，可不刑而化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168184_comment'></div>朝廷特官颜氏二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168184_comment'></div>祀明堂恩，度支除京西转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168184_comment'></div>邕州峒獠钞二广，边用不给，君以所部羡钱二十万缗助之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168184_comment'></div>充三司度支判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168184_comment'></div>至和元年五月初二日，终于京师之祖第，年四十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168184_comment'></div>夫人刘氏，旌德县君，贤而有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168184_comment'></div>男曰涓，大理寺丞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168184_comment'></div>曰澥、注、洞，皆太庙斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168184_comment'></div>鸿、汶及二女皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168184_comment'></div>君曾祖而下葬开封府开封县宰辅乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168184_comment'></div>才翁之殁汴，无资产以为生，诸孤就养江南，居润州，侍柩以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168184_comment'></div>某年某月某日，葬于丹阳某乡，使人请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168184_comment'></div>某与才翁兄弟游最久，今皆已亡矣，尚忍铭哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168184_comment'></div>初，才翁少年，欲以文词进，愿还官就科试，思与天下英豪角逐于笔研间，以力决胜，不得如其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168184_comment'></div>逮边隅兵兴，夙夜讲画谋策，要以术数剪屈夷虏，书屡上，不见省用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168184_comment'></div>大臣如前丞相贾公、丞相文公、故参知政事范公，皆持国秉，力推荐之，终以序进，志不得骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168184_comment'></div>平居谈辩唐数百年间，喜称魏郑公谏诤、裴晋公德业，李临淮将兵、卫公处边事、刘忠州通流财利、韩退之文章，类此数人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168184_comment'></div>其议当世人物，亦以之为标的，于人少所称许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168184_comment'></div>至有同班列、偕出入，漫不省记，以是与者益少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1168184_comment'></div>然莅官当事，定虑果决，所至制束强黠，敦尚风仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1168184_comment'></div>其为文不迹故陈，自为高古，虽所不与者亦不能掩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1168184_comment'></div>君善草隶，藏书数千卷，皆手自雠校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1168184_comment'></div>撰述《奏御集》十卷、《塞垣近事》二卷、奏议三卷、文集十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1168184_comment'></div>课子舍治经史，率有准程，所以诸子皆积学有立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1168184_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1168184'>龙渊之器，不投兕犀，孰知其利？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1168184_comment'></div>志古豪英，不任于权，孰知其智？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1168184_comment'></div>负才自高，不屈于人，与世或异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1168184_comment'></div>先民之载，德不必年，贤不必位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1168184_comment'></div>大江之南，顺卜之吉，庆延嗣世。</div><div id='poem_sentence_75_1168184_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　蔡襄上《乞不书张尧封碑石札子》<div id='poem_1167860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167860?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不书张尧封碑石劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167860")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167860_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167860'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167860'>臣今月二十六日上殿，奏为奉敕书张尧封碑石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167860_comment'></div>念臣备员词掖，忝列近侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167860_comment'></div>书写碑铭合归书艺待诏之职，臣侵其官，有亏事体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167860_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈许赐矜免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167860_comment'></div>臣寻诣中书，窃知前状已曾进呈，伏乞传宣中书，许令缴纳张尧封敕命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167860_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167860_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年6月24日</a>　蔡襄进摹刻御书拓本。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　蔡襄尝向杜衍请教家礼，并自制《家庭献寿仪》，亲书遗子弟遵行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年7月</a>　蔡襄迁龙图阁学士、权知开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　御史马遵、吕景初、吴中复因论梁适被诏罢出，蔡襄封还词头，辞不草制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年8月21日</a>　蔡襄作《与长官书》致杜衍谢问候。<div id='poem_1167936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与长官书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年8月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167936")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167936'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167936'>襄启：远承惠问，厚意所存，益有感著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167936_comment'></div>知日来体气佳胜，殊为慰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167936_comment'></div>近被命尹治，日以穰剧，居不得暇，移书致谢，不尽缕缕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167936_comment'></div>惟眠食自重，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167936_comment'></div>襄拜手，长官足下，八月廿一日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1167936_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年9月</a>　蔡襄上疏《乞罢园陵监护司》<div id='poem_1167726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢园陵监护司奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167726")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167726'>臣伏见贵妃近册温成皇后，监护葬事称园陵监护使及都监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167726_comment'></div>始者众议皆云便去西京又来，已于奉先权攒，恩礼备至，附近京城，岁时易为照管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167726_comment'></div>外边人言尚疑有西行别作园陵，口语纷纷，于事体非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167726_comment'></div>伏乞明降圣旨中书，温成皇后已权攒毕，所有园陵监护司一切并停，所贵晓谕外人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167726_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1167726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　蔡襄上疏《乞不作温成皇后志文》<div id='poem_1167727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不作温成皇后志文奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167727")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167727'>臣奉圣旨检阅温成皇后葬要志文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167727_comment'></div>臣遍检古今，并无皇后葬礼更有志文，盖以名号已尊，兼有哀册，不合为志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167727_comment'></div>臣别具状，备载唐以来故事，伏乞圣慈省览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167727_comment'></div>所有御制，更不可作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167727_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1167727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年10月</a>　蔡襄因处理礼直官事不力遭御史弹劾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月</a>　十一月初，蔡襄撰书《太常丞管勾河东安抚使机宜文字蒲君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168191' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168191' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168191?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常丞管勾河东安抚使机宜文字蒲君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168191")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168191_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168191'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168191'>蒲君叔范，天圣八年自阆州以进士贡至京师，年二十，第中乙科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168191_comment'></div>余时少君一岁，而第同籍，居同巷，出处相从，意气相得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168191_comment'></div>皇祐五年，君以太常丞管勾河东安抚使司文书，随其府君并州，而余为知制诰、权礼部贡举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168191_comment'></div>有以雄词壮论异于众者，验其名氏，曰蒲宗孟，其父师道，乃君讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168191_comment'></div>是年春，宗孟释褐，予喜君之有子，且将贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168191_comment'></div>宗孟归，亟以书讣曰：「我先子以四月一日终于官，孤宗孟扶丧以寓京兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168191_comment'></div>明年十一月一日，遂葬京兆府咸阳县龙首乡之北原，敢以告」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168191_comment'></div>余既吊之，而为之志其墓曰：君曾祖茂璘仕伪蜀为彭州判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168191_comment'></div>祖颖士善藏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168191_comment'></div>父伸赠大理评事，三以乡荐，退于春官，自号北谷散夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168191_comment'></div>君承父词，又得所蓄书以读，而性警悟，十馀岁能诵经传、属诗赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168191_comment'></div>陈渐以文学名于蜀，一见君所为词章，乃以女妻之，今延福县君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168191_comment'></div>太夫人陈氏，追封奉先县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168191_comment'></div>君少失所恃，事继母朱氏，封寿昌县太君，礼孝尤至，故乡党称其词行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168191_comment'></div>及莅官处事，又以材闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168191_comment'></div>初授成州团练推官，吏易君年少不更事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168191_comment'></div>君未旬月，已通法令簿书，擿其隐谩，惕惕畏服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168191_comment'></div>再调延州推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168191_comment'></div>元昊慢形见，君谓州将郭劝曰：「度元昊必变，变则延为寇冲，城圮堑堙，无以为备，愿建言治之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168191_comment'></div>郭劝以其言闻于朝，报不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168191_comment'></div>既而元昊果叛，诏城延州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168191_comment'></div>君曰：「役促民劳，未战而困也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168191_comment'></div>范雍以振武节度为陕西经略使，治延州，宦者卢守勤为兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168191_comment'></div>中贵人临边，自喜事必己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168191_comment'></div>尝欲决有所行，而雍难之，守勤怒发声色，引起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168191_comment'></div>君止之复坐，曰：「太尉为大帅，而军政不一，钤辖骄傲如此，何以帅下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168191_comment'></div>愿太尉斩之以徇众」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168191_comment'></div>守勤泣恨，日捃其过，至罢归，莫能塞所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168191_comment'></div>寻为武宁军节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168191_comment'></div>梁、洋二州人争水利，数十年竞讼，至破产不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168191_comment'></div>朝廷下其讼，转运使遣君按视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168191_comment'></div>君从二州人以行，随所曲直而辨之，为立约束，分水溉注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168191_comment'></div>二州之人各当所欲，迄今便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168191_comment'></div>以父忧去职，服除，除郓州观察判官、监杭州清酒务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168191_comment'></div>改太子中允，知京兆之高陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168191_comment'></div>高陵前号难治，君后威刑而先礼教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168191_comment'></div>有父兄告其子弟之不令者，君召其子弟语之曰：「顺于父为孝，顺于兄为悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168191_comment'></div>汝以悍父兄之心迁而为顺，则为善人，夫何难哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168191_comment'></div>我即坐汝，不人类矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168191_comment'></div>闻者爱服迁善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168191_comment'></div>县豪距县二十里作府君神祠，以巫觋蓄蛇怪，日言祸福，箫鼓歌舞通昼夜，男女往来，输金缯木石为之立庙，至有冒为尚方器服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168191_comment'></div>君与民期曰：「令将礼府君神」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168191_comment'></div>民闻令来，悉集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168191_comment'></div>既至，群豪翼巫觋以导，君曰：「未斋洁，未宜见神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168191_comment'></div>且汝能迎置府君神者，及能帅众力而庙者，巫能通神以下祸福者，果谁乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168191_comment'></div>众各指之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168191_comment'></div>君即麾缚数十人，绳以严法，籍其材而夷其庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168191_comment'></div>移知泉之晋江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168191_comment'></div>会宣徽使李昭亮知延州，奏君改发署判官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168191_comment'></div>宣徽徙澶州、并州，皆辟为从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168191_comment'></div>君感宣徽之知己，事无钜细，力为画议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168191_comment'></div>君沈静有识虑，压于贵势，必诤辨是非，平居鲜语人过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168191_comment'></div>喜察奸贪，梏其手则已，不务烦苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168191_comment'></div>善议论，上书言御戎、备蜀、广储嗣事，皆切于世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168191_comment'></div>而官止太常丞，年止四十有六，自初仕至终皆在幕府，助人为政，而未尝得专所为以见于人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168191_comment'></div>既卒，贫空，孤宗孟绍其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168191_comment'></div>有女七人，三嫁为士人妻，四人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168191_comment'></div>其称明年，至和元年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168191_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1168191'>才不必有位，而德不必有年，或曰命然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168191_comment'></div>生有善行，而殁有嗣传，孰与祉焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168191_comment'></div>已乎奈何，归安兹阡！</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1168191_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年11月4日</a>　蔡襄上《请杂买务以见钱市》奏章，诏从之。<div id='poem_1167799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请杂买务市物给见钱奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和元年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167799")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167799'>内东门市行人物，有累年未偿价钱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167799_comment'></div>请自今并关杂买务以见钱市之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167799_comment'></div>其降出物帛亦估直于左藏库给钱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1167799_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167799'><span class='label'>按：</span>《续资治通鉴长编》卷一七七。又见《宋会要辑稿》食货五五之一九（第六册第五七五六页）、食货六四之四二（第七册第六一二○页）。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167799_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年12月</a>　蔡襄承办宰相陈执中宠妾张氏笞死婢女案。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年</a>　尝在欧阳修处观碑本，并有题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年2月</a>　蔡襄以母老求知泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄有书寄余靖。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年3月</a>　诏准蔡襄所请知泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄有札致富弼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄为长子匀请荫职，并为其主婚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年4月</a>　蔡襄作《读乐天闲居赋》<div id='poem_249395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>读乐天閒居篇</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249395")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249395'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249395'>予年四十四，发白成衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249395'>非有高盖车，曷与贤者同。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249395'>嗟予出寒远<span class='inlineComment2'>（蔡本作素）</span>，家世尝力农。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249395'>十九登科第，圣彀参英雄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249395'>十年出吏选，校书蓬渚中<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：是年二十九。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249395'>天子设采拔，谓有谏诤风。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249395'>既叨言责地<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：三十二。）</span>，蹇蹇思匪躬。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249395'>窃不自度量，语剡奸邪胸。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249395'>一毫抗千钧，摈落无流踪。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249395'>同时皆骧首，金紫班著崇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249395'>唯予守长乐，幸就禄养丰<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：三十四。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249395'>八年江海外，再上螭阶东。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249395'>四十入西阁，宿仇司化工。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249395'>蒙锦投机阱，唯赖天听聪。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249395'>代言游禁密，侍从多从容。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249395'>寻行京兆事，击断露铦锋。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249395'>是职非所好，辄以死竭忠。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249395'>愿辟大幽都，为君囚四凶。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249395'>愿拂西省堂，为君延夔龙。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249395'>愿舒泰山云，甘泽成岁功。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249395'>愿回太清日，晴景破阴蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249395'>愿跻万人寿，夭扎终不逢。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249395'>愿令编户富，食衣无困穷。<div id='poem_sentence_22_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_249395'>群臣走率职，陛下居法宫。<div id='poem_sentence_23_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_249395'>文彩成礼乐，筹略羁夷戎。<div id='poem_sentence_24_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_249395'>意言亦良苦，精神庶潜通。<div id='poem_sentence_25_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_249395'>短步趋远道，心健力不充。<div id='poem_sentence_26_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_249395'>早衰鬓已华，忧伤乃自攻。<div id='poem_sentence_27_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_249395'>我知古人心，生德贯上穹。<div id='poem_sentence_28_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_249395'>何为论贵贱，贵畏非大公。<div id='poem_sentence_29_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_249395'>南归虽云乐，此念殊忡忡。<div id='poem_sentence_30_249395_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_249395'></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_249395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄作《因书答河东转运杨乐道》答杨畋。<div id='poem_249181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249181?labeling=true' target='_blank'>因书答河东转运杨乐道</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249181")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249181'>前岁君提岭外兵，国门南路送君行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249181'>由来成事多天幸，直向危时见世情。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249181'>勉力朝廷论大计，甘心江海就私荣<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：予请罢开封府，出知泉州。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249181'>牢愁应解侵人骨，未老先教白发生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249181_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　复致书李端懿，谢讯问，继又登门拜谢。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年4月24日</a>　蔡襄致书杜衍，谢信问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年5月</a>　奉亲眷离都，王素等设宴饯行。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ea8622d5c43744a5956e2145681c2c87_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ea8622d5c43744a5956e2145681c2c87");'><span id='ea8622d5c43744a5956e2145681c2c87_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1065')">1061-1065年</a>，50-54岁</div><div id='ea8622d5c43744a5956e2145681c2c87' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年4月</a>　四月中旬，蔡襄将入京畿，忽接诏令改授翰林学士、权三司使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄复上《泉州回交代启》<div id='poem_1167974' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167974' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167974?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泉州回交代启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167974")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167974_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167974'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167974'>膺命簉藩，交龟视事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167974_comment'></div>否德踰爵，无裨汉诏之严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167974_comment'></div>善政告新，幸服萧规之诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167974_comment'></div>喜及瓜而为代，伤折柳以赠行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167974_comment'></div>诣阙旌轩，淹致尧而有素；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167974_comment'></div>攀辕父老，思借寇以无阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167974_comment'></div>念祖礼之空疏，剩思心之愧结。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167974_comment'></div>去德未移于旬浃，因风频寄于年华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167974_comment'></div>敢图谦矩之光，加有公函之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167974_comment'></div>巽辞温密，诚虚长者之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167974_comment'></div>褒旨勤隆，似重宵人之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167974_comment'></div>永言佩刻，迥异等常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167974_comment'></div>顾水驿之阻修，逼年籥之遒暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167974_comment'></div>勉祈宝啬，前拜宠灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167974_comment'></div>祷系之私，剡濡曷既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167974_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1167974_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄拜会欧阳修，欧为其形容衰老所惊叹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄撰书《尚书屯田员外郎赠光禄卿刘公墓碣》<div id='poem_1168174' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168174' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168174?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田员外郎赠光禄卿刘公墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168174")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168174_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168174'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168174'>公讳若虚，字叔阳，姓刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168174_comment'></div>汉之衰，楚元王子孙不去彭城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168174_comment'></div>历魏晋以来，彭城刘犹为著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168174_comment'></div>至唐，司徒晏以雄材精智，用转流轻重之术，于乾元、上元之间饱国饥者二十年，至宰相，功名益显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168174_comment'></div>晏兄暹为汾州刺史，治有声称，生大理评事谈经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168174_comment'></div>评事生左常侍濛，常侍生吏部郎中埴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168174_comment'></div>自司徒至吏部四世，或居长安，或在汾晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168174_comment'></div>吏部生伎，实公之曾祖考也，为鄂州节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168174_comment'></div>湖南帅据其地自王，兵四起，乃以其孥循江入闽，居泉州，卒葬南安县，始为闽人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168174_comment'></div>鄂州生文济，是为祖考，徙家福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168174_comment'></div>闽王王审知以其女妻之，卒官吏部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168174_comment'></div>生皇考府君讳甫，闽亡，仕钱吴越王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168174_comment'></div>法自取所部以为俸，府君不入一钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168174_comment'></div>逮王归京师，而其官属大小皆得仕，府君以母老辞不就禄，至今乡闾称其孝廉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168174_comment'></div>娶李氏，生子九人，公其次子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168174_comment'></div>公严明有大略，始学，见钞录集书如《白氏六帖》类，即麾去，曰：「要当以法禁去之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168174_comment'></div>通五经大要，擿其旨义以为修身治官之用，不茍为利禄学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168174_comment'></div>咸平五年登进士第，授大理评事、知温州永嘉县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168174_comment'></div>还，上所为文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168174_comment'></div>真宗皇帝尚儒，每亲程自言者，召中书试，就迁寺丞、知隰州温泉县，移通判保定军，再迁太常博士、通判洪州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168174_comment'></div>大姓胡氏子杀人，以厚赀雇老贫者代死，举郡为之覆藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168174_comment'></div>狱且成，公曰：「被杀者年少壮强，今囚瘠老，岂能制其命」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168174_comment'></div>躬劾之，果老贫者自卖以资其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168174_comment'></div>于是捕弃胡氏子市，出受钱代死者，郡中惊伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168174_comment'></div>濒江民以渔为生，而土豪常半取之，曰：「江食我田，汝渔当吾田所也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168174_comment'></div>公按视，奏除没江田租，纵民渔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168174_comment'></div>改尚书屯田员外郎、知邵武军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168174_comment'></div>其俗鬼而不医，平居杀牛聚酒，侮欺善良，喜斗击，以气力加人，而得罪戮，意惬不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168174_comment'></div>公至，彻淫祠，禁巫觋，教病者药；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168174_comment'></div>朋醉群斗、贼窃恃强，寘于深法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168174_comment'></div>又治孔子庙，收学者为之开说孝弟之行，尊奖贤节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168174_comment'></div>吏民刷故所为，而听公之所以为，俗习大变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168174_comment'></div>年五十，终于官，天禧三年二月二十三日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168174_comment'></div>其年九月八日辛酉，葬福州怀安县越城里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168174_comment'></div>公以恩受其父之太子洗马致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168174_comment'></div>祖母冯翊县太君，母潘源县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168174_comment'></div>夫人新郑县君，赠工部侍郎潘吉甫之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168174_comment'></div>谨淑有礼，嫔于大家，承上以顺，睦众以和，终三十年，人未始闻其笑骂声，闺门之内肃然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168174_comment'></div>及公卒，愈自约，以奉时祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168174_comment'></div>敕诸子学，遂以有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168174_comment'></div>为妇为母，皆有称问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168174_comment'></div>男四人：长曰弇，不迩势利，负奇自隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168174_comment'></div>曰弈，有大材智；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168174_comment'></div>曰异，以文学知名，皆终尚书屯田员外郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168174_comment'></div>曰戒，未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168174_comment'></div>女适进士林孝伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168174_comment'></div>襄初与奕、异为同年进士，弈尝谓予言：丁谓为宰相私天下，士必归我乃得进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168174_comment'></div>闻公声名，欲屈一见，即推进之，公不肯往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168174_comment'></div>于是始知公之所以立身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168174_comment'></div>庆历中，余知福州，州人言公事亲，亲有疾，辄不食酒肉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168174_comment'></div>居亲侧，虽大暑中夕，必严衣冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168174_comment'></div>长幼内外皆有法度，乡人效之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168174_comment'></div>又知公之所以为家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168174_comment'></div>后为转运使，至邵武，邵武称公廉平，市人持物入廨舍以就善价，属官莫敢侵牟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168174_comment'></div>治事快于决疑，静于临剧，初若不更意虑，及施下皆当理要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168174_comment'></div>守法不贷，而民不敢怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168174_comment'></div>又知公之所以为政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168174_comment'></div>是三者，皆世人之所难者，故悉书以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168174_comment'></div>公以二子为郎，累赠光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168174_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1168174'>刘自汉文史载陈，唐有管萧晏其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168174_comment'></div>厥材绝特持国钧，晏兄而下八世孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168174_comment'></div>刚严明允惠在民，蟠于郡治屈所伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168174_comment'></div>种施必获后嗣振，孰从考信唯隧文。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1168174_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年4月19日</a>　蔡襄撰书《尚书屯田员外郎通判润州刘君墓碣》完成。<div id='poem_1168175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田员外郎通判润州刘君墓碣</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐六年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168175")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168175'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168175'>君讳奕，字蒙伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168175_comment'></div>其先，汉唐以来，世有显人，至祖考皆仕国朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168175_comment'></div>考讳若虚，尚书屯田员外郎，赠光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168175_comment'></div>光禄之碑，襄尝铭之，系次详焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168175_comment'></div>君天圣八年进士及第，授惠州推官，疾不果行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168175_comment'></div>次调南康军判官，移知洪州武宁县事，改大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168175_comment'></div>累迁尚书屯田员外郎，历知郑之荥阳、凤翔府判官、通判漳州、润州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168175_comment'></div>以皇祐三年五月二十三日终润州，年五十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168175_comment'></div>明年正月二十四日葬福州怀安县灵山乡越城里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168175_comment'></div>夫人陈氏，封宝应县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168175_comment'></div>子康夫、宁夫、岐夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168175_comment'></div>女，长适韩昌国，次明州慈溪令陈章，其季进士林回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168175_comment'></div>君于文章，要以道理为得，不茍声律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168175_comment'></div>其论性情，推明孔子之法，尤非浮屠所传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168175_comment'></div>力教于人，开晓其路，从之学者咸以吾道自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168175_comment'></div>久之，贫无以生，就举进士，中乙科，喜曰：「吾不能为时之文章，恐不复得仕进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168175_comment'></div>今幸中第，吾志得矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168175_comment'></div>其在武宁，民喜讼而易刑，为令者多严法以止之，犹不能胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168175_comment'></div>君虽细事，为之尽心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168175_comment'></div>有兄弟讼者，譬之亲爱之理以感动之，辄涕泣自咎引去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168175_comment'></div>刑省而民犕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168175_comment'></div>庆历中，元昊叛，陕西用兵，韩丞相为经略使，辟君，凤翔一道兵民剧事，多倚君办集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168175_comment'></div>连年兵败民穷，乃上书朝廷，言其兵所以败，民所以穷之状，其略曰：「陕西之要，练兵运粮最为首务，其策皆未为得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168175_comment'></div>都部署者，上将军之任也，而无专制之权，其偏裨才否，不敢辄去留之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168175_comment'></div>军无行阵之法，见利轻进，畏敌遽退，所以每战必败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168175_comment'></div>偏裨不死上将之令，士卒不知什伍之制，其理岂有胜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168175_comment'></div>边戍益多，廪粟益广，转运使职其事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168175_comment'></div>今之转运使皆以序进，不计其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168175_comment'></div>未更年岁，屡迁易之，文书凡目，曾未能知，其暇以民为意乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168175_comment'></div>一方之患，内靡度支，外辍两川之赋，调及天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168175_comment'></div>关陕之民流离穷困，而边储日窘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168175_comment'></div>不幸天下之患有大于此，何以支乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168175_comment'></div>盖由转运使不择其材，不久其任，无所归责也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168175_comment'></div>又言：「被边宜募土人，给其閒田，使之自卫其境，可以省费」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168175_comment'></div>言数十条，率多此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168175_comment'></div>事格不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168175_comment'></div>漳州漳浦有虔州民四百人，入县买官所卖盐，令捕之，民因斗拒，遂鞫其私贩而强捍，其法应死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168175_comment'></div>囚多系久，疫殍相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168175_comment'></div>君为直其非私贩，而出其不斗拒者，坐法数十人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168175_comment'></div>君初仕，愿天下事若无所为而可办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168175_comment'></div>历官二十年，所至施为谋议，多不能如其意，然后知不可以力为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168175_comment'></div>于是补吏南归，展省坟域，缅然有退耕之志，而未果也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168175_comment'></div>其终之岁，予适过润州，君病渍，以手书谓予曰：「吾止于此矣，惟稚子是托」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168175_comment'></div>既终，敛无新衣，囊无馀资，郡吏民集钱二百千以赙，夫人辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168175_comment'></div>归葬于闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168175_comment'></div>居无室庐，产无田园，勤劳其家，清节不渝，夫人之力焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168175_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168175_comment'></div>十年之间，康夫以学行自立，又能请文永其先烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168175_comment'></div>予既悲之，而又庆其有后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168175_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1168175'>文弊于词，在天圣初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168175_comment'></div>牵拘媲偶，华调剽肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168175_comment'></div>君于斯文，本末扶疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168175_comment'></div>世言性情，沦于浮屠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168175_comment'></div>君为中庸，圣哲之枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168175_comment'></div>经营万务，于时有需。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168175_comment'></div>既官于陕，昼思夕图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168175_comment'></div>条兵转饷，实究民痡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168175_comment'></div>上书于朝，事愿之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168175_comment'></div>漳有冤狱，十百其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168175_comment'></div>办处平治，脱释不辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168175_comment'></div>最后丹阳，声闻益敷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168175_comment'></div>斋终克明，归宅海隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168175_comment'></div>父子兄弟，次序不踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168175_comment'></div>既顺以安，斯其已乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168175_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1168175'>嘉祐六年岁次辛丑四月十九日，枢密直学士、尚书礼部郎中莆阳蔡襄撰并书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168175_comment'></div>陶翼模刻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1168175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1168175'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷三三。又见乾隆《福建通志》卷七三，《八琼室金石补正》卷一○一，《闽中金石志》卷七，民国《福建通志·金石志》石六，国家图书馆藏拓片·章专二五五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1168175_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年4月28日</a>　蔡襄正式授官翰林学士、权三司使。作品：《辞权三司使表》<div id='poem_1167814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞权三司使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年4月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167814")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167814'>臣襄言：四月二十八日，蒙恩授臣翰林学士、权三司使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167814_comment'></div>地亲任重，宠数殊优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167814_comment'></div>资薄才微，公议非允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167814_comment'></div>臣襄诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167814_comment'></div>伏念向繇枢职，出治泉山，奉高年之慈亲，还就养于旧里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167814_comment'></div>昨承诏旨，召还京师，屡降德音，不容让免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167814_comment'></div>驱驰百舍之远，趋伏九阍之严，曾未达于近畿，复迁处于大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167814_comment'></div>天下通流之术，非小智可以营为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167814_comment'></div>禁中命令之词，非空言可以润饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167814_comment'></div>加以支离之悴，久辞浩剧之权，今所领者益烦，顾于力而不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167814_comment'></div>茍失量度，是谓暗愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167814_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下特收涣汗之恩，更择长材而用，俾违要重，庶得安全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167814_comment'></div>有禄庇身，固能自足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167814_comment'></div>怀忠效国，誓竭素心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167814_comment'></div>谨具表辞免以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1167814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄又上《辞权三司使表》，不允。<div id='poem_1167814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞权三司使表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年4月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167814")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167814'>臣襄言：四月二十八日，蒙恩授臣翰林学士、权三司使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167814_comment'></div>地亲任重，宠数殊优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167814_comment'></div>资薄才微，公议非允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167814_comment'></div>臣襄诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167814_comment'></div>伏念向繇枢职，出治泉山，奉高年之慈亲，还就养于旧里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167814_comment'></div>昨承诏旨，召还京师，屡降德音，不容让免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167814_comment'></div>驱驰百舍之远，趋伏九阍之严，曾未达于近畿，复迁处于大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167814_comment'></div>天下通流之术，非小智可以营为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167814_comment'></div>禁中命令之词，非空言可以润饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167814_comment'></div>加以支离之悴，久辞浩剧之权，今所领者益烦，顾于力而不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167814_comment'></div>茍失量度，是谓暗愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167814_comment'></div>伏望尊号皇帝陛下特收涣汗之恩，更择长材而用，俾违要重，庶得安全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167814_comment'></div>有禄庇身，固能自足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167814_comment'></div>怀忠效国，誓竭素心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167814_comment'></div>谨具表辞免以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1167814_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《奏乞推恩卢侗状》<div id='poem_1167840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167840?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞推恩卢侗状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167840")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167840'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167840'>右，臣伏见潮州长史卢侗行实朴茂，学术优深，久在岭南，众所称服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167840_comment'></div>皇祐年中，蒙恩充补长史，先与差摄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167840_comment'></div>至和二年，就摄已满两考，转运司保明，解发赴铨除注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167840_comment'></div>铨司准嘉祐四年六月条贯，摄官须得三周年为满任，以此釐革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167840_comment'></div>缘侗发解在未降新敕以前，合依旧条施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167840_comment'></div>侗久居京师，不能自陈，栖栖南归，绝仕进意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167840_comment'></div>臣知侗最久，仰其学行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167840_comment'></div>昨于杭州遇侗，臣不欲盛时以毫末之愆失一贤士，遂与侗俱来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167840_comment'></div>伏望朝廷下流内铨与注一官，庶使寒悴之人上沾恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167840_comment'></div>如朝廷与官后，犯正入己赃，臣甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167840_comment'></div>其人在朝别无亲的骨肉，兼与臣不是亲属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167840_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1167840_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《奏为故崇信军节度副使尹洙为泾原路经略时借支官钱回易公用别无玷污已因此死于贬所臣以西事十年在边任使甚久今家贫无依乞朝举牵复旧秩与一子官庶使沉冤荷圣泽事状》作品：《奏为故崇信军节度副使尹洙为泾原路径略时借支官钱回易公用别无玷污已因此死于贬所臣以西事十年在边任使甚久今家贫无依乞朝举牵复旧秩与一子官庶使沉冤荷圣泽事状》<div id='poem_1167832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏为故崇信军节度副使尹洙为泾原路经略时借支官钱回易公用别无玷污已因此死于贬所臣以西事十年在边任事甚久今家贫无依伏乞朝举牵复旧秩与一子官庶使沈冤□圣泽事状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167832")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167832'>臣伏见故崇信军节度副使尹洙，庆历四年以司谏知渭州，兼泾原路经略部署。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167832_comment'></div>是时郑戬为陕西经略招讨安抚使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167832_comment'></div>建议脩永落城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167832_comment'></div>永落属泾原，泾原路相度，尹洙以为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167832_comment'></div>会郑戬罢四路经略，犹称前官移文刘沪、董士廉等，脩城如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167832_comment'></div>尹洙以刘沪属本路兵官，令其罢役，辄拒不从，将加之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167832_comment'></div>遂与郑戬互有奏论，洙移晋州，刘沪释放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167832_comment'></div>臣闻尹洙之说，郑戬已罢四路经略，移牒处分不属管辖路分军马，有郑戬之心则治，无郑戬之心则乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167832_comment'></div>刘沪等拒见属之帅命，从已罢之使符，按之军法，自当抵罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167832_comment'></div>洙之说理道甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167832_comment'></div>董士廉因此怨雠，构造词讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167832_comment'></div>朝廷遣台勘鞠，唯得承例借贷官钱，回易公用，其馀推穷至悉，无分毫玷污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167832_comment'></div>狱官法外饰润虚词，置之槛阱，洙寻死于贬所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167832_comment'></div>一触权贵，内外协攻，遂使衔冤九泉，不照白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167832_comment'></div>皇祐中，谏官李兑、右正言贾黯各有章疏言洙之罪太深，乞与一子官，书奏报罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167832_comment'></div>臣伏见西事十年，自始至终，尹洙在边，履历最久，至于饮食寤寐，力计狂寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167832_comment'></div>薄命无成，卒罹罪罟，物论怜之，至今不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167832_comment'></div>怀忠负义，身为国用，人情之大节也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167832_comment'></div>原情宥过，盖护善良，人主之盛德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167832_comment'></div>如洙之词学才器，名在天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167832_comment'></div>尽瘁营公，不恤当路，将欲有益于时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167832_comment'></div>一旦仇人捃摭，台官风闻，狱吏锻鍊，有司议法，谪则谪，死则死，岂暇自明哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167832_comment'></div>使洙且存至今，必自辨雪，不幸亡殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167832_comment'></div>知洙之详者仅五七人，十馀年间，死者已半，岁月益久，昭洗无期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167832_comment'></div>洙惟一子，家贫无依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167832_comment'></div>伏望陛下俯回天光，下烛幽壤，追还旧秩，官其一子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167832_comment'></div>使喑噎之魂，释禁锢之负，零丁衰绪，禄及其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167832_comment'></div>干渎圣慈，臣无任兢惧激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167832_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1167832_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《乞叙用吕溱状》<div id='poem_1167838' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167838' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167838?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞叙用吕溱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167838")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167838_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167838'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167838'>右，臣伏见南京分司中溱降官责废已来，闻诸道路，皆谓坐费公使钱，罪当夺官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167838_comment'></div>臣尝见吕溱历典苏、楚、杭、徐数州，所至皆有风称，绝无贪名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167838_comment'></div>况其壮年已在近侍，岂肯自弃如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167838_comment'></div>然其为人，资性疏阔，脱略细务，诚恐检防不至，致陷深法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167838_comment'></div>臣窃见顷年苏舜钦监进奏院日，卖官故纸为伶人之费，坐监主自盗，除名为民，遂卒贬所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167838_comment'></div>事出仇人，情轻法重，至今天下冤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167838_comment'></div>臣恐吕溱所犯，多或类此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167838_comment'></div>兼溱素贫，夺禄閒居，便至失所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167838_comment'></div>伏望朝廷矜悯，特赐牵复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167838_comment'></div>使溱少加检防，不忽鄙碎，尽心临事，其于补报陛下，未可量也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167838_comment'></div>干浼圣慈，臣无任战惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167838_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1167838_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《乞叙用孙沔状》<div id='poem_1167839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞叙用孙沔状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167839")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167839'>右，臣伏见分司南京孙沔以罪谴谪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167839_comment'></div>臣以守官海域，去京师至远，事出传闻，不得真实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167839_comment'></div>然观贬降之重，及有履秽之词，皆谓孙沔知杭州日，有赵氏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167839_comment'></div>沔诚有之，固当重责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167839_comment'></div>然沔之治杭州，刬除蠹弊，击擿豪强，令行禁止，与浮屠、大族日为雠敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167839_comment'></div>其间虽有过当，而风俗混淆，至今衰息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167839_comment'></div>所为如是，虽至愚之人，必能自察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167839_comment'></div>沔虽阔略，然老于人事，以严明自处，而辄为不法至此，使一日罢去，小人共怨，何恃而得安全？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167839_comment'></div>是明目而投槛阱，孰肯为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167839_comment'></div>臣恐审问体量之际，未得其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167839_comment'></div>臣闻赵氏与父同日下审问所，其父一夕而死，所以道路之言皆谓搒掠以成其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167839_comment'></div>古者大臣不理沈冤，沔以尝副枢宥，待罪而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167839_comment'></div>臣恐继今以后，大臣有罪，不能自明，由沔而始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167839_comment'></div>顷年侬贼寇钞二广，近侍至多，独沔被遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167839_comment'></div>瘴毒恶地，干戈危处，沔亲当之，是亦有劳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167839_comment'></div>今以累赦之馀，三州检索，安能无过？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167839_comment'></div>沔且老矣，摧落之馀，岂复自振，然臣子之分，恶名难受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167839_comment'></div>伏乞陛下哀怜，念已用之效，察难明之咎，湔洗拂拭，有所任用，必能修省，以报陛下天地再生之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167839_comment'></div>干浼圣慈，臣无任战惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167839_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167839_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1167839'>能修：原无，据宋本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1167839_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167839'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1167839_0'>⑴ 《蔡忠惠集》卷二一。又见《皇朝文鉴》卷四八，《历代名臣奏议》卷一三二。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1167839_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《奏乞李端恩泽》状。<div id='poem_1167841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167841?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏乞李端恩泽状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167841")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167841'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167841'>右，臣伏见建州李端，素习医方，久敦善行，尽心博济，为众所称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167841_comment'></div>兼臣抱病闽中，仰其药石，敢援近例，辄冀推恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167841_comment'></div>伏望朝廷特与试秩，以劝辈流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167841_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1167841_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《举知抚州黄虞部状》<div id='poem_1167835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举知抚州黄虞部状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167835")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167835'>右：臣伏见朝报，知抚州军州事、尚书虞部员外郎黄瑊，近为举官事不得原赦，追官勒停者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167835_comment'></div>臣窃以法令之设，贵于必行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167835_comment'></div>人情之来，亦有可恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167835_comment'></div>如瑊之过，本非故为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167835_comment'></div>知人之难，保任之失，亦所难免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167835_comment'></div>然连坐之科，固当责励，斯法令之所以必行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167835_comment'></div>今闻其迁延日月，缘其家有葬事，未即之官，遂坐滞留，不原恩霈，其情似有可恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167835_comment'></div>臣窃见瑊材器明敏，资性公廉，所至有声，临事不茍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167835_comment'></div>惜其年齿渐以衰暮，欲望朝廷许令检责归里，如实有事故，特许原赦，与之重难处勾当差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167835_comment'></div>如蒙允用，后有犯正入己赃及当官不职，臣并甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167835_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1167835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄上《启请里正衙前札子》<div id='poem_1167863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>启请里正衙前劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167863")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167863'>臣伏见去年张问启请里正衙前条贯，第一户充衙前已经五年，许令人户纠决，却充衙前，要得宽纾次第人户，已颁行天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167863_comment'></div>臣前知泉州、福州，备见乡户衙前旧来敕条，约每州合用人数、存留，上等人排定姓名，逐年勾差，以物产高下为重难分数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167863_comment'></div>只如合用十人，存留百户，是十年一次充役，十贯产钱合差重难十分，七贯只差七分，最为均平，兼绝词讼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167863_comment'></div>若今五年却充衙前，二十年间便充四次，虽有富强，无不破产，于理未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167863_comment'></div>臣昨离福建，已见民间词讼，妄相纠决，久远不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167863_comment'></div>臣欲乞下本路转运司相度，如是旧来条贯实利便，乞令转运司便行指挥，依旧排名差遣讫奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167863_comment'></div>臣今建言，只是福建一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167863_comment'></div>切缘南北风俗事体不同，别路州军亦乞下转运司相度利害施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167863_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年8月</a>　闰八月，蔡襄作《致崇班书》<div id='poem_1167901' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167901' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167901?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与崇班书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167901")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167901_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167901'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167901'>襄启：为别日久，倾系良多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167901_comment'></div>自抵京都，首承问书，感激！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167901_comment'></div>贤郎回日，适以萦冗，不果裁答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167901_comment'></div>秋凉，官下安鬯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167901_comment'></div>未期展晤，更自寿，不一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167901_comment'></div>襄白，崇班足下，闰月十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167901_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1167901'>榷局为新条，在任不得举，恐知之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1167901_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年9月9日</a>　蔡襄参加重阳北园赐宴，作《北园登高即事呈诸同僚》<div id='poem_249172' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249172' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249172?labeling=true' target='_blank'>北园登高即事呈诸同僚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249172")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249172_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249172'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249172'>江云寒薄不成霜，九月登高菊未黄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249172'>飞镝有声弓已力，小槽分溜酒初尝。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249172_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249172'>秋容行见丹枫老，客意难胜紫陌长<span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄作《致张安道尚书书》<div id='poem_1167922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与张安道尚书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1167922'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167922'>违去门阑之日滋久，近得还都，以旧疾未平，加之人事，故疏驰问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167922_comment'></div>詹跂风采，不胜倾系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167922_comment'></div>气候寒凛，伏惟镇抚藩圉，神体休泰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167922_comment'></div>某叨此计局，通流之术，本非所能，超据要地，第负兢陈，日祈柄用，比芘末游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167922_comment'></div>区区下诚，莫由敷叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167922_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167922_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄作《致彦猷侍读书》》<div id='poem_1167895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与彦猷侍读书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167895")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167895'>襄再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167895_comment'></div>远蒙遣信至都，披奉教约，感戢之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167895_comment'></div>彦范或闻已过南都，旦夕当见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167895_comment'></div>青社虽号名藩，然交游殊思君侯之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167895_comment'></div>近丽正之拜，禁林有嫌，冯当世独以金华召，亦不须玉堂，唯此之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167895_comment'></div>霜风薄寒，伏惟爱重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167895_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167895_comment'></div>襄上，彦猷侍读阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167895_comment'></div>谨空。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167895_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄次女某出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　有人向三司告发大理寺丞杨忱贩纱漏税，杨自言与蔡襄有宿怨，乞下御史台推鞠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年1月15日</a>　上元，蔡襄偕同僚伴驾御宣德门观灯，应制作《上元进诗》<div id='poem_249156' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249156' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249156?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上元进诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249156")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249156_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249156'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249156'>叠耸青峰宝炬森，端门初晚翠华临。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249156'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_249156", 249156, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>宸游</span>不为三元夜，乐事全归万众心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249156'>天上清光开夜色，人间和气阁春阴。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249156'>要知尽作华封祝，四十年来惠爱深。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249156_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249156'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249156_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年1月</a>　蔡襄撰书《尚书职方员外郎吕君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书职方员外郎吕君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐七年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168192")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168192'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168192'>吕君讳士昌，字子弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168192_comment'></div>天圣八年举进士及第，调吉州永新尉、婺州司法参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168192_comment'></div>用举者改大理寺丞，监常之商税务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168192_comment'></div>移知益州灵泉县，以太夫人高年，愿监舒州皖口仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168192_comment'></div>未行，服丧，外除知江之德安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168192_comment'></div>罢归，三司使田公况辟君编《三司例策》，书成二百卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168192_comment'></div>权知功州，五迁为尚书职方员外郎、知润州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168192_comment'></div>以代期未至，寓居江阴军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168192_comment'></div>嘉祐五年七月十九日终，年六十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168192_comment'></div>七年正月十三日，遂葬之江阴之江阴县化龙乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168192_comment'></div>曾祖讳裕，东平寿张人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168192_comment'></div>祖讳某，赠大理评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168192_comment'></div>父讳延之，终湖州节度判官，因家真州之扬子县，赠屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168192_comment'></div>母赵氏，赠永宁县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168192_comment'></div>继母孙氏，仙游县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168192_comment'></div>娶葛氏，封寿昌县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168192_comment'></div>男三人：曰袤，许州临颍尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168192_comment'></div>裘、褒，皆进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168192_comment'></div>女二人，长适杨潍，次未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168192_comment'></div>范文正公荐君馆阁之职，田公又荐为提点刑狱，皆未及用而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168192_comment'></div>子弼宽恕浑厚，与之言，初若可见其际，及游泳益久，即不知其所之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168192_comment'></div>视世俗穷通寿夭、荣悴忧喜，无一事可系其志，居閒读书为文，优游终岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168192_comment'></div>其与人处，若槩取之，从容而论当世士，盖所与者无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168192_comment'></div>尝得伪造印文者，其法应免远官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168192_comment'></div>及移蜀，或谓用此可免，君曰：「幸人之死，以逭移蜀，吾不忍为」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168192_comment'></div>其所以为人，大率如此，此前世所书有德义量度君子，不能过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168192_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1168192'>内全于德，不与世异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168192_comment'></div>官无显功，进不近利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168192_comment'></div>古有君子，其道斯类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168192_comment'></div>嶷然高风，薄夫之愧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1168192_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_2_1167930_comment'></div>三期之内，流转如此，来者略知案分，则又置之，欲事日脩举，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167930_comment'></div>及夏便即解去剧任，不可以久处也。<div class='inline'
