ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　蔡襄上《代贺老人星表》<div id='poem_1167807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代贺老人星表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167807")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167807'>金德治时，玉衡揆度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167807_comment'></div>仰星文之发耀，丽霄极以凝祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167807_comment'></div>符圣历之永昌，举人区而胥悦<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167807_comment'></div>恭以尊号皇帝陛下至诚育物，中道纳民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167807_comment'></div>仁如天之广生，化与神而无迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167807_comment'></div>诸福并效，成功罕名，幽感察于上灵，经次示乎休应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167807_comment'></div>秋琯方仲，宵筹向晨，直景位以垂光，映社躔而昭庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167807_comment'></div>考厥候台之验，资夫睿算之延。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167807_comment'></div>臣等叨列宰司，悚窥乾象，罄一心而有祝，期万寿以无垠。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167807_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　蔡襄上《代谢御殿复膳表》<div id='poem_1167808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代谢御殿复膳表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167808")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167808'>臣襄等言：前贡封章，请御殿复膳，蒙降批答俞允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167808_comment'></div>侧躬修德，祗畏天明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167808_comment'></div>吁帝造辞，恭回宸虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167808_comment'></div>正路朝之法坐，复内饔之燕羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167808_comment'></div>温诏下临，舆情胥悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167808_comment'></div>臣襄诚欢诚感、顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167808_comment'></div>窃以天子之尊至重，唯上灵是钦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167808_comment'></div>人君之德莫偕，惟大明可况。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167808_comment'></div>考阳精之阙壤，抑历象之常经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167808_comment'></div>然《春秋》书之于经，汉唐载之于《志》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167808_comment'></div>作善者有消伏之感，失政者有修举之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167808_comment'></div>茍立志以通幽，必转灾而为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167808_comment'></div>恭惟尊号皇帝陛下仁涵万物，诚贯三灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167808_comment'></div>动法祖宗之规，言合天人之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167808_comment'></div>属史官之建白，验日象以亏明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167808_comment'></div>陛下顺稽眚异之来，虔承警告之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167808_comment'></div>贬太官之常举，即便坐以周询。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167808_comment'></div>发廪蓄以恤穷，启狴犴而释罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167808_comment'></div>晦朔之际，变旱暵以为霖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167808_comment'></div>未申之交，减食分而复景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167808_comment'></div>有来列辟，咸肃外庭，愿端黼扆之居，仍还珍膳之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167808_comment'></div>下情兢惕，越至再三之勤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167808_comment'></div>睿意宽冲，俯从众庶之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167808_comment'></div>臣等预参宰辅，无裨圣神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167808_comment'></div>仰休应之同臻，等欢心而称颂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167808_comment'></div>谨奉表诣东上閤门称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167808_comment'></div>臣等诚欢诚感，顿首顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1167808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　蔡襄上《乞戒约体量放税札子》<div id='poem_1167864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞戒约体量放税劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167864")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167864'>臣伏见今年开封府界、京西、陕西等诸路，春夏愆雨，麦苗不遂，已有朝旨，诸路更不检覆，只今体量放税，兼续有奏，乞省仓赈贷，亦有朝旨，遂其所请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167864_comment'></div>此朝廷爱民之意，推而行之，为惠深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167864_comment'></div>然臣窃恐开封府、诸路转运司所差官员不能尽心，或旱损处多，蠲放数少；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167864_comment'></div>或旱损处少，蠲放数多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167864_comment'></div>至于赈贷，亦不酌量轻重分数均济，回顾军储有无准备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167864_comment'></div>只陕西近奏，去年霜雹，秋税放一百万馀石；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167864_comment'></div>今年二月，赈贷军储六十万馀石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167864_comment'></div>即今夏税未见申报，已累有申奏，乞从京拨银绢应副，籴入军储，乞将黑锡中纳斛斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167864_comment'></div>以此言之，若诸路放税不得其实，赈贷又无分数，一旦却阙军储，三司虽有钱帛，亦是临时置办，迁移不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167864_comment'></div>伏况见在帑藏，岁入岁支之数有限，何以济办？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167864_comment'></div>臣非不知宽贷百姓以为美事，职在国计，诚虑一朝窘阙，重烦朝廷，臣虽责罪甘心，而事几既失，言不可及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167864_comment'></div>欲乞下臣所陈于转运司，戒约体量放税官员，委须得实赈贷，州郡亦须军储有备，如后检得别有阙误，乞行朝典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167864_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年9月</a>　蔡襄上《祫享陈乞恩泽状》，为堂侄蔡彝奏乞恩荫。<div id='poem_1167833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祫享陈乞恩泽状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167833")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167833'>右，臣伏以礼修庙享，实讲于遗文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167833_comment'></div>祫举宗祧，克昭于纯孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167833_comment'></div>凡预从臣之例，悉推延赏之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167833_comment'></div>窃念臣有亲堂兄之子彝，粗习艺文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167833_comment'></div>幸逢圣旦，冀沾荣泽，获耀私门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167833_comment'></div>伏望睿慈于文资内特与一官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167833_comment'></div>臣无任祈天俟命、激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167833_comment'></div>谨具状奏，陈乞以闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1167833_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　蔡襄应兵部郎中沈立之求，为其父沈平撰写墓志铭《赠光禄少卿沈君墓志铭》》<div id='poem_1168193' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168193' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168193?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠光禄少卿沈君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168193")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168193'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168193'>府君讳平，字遵道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168193_comment'></div>曾祖曰籍，衢州常山令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168193_comment'></div>祖曰德饶，越州剡县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168193_comment'></div>父曰仁谅，海州朐山令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168193_comment'></div>其先吴人，剡县丞卒，葬会稽，后朐山退老于和州，因而家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168193_comment'></div>君少与伯兄曰及举进士，为文章，通书史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168193_comment'></div>既而伯兄景德及第以仕，而朐山致政事还归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168193_comment'></div>君曰：「吾其养亲乎历阳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168193_comment'></div>辟田畴，因物适变，遂以富饶，计乡党亲戚，厚而周施之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168193_comment'></div>逮亲终，伯兄服丧，乃籍所有以奉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168193_comment'></div>伯兄曰：「吾利汝财乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168193_comment'></div>于是悉力以治丧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168193_comment'></div>久之，族子欲异产，与之利田宅，而自取其中下者，众益义之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168193_comment'></div>君曰：「吾有五子，教以儒术，清白足矣，其不富之患乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168193_comment'></div>以天圣二年四月二十二日终，是月二十八日葬于龙场冈之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168193_comment'></div>夫人胡氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168193_comment'></div>男五人，曰立、齐、京、言、充。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168193_comment'></div>女三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168193_comment'></div>君早殁，夫人贤而有礼，训育诸孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168193_comment'></div>立以进士中科，为尚书兵部郎中、两浙转运使，迎养三十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168193_comment'></div>累赠君光禄少卿，叙封夫人寿昌县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168193_comment'></div>嘉祐六年，夫人卒，明年，举祔旧茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168193_comment'></div>兵部博学有文，藏书二万卷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168193_comment'></div>又所至称职，将以材能进于时，宦仕显荣，其可量哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168193_comment'></div>所以知君识虑之远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168193_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1168193'>不仕而耕，以养其亲，而终其身，于嗟孝兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168193_comment'></div>力而丰有，施及州里，推其族子，如其义兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168193_comment'></div>守法儒学，教厉子孙，实大其门，不亦智兮！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168193_comment'></div>龙场之下，卜吉而藏，勒文前冈，孰与寿兮！</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1168193_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年11月</a>　蔡襄赠墨与欧阳修。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年12月23日</a>　蔡襄偕同僚伴驾在龙图阁、天章阁观览太祖、太宗、真宗“三圣御书”，作《观三圣御书应制》，又到宝文阁观帝作飞白字分赐从臣。<div id='poem_249185' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249185' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249185?labeling=true' target='_blank'>观三圣御书应制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年12月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249185")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249185_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249185'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249185'>圣业存功德，宸毫冠艺文。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249185'>势开千里浪，光动九天云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249185'>法驾乘时至，仙都与世分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249185'>皇心钦宝训，求治益精勤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249185_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249185'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249185_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年12月27日</a>　蔡襄复奉敕在宝文阁参观太宗《游艺集》、真宗文集及皇家所珍藏的“瑞物”，并参加群玉殿赐宴，作《群玉殿赐宴》<div id='poem_249418' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249418' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249418?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群玉殿赐宴</a><span class='authorDate'>（1062年12月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249418")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_249418_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249418'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249418'>治道承炎历，皇基亘万年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249418'>深仁涵海岳，至德著坤乾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249418'>文物归元首，臣邻必巨贤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249418'>蓼萧思及下，奕叶力追先。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249418'>昕色方群进，胪音忽四传。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249418'>衣冠纷杂遝，台殿郁蟺蜎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249418'>宝字崇三圣，瑶图秘九天。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249418'>荣河祥气彻，昭汉晓光旋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249418'>磊砢珠玑在，峥嵘岁月迁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249418'>家声终卓越，上意益恭虔。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249418'>书观开铺首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>，宸毫落彩笺。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249418'>烟云初不定，鸾凤互相鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249418'>拜赐兼金重，珍藏尺璧全。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249418'>人人皆自得，事事独超先。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249418'>睿藻敦风教<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>，冥搜出化权。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249418'>来从玉山府，远过柏梁篇。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249418'>回驭临高馆<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：赐宴群玉殿。）</span>，推恩锡广筵。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249418'>迷魂游帝所，休应动星躔。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249418'>申命严樽俎<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>，新章被管弦。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249418'>千龄叨际会，旷古绝寅缘。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249418'>大施难论报，精诚第祝延。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249418'>唯应歌盛美，乐石可磨镌。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249418'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_249418_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249418'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_249418_0'>⑴ 自注：嘉祐七年十二年二十三日，诏宰臣以下龙图、天章阁观三圣御书。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_249418_0'>⑵ 自注：又幸宝文阁作飞白字，召臣寮观，人赐一轴，兼赐纸笔墨各有差。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_249418_0'>⑶ 自注：赐御诗一首，令群臣次韵和进。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_18_249418_0'>⑷ 自注：二十七日幸宝文阁，召宰臣以下观太宗游艺集瑞物十三种，仍赐御书，宴群玉殿，宣谕太平无事，令群臣尽醉。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249418_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1062&endYear=1062')">1062年</a>　本年，以澄心堂纸和李廷珪墨作各体书遗子孙珍藏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年1月8日</a>　蔡襄作《群玉殿曲宴记》<div id='poem_1168103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>群玉殿曲宴记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐八年正月八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168103")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168103'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168103'>嘉祐七年十二月二十七日，上幸天章阁，召辅臣近侍，出太宗《游艺集》、真宗文集以示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168103_comment'></div>又出瑞物，石之类五：一曰「赵二十一帝」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168103_comment'></div>二曰「真君王万岁」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168103_comment'></div>三曰「天下太平」，石本如拳，皆隐起成字；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168103_comment'></div>四曰佛像石，一面平，有黑理如浮屠像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168103_comment'></div>五曰软石，状如界尺，可长五六寸，持其两端而曲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168103_comment'></div>木之类一，不知何木，长一尺许，中分之，白质黑文，曰「大连宋」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168103_comment'></div>竹断两节，直剖之，双弦属其上下，命曰「君臣合欢竹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168103_comment'></div>龙凤卵二，龙卵可容三升，凤卵可一升，皆中空，以黄金饰之，为瓶状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168103_comment'></div>金珠之类四：生金山一，重七斤十四两，嵌嵓峭突，有山状；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168103_comment'></div>丹砂一，重十二斤八两，色黑若铁，间有芙蓉头；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168103_comment'></div>七星珠一，径寸之四分，有北斗星文，旁出辅星，皆隆如粟粒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168103_comment'></div>袅蹄金三，汉武帝诏所制以应祥瑞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168103_comment'></div>凡一十三种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168103_comment'></div>既已，移幸宝文阁，亲书飞白四十馀字，遍赐群臣，遂宴于群玉殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168103_comment'></div>是日，名香珍饵、金缕䌽花，皆自中出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168103_comment'></div>宣谕以太平无事，卿等尽醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168103_comment'></div>乃索鹿头酒，易以大杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168103_comment'></div>丞相韩公得金蕉叶，一引空杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168103_comment'></div>上举盏以属曰：「可更饮否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168103_comment'></div>又引一杯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168103_comment'></div>上喜甚，左右顾，令尽饮，恩意隆厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168103_comment'></div>伏惟陛下临御天下四十一年，宴享之勤，未有如群玉曲宴之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168103_comment'></div>群臣感激际会，咸进诗歌，称咏其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168103_comment'></div>明年正月八日，翰林学士、尚书吏部郎中、知制诰、权三司使臣蔡襄谨记。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1168103'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1168103_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年1月24日</a>　蔡襄与韩琦等观赏唐人摹本王羲之《平安》、《何如》、《奉橘》三帖，并各题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月</a>　四月上旬，蔡襄作《仁宗皇帝挽词》七首。作品：《仁宗皇帝挽词七首》<div id='poem_249165' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249165' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_249165_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249165'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249165'>向近千秋节，何言七月期。<div id='poem_title_249166_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249166'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249166'>道德由来太古同，生灵休养至仁中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249166'>五兵不试归神武，万物无私是化工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249166_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249166'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249166_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月22日</a>　蔡襄奏乞内藏银娟用于建仁宗陵及赏赍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月22日</a>　蔡襄奏陵寝拟用永定陵之制。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年夏</a>　蔡襄在山中负责督修仁宗永昭陵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年7月12日</a>　蔡襄作《与亲家茂才书》<div id='poem_1167948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与亲家茂才书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167948")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167948'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167948'>襄启：秋暑犹盛，不审动止佳否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167948_comment'></div>叶迁回，正旦蒙示书信，感荷之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167948_comment'></div>门中休豫，老亲以下各得平善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167948_comment'></div>省廷日来事绪渐简，今夏病躯全获轻安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167948_comment'></div>乡亲未及一一通书，因会集为言，恳恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167948_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167948_comment'></div>襄启，亲家茂才足下，七月十二日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1167948_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年7月</a>　欧阳修为蔡襄所书《永城县学记》、《荔枝谱》题跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年7月28日</a>　蔡襄访唐询，并在其书斋撰书《洮河石砚铭》<div id='poem_1168123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洮河石研铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年7月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168123")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168123'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168123'>七月二十八日，瑞卿老友以洮河石砚惠予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168123_comment'></div>甚可爱，兼能下墨，隔宿洗之亦不留墨痕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168123_comment'></div>其肌理细腻莹润，不在端溪中洞石下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168123_comment'></div>色微白，有红丝，俗传为红丝研者殆是邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168123_comment'></div>尝考前人论砚之优劣详矣，不费笔，即退墨，二德难兼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168123_comment'></div>世人每爱鸲鹆眼，第未□眼为石病，然有眼亦未始不可，总以活眼为上乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168123_comment'></div>质之粗者概勿论矣，至于雕文刻理，花藻缤纷，以俗手出之，纵有良材，乃遭其厄，予所弗取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168123_comment'></div>明窗净几，无尘事相接，磨墨伸□，随意作大小数十字，此时如无良砚，则兴趣孛然矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168123_comment'></div>予因瑞卿之惠，而书其大略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168123_comment'></div>蔡襄书于瑞谷山房。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1168123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月</a>　蔡襄迁给事中，拜三司使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　蔡襄书答欧阳修《与蔡君谟求书集古录序书》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　蔡襄书欧阳修《集古录序》完成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月</a>　八月中旬，蔡襄作《尹夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168194' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168194' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168194?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尹夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐八年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168194")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168194_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168194'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168194'>夫人姓尹氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168194_comment'></div>父尚书职方郎中、直昭文馆，讳少连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168194_comment'></div>郎中有数子，而女独夫人，又少聪警，识图书，辨音律，故加爱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168194_comment'></div>及长，以归国子监丞葛君寔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168194_comment'></div>丞晚得官，当未仕，与夫人治家事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168194_comment'></div>夫人事姑，勤谨不懈，而于夫人之族亲，抚接皆有礼意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168194_comment'></div>母杨氏，诸子随官远方，夫人念母之老，迎归以养，年八十馀，终于夫人之家，即葬近墅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168194_comment'></div>其于孝爱深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168194_comment'></div>丞以文进，而久不第，夫人未尝戚戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168194_comment'></div>岁时奉祀，与娣姒族亲宴饮，列女僮，鸣管弦，以相和乐，观世之休悴，初不经虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168194_comment'></div>益喜浮屠书，颇知其指归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168194_comment'></div>有男令彦、汝奇，皆举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168194_comment'></div>女适真定元氏主簿施砚，其季幼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168194_comment'></div>内外孙八人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168194_comment'></div>享年六十，以嘉祐六年八月初九日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168194_comment'></div>八年八月十五日甲申，葬江阴军江阴县化龙乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168194_comment'></div>丞曰：「吾妻之贤，君不可以不志」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168194_comment'></div>间千里之远以来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168194_comment'></div>某铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1168194'>《诗》称公侯，首考其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168194_comment'></div>均一之德，法度是循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168194_comment'></div>唯彼妇道，于斯则难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168194_comment'></div>呜呼夫人，兹有尚焉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1168194_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年8月29日</a>　蔡襄收欧阳修谢惠砚信。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年9月9日</a>　蔡襄作《澄心堂纸帖》<div id='poem_1167967' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167967' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167967?labeling=true' target='_blank'>澄心堂纸帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167967")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167967'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167967'>澄心堂纸一幅，阔狭厚薄坚实皆类此乃佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167967_comment'></div>工者不愿为，又恐不能为之，试与厚直莫得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167967_comment'></div>见其楮细，似可作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167967_comment'></div>便人只求百幅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167967_comment'></div>癸卯重阳日，襄书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1167967_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年9月28日</a>　蔡襄作《墨辩》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年冬</a>　入冬，蔡襄送程师孟出守洪州，作《送程刑部出守洪州》<div id='poem_249244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送程刑部出守洪州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249244")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249244'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249244'>何事名郎出计台，钟陵都会久须才。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249244'>江山不是人间有，旗鼓初从日下来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249244'>列郡五符归总制，故乡三组少徘徊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249244'>勿嗟南国多怀感，宝气还应彻斗魁<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《蔡忠惠集》卷八）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249244'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249244_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年10月</a>　蔡襄扈从至永昭陵，作《昭陵行》<div id='poem_249071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昭陵行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1063年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249071")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249071_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249071'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249071'>宫人上临候昏钟，帘外香烟烛影红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249071'>庭柏飞霜陵漏永，可怜今夜月明中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249071_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年</a>　蔡襄扈从还归城中，作《扈从帖》致李端愿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年12月</a>　蔡襄再作《致程修撰帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年1月</a>　蔡襄多次到欧阳修家观赏商鼎铭、石鼓文及古碑帖，各有提跋。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄致书成都韩绛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年2月</a>　蔡襄应邀游览李端愿家园，作《甲辰寒日游公谨园池》诗，李将襄诗刻于石壁。<div id='poem_249179' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249179' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249179?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲辰寒日游公谨园池</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249179")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249179_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249179'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249179'>二月名园蓊郁青，为怜佳节此閒行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249179'>偶因觞咏心还适，暂离尘埃眼倍明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249179'>风静落花深一寸，日迟啼鸟度千声。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249179'>主公高意何须道，芳物于人自有情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249179_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249179'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249179_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄作《致李观察帖》，谢李端愿之约。<div id='poem_1167931' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167931' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167931?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与李观察帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167931")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167931_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167931'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167931'>昨日蒙手教见招，乃素所愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167931_comment'></div>然前朝暴暖，省中解衣，晚为冷气所侵，至今犹未甚解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167931_comment'></div>夜来并服饵，明日料之出未得，且那后时，可否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167931_comment'></div>惜此春物已阑，私心殊不快也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1167931_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄作《寒食乐词》<div id='poem_249405' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249405' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249405?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒食乐词</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249405")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249405_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249405'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249405'>皇州令节已藏烟，帝渥乘时锡广筵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249405'>和气去添春色重，恩光来助日华鲜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249405'>千声凤吹朱门里，一番花香谷雨前。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249405'>更喜簪裳嘉宴日，亲逢干羽治平年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249405_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249405'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249405_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年5月</a>　五月下旬，蔡襄撰书《光禄少卿致仕张公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168195' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168195' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168195?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光禄卿致仕张公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平元年五月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168195")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168195_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168195'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168195'>公讳温之，字景山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168195_comment'></div>其先黄帝之孙，始作弓矢，主祀弧星，以官受氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168195_comment'></div>周衰，六国争雄，而张氏五世相韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168195_comment'></div>良佐汉有功，侯于留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168195_comment'></div>留侯之后，丞相禹、司徒歆，子孙益多，散居四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168195_comment'></div>其居东南，继为大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168195_comment'></div>曰简者，广陵人，生升，仕唐为滁州清流令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168195_comment'></div>升生约，金吾卫长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168195_comment'></div>约生训，公之曾祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168195_comment'></div>以勇谋事杨行密，为黄州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168195_comment'></div>祖讳璆，仕伪唐，校书郎，后典亲兵，赠尚书屯田郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168195_comment'></div>祖妣颜氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168195_comment'></div>考讳佖，右内史学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168195_comment'></div>太祖平金陵，从后主归京师，授赞善大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168195_comment'></div>在太宗朝建言时务，评谳法令，多所施用，终给事中，累赠太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168195_comment'></div>妣马氏，赠清河郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168195_comment'></div>公少孤，知力学问，有名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168195_comment'></div>大中祥符八年擢进士第，授温州乐清尉，再调润州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168195_comment'></div>召还，校馆阁书，迁殿中丞、集贤校理、通判常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168195_comment'></div>常饥，发运使急于官籴，谷益贵，公奏罢籴，而民不流亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168195_comment'></div>蔡文忠公荐其材可任监司之职，时辅臣不公悦者，出知温州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168195_comment'></div>文忠公又荐之，徙淮南提点刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168195_comment'></div>杨崇勋以恩倖横恣，护吏渔民，县令有不己从者，崇勋怒，下令狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168195_comment'></div>公往察问而出之，流所护吏数十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168195_comment'></div>崇勋怗怗顾首尾，于是部郡相视以法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168195_comment'></div>移广南东路转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168195_comment'></div>广之夷落有罪，任其酋以夷刑，夷刑惨酷，公请以律令论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168195_comment'></div>海外舶𦨴岁至，犀珠玳瑁、诸香奇物，官取十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168195_comment'></div>城中濠与海通，恶少年暮夜乘潮汐苞藏奇货重物，不肯输官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168195_comment'></div>前有欲为水栅以制之者，卒中毒死，事遂寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168195_comment'></div>公治材他所，一日移置濠上，水栅立成，货利稍稍入官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168195_comment'></div>海有群盗，声指广城，民相传动惊走，郡为备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168195_comment'></div>公料贼来，不先声，彻备张饮，人得以安，贼亦果不来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168195_comment'></div>代归，权三司度支判官，未几除户部，踰月出为京西转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168195_comment'></div>且行，加直史馆，改授河北，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168195_comment'></div>是时契丹频年遣使，道路交衽，供具百名，取办于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168195_comment'></div>边郡益戍兵，调用滋广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168195_comment'></div>公计其所必用取之，择其所不急去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168195_comment'></div>不以名使人，要必功实，虽米盐下吏，莫不延问称荐，禁束侵牟，故吏畏而为用，民以是便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168195_comment'></div>转工部郎中，召还为三司盐铁副使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168195_comment'></div>其职文书繁夥，公一省不忘，条理出入，下不敢欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168195_comment'></div>三司使奏他事，上见公姓名，独语曰：「必须再去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168195_comment'></div>又首肯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168195_comment'></div>明日，除天章阁待制、河北都转运使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168195_comment'></div>入辞，上曰：「卿之行，出朕意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168195_comment'></div>既至，玺书委以密察边事、军马重轻与兵官材否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168195_comment'></div>公感激天子所以推信，励力以安百姓，实边塞，选兵择吏，为国久计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168195_comment'></div>未几，保州兵叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168195_comment'></div>州兵几万人，号都巡检司，先尝从太祖北伐有功，敕其军每出巡，别给金粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168195_comment'></div>兵分三部，州将领其一，裨将领其二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168195_comment'></div>其后州将典城，兵不出巡，亦不复给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168195_comment'></div>裨将皆中贵人，月必出巡，出则给之，或言其不均者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168195_comment'></div>朝廷委公其事，即允以武臣代中贵人，总三部之兵，更其出入而廪给均焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168195_comment'></div>中贵人罢去，悒悒怀恨，未有以危公者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168195_comment'></div>会监郡与主兵官不相能，辱之，兵怒，杀监郡，闭城叛，而以公罢其金粟之给为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168195_comment'></div>公驰至城下，乃即以兵环之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168195_comment'></div>朝廷累下敕榜招降，而门其东西至坚，且怀疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168195_comment'></div>太子少傅田公况时总其事，遣部将郭逵入城晓谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168195_comment'></div>门开，诸将入，其唱为乱者千馀人，众恐其为变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168195_comment'></div>公谓田公曰：「保界虏壤，兵骄叛乱如此，反覆未可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168195_comment'></div>今不芟除，所谓养虎自遗患也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168195_comment'></div>于是悉坑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168195_comment'></div>保州平，夺职知虢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168195_comment'></div>居三年，贝州军乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168195_comment'></div>先其所欲危公者谓公前使河北，有妖人李教坐法，公宽之，贝卒得李教为师以乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168195_comment'></div>冀人段得政将诣登闻自陈，常为李教狱词，逮连教父昙，转以私书属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1168195_comment'></div>同职者得词，绝至澶州监河桥，索其藁以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1168195_comment'></div>事下御史府，贝之乱实无李教，而得政所讼无根，犹追三官，监鄂州商税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1168195_comment'></div>复工部，知汉阳军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1168195_comment'></div>祀明堂恩，迁刑部，复待制，知湖州，又移扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1168195_comment'></div>公自以直廉，遇天子任使，欲以所有唯上所用，不幸一跌摧落，不复自振，年且至矣，遂上书乞还官职之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1168195_comment'></div>徙润州，申请益坚，除光禄卿致仕，还老常州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1168195_comment'></div>以嘉祐七年十一月二十九日终，年七十八，遗命葬滁州清流县昌城乡杜沛村，从先人之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1168195_comment'></div>诸孤以治平元年五月二十六日克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1168195_comment'></div>先夫人任氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1168195_comment'></div>后夫人鲁氏，参知政事肃简公宗道之女，封□寿郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1168195_comment'></div>男曰次卿，试将作监主簿，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1168195_comment'></div>曰次山、次元、并大理评事，有材能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1168195_comment'></div>女六人：长适京西提点刑狱宋任，次适广东路转运使、秘阁校理蔡抗，次秘书郎田沇，次著作佐郎蔡天球，次新乡令石约，次大理评事吕希哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1168195_comment'></div>公忠廉鲠直，以节义自尚，爱友亲族甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1168195_comment'></div>谋于国，不以其身之安危；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1168195_comment'></div>笃于亲，不以其人之厚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1168195_comment'></div>吏治精明，施设若烦密难通，而公持之简易，所至民怀其惠而不触其令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1168195_comment'></div>尤于本朝故事详悉，自建隆以来史所不纪，每指一事，即疏其人姓名年月，最为审据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1168195_comment'></div>家居，或客使造门，语及天下利病，慷慨议论，忧发颜面，忘其身之老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1168195_comment'></div>夫士之处世，立一节一行，已能自见于后，况其多者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1168195_comment'></div>然必有志录，乃可传信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1168195_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1168195'>砺世之速，先于饬身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1168195_comment'></div>防吏之严，本乎爱民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1168195_comment'></div>资国以富，其要曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1168195_comment'></div>佑武以制，其威曰神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1168195_comment'></div>力志于斯，庶用自伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1168195_comment'></div>矫矫在公，卒覂于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1168195_comment'></div>顾言返葬，杜沛之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1168195_comment'></div>寘文坎中，名与石存。</div><div id='poem_sentence_94_1168195_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄重定重书《茶录》，付刻石永传，并作《后序》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年5月</a>　闰五月，蔡襄作《甲辰闰月初伏快雨凉风昼眠初觉庭前小栏花木各有意气效柏梁体》<div id='poem_249339' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249339' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249339?labeling=true' target='_blank'>甲辰闰月初伏快雨凉风昼眠初觉庭前小栏花木各有意气效柏梁体</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249339")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249339_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249339'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249339'>闰夏天地<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_249339", 249339, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>热焰</span>烘，崇朝快雨随清风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249339'>昼轩梦觉开前栊，画栏花草意气雄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249339'>侧枕遥问数异同，如子微物烦化工。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249339'>盍各言尔之所从，繁葩富艳生朱红<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：川海棠。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249339'>枯条大蕊千万重<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：绛桃。）</span>，修干点缀赤日中<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：蜀葵。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249339'>蠲去忧忿谁与功<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：萱草，）</span>，采摘烹煮祛烦胸<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：百合。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249339'>秋霜钜实垂如瓮<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：木瓜。）</span>，横柯远引交加丛<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：红枚瑰。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249339'>叶抽绿剑端黄茸<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：山姜。）</span>，直立开拂泉货通<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：金钱。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249339'>叠绕翠羽翻虬龙<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：薜荔。）</span>，误入畦町非余公<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：顷麻。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249339'>助涤渴肺思匪躬<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：麦门冬。）</span>，物物自名词不穷。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249339'>愿当我意乃汝容，负汝不饮惭衰翁。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249339_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249339'></div><div id='poem_sentence_11_249339_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄作《大研帖》致唐询。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年夏</a>　蔡襄上《国论要目》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年夏</a>　蔡襄上《论兵十事》<div id='poem_1167790' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167790' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167790?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论兵十事奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平元年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167790")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167790_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167790'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167790'>一事：臣近上《国论要目》十二篇，以谓当今之急务，彊兵为第一事，富国为第二事，欲修治道，自此而始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167790_comment'></div>兵不彊则国不富，国不富则民不安，是故始于彊兵而终于安民，本末之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167790_comment'></div>彊兵之说如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167790_comment'></div>一曰消冗，谓冗兵不可以暴减，当有术以消之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167790_comment'></div>二曰选择，谓老弱疾病不堪战陈之人即拣择而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167790_comment'></div>三曰省兵，谓不应置兵处与置之过多者则省之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167790_comment'></div>四曰训练，谓兵虽少壮，而训练不得其术，与不教同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167790_comment'></div>五曰立兵法，今之兵法绝无统制，故不可用，用之则败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167790_comment'></div>此五者备修，则兵少而精矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167790_comment'></div>兵少则财用饶，财用饶则国富矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167790_comment'></div>兵精，以战则胜，以守则固，而兵彊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167790_comment'></div>其说皆世人之常论也，然而行之，则为治道之始，不行，则为天下大患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167790_comment'></div>是世人之常论，乃当今之急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167790_comment'></div>臣故谓之第一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167790_comment'></div>一事：中书不与知兵，增兵多少不知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167790_comment'></div>枢密院要兵则添，财用有无不知也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167790_comment'></div>管军将帅少兵则请，曾不计较今日兵籍倍多，何故用不足也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167790_comment'></div>三司但知支办衣粮，日日增添，不敢论列，谓兵非职事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167790_comment'></div>四者各为之谋，以至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167790_comment'></div>若通而为一，则可以计较兵籍多少、财用有无，不致于冗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167790_comment'></div>臣欲乞招置增添兵数，枢密院、中书共议之，先令三司计度衣粮如何足用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167790_comment'></div>管军每乞招添，边臣每乞增置，必须诘问其所少之因，必不得已，方可其奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167790_comment'></div>如此慎重，乃省兵之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167790_comment'></div>一事：近年置诸路安抚、钤辖，添屯禁军，自京西、江南东西、广南东西、两浙、福建等驻泊禁军，皆是北人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167790_comment'></div>南方风土异宜，水行不知舟楫之利，山行不堪阻阨之险，一往三年，死亡殆半，其不便一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167790_comment'></div>只如差二万人驻泊，及至当替，又须二万人，常须四万人可了办，以此屯戍之多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167790_comment'></div>军还到营，未及三两月，又复出军，不惟道路劳苦，妻孥间阔，人情郁结，其不便二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167790_comment'></div>今欲除京东、淮南外，诸路钤辖、安抚司所管驻泊禁军，候其年满，量留合要人数差补外，并只放还本营，更不填阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167790_comment'></div>或问：南方难用北军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167790_comment'></div>祖宗平定南方尽是北军，今来何故难用？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167790_comment'></div>曰：祖宗之兵，诛讨大计也，诛讨大计未有不从中出兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167790_comment'></div>今者南方但当作御盗贼之计，若御盗贼，诸路各有招置禁军，练习精熟，可以驱使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167790_comment'></div>贼势大者，暂遣北军，不为失策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167790_comment'></div>此省兵之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167790_comment'></div>一事：陕西、河东自庆历以来，用兵之际，添置寨栅数多，所以添兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167790_comment'></div>寨栅本以通粮道、护耕农，非有益于攻守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167790_comment'></div>今当先去无用寨栅，或只量留兵卒，随宜罢遣，以宽置粮草之费，亦省兵之一端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167790_comment'></div>一事：防边兵卒，老弱病患先须拣选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167790_comment'></div>若在边鄙，不唯虚费粮储，兼亦不堪战斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167790_comment'></div>千兵若有百人老弱，遇敌而先奔，即是千人皆废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167790_comment'></div>如此为患，须至选拣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167790_comment'></div>马有不堪入阵者，而为患与老弱之兵同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167790_comment'></div>陕西、河东方今无事时，若先选拣，不唯训练精熟，仓卒有备，大可减省粮草，以宽国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1167790_comment'></div>一事：或曰：招置土兵如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1167790_comment'></div>曰：陕西弓箭手之类只给与田，不给与衣粮，于事为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1167790_comment'></div>且如河北招置土兵，为害深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1167790_comment'></div>土兵一人可给戍兵三人，兼又父子相承，未尝出城，坐窘边费，骄蹇难动，故曰为害深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1167790_comment'></div>河北义勇十九万人，昔年差点，人情惊动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1167790_comment'></div>今耳目已熟，但须整缉训练，缓急得力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1167790_comment'></div>于其间更选彊壮，须及十万人，不费衣粮，可与土兵相制，屯戍之兵可减也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1167790_comment'></div>一事：养兵之费，禁军一兵之费，以衣粮、特支、郊赉通计，一岁约费钱五十千，厢军一兵之费岁约三十千，通一百一十八万馀人，一岁约费四千八百万缗，此其大较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1167790_comment'></div>若减禁军十万，岁减缗钱五百万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1167790_comment'></div>减厢军十万，岁减缗钱三百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1167790_comment'></div>欲减禁军，先减屯戍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1167790_comment'></div>欲减厢军，先减纲运，此其要也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1167790_comment'></div>一事：诸路厢军，一指挥有六七百人，检寻旧额，并无条制，盖年岁既远，亡失旧文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1167790_comment'></div>今若朝旨，诸军指挥并将校以下不得过五百人，旧额不满五百人即依旧额；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1167790_comment'></div>今日以前有剩数者，并令依旧，候及五百人，一依今来指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1167790_comment'></div>今后辄敢额外添人，并以违制论，不在去官原赦之限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1167790_comment'></div>一事：禁军指挥近年添置军额，名目数多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1167790_comment'></div>指挥将窠，虽全兵卒，只有三二百人，虚费将窠请受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1167790_comment'></div>今若逐路军额先与条约，谓若兵士三百人，即有将窠三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1167790_comment'></div>见在人数已多者仍旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1167790_comment'></div>或移补别军，候及三百人，更不补填，渐可并省也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1167790_comment'></div>一事：欲减厢军，先减纲运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1167790_comment'></div>今天下无名纲运，最为枉费兵士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1167790_comment'></div>边郡兵官替移，迎候送还，厢军动皆数百人，多者至千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1167790_comment'></div>自来明有条制，州郡皆以人情，不敢自约，此一事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1167790_comment'></div>南方替罢官员，近由江浙，远自湘潭，一舟十人至二十人，大者倍之，一岁往还京师可了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1167790_comment'></div>一次一舟之费，小者五百千，大者七百千，所载官物不过数千缗之直，衣粮所费几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1167790_comment'></div>此二事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1167790_comment'></div>天下州郡，自太平以来，廨宇亭榭，无有不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1167790_comment'></div>每遇新官临政，必有改作，土木之功，处处皆是，不惟枉费财用，必须多役兵卒，此三事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1167790_comment'></div>天下持送官物入京，如牛皮、兵器之类，多由陆路，若委本路转运司，不急用者罢省之，或令水路，可以减省兵役，此四事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1167790_comment'></div>养兵挽船不若和雇，和雇则止于程限之资，养兵终岁给之，其费必倍，此五事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1167790_comment'></div>大要举此五事，严与条约，厢军可省矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1167790'>禁军六十九万三千三百三十九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1167790'>厢军四十八万八千一百九十三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1167790'>共计一百一十八万一千五百三十二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1167790'>钱：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1167790'>收三千六百八十二万二千五百四十一贯一百六十五文<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1167790'>支三千三百一十七万六百三十一贯八百八文<span class='inlineComment2'>（南郊赏给不在数内。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1167790'>管军及军班兵士九百九十四万一千四十七贯九百三十三文<span class='inlineComment2'>（十分中三分有馀。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1167790'>匹帛绢䌷絁：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1167790'>收八百七十四万五千五百三十五匹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1167790'>支七百二十三万五千六百四十一匹<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_84_1167790'>管军及军班兵士七百四十二万二千七百六十八匹半<span class='inlineComment2'>（十分有馀。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1167790'>粮：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_85_1167790'>收二千六百九十四万三千五百七十五石<span class='inlineComment2'>（内税一千八百七万三千九十四石。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_86_1167790'>支三千四十七万二千七百八石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_87_1167790'>管军及军班兵士二千三百一十七万二百二十三石<span class='inlineComment2'>（八分。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1167790'>草：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_88_1167790'>收二千九百三十九万六千一百一十三束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_89_1167790'>支二千九百五十二万四百六十九束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_1167790'>管军及军班以下二千四百九十八万四百六十四束<span class='inlineComment2'>（八分。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1167790'>夏秋税所纳：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1167790'>钱四百九十三万二千九百九十一贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_92_1167790'>匹帛二百七十六万三千五百九十二匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_93_1167790'>斛㪷一千八百七万三千九十四石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_94_1167790'>已上三件更有折变在内，其馀所阙粮草匹帛并是见钱和买，并课利折科诸般博买应副得足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1167790_comment'></div>一岁所用，养兵之费常居六七，国用无几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1167790_comment'></div>臣恳恳而言，盖见其本末，不早图之，是谓失策矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_97_1167790'>右谨具进呈，取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1167790_comment'></div>年月日，某劄子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_98_1167790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167790'><span class='label'>按：</span>《国朝诸臣奏议》以第一事为总论，不作一事，故题为《论兵九事》。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_79_1167790_0'>⑴ 内夏秋税只有四百九十三万二千九百九十一贯文。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_82_1167790_0'>⑵ 内税绢二百七十六万三千五百九十二匹。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_83_1167790_0'>⑶ 南郊赏格不在数内，绫罗锦绮不在数内。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1167790_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄作《暑热帖》致李端愿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年8月</a>　蔡襄应韩琦请书《韩中令赞》及《孝宗崇福院》牌额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年9月</a>　蔡襄为张焘撰书《赐御书记》<div id='poem_1168104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168104?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐御书记</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平元年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168104")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168104'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168104'>天子即位之明年，建仁宗皇帝别庙于景灵宫，三司户部副使张焘修奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168104_comment'></div>九月三日，御篆题榜曰「孝严之殿」，命焘誊摹，既成，即以其本赐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168104_comment'></div>伏惟陛下思慕孝烈，躬洒宸翰，岂特以字画纯厚、势力端劲、高出前古以为美观？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168104_comment'></div>盖所以昭示孝诚于外，而令臣民瞻谛，知天子念亲之深、追远之谨如此其著，靡然而化者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168104_comment'></div>焘以职事，首荷恩赐，虽丘山之冠无以喻其重，传之子孙，为盛时之荣遇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168104_comment'></div>三司使、给事中蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168104_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄作《送子真给事出守常山》，送周沆出知成德军。<div id='poem_249240' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249240' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249240")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249240_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249240'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249240'>安得长材护北州，暂烦儒将拥轻裘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249240'>声名不啻一敌国，功业何须万里侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249240'>设馆高牙延永昼，猎场飞骑入清秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249240'>天枢严近恩荣重，归梦应思帝所游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249240_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249240'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249240_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年冬</a>　蔡襄上《乞封椿钱帛准备南郊支赐札子》作品：《乞封椿树帛准备南郊支赐札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年冬</a>　蔡襄上《财用总要札子》<div id='poem_1167866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上财用总要劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年冬）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167866")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167866'>臣待罪三司，已踰三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167866_comment'></div>伏念金谷货殖之职，颛总大计，民齿耗登，财用丰寡，日考而月课之，乃见虚盈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167866_comment'></div>然而知识昏冥，不知通流之术，无补于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167866_comment'></div>又当此冗费无极之时，每一念之，窃禄茍安，惭死无地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167866_comment'></div>谨撰成《天下财用总要》一册上进，伏惟陛下揽之，可以知当今天下之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167866_comment'></div>选求长材，俾临是职，与臣閒地，廪食养亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167866_comment'></div>臣不胜激切惶惧之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167866_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1167866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　蔡襄收葛密寄来之诗，感慨有加，依韵和之，作《和子发》<div id='poem_249059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249059' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249059'>空梁诗板岁年多，唯有秋虫占作窠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249059'>闻道故人时拂拭，此生无奈旧情何。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　岁末，蔡襄填《好事近》一阙，抒发胸中之块垒。<div id='poem_249432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>好事近</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249432")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249432'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249432'>瑞雪满京都，宫殿尽成银阙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249432'>常对素光遥望，是江梅时节。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249432_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249432'>如今江上见寒梅，幽香自清绝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249432'>重看落英残艳，想飘零如雪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249432_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249432'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249432_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年1月1日</a>　蔡襄作《茶记》<div id='poem_1168125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>茶记</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168125")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168125'>王家白茶闻于天下，其人名大诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168125_comment'></div>白茶唯一株，岁可作五七饼，如五铢钱大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168125_comment'></div>方其盛时，高视茶山，莫敢与之角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168125_comment'></div>一饼直钱一千，非其亲故不可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168125_comment'></div>终为园家以计枯其株。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168125_comment'></div>予过建安，大诏垂涕为余言其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168125_comment'></div>今年枯蘖辄生一枝，造成一饼，小于五铢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168125_comment'></div>大诏越四千里特携以来京师见予，喜发颜面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168125_comment'></div>予之好茶固深矣，而大诏不远数千里之役，其勤如此，意谓非予莫之省也，可怜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168125_comment'></div>乙巳初月朔日书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1168125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年2月</a>　诏准蔡襄辞三司使，以端明殿学士、礼部侍郎知杭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年2月</a>　二月下旬，欧阳修贻简慰问，蔡襄作《与欧阳永叔书》复之。<div id='poem_1167887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与欧阳永叔书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167887")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167887'>襄再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167887_comment'></div>尝已拜违，伏蒙赐手牍，展绎荷戢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167887_comment'></div>波流虽云未增，载轻可行，少候舟人办治，便即解去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167887_comment'></div>浩然之心，壮年尚能持习，今老矣，复何系哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167887_comment'></div>无入而不自得，唯恐智短而道远，求之行之，没世而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167887_comment'></div>佳山水，美鱼稻，我自有之而乐，孰能御哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167887_comment'></div>承教，固知有见慕之怀，何可得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167887_comment'></div>谨奉手启上谢，不一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167887_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167887_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年3月</a>　蔡襄参加唐询丧葬，作《唐彦猷挽词二首》<div id='poem_249248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐彦猷挽词<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249248")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249248'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249248'>鲠亮驰名久，孤高进路难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249248'>富文平日业，劝学晚年官。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249248'>隧外春江静，林边晓露漙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249248'>唯应坟上土，犹解是<span id='poem_sentence_2_249247_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249247'>生平无复见，流涕送幽堂。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249247_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《与提刑方郎中书》<div id='poem_1167891' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167891' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167891?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与提刑方郎中书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1167891'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167891'>襄启：蒙教精密，见望殊深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167891_comment'></div>然襄久处繁剧，五年之间，无一日不在思虑之内，以是神明自耗，不独筋力之难胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167891_comment'></div>虽得钱塘而多事，甚非自适之所，岂暇作区区事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167891_comment'></div>目前遣了，以免官责而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167891_comment'></div>倘一日得自遂，乃天幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167891_comment'></div>因风示诲，不一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167891_comment'></div>襄上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1167891_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《与知郡陈驾部书》<div id='poem_1167892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1167892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167892'>襄启：辇毂之下，号为劳苦，况兹计省，罔有暇日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167892_comment'></div>退休，宾客续续无穷，至或亲知不暇交言而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167892_comment'></div>朝车临访，无缘从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167892_comment'></div>今兹出守，复尔睽阔，瞻驰之素，岂胜郁邑！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167892_comment'></div>谨奉手启叙别，不一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167892_comment'></div>襄顿首。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a id='poem_title_249295_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249295'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249295'>先帝传基固，真人嗣统平。<div 南平
