-----title
莆田
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f91a91c862fa4066811e9b95cd3ab55d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f91a91c862fa4066811e9b95cd3ab55d");'><span id='f91a91c862fa4066811e9b95cd3ab55d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>，19岁</div><div id='f91a91c862fa4066811e9b95cd3ab55d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1030&endYear=1030')">1030年</a>　蔡襄过囊山，入寺叩宏法师。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='5707c301bdb14fd8bd7f0bd98b20e75c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5707c301bdb14fd8bd7f0bd98b20e75c");'><span id='5707c301bdb14fd8bd7f0bd98b20e75c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='5707c301bdb14fd8bd7f0bd98b20e75c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年9月</a>　蔡襄离家返京复职，过莆田囊山，应寺僧邀书陈伯孙诗，勒于石。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　蔡襄应林休复之子所请，作《林比部送行诗序》<div id='poem_1168052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林比部送行诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168052")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168052'>故尚书比部员外郎林公，祥符中自梓州郪县罢还，由大理寺迁与朝班，通判蔡州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168052_comment'></div>陛辞之日，伏奏：「以父母垂老，得他官不满意，愿幸而补臣闽中一便地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168052_comment'></div>臣奋罢驽之气，奉法遵职，早暮侍问恭养，以尽子道，非徒伸愚臣勤恳之志，抑亦广圣王孝治之体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168052_comment'></div>上嘉悯其诚，诏改建安郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168052_comment'></div>时著令：自蜀还者必再为县，然后升监郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168052_comment'></div>公以才能，为众所荐引，故特升，不与例比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168052_comment'></div>将行，又以言词动人主，全其孝心，于是朝之钜贤咸作歌诗庆美其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168052_comment'></div>初，公入蜀，居三年，不茹荤饮酒，日诵浮屠书，祈幸安归，以慰其亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168052_comment'></div>爱慕之心，岂不至哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168052_comment'></div>公讳休复，字某，居官决治，所向无留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168052_comment'></div>末年知漳州，襄适为从事，间有关白，多所称奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168052_comment'></div>今年被告还家，道出于闽，嗣子世矩袖所藏诗来谒序述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168052_comment'></div>襄尝读《诗》，至《南陔》、《白华》篇，感其孝养之心，求其词以讽咏，不可得已，而得世之诗意谓之似者，亦足观矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168052_comment'></div>以公之力行，而作诗者咸乐于称道，其嗣子又能追扬先美，是皆可书也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1168052_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5aed49a7193d4482baa2480e16778245_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5aed49a7193d4482baa2480e16778245");'><span id='5aed49a7193d4482baa2480e16778245_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>，37岁</div><div id='5aed49a7193d4482baa2480e16778245' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　蔡襄上《乞复五塘札子》，后蒙恩准，莆民德之，为立生祠于塘侧。<div id='poem_1167845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞复五塘劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167845")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167845'>臣昨至兴化军，访闻得莆田县有陂塘五所：胜寿、西冲、太和、屯前、东塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167845_comment'></div>自来积水灌注塘下沿海咸地一千馀顷为田，约八千馀家耕种为业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167845_comment'></div>大中祥符年中，有百姓陈清等陈状，于秋芦陂开渠引水灌注屯塘下民田，却决去五所陂塘，以地为田，官司妨碍，不与检给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167845_comment'></div>天圣年中，陈潭知军日，其陈清却与官户形势计会，同共请上件塘内地土，州县徇私曲理，先次给却屯前、太和、东塘陂塘三所，去水为田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167845_comment'></div>旧日仰塘水灌注之地尽皆焦旱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167845_comment'></div>百姓争讼，州县一向抑迫，不与申理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167845_comment'></div>至李馀庆知军日，陈清又请胜寿、西冲二塘为田，其时不与检给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167845_comment'></div>宝元年中，汪随政内，徇私顺情，一向检给，科率产钱，供输税赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167845_comment'></div>臣体问得自决去五所陂塘已来，沿海咸地只仰天雨，有种无收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167845_comment'></div>州县多是不与放免税赋，是致人户逃移，见居者只括土煎盐，枉陷刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167845_comment'></div>庆历二年秋旱，官司检放产税，例及九分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167845_comment'></div>切缘旧作陂塘，灌田一千馀顷，济活八千馀家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167845_comment'></div>及决塘为田已来，收得塘内田一百馀顷，丰赡得官势户三十馀家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167845_comment'></div>又年年雨水不充，放却税赋至多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167845_comment'></div>前后百姓论诉不绝，官司为见已出却产钱，经属省帐，难为除落，不与受理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167845_comment'></div>若以民间利害，即贫困却八千馀家，只丰赡得官户三十馀家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167845_comment'></div>若以官中租赋，即每年蠲放千顷租赋，只得百顷租赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167845_comment'></div>其为利害，公私灼然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167845_comment'></div>所有上件田土，虽是臣乡里，即本家及亲戚无有一亩相连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167845_comment'></div>臣欲乞下本路转运司，选清强一员，取索应是干连案卷看详，亲诣五所陂塘处定夺闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167845_comment'></div>如与臣所陈利害稍同，乞赐除落塘内新定产钱，依旧积水为塘，利济民户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167845_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1167845_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9fb806288a1d40b091f4f7b4b5d3dcd7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9fb806288a1d40b091f4f7b4b5d3dcd7");'><span id='9fb806288a1d40b091f4f7b4b5d3dcd7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，45岁</div><div id='9fb806288a1d40b091f4f7b4b5d3dcd7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年5月24日</a>　蔡襄自枫亭抵兴化军城。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年5月</a>　五月下旬，蔡襄仍寓兴化军转运厩舍候诏命，作《见匀亲抄书涕悼卷末》<div id='poem_249032' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249032' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249032?labeling=true' target='_blank'>见匀亲抄书泣悼卷末</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249032")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249032_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249032'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249032'>得汝抄书心自喜，古来清白绍家难。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249032'>谁知向老秋灯下，一见亲踪不忍看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249032_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249032'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249032_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄仍寓兴化军转运厩舍候诏命，作《寓居兴化军转运厩舍》作品：《寓居兴化转运廨舍》<div id='poem_249266' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249266' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249266?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寓居兴化转运廨舍</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249266")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249266_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249266'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249266'>病恼连春夏，居閒意味长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249266'>海风生永昼，山雨送微凉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249266'>书帙梅蒸润，衣巾荔实香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249266'>尘缘消遣尽，物我两相忘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249266_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249266'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249266_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄仍寓兴化军转运厩舍候诏命，作《丙申五月游兴化西门上溪》<div id='poem_249169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙申五月游兴化西门上溪</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249169")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249169_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249169'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249169'>寻溪因过上溪游，雨后溪浑水乱流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249169'>因傍堤松却飞盖，为闻山鸟辍鸣驺。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249169'>平田䆉稏青云合，满谷芭蕉碧玉抽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249169'>开济无功须早去，故时瓜陇有通侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249169_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249169'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年6月</a>　六月上旬，蔡襄患疮疖，仍在莆田调息。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年6月</a>　蔡襄捎寄陈家紫荔枝给晋江谢氏亲家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年6月15日</a>　蔡襄应邀到莆田城厢宋諴家品尝宋家香荔枝。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年6月18日</a>　蔡襄贻书枫亭乡人集资修建太平驿堂。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄撰书《光禄少卿方公神道碑》<div id='poem_1168169' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168169' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168169?labeling=true' target='_blank'>光禄少卿方公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168169")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168169_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168169'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168169'>方姓，周方叔之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168169_comment'></div>东汉纮避地丹阳，因居歙县，世为豪长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168169_comment'></div>唐泉州刺史取述者，纮之苗裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168169_comment'></div>歙、睦最近，公之六世祖，唐季之乱，由睦州徙家泉州兴化县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168169_comment'></div>曾祖讳京，仕伪唐为清源长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168169_comment'></div>祖讳守禋，漳州漳浦县主簿，有诗三百篇，曰《仙岩集》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168169_comment'></div>父讳鼎，太平兴国初，陈忠顺王以其地归朝廷，即泉之莆田立兴化军，又徙为莆田人，累赠工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168169_comment'></div>公讳偕，字齐古，少聪警，十四能为文词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168169_comment'></div>薛公奎知县事，公以文见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168169_comment'></div>薛意其少年，倩词于人，延坐，令作赋一篇，立就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168169_comment'></div>薛公器其远至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168169_comment'></div>二十进士及第，授温州军事推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168169_comment'></div>校其州进士，州守以客不私托，公曰：「贡举无容私」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168169_comment'></div>黜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168169_comment'></div>守导客诉于监司，覆校不私，守以是免罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168169_comment'></div>岁大饥，民有欲隶官军以就廪食，而兵有定数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168169_comment'></div>吕公夷简为提点刑狱，公白之曰：「温民饥且死，势将聚而为盗，岂若署壮强以尺籍，且消患于未萌，而公私交利乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168169_comment'></div>吕即移文于州县，点七千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168169_comment'></div>再调涟水军判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168169_comment'></div>部有浮屠人曰娄道者，能以术却寒暑，惊眩民俗，所至受施金缯无量，其徒以高赀为奸横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168169_comment'></div>公密捕，一夕辄病死，没入其财而逐其党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168169_comment'></div>转运使梁楚闻公材能，每委以难事，因而保荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168169_comment'></div>代还，吏部铨将上举者姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168169_comment'></div>或谕公曰：「保章固多，宜置梁楚，宰相之所甚恶者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168169_comment'></div>公曰：「梁知我者，倖迁而置之，吾不为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168169_comment'></div>及绩最上中书，丁谓果没之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168169_comment'></div>又为汀州军事判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168169_comment'></div>唐公肃使福建，建之建安讼日数十百，命公权涖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168169_comment'></div>旬月之间，至于閒静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168169_comment'></div>县筦茶山，先社集民数千噪山谷中，助达阳气以发茶茗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168169_comment'></div>公曰：「害吾农时而作无益耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168169_comment'></div>是岁不用，后亦遂止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168169_comment'></div>丁侍郎忧，去官，外除，改著作佐郎，知福之福清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168169_comment'></div>吏质衣以自给，人至今颂之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168169_comment'></div>徙监南剑州石牌场，月入白金三万两。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168169_comment'></div>就迁秘书丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168169_comment'></div>久之，徙知资州资阳县，迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168169_comment'></div>未行，丧太夫人，行服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168169_comment'></div>景祐二年，迁尚书屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168169_comment'></div>御史中丞杜公衍判审官院，与公无雅故，因视阀阅，曰：「唐公高洁，于人少可，今力慰荐如此，子之才行可知已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168169_comment'></div>会被诏举属官，即乞公殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168169_comment'></div>朝廷以实无资历，不如诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168169_comment'></div>又请御史里行，其官久废，罢之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168169_comment'></div>杜公奏曰：「臣所知者无如方某，即不如例，愿令他官举荐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168169_comment'></div>于是除推直官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168169_comment'></div>雷孝杰知代州，贪赃不法，屡鞠失实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168169_comment'></div>公驰驿往劾，即正其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168169_comment'></div>还见，赐绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168169_comment'></div>澧州逃卒从民李某就佣，而歉其直，遂诬其家事摩驰神，岁杀十二人以祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168169_comment'></div>州捕其族三百人，荐棘于州门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168169_comment'></div>狱久不决，诏遣治之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168169_comment'></div>公诘之曰：「必得被杀者主名」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168169_comment'></div>乃疏其姓氏乡县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168169_comment'></div>移问所疏，或存或亡，悉有根柢，无见杀者，告者伏法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168169_comment'></div>御史知杂事庞公籍荐为殿中侍御史里行，二年即真命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168169_comment'></div>又迁侍御史，使南都，降虑狱囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168169_comment'></div>时鸿庆宫灾，将议脩复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168169_comment'></div>公引汉唐罢原庙故事，疏勿复治，以答天戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168169_comment'></div>元昊叛边，寇塞门寨，鄜延路副都部署赵振闭城不救，塞门没贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168169_comment'></div>大帅言振畏懦，当寘于法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168169_comment'></div>公将命按问，振以逗挠，其当弃市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168169_comment'></div>公入为上言：「振兵众寡不敌，出亦为饵矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168169_comment'></div>振得不死流窜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168169_comment'></div>改开封府判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168169_comment'></div>时西兵未解，军资百出，取办临时，民苦不聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168169_comment'></div>朝廷遣使四出以安抚之，公往江南东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1168169_comment'></div>陛辞之日，曰：「民所甚急者，行而后奏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1168169_comment'></div>事大而缓者，请以须报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1168169_comment'></div>庶乎惠泽速逮于下也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1168169_comment'></div>比至，去贪暴，荐循良数十人，平冤死，决滞讼，威动所部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1168169_comment'></div>先时，转运使第民产高下，给以乳香，令其输绢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1168169_comment'></div>民输之绢，而吏夺其香，率空手去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1168169_comment'></div>三司出绵绮之类下州郡鬻之，促期敛钱，而帛无所用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1168169_comment'></div>公一切罢绝，而上其为害之状，转运使坐免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1168169_comment'></div>其恤民疾，宣风旨，率多此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1168169_comment'></div>入为三司判官，使契丹，复命，拜兵部员外郎兼御史知杂事，判大理寺，赐金紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1168169_comment'></div>纠大臣之不循礼法者数人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1168169_comment'></div>九十六日，擢副三司度支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1168169_comment'></div>是时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1168169_comment'></div>江淮发运使与诸路转运使事皆违异，岁漕阙其旧常，除公天章阁待制，充使江淮，东南乃办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1168169_comment'></div>发运以近侍处之，自公始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1168169_comment'></div>移知杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1168169_comment'></div>杭于吴最为繁穰，公时与宾从载酒殽，鸣丝管，周游湖山之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1168169_comment'></div>牒讼至前，谈笑遣之，若无可为治者，二年未尝有留狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1168169_comment'></div>迁刑部郎中，以疾得太常少卿，分司西京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1168169_comment'></div>祀明堂恩，为光禄卿，归休里闬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1168169_comment'></div>至和二年七月二十七日终于家，年六十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1168169_comment'></div>诏中使赗赠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1168169_comment'></div>明年正月八日，葬侯官村之灵隐山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1168169_comment'></div>公严明洁廉，察民情数，民事尤剧，益以精敏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1168169_comment'></div>其下少欺，必擿之，惕惕畏伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1168169_comment'></div>在三司、开封，每议刑平狱，钩簿领，通财利，率有条理，后以为法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1168169_comment'></div>性乐人善，汲引后进，常若不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1168169_comment'></div>生平所任保二百馀人，多显达者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1168169_comment'></div>尤善饮酒，遇酒，聪明过于常时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1168169_comment'></div>知福清，吏乘醉白事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1168169_comment'></div>明日覆之，吏隐其一，公曰：「有某事在」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1168169_comment'></div>吏叩头谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1168169_comment'></div>使契丹，其主酌大金瓢，属之曰：「此所以侑劝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1168169_comment'></div>公不辞，酌之，契丹大惊喜，遗以名马，号其器为方家瓢云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1168169_comment'></div>母王氏，赠太原郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1168169_comment'></div>妻陈氏，封安定郡君，故秘书丞讳靖之孙女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1168169_comment'></div>子四人：浃，漳州长泰令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1168169_comment'></div>洽，守将作监主簿，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1168169_comment'></div>沃，太常寺太祝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1168169_comment'></div>泽，郊祀掌坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1168169_comment'></div>女七人，适刘孝先、陈励、王拱，并进士，宣州泾县尉郑伯齐、福州连江县尉李昭文；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1168169_comment'></div>二人尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1168169_comment'></div>浃既克葬，乃以书载公之官籍拜除、卒葬之岁月，请于襄曰：「先君之于法，有碑，其文将谁托乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1168169_comment'></div>襄谨序而铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_109_1168169'>任职于朝，志不上屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1168169_comment'></div>作政于藩，势必己出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1168169_comment'></div>临剧以简，明谨惟刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1168169_comment'></div>为利以宽，矜恤惟民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1168169_comment'></div>要望是更，法从之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1168169_comment'></div>何命之啬，疾其末年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1168169_comment'></div>寿兮必终，德则滋久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1168169_comment'></div>铭以著之，唯公之有<span class='inlineComment2'>（《蔡忠惠集》卷三三。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1168169_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_117_1168169'>「不」字疑误，或衍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_117_1168169_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄应兴化军知军之邀到州峰共乐亭赏月。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e8367959d42a49209fc382d7978bd85f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8367959d42a49209fc382d7978bd85f");'><span id='e8367959d42a49209fc382d7978bd85f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄尝游紫霄岩。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年8月</a>　八月初，蔡襄赴福州之任，途径渔溪驿，作《丙申八月过渔溪驿驿旧有梅数株尝题诗记今无有也》诗。作品：《丙申秋八月过渔溪驿驿旧有梅数株尝题诗记今无有也二首》<div id='poem_249316' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249316' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249316?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙申秋八月过渔溪驿驿旧有梅数株尝题诗记今无有也二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", id='poem_sentence_0_249316'>曾把早梅枝，思君在别离。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249316'>别离虽云远，万里有还期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249316'>树枯根已拨，人去复何之。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249316_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月</a>　蔡襄致书问候友僧宝月广上人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月</a>　蔡襄有书致林郎。<br /><a -----title
漳州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cc292b21f97942c8b6753f44465d4342_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cc292b21f97942c8b6753f44465d4342");'><span id='cc292b21f97942c8b6753f44465d4342_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1034')">1031-1034年</a>，20-23岁</div><div id='cc292b21f97942c8b6753f44465d4342' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　蔡襄在漳州军事判官任。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　蔡襄颇得郡守林休复信任，宾从与主官相处融洽。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1031&endYear=1031')">1031年</a>　蔡襄作《士伸知己赋》<div id='poem_1167455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>士伸知己赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1031年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167455")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167455'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167455'>古有云：贱而达己者，道必有裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167455_comment'></div>贵而得士者，礼必与钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167455_comment'></div>意关荣以高世，朅游名于大人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167455_comment'></div>威凤下而览德，微蠖屈而求伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167455_comment'></div>谓周公多才，挥沐吐餐而延白屋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167455_comment'></div>颜子具圣，砥名砺行而附青云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167455_comment'></div>故我浩气集义，游于天真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167455_comment'></div>默守节而无闷，动会时而益振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167455_comment'></div>彬文薄乎河汉，长算骛乎臣邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167455_comment'></div>指素丝而禀洁，纫香草兮生春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167455_comment'></div>彼美君子，风度瑰伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167455_comment'></div>乌在其蔓葛以均戚，宁藉乎树枌而接里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167455_comment'></div>夷廉嶷而索言，诣幽𦕈而钧旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167455_comment'></div>判柔植于异畦，决断泾于东水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167455_comment'></div>始倾昆而娱玩，遽倒廪而矜侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167455_comment'></div>耽圣域以同奥，秩皇涂而并轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167455_comment'></div>虽韬瑕可以取璧，兼体可以收菲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167455_comment'></div>矧或太公蜕北海之居，安石翔东山而起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167455_comment'></div>我拒其归，谁执兹耻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167455_comment'></div>必使右雪苑之席，屣绣衣之履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167455_comment'></div>绳引尧舜以致君，蒙合燕赵之多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167455_comment'></div>茍气协而声同，皆克济乎薰美者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167455_comment'></div>且夫虹玉隐乎巉石，玭珠沦乎层漪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167455_comment'></div>麒麟非犬羊之比，鳣鳝岂蝼蚁之持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167455_comment'></div>沕明渊而自得，曷怵迫而外移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167455_comment'></div>华屋千榱，柔缯百帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167455_comment'></div>积粟乎京坻，跃马乎騧骊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167455_comment'></div>匪衷藏之雅尚，虽得志而弗为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167455_comment'></div>何蕴谀以发颜，何挟巧而谰辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167455_comment'></div>宜乎厚德表世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167455_comment'></div>嘉闻盖时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167455_comment'></div>身享崇高之贵，目瞻咫尺之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167455_comment'></div>谓朽株可万乘之器，廊庙非一木之支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167455_comment'></div>得于道不伐乎众公，推于室不𢅴乎内私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167455_comment'></div>举岩穴而悚观，峨冠佩而来思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167455_comment'></div>上弗求焉，无曰蔑当吾取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167455_comment'></div>下弗进焉，无曰胡为我知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167455_comment'></div>然则人之胶于今者或安于近，泥乎古者或昧乎通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167455_comment'></div>择其粉墨之异，考以宫商之同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167455_comment'></div>射乃墉上，𤑒乎日中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167455_comment'></div>鸣鹤阴而子和，雕虎啸而生风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167455_comment'></div>不然，则名位相雄，师学相攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167455_comment'></div>耕石田而待稔，怀珍剃而适戎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1167455_comment'></div>故非五难而吐论，和再刖而处穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1167455_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1167455_comment'></div>木秀林而必摧，士入朝而见嫉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1167455_comment'></div>绛灌隐堤而贾迁，椒兰发机而原黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1167455_comment'></div>子冉膏舌而墨幽，臧仓圜睛而轲逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1167455_comment'></div>夜光明月，招诃按剑之年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1167455_comment'></div>流水高山，沈思绝弦之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1167455_comment'></div>在孤见之卓越，发群蔽之丰密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1167455_comment'></div>借如说困刑戮，何撷其芳？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1167455_comment'></div>尹恬耔耨，何铺其香？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1167455_comment'></div>若岁旱而泽及，卒阿衡而自将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1167455_comment'></div>惟圣睿之觏逢，俾业履之猗昌，奚仕虞而弭废，由自戎而虏亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1167455_comment'></div>秦何售之而遂用，遽厚帑而遐疆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1167455_comment'></div>仲负弩而仇君，鲍何夺徽纆与锋铓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1167455_comment'></div>弗芥虿乎左右，麾千侯而拱天王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1167455_comment'></div>设陨越于九渊，几夷衽而易乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1167455_comment'></div>宁倚辀而鸣嗌，桓何宝其琅琅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1167455_comment'></div>鬷肆语而靡著，向何悟而趋下堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1167455_comment'></div>伊郤勋之末图，胥何利乎锡土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1167455_comment'></div>越石娱薪以相佯，婴何次骖而奄取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1167455_comment'></div>平负郭而久贫，何梯魏而康县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1167455_comment'></div>信鼓刀以周身，何翼萧而登辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1167455_comment'></div>节信疲于游宦，何怵心于皇甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1167455_comment'></div>正平蹶于羁雌，何衒能于文举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1167455_comment'></div>亮觇时而养晦，蜀何奋之于圳亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1167455_comment'></div>蒙署籍而委质，吴何抗之于卒旅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1167455_comment'></div>謇斯类之有徒，殚筠素而曷叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1167455_comment'></div>被王公之宏略，岂数子智谋之补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1167455_comment'></div>畏遗德于冥鸿，思洒恩乎施雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1167455_comment'></div>向使失风云之会，构奇邪之伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1167455_comment'></div>或侘傺于草茅，或歼危于俘虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1167455_comment'></div>亘天地以寂寥，尚何流嘉风而建英矩者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1167455_comment'></div>今兹有人，远陶圣世，少齿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1167455", 1167455, "Clauses/153/Comments/0")'>乡黉</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1167455_comment'></div>根云英之节奏，表畛域而垦耕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1167455_comment'></div>跻陵隅之峻巀，泳垠埃之渊渟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1167455_comment'></div>若夫名山首乎黄老，鬼谷谲乎纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1167455_comment'></div>桑羊役乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1167455", 1167455, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>术计</span>，商鞅刻乎刑名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1167455_comment'></div>姑还车而却步，目吾肆之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_80_1167455", 1167455, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>丰赢</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1167455_comment'></div>既披闽吴而侨贡，未几唱第于天楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1167455_comment'></div>赋从军兮南土，天盖五而回星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1167455_comment'></div>莽万端而外眩，愚幽墨而无营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1167455_comment'></div>憧百趾以高附，愚邅环而后行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1167455_comment'></div>噂决辨以旁肆，愚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_85_1167455", 1167455, "Clauses/173/Comments/0")'>抑阏</span>而钳声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1167455_comment'></div>纷结游以走誉，愚友益而尽倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1167455_comment'></div>亲冒颐而双白，又齐伐乎大庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1167455_comment'></div>第假田不足以羞旨，乌敢蕲外物而荐荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1167455_comment'></div>睎往躅而结援，坱回泬而峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1167455_comment'></div>介语默于蔀室，其谁烛之而使明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1167455_comment'></div>勾檗芽于瘠壤，又其谁育之而使成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1167455_comment'></div>岂云病畦而谄笑，哀弦而卖名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1167455_comment'></div>然世主炎黄之化，鼎连邴魏之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1167455_comment'></div>时乎时者难值，旦复旦以亲逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1167455_comment'></div>倘率道而自进，立诚知命抑在乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1167455_comment'></div>乱曰：善知人者，岂古有而今无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1167455_comment'></div>善求知者，岂彼智而兹愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1167455_comment'></div>倘固其窳而厚其薄，必幽者绠而阽者扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1167455_comment'></div>进抑时而退抑命，尔其守约而于于者乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1167455_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，常与同僚游览名胜古迹，作《漳南十咏》<div id='poem_249422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249422'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249422'>试看初日照龙台，白玉堂高锦障开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249422'>树色一番连雨净，溪光几曲抱山来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249422_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249422'>云归深洞天形瘦，风落前村笛弄哀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249276'>年来意气多羁束，无复长楸带酒归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249276'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249276_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，常与同僚游览名胜古迹，作《序宾亭》<div id='poem_249296' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249296' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249296?labeling=true' target='_blank'>序宾亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249296")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_249296_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249296'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249296'>师律先忧寄，朝家此得人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249296'>门庭环剑佩，胸胆贯星辰。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249296'>今已閒戎略，畴能卜宴申。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249296'>楼高休暇日，台迥厌登春。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249296'>珍馆瑶甍举，璇题宝篆新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249296'>鸭栏回斗颈，龙壁活盘鳞。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249296'>夹幕寒波颤，前峰古黛皴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249296'>始知仙有路，尽恐世无尘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249296'>武驭来金虎，儒簪下石麟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249296'>机分荣辱主，觯序去留宾。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249296'>揖让盈三魄，雌雄竞一神。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249296'>气横飞客箭，歌协大夫蘋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249296'>万古浮云片，劳生断梗身。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249296'>即时欢未已，往事梦非真。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249296'>席久疑枯海，琴幺似隔邻。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249296'>釭花明雨暮，瓮酎压霜晨。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249296'>鸦动残丝柳，鲈肥滑线莼。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249296'>晴霞上丹叶，熟粉护青筠。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249296'>赋景呵吟笔，挥谈密醉茵。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249296'>流年祇容易，嘉会可因循。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249296_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249296'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_249296_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，常与同僚游览名胜古迹，作《奉酬王知县赏春不与以诗见赠》<div id='poem_249225' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249225' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249225?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉酬王知县赏春不与以诗见赠</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249225")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249225_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249225'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249225'>仙陬翠观尽繁英，朱白相兼照眼明。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249225'>池浸岚光生晚碧，鸟惊人语断春声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249225'>谈谐遽喜开怀久，骪骳终惭走笔成。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249225'>佳致可能陶靖节，庭柯斜眄独忘情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249225'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249225_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，常与同僚游览名胜古迹，作《净众院尝荔支（枝）》<div id='poem_249058' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249058' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249058?labeling=true' target='_blank'>净众院尝荔支</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249058")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249058_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249058'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249058'>霞树珠林暑后新，直疑天意别留春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249058'>京华百世争鲜贵，自是芳根著海滨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249058_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249058'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249058_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1032&endYear=1032')">1032年</a>　蔡襄作《上运使王殿院书》反映福建民情。<div id='poem_1167872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上运使王殿院书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1032年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167872")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167872'>襄谨斋沐裁书，再拜献于运使殿院执事：襄尝读《书》，识其语曰「克明俊德」，又曰「后非贤罔乂」，是知君人者用贤如左右手也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167872_comment'></div>又闻仲尼摄鲁相，喜见于色，曰：「吾喜斯民之得吾也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167872_comment'></div>伊尹居畎亩，汤三聘之，然后幡然曰：「曷若使是君为尧舜之君，斯民为尧舜之民欤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167872_comment'></div>又知圣贤求道，不为已吝，明白疏畅，翼时君之政化，剔愚民之耳目，尽力而后已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167872_comment'></div>又闻周公待白屋之士，一沐三握发，一饭三吐哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167872_comment'></div>又知职设滋多，无有巨细，必在贤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167872_comment'></div>是虽有圣贤之材，处崇高之位，一良木不能成林薮，一龙驹不能备骖服，广求其合，同声呼报，以成厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167872_comment'></div>夫如是，则君臣相须之道一不可去明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167872_comment'></div>中古之世，诸侯有地以自保，继承不息，而治乱反乎耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167872_comment'></div>嬴秦一天下而为家，罢侯置守，赋征毕入王帑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167872_comment'></div>汉晋而下，悉案前武，故至于今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167872_comment'></div>方地百里为之尹，百里之民，赋税徭役之轻重，䜣讼争竞之是非，咸得决之于尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167872_comment'></div>数尹之地为之牧，以尽统其属尹之政，彼有所失，及其事之大者，皆决之于牧，是牧之政亦已重矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167872_comment'></div>然虑乎提封广而员吏多，牧尹时有弗明，天高靡闻，日不陈于上前，奈何盘冤愤于人人之臆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167872_comment'></div>于是条天下之郡，分命使以按察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167872_comment'></div>牧尹之政有所得失，执事之务有所废兴，人民之情有所曲直，使皆得振举而与夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167872_comment'></div>则是使之寄又愈重也，使之命难于任人也必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167872_comment'></div>七闽之地，南远宫庭三千馀里，边江海而围山岳，土地硗确。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167872_comment'></div>所居之地，家户联密，有欲耕而无尺土者，有畜积踰年即为陶朱猗顿之富者，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167872_comment'></div>昔者僭王相继，竞取良民膏腴之田以入浮屠氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167872_comment'></div>国朝以来，因而不改，故学浮屠者绝无徭役，第食不乏而衣有馀耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167872_comment'></div>人恶焦苦，而竞乐为之，版籍何遽不因而减之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167872_comment'></div>矧又谍诉倥偬，与民争利，故财屡屈而人愈贫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167872_comment'></div>加以建安之郡、延平之壤，或收罗茗荈，或筦榷酤齐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167872_comment'></div>福唐南直数州，煮浪以咸鹾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167872_comment'></div>国家念边储钜费，是三者利悉入公，温陵、临漳、莆阳三郡之民岁输镪以税其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167872_comment'></div>穷民妻孥无营，不能缄口待绝，所谓利悉入公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167872_comment'></div>之三者出于己者薄，而获于人者丰，虽焦手于猛火，残肌于白刃，必冒热当锋而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167872_comment'></div>故强宗右族力于兼并，游手惰农因之以流荡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167872_comment'></div>然后丹笔不及乾，邮牒不及息者，由来尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167872_comment'></div>必使当其人，则列郡有准绳，下民知教劝，于是宽猛得中，物遂其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167872_comment'></div>今执事衔天子命而来，七闽之人素仰执事德望威名，莫不谓执事可以目注口授，春和秋肃，不俟期月而罔有不利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167872_comment'></div>襄窃谓俾列郡有准绳，人民知教劝，宽猛得中，物遂其所，在今日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167872_comment'></div>然封圻僻在轩车罕至之地，萌庶之细微者不得自振，又宜择属吏而委任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167872_comment'></div>属吏既多，则真伪得无相蒙哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167872_comment'></div>有昏钝而柔懦若能仁者，有贪墨而谄媚若能恭者，有简傲而恶倔若能忠者，有别白而私徇若能断者，有行加乎人而众毁之者，有明智而力不足者，执事又宜黑白清浊以详之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167872_comment'></div>进之可，退之否，激昂士流，宣赞风美，则执事之化无不至，良吏之志有所伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167872_comment'></div>襄前所谓君人者宜用贤，贤人宜辅君化民，又宜求其类之者为之助，亦在兹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167872_comment'></div>此盖执事之所素知而能行者也，岂复假襄陈熟之言，重复而陈于执事之前耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167872_comment'></div>然襄亦占一数于吏也，奈何性钝识鄙，不足当吏之贤者必矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167872_comment'></div>然其可念者，家世无显荣，幼而从学，龆龀之岁偶能习诗赋，既而孜孜刻志，临文自省，不陷邪说于师道久废之世，自强不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167872_comment'></div>年甫十五，再求举于乡里，皆不利用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167872_comment'></div>前岁间携幼弟徒步西上，艰难困厄，侨举王府，偶先多士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1167872_comment'></div>未几得就吏禄，佐幕偏州，实贰郡政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1167872_comment'></div>大之则生杀鞭掠之权，小之则勾稽簿领之务，皆所参画而职掌之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1167872_comment'></div>以襄播迹穷阎，心灵局隘，当此委任，亦以难矣，敢不兢战，昼研夕味，益其尚短，晔其未明，旁搜远探，期于有得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1167872_comment'></div>然后知从政之术无他也，必先本诸先圣人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1167872_comment'></div>宪网虽密，参酌而用之者在乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1167872_comment'></div>折狱必先本其情，干局必预防其弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1167872_comment'></div>正其心以临下，尽其心以率职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1167872_comment'></div>如是者亦以期年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1167872_comment'></div>然才薄位下，固未能振发纲领，宣畅王化，但求内无愧于心，外无怍于人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1167872_comment'></div>其如有所可忧者，亦能自料之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1167872_comment'></div>赋受愚直，不能取容于人，在己上者有所枉道则咨之，在己列者有所罔心则评之，在己下者有所干犯则惩之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1167872_comment'></div>介介而行，一无所屈，故知获誉必少，而得谤必多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1167872_comment'></div>今遇执事使此一方，察郡以来，将及半载，所谓目注口授，春和秋肃，诚哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1167872_comment'></div>吏之不肖者必黜，贤者必升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1167872_comment'></div>政之弛者必张，成者必奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1167872_comment'></div>列郡畏服，不俟一二提振，皆以改革，势若建瓴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1167872_comment'></div>襄既在属吏之列，遇执事明白若是，倘或缄其诚而不吐，钧是流而偕进，则执事以襄为何人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1167872_comment'></div>今虽覼缕于下座，亦非有所冀私恩而垂曲庇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1167872_comment'></div>所以勤勤者，但不知量于吾道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1167872_comment'></div>每念周汉之际，由其臣之文章事业，使后世知其时之治乱废兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1167872_comment'></div>至于唐室全盛，馀三百年，今之推其知道能文者数公耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1167872_comment'></div>迨于我朝，能以文章为己任，提挽党类，恢宏词于天表，挹清醇于笔下，焕赫洋溢，流于无穷，若执事先君子者几何人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1167872_comment'></div>而位未跻于台辅，功不遍于寰区，人到于今惜之，得非臧孙有后，毕万必大，是生执事，以翊王道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1167872_comment'></div>况今天子仁圣，远夷怀柔，戈甲生蠹，务农桑，竭地脉，政教流行，罔知帝力，执事岂特享富贵、足志气而已耶，亦将有以羽翼明主、康济斯民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1167872_comment'></div>襄又岂特茍刍豢、保妻孥而已耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1167872_comment'></div>亦将有以驱策驽钝、黾勉展效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1167872_comment'></div>惟吾君克明峻德，求贤共乂，岂宜晚用执事也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1167872_comment'></div>执事喜斯民之得吾也，使君为尧舜之君，民为尧舜之民，职设无有巨细，必在贤者，又岂宜不竭衷于吾君，而求其类之者同声呼报以成厥功也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1167872_comment'></div>执事一朝曳履岩廊，恢张先德，崇大邦基，不敢于人则已，将取人则在乎熟其学行，饱其声猷，然后用之而无疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1167872_comment'></div>襄今日为属吏，是亦亲而且迩也，可以察而知之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1167872_comment'></div>茍不受知于左右，则他日之望必疏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1167872_comment'></div>愿执事熟思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1167872_comment'></div>譬诸立明堂焉，大之为栋梁，小之为欂栌榱桷，俾其高下各得其所，则我朝文物声名日益乎郁茂，礼乐刑政日益乎修举，惟吾君高出于古之能为君者，执事一无屈于古之能为臣者，岂不盛欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1167872_comment'></div>傥执事不罪其愚，箴其过使革之，赐之教使遵之，长育以成其材，使可就用，必出于门下也，幸甚幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1167872_comment'></div>干渎威明，不胜愧汗，察之怜之，在执事而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1167872_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1167872_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1167872'></div><div id='poem_sentence_79_1167872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，作《耕园驿佛桑花》<div id='poem_249254' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249254' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249254?labeling=true' target='_blank'>耕园驿佛桑花</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249254")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249254_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249254'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249254'>溪馆初寒似早春，寒花相倚醉于人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249254'>可怜万木彫零尽，独见繁枝烂熳新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249254'>清艳夜沾云表露，幽香时过辙中尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249254'>名园不肯争颜色，的的夭红野水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249254_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249254'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249254_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　蔡襄在漳州任上，作《溪行》<div id='poem_249417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>溪行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249417")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249417'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249417'>秋色已寥落，清溪才此行。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249417'>船移酒杯侧，鱼得鲙刀鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249417'>日色浮兼动，风痕灭又生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249417'>从知隐者趣，不独傲荣名。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249417_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249417'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　蔡襄长女出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1033&endYear=1033')">1033年</a>　蔡襄作《曹女传》<div id='poem_1168167' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168167' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168167?labeling=true' target='_blank'>曹女传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1033年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168167")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168167_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168167'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168167'>曹氏女，建安郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168167_comment'></div>其父修古，博学而文，善议论，外和内刚，所至以直气闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168167_comment'></div>明道初，以御史知杂事言事触罪，降工部员外郎、知兴化军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168167_comment'></div>明年不召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168167_comment'></div>夏四月，疾暴作，一夕而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168167_comment'></div>修古持己洁廉，仰禄自足，有馀则推之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168167_comment'></div>既死，妻孥益贫，殆无以奉其丧以还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168167_comment'></div>其属吏民思之，相与稡钱三十万，用资其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168167_comment'></div>拜酹堂下，前白所以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168167_comment'></div>家人未及言，女哭曰：「我先君居朝为闻人，以清节自立，不幸天不与年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168167_comment'></div>终于贬所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168167_comment'></div>今临财苟得，尚何面目」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168167_comment'></div>旦夕哭泣帷中：「幸趣持归，无吾先君累也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168167_comment'></div>吏民闻之惭，罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168167_comment'></div>明道二年，女生之十六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168167_comment'></div>先以父命配其里中人徐生，未及归而父殁云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1168167_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　蔡襄作乡信贴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1034&endYear=1034')">1034年</a>　蔡襄闻弟高登第讯，喜作《喜弟及第》诗志贺。<div
