id='poem_title_249421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249421'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249421'>虚堂永昼来风长，石枕竹簟寒生光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249421'>文园肺渴厌烦热，更要夫君在侧傍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249421_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249421'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年夏</a>　蔡襄离漳时，与颜慥饯别于通源驿，作《通源驿别颜茂才》作品：《通源驿饯别颜茂才》<div id='poem_249092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通源驿别颜茂才</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年夏）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249092")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249092'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249092'>跃马东来不记时，酒醒寒色入征衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249092'>垂杨官道连天<span class='inlineComment2'>（蔡本作人争）</span>去，落日邮亭别我归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249092_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249092'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249092_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
漯河
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='67c567ffd0de413e948a573cf843a81b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("67c567ffd0de413e948a573cf843a81b");'><span id='67c567ffd0de413e948a573cf843a81b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，25岁</div><div id='67c567ffd0de413e948a573cf843a81b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>　蔡襄过武阳，作《新泉记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（颍昌府有舞阳而无武阳。）</span><div id='poem_1168105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>新泉记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168105")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168105'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168105'>功不益于世，望不悚于物，抱美而渊潜者，盖徯昌于时、期大于人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168105_comment'></div>徯得乎昌，期得乎大，则益世之功、悚物之望固不加少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168105_comment'></div>若新泉者，斯之谓耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168105_comment'></div>予顷年求荐天都，道武阳之西鄙，暮邸蘧庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168105_comment'></div>时适新夏，思以绠泉煮茗，招神宅府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168105_comment'></div>而所居之民啜浆熟膳，日汲溪隅之水，帚遗而沟泄者有之，足涤而面沬者有之，则向之绠泉之发，莫有所㥦焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168105_comment'></div>循溪而下，巨石盘互，有罅然中断者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168105_comment'></div>平沙之间，泉窦如缕，流润数咫，若披而决焉，若掊而浚焉，激乎浑然，止乎洼然，甘出天味，清鉴人骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168105_comment'></div>焚葭植鼎，且偿昔意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168105_comment'></div>既而莫知其为瓦砾之遂堙乎，为罂缶之给用乎，五年于今矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168105_comment'></div>不意解官就道，迹追旧赏，所谓新泉者砻石以环，植宇以覆，居者行者，且引且酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168105_comment'></div>德哉泉乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168105_comment'></div>独曰惟其时乎，则日迁稔革，孰泉之顾？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168105_comment'></div>独曰惟其人乎，则冰莹玉澈，孰泉之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168105_comment'></div>泉莫克明，予得肆辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168105_comment'></div>间使弗披而决，弗掊而浚，诚有甘出天味，清鉴人骨，兹焉之美，适以下滋蛰蚓之壤，上沃栖凫之莽，岂复居者行者，且引且酌之为利哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168105_comment'></div>且夫崒天之干，惟工之斧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168105_comment'></div>剸玉之锋，惟工之砥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168105_comment'></div>物莫不然，斯亦固然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168105_comment'></div>予倡厥初，是为《新泉记》云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1168105_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bacd0a8be9a6474aa018568d8b8b02b0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bacd0a8be9a6474aa018568d8b8b02b0");'><span id='bacd0a8be9a6474aa018568d8b8b02b0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，25岁</div><div id='bacd0a8be9a6474aa018568d8b8b02b0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年7月</a>　蔡襄在西京留守推官任上，致书太常博士王洙，作《答王太祝书》<div id='poem_1167876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答王太祝书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167876")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167876'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167876'>七月十五日，新授西京留守推官蔡襄顿首白太祝王君足下：前数日幸辱肯临，后二日又惠书累纸，何意勤眷之厚殊甚如此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167876_comment'></div>仆资性椎钝，不识他伎，缀文绩学，以植厥中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167876_comment'></div>虽浑浑乎进而不画，逾久益远，不知何时至且成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167876_comment'></div>足下过听，一至吾庐，遽以道义滋益为谋，非欲善之速，孰肯为此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167876_comment'></div>谋之贤明，犹将敛衽避席，如仆之固陋，适邅回而不敢承足下之赐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167876_comment'></div>然足下谓速得话言以诏之，无以世胄顾我，此岂得不自辨而已乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167876_comment'></div>商周而上，开设庠学，以教胄子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167876_comment'></div>合考其能，施于民上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167876_comment'></div>故材必育成，而赏不虚授也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167876_comment'></div>秦汉以还，侯王世袭，其大臣宿政有父任之科，有家调之泽，咸得与政，而庠学之设，名存实亡，非如古者之必计其能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167876_comment'></div>故右姓子弟，出襁抱而享贵爵，一日用，毕愿，学与不学，在其志耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167876_comment'></div>乃有自甘沦败，不图树立，蠹美材而辜厚赏，诚可嗟愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167876_comment'></div>至于道义砥焉，惟能者之所存，非有布衣纨裤之异而彼轻此重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167876_comment'></div>处约者虑深，意满者志肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167876_comment'></div>虑深故能图树立，志肆故善甘沦败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167876_comment'></div>虽常人之情，未足为贤材议，然由此而立、由此而败者岂少哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167876_comment'></div>足下家故相，旌躬为善官，退托穷约，好学乐闻，树立于斯时也有日矣，仆何敢置长短于鄙心也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167876_comment'></div>穷通不实于中，毁誉必至于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167876_comment'></div>而足下惜仆仕宦之未达，而自叹名誉之不彰，此宜仆与足下皆不得怵其心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167876_comment'></div>盖非我营者，吾不能知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167876_comment'></div>如何如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167876_comment'></div>穷居多故，不时前谢，具舟旦夕东下，必造门为别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167876_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167876_comment'></div>襄顿首白。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1167876_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年秋</a>　蔡襄作《慈竹赋》<div id='poem_1167457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>慈竹赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1036年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167457")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167457'>种植至多，强名万汇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167457_comment'></div>物拔其萃，兹乃当天地之正气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167457_comment'></div>有美竹兮特禀，挟慈名而荣被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167457_comment'></div>岂有怀于本根兮，何千竿蓊然而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1167457", 1167457, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>环侍</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167457_comment'></div>若夫吴郡名园，王家新第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167457_comment'></div>远阁斜栏，横塘静水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167457_comment'></div>或薰风昼来，或秋露宵坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167457_comment'></div>日迟留兮檐外阴移，人悽悄兮屏间籁起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167457_comment'></div>方且濯峭格而清举，足檀栾之生意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167457_comment'></div>或翘而举者，若堂有高年兮，动素风而讲议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167457_comment'></div>或亚而侧者，若家有令子兮，感话言而沉思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167457_comment'></div>伥如出门而事远游兮，滋宿雨之清泪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167457_comment'></div>雍如奉卮而介眉寿兮，幕春烟而怡醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167457_comment'></div>紫芽蟠联，馨儿季稚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167457_comment'></div>去者奔追，迎者嬉戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167457_comment'></div>竦者如招，并者如倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167457_comment'></div>虽复贯千状于巧笔，曾莫形其仿佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167457_comment'></div>借如<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1167457", 1167457, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>秋晚</span>霜重兮，万木零零而僵悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167457_comment'></div>陇榆尽兮塞月高，堤枫丹兮楚江紫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167457_comment'></div>此君乃束蓝田之苗玉，刻炎州之梢翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167457_comment'></div>固节虚心兮，虽大钧不能夺其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167457_comment'></div>于是揖三荆于堂下，结蔓藟于河涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167457_comment'></div>袭气同根之豆，交驩承萼之棣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167457_comment'></div>顾威凤之时下，亦孝乌之来寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167457_comment'></div>设有用于律筒，天声发兮太和备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167457_comment'></div>睹此芳物，悲哉远人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167457_comment'></div>昔我从军兮南之海滨，今我辞家兮西游洛尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167457_comment'></div>畅然于旧国旧都，感庄生之论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167457_comment'></div>恭止乎维桑与梓，讽周傅之陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167457_comment'></div>指白云兮天远，采幽兰兮露新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167457_comment'></div>嗟碧鲜之得地，乃丛茆而相亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167457_comment'></div>吾议尔德，岂止乎千亩之渭侯，当订万石之封君者也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1167457_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d24b0d049d32437cad75b3cd6ca28770_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d24b0d049d32437cad75b3cd6ca28770");'><span id='d24b0d049d32437cad75b3cd6ca28770_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1040')">1037-1040年</a>，26-29岁</div><div id='d24b0d049d32437cad75b3cd6ca28770' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄在西京留守推官上任，主宾关系融洽。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年闰4月</a>　蔡襄作《上庞端公书》，敦请再向朝廷奏免漳、泉、兴三郡身丁税。<div id='poem_1167875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上庞端公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年闰4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167875")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167875'>闰四月日，具官蔡襄，谨遣公仆献书于端公执事：间者襄取孥江南，会执事受诏还台，尝获承颜坐隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167875_comment'></div>执事以襄闽人，又素官于闽，与之言老儒茅知至，及泉南、临漳、莆阳三郡税丁事，颇自嗟邑，盖将归而为上言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167875_comment'></div>襄窃思，自谓执事美实副于大名，不为常俗之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167875_comment'></div>夫俗吏狃禄食，矫声誉，计己之利而忘民之勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167875_comment'></div>苟安三年，幸而代归，视旧所涖之地之民若踵迹之遗，岂皇反顾哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167875_comment'></div>使主泽不宣，时弊不改，职此之由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167875_comment'></div>而执事视三郡之民，有失职者，少选必念，非恤隐之厚，其孰能若是乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167875_comment'></div>及来京师，乃知茅君先时，朝廷用执事之请，以助教官宠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167875_comment'></div>襄每以茅君之德，宜享束帛之聘，亦既宠已，不应复论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167875_comment'></div>惟身丁之税，宜有闻而未闻，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167875_comment'></div>岂执事尝言之，而襄远贱，不得知之欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167875_comment'></div>将未尝言之，姑有待欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167875_comment'></div>抑亦遂弃之而都不记录欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167875_comment'></div>其已尝言而行之也，则襄不独庆三郡之民之受大赐，而庆本朝力太平而粹王道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167875_comment'></div>其未尝言之而姑有待也，则凡事过久，易于因循，重于建白，今兹惟时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167875_comment'></div>其遂弃之而都不记录也，则执事非宜得此望于人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167875_comment'></div>昔者五代之季，群豪列壤，连兵恣欲，国用不给，故无名之税兴焉，民不相聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167875_comment'></div>天祚真主，方内一统，人人自谓再生，欢欣顺命，无待威震。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167875_comment'></div>盖欲去向者之苦，而蒙今者之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167875_comment'></div>谓何其三郡之人引领伫望四五十年，未之或省？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167875_comment'></div>意者，建议者之不明，而吾君、吾相未悉闻之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167875_comment'></div>闻之，岂不为之动心哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167875_comment'></div>南方地狭谷鲜，又浮海通商，钱散不聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167875_comment'></div>丁男日佣不过四五十文，身丁之直岁率三百，衣食之馀，终年不能足之，必僦产子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167875_comment'></div>不幸而疾病若岁旱而力不售，与掌输之官弗严而有遗失之患，顾无他营，死焉耳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167875_comment'></div>力能扶持老弱，流冗他郡，自为胜策，而又名书不减，害延乎司里者，其哀劳之状不可尽数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167875_comment'></div>先朝时，诏书特免江浙诸身丁钱，以贯计者五十馀万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167875_comment'></div>斯时，七闽有不材使，以谓诏书所免者身丁钱耳，三郡身丁之输者斗斛也，非在免中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167875_comment'></div>不能举而覆奏，故先皇帝育物之仁均而有遗，岂不恨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167875_comment'></div>伏念主上圣神慈爱，设或一日推烈考之遗仁，鞠一方之捐瘠，无亦裨大化之万一乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167875_comment'></div>诚未欲尽免，固宜先舍贫民之无田业者，与无货财之为商贾者，分别其条，深为之防，使贫富判异，而人全其生，此急务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167875_comment'></div>文王为政，先于鳏寡孤独，若先免贫民，无害于国力大计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167875_comment'></div>愿执事恳至陈之，庶乎必行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167875_comment'></div>执事以言用，天下之所望者本务大体也，而襄徒言其近者，亦跬步之发焉，伏惟财察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167875_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167875_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1167875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄作《答谢景山书》<div id='poem_1167873' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167873' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167873?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答谢景山书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1037年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167873")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167873_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167873'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167873'>襄顿首景山足下：夏中辱示新文数十篇，其间景山所称道而仆所不愿为者，因事往问，幸而时中，欲景山思而从之，不敢陈于文辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167873_comment'></div>近蒙示书，盈千百言，引喻称类，若固守而不移者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167873_comment'></div>某欲终不言，然使景山固而不移，特唱于人，亦某过之大者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167873_comment'></div>某尝病景山好称学韩杜笔，语于人，今而曰：「既师其意，又师其辞，何患？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167873_comment'></div>且嗜退之文辞，欲诱人同所乐也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167873_comment'></div>某谓由道而学文，道至焉，文亦至焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167873_comment'></div>由文而之道，困于道者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167873_comment'></div>是故道为文之本，文为道之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167873_comment'></div>与其诱人于文，孰若诱人于道之先也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167873_comment'></div>景山前书主文辞而言，故有是云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167873_comment'></div>襄岂敢鄙文词哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167873_comment'></div>顾事有先后耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167873_comment'></div>襄之为文，无能过人，其句读高下，时亦类乎古人，无足怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167873_comment'></div>又病景山嗟世人之不知己，务以文词求于有位，今而曰：「吾以文求正于有位，于道为无枉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167873_comment'></div>古之人重其自进，我仕且困坠，求知于人无愧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167873_comment'></div>又云：「有数顷田，必归耕海上」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167873_comment'></div>景山何乐于自进，而勇于自退乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167873_comment'></div>是未离乎躁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167873_comment'></div>妄者易进而难退，狷者难进而易退，妄与狷，君子皆不由也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167873_comment'></div>君子之于进退，唯其道而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167873_comment'></div>景山又多取前世重人自进为比，苟有异于襄之说，虽前世重人，襄不从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167873_comment'></div>其称仲尼，佛肸召而欲往，孟子不遇于鲁侯，斯二者何求哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167873_comment'></div>委乎天而待用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167873_comment'></div>又病景山恤仕宦之颠踬，今而曰：「非恤美仕之未得，愤意外之横辱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167873_comment'></div>斯亦景山未之思与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167873_comment'></div>夫圣人之言，吾畏之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167873_comment'></div>贤者之规，吾愧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167873_comment'></div>有人加言于我，吾置其喜怒而辨其枉直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167873_comment'></div>使其言蹈乎圣人贤者之说，吾畏而且愧焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167873_comment'></div>其言异于是，吾将悯之，岂暇受而为辱乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167873_comment'></div>小人之辱，君子不辱也，景山取之哉，取之哉，抑愤之心日益损矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167873_comment'></div>景山又云：若使襄年四十而卑辱，未必能如己之恬然不茍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167873_comment'></div>襄又复而读之，益悲，岂行己之谬与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167873_comment'></div>如景山且不能见信，尚何望于众人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167873_comment'></div>虽然，襄无求信于人，自信甚明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167873_comment'></div>身之穷泰，不得而知之，为学远近，力穷则已，其所自信者，不却行而利动也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167873_comment'></div>今日视前日，犹能乐其所是，而恨其所不至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167873_comment'></div>使年益加而虑益广，岂肯舍所乐而从所恨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167873_comment'></div>与景山别久，思一相见，以道所怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167873_comment'></div>今虽谆谆其词，非求胜于景山，盖陈己之所守，抑未知景山以为非是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167873_comment'></div>诚以为非是，幸亦语焉，襄不敢惮烦于屡告也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167873_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167873_comment'></div>襄顿首上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1167873_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄构绿竹堂于洛阳寓处，常同僚友聚会堂中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄常与僚友游宴于史馆园、普明寺等胜地。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄尝同尹源等游龙门。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄尝游寿安（宜阳）福昌院、三乡寺诸胜景。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄尝同尹源游嵩山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1037&endYear=1037')">1037年</a>　蔡襄尝书名帖谒吕姓推官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年3月</a>　范雍继任西京留守，对蔡襄印象亦甚佳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　蔡襄长子匀出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　蔡襄作《再答谢景山书》<div id='poem_1167874' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167874' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167874?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再答谢景山书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167874")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167874_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167874'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167874'>襄启：去年得景山新文，心窃喜慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167874_comment'></div>且襄与景山游最旧，其有疑者，不敢自嘿，因而往告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167874_comment'></div>景山始未之从，又往告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167874_comment'></div>今再辱书，复说勤辨，将有以开发愚陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167874_comment'></div>然襄前者所论，罔不尽心，景山自取舍之，襄不能移也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167874_comment'></div>于其间取一二事以自辨焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167874_comment'></div>夫传道莫若言，传言莫若文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167874_comment'></div>言者道之所由，而文者言之所存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167874_comment'></div>道充乎中，造次而言，无有不极于文也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167874_comment'></div>其道馁焉，而其文虽工，终亦莫之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167874_comment'></div>襄前书云：「由道而学文，道至焉，文亦至焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167874_comment'></div>由文而之道，困于道者多矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167874_comment'></div>此所谓学者先于学道，而后于学文耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167874_comment'></div>而景山谓六经之道皆由文而后明，未闻先由文而失道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167874_comment'></div>景山离前书之意而言，固不异其所归，复而从之则通矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167874_comment'></div>景山又云：某前所论书传示于人，恐醇识君子以襄为取友之短、售己之长而取名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167874_comment'></div>诚得世人人皆醇识君子，宜不以是过襄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167874_comment'></div>且一言之发，终莫之御，况为文词，其传固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167874_comment'></div>景山示襄之书已传于人也，而襄之文独安能止众人之无传焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167874_comment'></div>夫道至大也，至公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167874_comment'></div>以其至大也，故学者莫能悉其要，于是异端偏说兴焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167874_comment'></div>君子畏道之不明，然后是是而非非，以其至公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167874_comment'></div>君子是是而非非，咸一于至当，不得私而让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167874_comment'></div>柳子厚于韩退之，其友也，子厚论史事，辞意甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167874_comment'></div>张籍于退之，师弟子也，亦讥其駮杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167874_comment'></div>子厚与籍岂欲暴其师友之失而自取胜乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167874_comment'></div>以道有所明，不得私而让其师友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167874_comment'></div>其书传于今，人莫或非之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167874_comment'></div>刘歆之于父向也，论《春秋》义，率多异同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167874_comment'></div>歆，汉名儒，又岂欲前其父乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167874_comment'></div>以道有所明，虽其父不得私而让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167874_comment'></div>其书亦传于今，莫或非之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167874_comment'></div>伊尹陈训戒于君太甲，教告切深，其自称功德，无与为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1167874_comment'></div>伊尹，圣人之徒，又岂欲昭其君之所昧，而耀己乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1167874_comment'></div>以道有所明，虽其君不得私而让焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1167874_comment'></div>其书，仲尼取之以为世法，无有疑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1167874_comment'></div>弟子于其师，子于其父，臣于其君，不自嫌于不让而辨之，惟道故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1167874_comment'></div>故其师也，父也，君也，亦惟道之恤，闻其不让而辨之，必以为当然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1167874_comment'></div>况朋友之切劘规诲，理固然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1167874_comment'></div>《春秋》之法，为亲者、尊者、贤者讳其恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1167874_comment'></div>传曰「恶讦以为直」者，谓不暴于人之隐慝耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1167874_comment'></div>若夫论义曲直，必章章然大辨，以传于世，岂比家人温寒劳苦语言，务相承取而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1167874_comment'></div>然景山曾不是虑，而谓襄售己之长以取名，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1167874_comment'></div>名吾者谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1167874_comment'></div>于何而售？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1167874_comment'></div>取名于贤者，贤者进人以德，不进人以名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1167874_comment'></div>取名于庸人，庸人足名吾哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1167874_comment'></div>襄不置心于名也且久，况期售乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1167874_comment'></div>古君子之于人，一有贤己，从而学焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1167874_comment'></div>一有未至，从而告焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1167874_comment'></div>学焉者，欲人之速至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1167874_comment'></div>告焉者，欲人之速贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1167874_comment'></div>朋友道衰，人务自高，读书指古人姓名，咿嚘称慕，以不见为恨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1167874_comment'></div>使其人同世而处，莫肯公其是非，而相推先以道义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1167874_comment'></div>呜呼，欲朋友之义存而道之兴也，不亦难乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1167874_comment'></div>襄以是于景山勤而不已，自谓于朋友之义为得，而速望于景山者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1167874_comment'></div>今反过疑于襄，非敢闻命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1167874_comment'></div>景山文日益高，济之深虑，至乎至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1167874_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1167874_comment'></div>襄顿首上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1167874_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年</a>　蔡襄权知洛阳县事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1038&endYear=1038')">1038年12月</a>　蔡襄为尹洙父仲宣作《尚书虞部员外郎尹公墓表》<div id='poem_1168171' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168171' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168171?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书虞部员外郎尹公墓表<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元元年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1038年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168171")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168171_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168171'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168171'>公讳仲宣，咸平三年明经登第，历梓州铜山、凤翔麟游二簿，调永兴司理参军，又为潞州襄垣主簿，迁汝州梁县、怀州武陟二令，又迁蜀州军判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168171_comment'></div>荐公之行能于朝者十数人，由是除大理寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168171_comment'></div>又四迁为尚书虞部员外郎，历知汝州叶、郑荥阳二县，又知大宁监、通判华州，华州由知资州，最后知郢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168171_comment'></div>以景祐四年三月七日卒于官，春秋七十一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168171_comment'></div>公之为治，应事辄决，未尝迎立科指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168171_comment'></div>辨词周复，细民自得尽其情实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168171_comment'></div>然慈恕，虽发见巧伪，不忍置之深法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168171_comment'></div>所至之州若县，其人至今皆曰：「尹思公为我主曲直，宁可得也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168171_comment'></div>其尤著明者，许州进士朱公祐尝游资州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168171_comment'></div>当是时，公初卒，资州闻之，廛巷传道，老稚相扶携涕泣，入浮屠宫哀号吊问，道交踵，往来数日而后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168171_comment'></div>公祐于公父子间无平生之旧，美公爱于资，遂记之以传于人，曰《遗爱录》云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168171_comment'></div>呜呼，公乎，其厚德者欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168171_comment'></div>古者太守、刺史权大官久，能以威惠滋其下，故时有思者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168171_comment'></div>今之为郡，沾三岁辄更罢去，事小大率有法令，虽材者巧摘奇断，立威刑以为强名，然其居也民畏之，去则已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168171_comment'></div>公平易，不设垣堑，悉驱所治之民而内之，俾其自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168171_comment'></div>公存，无能指引一二事以称说，及其终，乃怀思无穷，岂非尽其中者，其迹愈隐而其感益深乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168171_comment'></div>公始至郢州，以书语其子洙曰：「吾州土风和，民俗厚，所治有池台树石观游之美，可以休吾心焉，终此观吾老矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168171_comment'></div>署事始三日，早作被疾，比呼医至，已大剧，志莫克遂，可悲也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168171_comment'></div>公之先世居太原，祖某赠光禄卿，葬河南寿安，其后子孙遂居河南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168171_comment'></div>考文化，仕至尚书都官郎中，以才能名当时，累赠刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168171_comment'></div>母郑氏，追受德兴县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168171_comment'></div>夫人张氏，寿安县君，以贤德称于内外族，前公七年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168171_comment'></div>子男源、洙、湘、冲、淑、沂、澄七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168171_comment'></div>源、洙、澄皆中进士科，湘以荫补官，冲、淑并早亡，沂尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168171_comment'></div>公之卒，明年十一月，从葬祖考之兆，其孤谓襄曰：欧阳永叔既铭吾先君子之行藏圹中，冀千万年以永存，子且无词慰予哀乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168171_comment'></div>襄谨次其始末，用考信于后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168171_comment'></div>其年十二月日，刻石以表于墓下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1168171_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　蔡襄敕加朝奉郎、试大理评事，仍在西京留守推官任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　宋绶接任西京留守，常同蔡襄切磋书法，主宾更相得。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　蔡襄作楷书《三略》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　蔡襄撰《仙游县学进士题名记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《通远桥记》<div id='poem_1168107' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168107' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168107?labeling=true' target='_blank'>通远桥记<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元二年十二月二十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168107")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168107_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168107'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168107'>隋都洛阳，负城封地以为苑圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168107_comment'></div>唐全盛时，距城西，绝谷水，治两上阳宫，梁其水以通之，益修临幸观游池馆，回绕几百里，禁民无得至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168107_comment'></div>自天子在汴，河南为别都，悉弃故苑囿地与民，耕而为田，复旧梁以达东西道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168107_comment'></div>谷水发源甚近，于其常也特渐车之渎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168107_comment'></div>然北并山阜，乘积雨，支流之势，湍注益悍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168107_comment'></div>虽钜木丛贯，而力不堪植，漂浮判散，行者艰济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168107_comment'></div>即又新之，雨辄复坏，若是岁或再三焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168107_comment'></div>宝元二年，资政殿大学士、礼部尚书常山公既莅河南，视民之所以利与其所以病，必兴而置之，物制事办，罔不脩举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168107_comment'></div>其夏，谷水败桥，公曰：「道吾疆而有病涉者，孰使然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168107_comment'></div>吾思惩数劳而图久利，无所事木，必伐石为之乃可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168107_comment'></div>于是命三班奉职、勾当桥道司王怀吉专董其役，复以内侍高品、监修大内任修己、府推李昭逢总其区处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168107_comment'></div>考规度，商功费，谨财用，庀工徒，罔懈以力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168107_comment'></div>始作于八月丁亥，迨十月癸未，以既事告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168107_comment'></div>公谓襄曰：「桥抵宫城七里，旧以七里为号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168107_comment'></div>今新矼益壮大，子其择所宜称者名且记之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168107_comment'></div>襄退而次其道所从来，盖西属于陕，达于秦雍，尽关中，地方数千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168107_comment'></div>又西南，踰襄汉，通巴蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168107_comment'></div>其王官之奔职，邦士之修贡，传邮之将命，商旅之迁货，若方外羌夷荒忽之域涵泽而内附，凡东走京师以往来者，车蓄辇负，蹄轨相轧，莫不出此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168107_comment'></div>远哉其为利乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168107_comment'></div>请以「通远」名之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168107_comment'></div>古诸侯国咸有史官，事大小悉存于简册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168107_comment'></div>鲁新作延厩，而书之《春秋》，盖无不录也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168107_comment'></div>后世州郡无以纪事职其官者，有所兴治，非特识焉，则泯昧而不传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168107_comment'></div>襄谨载其实，揭石道周，异日职方氏访通远桥作之所始，于是乎考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168107_comment'></div>十二月二十五日，留守推官、朝奉郎、试大理评事蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1168107_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《导伊水记》<div id='poem_1168108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>导伊水记<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元二年十二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168108")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168108'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168108'>伊水出伊阳县西南山，北流至阙塞，折东会于洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168108_comment'></div>自阙塞治渠酾水，行一十八里，以贯郡城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168108_comment'></div>伊濒大山，属连数百里，其生植深远无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168108_comment'></div>多材木林竹、薪蒸橡栗之饶，岁取之，设方桴以载，浮伊而下，循渠引行，萃于城中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168108_comment'></div>物众售平，人用赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168108_comment'></div>其后渠废水涸，昔之可浮而至者悉载且负，久之莫或复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168108_comment'></div>宝元元年，今振武军节度使、知延州范公以资政殿学士、吏部侍郎居守西都，首图伊渠之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168108_comment'></div>乃命知河南县事尚书虞部员外郎王益恭、右侍禁皇城巡检李昭庆迹视其故，计费度功，以三班借职、监竹木务刘信、河南主簿欧阳昱总庀工徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168108_comment'></div>秋九月二十七日始作，冬十一月十六日役休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168108_comment'></div>纳石竹落，以障大川，更起堤防，壅其来势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168108_comment'></div>及城且五里，洛渠横前，不得绝其流而度，编木为槽，承以石趾，架而通之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168108_comment'></div>向之载负者复舍陆而浮矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168108_comment'></div>官寺民舍往往支取其饶，溉注园池碾硙，为利滋博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168108_comment'></div>其年，公持节守边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168108_comment'></div>明年，以书与襄，俾述渠以遗后人，庶完治勿坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168108_comment'></div>襄窃谓近世官守亟更易无常处，所临之郡，官称姓名适在人耳目，则又罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168108_comment'></div>虽良吏，势不能施发德惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168108_comment'></div>积染风俗之久而必从，三年而迁，视其地与民置之若遗迹，非志于民者，孰去而思之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168108_comment'></div>公方专制羌虏，早夜设方略，审机势，以攻取决胜为事，今乃勤勤洛人之利而不忘，可谓志于民者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168108_comment'></div>二年十二月日，留守推官、朝奉郎、试大理评事蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1168108_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《白波发运使厅壁记》<div id='poem_1168109' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168109' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168109?labeling=true' target='_blank'>白波发运使厅壁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168109")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168109'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168109'>唐开元中，裴耀卿建言，濒河设仓廪，治舟以漕湘、衡、吴、楚、淮、泗之粟，水行数千百里，浮鸿沟，达河，溯渭，以食长安，用是国富以强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168109_comment'></div>其后刘晏修旧制，费益损而力益赡，号为材能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168109_comment'></div>自天子居其大梁，南方之饶萃而不西，乃取关中地水以东下，而三门、白波、河阴咸设官莅治发运之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168109_comment'></div>其治白波者，增使名而重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168109_comment'></div>金部员外郎陈君既总使职，凡邦计之所赖，货财百物，迁徙上下，必精思以行之，故事无留者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168109_comment'></div>因视其所治介于河洛之间，南北有嵩山、少室、天坛、太行，群山绝特之美，远近环合，登临而观之，可以娱游而宴处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168109_comment'></div>于是累高以为台，诛榛以为圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168109_comment'></div>植宇联属，互作佳致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168109_comment'></div>图志记书，盈溢几案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168109_comment'></div>官事且休，日出其下，彷徉而自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168109_comment'></div>夫治繁而简者，其中有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168109_comment'></div>以静而动者，于外无累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168109_comment'></div>君处尤剧之务，而未始离乎淡漠，其为心也，岂不裕哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1168109_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《谢公堂记》<div id='poem_1168110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢公堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（宝元二年十二月二十五日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168110")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168110'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168110'>副阁舍人阳夏公天圣中通判府事，首议以河南天子西都，学馆宜鉴唐故事，建名比上京，遂请易其号为国子监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168110_comment'></div>延致旧儒，讲解经术，以教学者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168110_comment'></div>公雅以文重于时，又躬与诸生立程准、评辞章，每更品目，声闻辄随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168110_comment'></div>而上下咸益奋厉，业成而登仕者比旧加众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168110_comment'></div>自公捐世，诸生日相视嗟戚，皆曰：「孰从而求导予者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168110_comment'></div>既又曰：「逝者不作，而思者无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168110_comment'></div>昔后魏刘道斌治弘农，脩建学校，郡人追绘其像于孔子祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168110_comment'></div>唐杨玚为国子祭酒，其徒即而立颂，称载休德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168110_comment'></div>今或图公像于学，以厌群慕，不为无所则」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168110_comment'></div>乃疏其说于府，而遂图之，以时礼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168110_comment'></div>公气和志直，内外修明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168110_comment'></div>文章谨于法度，叙史体、述制命尤为深约典重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168110_comment'></div>临事通敏，虽众所难能，论致公前，立断可不可，已而皆宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168110_comment'></div>设于政治，依放物情，裁以教义，故所至令顺而民怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168110_comment'></div>乐推进人善，器其所存，不强其力所不逮，士无贤愚，一造门下，满意而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168110_comment'></div>议者以公材全而德盛，使且贵显，必霈然大施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168110_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168110_comment'></div>享年之薄，天下所以重为之哀悼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168110_comment'></div>况洛之士民，亲沐而薰者，于是举也宜矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168110_comment'></div>公讳绛，字希深，以宝元二年十一月终于邓州，春秋四十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168110_comment'></div>其年十二月二十五日，留守推官、朝奉郎、试大理评事蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1168110_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　蔡襄与杨叔武、安子正常聚寓所畅谈。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1039&endYear=1039')">1039年</a>　蔡襄作《送郭学士序》<div id='poem_1168049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送郭学士序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1039年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168049")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168049'>自某来河南，去家远甚，亲戚之好，无一在河南焉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168049_comment'></div>举河南日与之游者，又未尝有交言之旧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168049_comment'></div>居常反虑自明，岂隘乎哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168049_comment'></div>何其与己之少也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168049_comment'></div>盍求诸善容者以质乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168049_comment'></div>某得足下声名且久，今乃见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168049_comment'></div>足下服丧退居，而老官重德岁时使使谢问，交踵门下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168049_comment'></div>乘传东西者，止道问舍之所之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168049_comment'></div>暮夜必见郡之学者持文章以就衡尺，得轻重长短乃去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168049_comment'></div>虽纷纶过前，而区处等级高下，能尽得其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168049_comment'></div>惟莅官于郡县者以事咨焉，反自闭不知愈牢，终不开一言、别是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168049_comment'></div>隘者质焉，其亦有志于善容乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168049_comment'></div>且退居閒默，非有加人之势，而能使人欢欣悚慕之如是；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168049_comment'></div>使之乘加人之势，曷施而不济哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168049_comment'></div>于是行也，某既序之已，又系之以诗云：「以文自高，或病为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168049_comment'></div>以吏自嘉，或守一器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168049_comment'></div>君有文称，不鄙吏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168049_comment'></div>驱马在道，爰遵其辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168049_comment'></div>今天子明，唯知人易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168049_comment'></div>必得其位，而达其志」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1168049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1040&endYear=1040')">1040年</a>　蔡襄迁调入都，任秘书省著作佐郎，充馆阁校勘。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e760c2b6712e4d638b66c65fc82128ba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e760c2b6712e4d638b66c65fc82128ba");'><span id='e760c2b6712e4d638b66c65fc82128ba_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年</a>，25岁</div><div id='e760c2b6712e4d638b66c65fc82128ba' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1036&endYear=1036')">1036年12月</a>　蔡襄游浙江径山，作《游径山记》<div id='poem_1168106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168106?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游径山记</a><span class='authorDate'>（景祐三年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168106")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168106'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168106'>记径山之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168106_comment'></div>馀杭县之北鄙，直四十里，有径山在焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168106_comment'></div>山有佛祠，号曰承天祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168106_comment'></div>有碑籀述载，本初唐崔元翰之文，归登，书之石，今传于时云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168106_comment'></div>始至山之阳，东西之径二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168106_comment'></div>登自其西，壁绝襟绕，轿行百休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168106_comment'></div>松桧交错，盘折蒙翳，寻丈之间，独闻语声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168106_comment'></div>跻棱层，披翠茜，尽十里许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168106_comment'></div>下视来径，青虬蜿蜒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168106_comment'></div>抟岩腾霄，且及其巅，峡束洞隐，几不容并行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168106_comment'></div>已而内括一区，平盈坦壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168106_comment'></div>四面五峰，如掌竖指，一峰南绝，卓为巨擘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168106_comment'></div>屋盖高下，在掌中矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168106_comment'></div>庭间小井，或云故龙湫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168106_comment'></div>龙亡湫在，岁率尝一来，雷雨暝曀，而乡人祠焉者憧憧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168106_comment'></div>环山多杰木，丝杉翠柽，殆千千万万，若神官苍士，联幢植葆，骈邻倚徙，沈毅而有待者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168106_comment'></div>导流周舍，锵然璆然，若銮行佩趋而中节者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168106_comment'></div>由西峰之北数百步，矻然钜石，屏张笏立，上下左右可再十尺，划而三之，若「川」字，隶文曰「碣石岩」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168106_comment'></div>其传甚神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168106_comment'></div>并岩被谷，修竹茂密，尝以契刀刻竹两节间，成「景祐三年十二月十五日」字云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168106_comment'></div>由东径而往，坎窞为池，游鱼旷空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168106_comment'></div>其西径东折，蹴南峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168106_comment'></div>领脰之间，平地砥然，盈亩而半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168106_comment'></div>偃松一本，其高丈，其荫四之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168106_comment'></div>横柯上竦，如芝孤生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168106_comment'></div>松下石泓，激泉成沸，甘白可爱，即之煮茶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168106_comment'></div>凡茶出北苑，第品之无上者最难其水，而此宜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168106_comment'></div>偃松之南，一目千里，吴江之涛可挹，越岫之桂可攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168106_comment'></div>云驳霭褰，状类互出，若古图画，虫蠹断裂，无有边幅，而隐显之物，尚可名指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168106_comment'></div>群山属联，呈露冈脊，矫矫剪剪，咸自意气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168106_comment'></div>若小说百端，欲圣智之亢，而不知其下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168106_comment'></div>临观久之，魁博通幽之思生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168106_comment'></div>古人有言曰：「登高能赋，可为大夫」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168106_comment'></div>旨乎哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168106_comment'></div>予于斯见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168106_comment'></div>曷止大夫之为也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168106_comment'></div>大凡言之，天邻地绝，山回物静，在处神巧，举可人意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168106_comment'></div>虽穷冬阒寂，未睹夫春葩之荣、薰风之清、秋气之明，然取于予者犹在也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168106_comment'></div>既归无几何，而曩所历者重钩复结，无一见焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168106_comment'></div>追而言之，若觉而言梦，使人悄怆，而不知其自也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168106_comment'></div>同游者，建安黄瑊君度、岳阳朱师德宗哲，又君度之侄曰子常、子美、甥杜沂皆从游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168106_comment'></div>其前与谋而后以事已之者，朱宗哲之兄师道希圣、杜沂之父叔元君懿、揭阳卢几举之三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168106_comment'></div>莆阳蔡襄一与之善，惜乎不及俱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168106_comment'></div>书所经见往贻之，人一通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168106_comment'></div>尝刻竹两节间之十字，其游之年月日也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168106_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1168106'>「并」下原衍「傍」字，据宋本、《两浙金石志》删。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1168106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1168106'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_44_1168106_0'>⑴ 《蔡忠惠集》卷二五。又见《咸淳临安志》卷二五，万历《杭州府志》卷二四，《径山志》卷七，《名山胜概记》卷一六，《八代文钞》第三六册，《古今图书集成》职方典卷九五三、山川典卷一○八，雍正《浙江通志》卷一○，嘉庆《馀杭县志》卷八，《两浙金石志》卷五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1168106_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3ba7f27937bd4c798278622529144466_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ba7f27937bd4c798278622529144466");'><span id='3ba7f27937bd4c798278622529144466_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='3ba7f27937bd4c798278622529144466' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄到杭州，游西湖名胜古迹，作《经钱塘故宫》<div id='poem_249231' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249231' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249231?labeling=true' target='_blank'>经钱塘故宫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249231")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249231_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249231'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249231'>废苑芜城裹故宫，行人苑外问秋风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249231'>当时歌舞何年尽，此意古今无处穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249231'>往事萧条随败叶，客情迢递寄孤鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249231'>扁舟欲去更回首，寒树苍苍夕照东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249231_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249231'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249231_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄到杭州，游西湖名胜古迹，作《经林逋旧居二首》<div id='poem_249066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>经林逋旧居二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249066")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249066'>修竹无多宅一区，先生曾此隐西湖。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249066'>诗言不喜书封禅，亦有馀书补世无<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249066'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249066'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_249066_0'>⑴ 自注：逋诗云：茂陵异日求遗草，犹喜曾无封禅书。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249066_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_249065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249065?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249065'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249065'>山色凝岚水色清，山云长与水云平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249065'>先生来举持竿手，钓得人间亢俗名。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249065'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄到杭州，游西湖名胜古迹，作《离钱塘》<div id='poem_249090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249090?labeling=true' target='_blank'>离钱塘</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249090")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249090'>迎潮小舸满旗风，回首津亭暮霭中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249090'>惆怅今宵归去梦，迢迢直至海门东。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249090'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249090_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄经建德。作《至睦州》<div id='poem_249047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>至睦州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249047")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249047'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249047'>一带沧波两面山，扁舟中去几时还。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249047_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249047'>浮生多半在离别，此意明知未肯閒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249047_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249047'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249047_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='2c58194b5e364391a1185f74b08fb83e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年2月</a>　二月上旬，蔡襄抵杭州，因运河未解冻，不能航行，遂在杭逗留近两个月，受到杭州太守张方平殷勤招待，诗酒流连。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄作《自书诗帖·杭州临平精严寺西轩见芍药两枝追想吉祥院赏花慨然有感书呈才翁》寄苏才翁。作品：《书呈苏才翁》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄过杭州吉祥院，重访璘上人，作《杭州过璘上人花圃》<div id='poem_249063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_249063'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249063'>封培剪剥夺天工，栏下长年见万红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249063'>投老暗知心力少，自开还落信春风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249063_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249063'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年5月26日</a>　蔡襄到杭州任，作《杭州谢上表》<div id='poem_1167815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杭州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年5月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167815")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167815'>臣襄言：伏奉敕差知杭州军州事，已于五月二十六日到任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167815_comment'></div>国家委之大计，材非所宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167815_comment'></div>朝廷与其便藩，恩为至倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167815_comment'></div>俯循孤远之甚，已惊涯分之逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167815_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣儒学未优，天资尤拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167815_comment'></div>谓忠义可以立身，而一于事上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167815_comment'></div>谓强明可以为吏，而果于奉公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167815_comment'></div>于时益疏，以道自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167815_comment'></div>乃者偶承大农之乏，辄当会府之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167815_comment'></div>徒历岁年，蔑修官政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167815_comment'></div>伏蒙皇帝陛下大明垂照，洪覆均仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167815_comment'></div>察孤臣之尽心，知小人之兴谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167815_comment'></div>特推恩数之厚，俾就思养之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167815_comment'></div>已涓吉辰，祗临治所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167815_comment'></div>敢不询求民隐，阅鍊师钤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167815_comment'></div>人情莫不乐于便安，任之宽简；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167815_comment'></div>兵法所谓先于节制，示以庄严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167815_comment'></div>誓竭驽材，上酬鸿造。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1167815_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167815'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167815_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年5月26日</a>　蔡襄到杭州任，作《杭州谢两府启》<div id='poem_1167970' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167970' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167970?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杭州谢两府启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年5月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167970")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167970_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167970'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167970'>右，襄奉敕差知杭州军州事，已于今月二十六日赴任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167970_comment'></div>剡奏陈情，幸谐于俞命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167970_comment'></div>自中易外，获领于便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167970_comment'></div>切念襄学术迂疏，器能朴陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167970_comment'></div>早际重熙之旦，寖阶膴仕之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167970_comment'></div>徒知执节以致忠，不能应机而趋务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167970_comment'></div>岁月持久，宠光益蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167970_comment'></div>虽要职之屡更，顾微勤之靡效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167970_comment'></div>间以亲闱之养，恳辞计省之劳，旋改近班，俾分外镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167970_comment'></div>矧东南之奥壤，号繁剧之名都，遂其夙心，实亦优寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167970_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某人协和元化，俯徇物情，议论系乎重轻，任使均其劳逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167970_comment'></div>敢不益坚素守，勉布宽条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167970_comment'></div>上酬覆露之仁，次答陶镕之力。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167970_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年6月13日</a>　蔡襄跋《萧子云出师颂》<div id='poem_1168067' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168067' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168067?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋萧子云出师颂</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年六月十三日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168067")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168067_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168067'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168067'>章草法今世少传，此书尤精劲而完篇，殊可爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168067_comment'></div>借临一本，然眼力已昏，多亦失真，他日或移石本，可分遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168067_comment'></div>治平二年六月十三日，端明殿学士、知杭州军州事蔡襄题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1168067_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1168067'><span
