ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年7月14日</a>　蔡襄致书章岷，盼早日来杭会面。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《与程修撰帖》致程师孟，通问候。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年7月</a>　蔡襄作《判府相公问候启》致富弼。<div id='poem_1167982' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167982' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167982?labeling=true' target='_blank'>判府相公问候启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167982")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167982_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167982'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167982'>近以国家载烦旧德，专镇大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167982_comment'></div>阻窥上衮之严，莫簉翘材之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167982_comment'></div>明神荐佑，景福如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167982_comment'></div>伏以某官大方无倪，全德若隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167982_comment'></div>武公之政，宜在国人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167982_comment'></div>文子之勋，复刊盟府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167982_comment'></div>然且解魁衡之务，重屏翰之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167982_comment'></div>孟津三门，已结甘棠之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167982_comment'></div>《豳》诗《七月》，载歌零雨之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167982_comment'></div>庸副具瞻，大庇群品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167982_comment'></div>敢祝善为毗倚，精调寝兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167982_comment'></div>私所祷祈，坐劳恳悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167982_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167982_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《贺文相公枢密使启》，贺文彦博拜枢密使。<div id='poem_1167975' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167975' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167975?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺文相公枢使启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167975")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167975_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167975'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167975'>窃审拜恩宸阙，正位枢庭，伏惟欢庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167975_comment'></div>恭惟枢密相公望重本朝，声加殊俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167975_comment'></div>抱夔龙明允之业，会尧舜光华之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167975_comment'></div>忠言嘉谋，尽上前之启沃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167975_comment'></div>入辅出帅，系天下之安危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167975_comment'></div>四方于宣，二府更践。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167975_comment'></div>上方尊任旧德，图回太平，委大柄于机衡，运深筹于帷幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167975_comment'></div>虽本兵之地，载副于具瞻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167975_comment'></div>而当轴之司，伫还于大任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167975_comment'></div>襄耸闻成命，增抃鄙悰，恨守外藩，阻趋崇屏。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1167975'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167975_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《吕枢密启》，贺吕公弼拜枢密使。<div id='poem_1167978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕枢密启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167978")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167978'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167978'>伏审显膺中旨，荣贰内枢，伏惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167978_comment'></div>恭惟某官资以天高，美由世济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167978_comment'></div>亲观亨嘉之会，自祈睿圣之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167978_comment'></div>材用之全，所临必最；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167978_comment'></div>禁严之选，其历殆周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167978_comment'></div>由右蜀之召还，领中都之经费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167978_comment'></div>上心已简，师锡攸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167978_comment'></div>筹幄深严，已参于坐论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167978_comment'></div>国钧繁委，即应于具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167978_comment'></div>某限守藩方，阻趋宾屏，侧聆涣号，徒抃深衷。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167978_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄作《省主端明韩侍郎启》，贺韩绛拜三司使。<div id='poem_1167977' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167977' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167977?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省主端明韩侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167977")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167977_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167977'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167977'>伏审祗奉制书，总司计籍，伏惟庆慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167977_comment'></div>恭以某官至诚格物，奥学际天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167977_comment'></div>飞步书林，文采昭于群听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167977_comment'></div>正冠宪府，风声凛乎四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167977_comment'></div>厌从事物之劳，继得藩宣之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167977_comment'></div>化行右蜀，入尹上京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167977_comment'></div>理状亟闻，帝衷弥简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167977_comment'></div>领县官之经费，尚屈周才；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167977_comment'></div>代天工而燮调，伫谐佥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167977_comment'></div>襄属婴官守，阻簉宾除，抃蹈兹深，名言罔既。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167977_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄游西湖孤山，访释惠勤，作《七月过孤山勤上人院》<div id='poem_249018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249018?labeling=true' target='_blank'>七月过孤山勤上人院</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249018")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249018'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249018'>青林蔼蔼日晖晖，薄晚凉生暑气微。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249018'>湖上清风如可载，画船十只不空归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249018'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249018_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年7月</a>　七月下旬，蔡襄撰书《工部尚书集贤院学士赠刑部尚书谥曰襄余公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168196' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168196' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168196?labeling=true' target='_blank'>工部尚书集贤院学士赠刑部尚书谥曰襄余公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168196")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168196_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168196'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168196'>治平元年六月癸亥，工部尚书、集贤院学士、前知广州军州事余公薨于江宁府之行舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168196_comment'></div>以闻，天子为之不视垂拱朝一日，赗赙有加，赠刑部尚书，谥曰襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168196_comment'></div>其孤奉公，明年七月二十七日葬，以讣来，且求志其圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168196_comment'></div>某为次，哭之已，谨序之曰：余氏自闽徙于韶之曲江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168196_comment'></div>曾大父从，大父营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168196_comment'></div>父庆，累赠太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168196_comment'></div>母黄氏，追封吴郡太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168196_comment'></div>公讳靖，字安道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168196_comment'></div>天圣二年中进士第，尉虔州之赣县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168196_comment'></div>又中书判拔萃科，改将作监丞、知洪州新建县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168196_comment'></div>再迁秘书丞，入崇文馆，校三史谬误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168196_comment'></div>景祐三年，充集贤校理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168196_comment'></div>范文正公知开封府，屡言丞相过失，贬饶州，言事者畏缩不敢论列，公即上疏，曰：「古之帝王逐谏臣，终为盛德之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168196_comment'></div>仲淹宜在朝，不宜远谪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168196_comment'></div>坐是落职监筠州税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168196_comment'></div>尹公师鲁、欧阳公永叔继之，皆以朋党斥去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168196_comment'></div>某官微，不得自达，作诗四篇以直之，一日传于京师，故天下目为「四贤」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168196_comment'></div>移监泰州税，又徙知英州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168196_comment'></div>丁太夫人忧，还朝，复集贤校理、同判太常礼院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168196_comment'></div>庆历三年，上念西夏乱边，官军屡败，四方困于供亿，因增置谏官四员以补聪明，向之触丞相而得罪者颇引用，除公右正言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168196_comment'></div>于是朝廷之大议，政事之得失，权臣材德之是否，士大夫之贤不肖，莫不尽心而举正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168196_comment'></div>元昊为患日久，时议有金缯之赐，辄首罪称藩，将从其请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168196_comment'></div>而契丹聚兵燕朔，曰我为南朝皇帝讨夏人，勿宥其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168196_comment'></div>朝廷谓借契丹之兵以讨贼，则彼自矜功，拒元昊之请，绝其向顺之路，必也却契丹而纳元昊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168196_comment'></div>当得使者以成其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168196_comment'></div>公亦屡言二鄙利害，乃遣公使契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168196_comment'></div>既至，辨其曲直，以理夺之，比还，契丹收兵，元昊称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168196_comment'></div>四年，知制诰、史馆修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168196_comment'></div>其年再使，坐习虏语，出知吉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168196_comment'></div>数十年间，天下风俗以谨默自守、掩覆瑕垢为长者，一日刺举弹绳，多或罢免，又尝所言者进持国柄，仇人乘势中以事，授将作少监，分司南京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168196_comment'></div>久之，改光禄少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168196_comment'></div>天子且欲复用，权臣以诸卫将军、寿州钤辖、处州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168196_comment'></div>服父丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168196_comment'></div>侬智高陷邕州，循流东下，破九郡，次广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168196_comment'></div>以秘书监起公丧庐，知潭州金革之事，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168196_comment'></div>改知桂州，经制广南东西路贼盗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168196_comment'></div>广城坚，不下，贼大掠西归，所向无前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168196_comment'></div>趋邕州，欲倚峒穴为久居计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168196_comment'></div>公先移檄交趾及诸峒，使之捍贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168196_comment'></div>智高至，外无助援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168196_comment'></div>会朝廷命狄宣徽青将兵至，公与孙公元规实共其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168196_comment'></div>智高败走，复邕州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168196_comment'></div>乞解官，追终丧制，诏不允，除给事中，仍治旧府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168196_comment'></div>御史梁茜言赏不当功，又迁工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168196_comment'></div>选死士入特磨道，生擒智高母与弟送阙下戮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168196_comment'></div>充集贤院学士，寻迁户部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168196_comment'></div>自言久官岭外，瘴毒所侵，惟陛下哀怜，又移潭州、青州，迁吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168196_comment'></div>嘉祐五年，交趾入邕界，杀巡检五人，驿召公于青州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168196_comment'></div>上谕之曰：「卿熟南方事，已授卿广西体量安抚使，其勿辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168196_comment'></div>公至邕，召交趾用事者费嘉祐诘之曰：「汝主世为藩臣，何敢尔耶」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168196_comment'></div>边民私忿相酬，不知官军，误犯之，幸得自新，当送首恶者归命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168196_comment'></div>既而械致五人，莅刑于钦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168196_comment'></div>归奏所以治蛮之状，授尚书左丞、知广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168196_comment'></div>今天子即位，迁工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168196_comment'></div>广多奇货，南官者蓄以为利，公戒其北归勿得持南物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168196_comment'></div>其俗轻扬，教之礼法，简而不苛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168196_comment'></div>去之日，百姓怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168196_comment'></div>公薨，年六十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168196_comment'></div>娶林氏，赠尚书工部侍郎从周之女，封鲁郡夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168196_comment'></div>男三人：伯庄，殿中丞，早亡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168196_comment'></div>仲荀，太常博士；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168196_comment'></div>叔英，太常寺太祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168196_comment'></div>女六人：长适尚书屯田员外郎郭师愈，次秘书丞孙邵，次建州司法参军周熊，次秘书省校书郎章惇裕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1168196_comment'></div>二尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1168196_comment'></div>男孙四人：嗣恭、嗣昌，皆太常寺奉礼郎，嗣隆、嗣徽未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1168196_comment'></div>女孙五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1168196_comment'></div>文集二十卷，奏议五卷，《三史刊误》四十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1168196_comment'></div>公之在馆阁、居谏院，某尝同职事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1168196_comment'></div>其斥筠州、使北虏、经制二广贼盗、平定交趾、知广州，皆见其行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1168196_comment'></div>故其学术文章、忠义谋画，知之最深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1168196_comment'></div>居常谦畏寡言，不敢少忤于人，及论事上前，分解落落，诋刺大臣，易于褐夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1168196_comment'></div>出入兵戎危难之地，若在宴处，何其壮哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1168196_comment'></div>已之无闷，用之有为，斯其蹈夫道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1168196_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1168196'>公进于朝，卓尔辞艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1168196_comment'></div>任之谏诤，直言警世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1168196_comment'></div>西夏乱常，寇攘荐岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1168196_comment'></div>翻然向内，愿输信誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1168196_comment'></div>契丹横议，集兵幽蓟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1168196_comment'></div>单车出使，安危是系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1168196_comment'></div>胡骑引归，羌酋受制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1168196_comment'></div>风云指麾，天日清霁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1168196_comment'></div>峒獠猖狂，自西而东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1168196_comment'></div>起于丧庐，经制顽凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1168196_comment'></div>贼窜穷荒，生致其母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1168196_comment'></div>戮之马市，腰领殊处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1168196_comment'></div>交趾来扰，再往南土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1168196_comment'></div>呼其种豪，屈之一语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1168196_comment'></div>二广十年，恩威是宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1168196_comment'></div>公薨民啼，其何使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1168196_comment'></div>返于故□，□终斯全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1168196_comment'></div>我铭公墓，唯信之传<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1168196_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_91_1168196'>「权臣」句：按据《宋史》卷三二○《余靖传》：「授左神武军大将军、雅州刺史、寿州兵马钤辖，辞不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1168196_comment'></div>再迁卫尉卿、知虔州」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1168196_comment'></div>此处文字有脱误。</div><div id='poem_sentence_93_1168196_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1168196'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_90_1168196_0'>⑴ 《蔡忠惠集》卷三六。又见《莆阳文辑》卷四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1168196_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年8月</a>　蔡襄作《戒弄潮文》<div id='poem_1167869' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167869' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167869?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杭州戒弄潮文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167869")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167869_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167869'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167869'>斗牛之分，吴越之中，唯江涛之最雄，乘秋风而益怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167869_comment'></div>乃其俗习，于以观游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167869_comment'></div>厥有善泅之徒，竞作弄潮之戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167869_comment'></div>以父母所生之遗体，投鱼龙不测之深渊，自为矜誇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167869_comment'></div>时或沈溺，魂魄永沦于泉下，妻孥望哭于水滨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167869_comment'></div>生也有涯，盍终于天命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167869_comment'></div>死而不吊，重弃于人伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167869_comment'></div>推予不忍之心，伸尔无穷之戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167869_comment'></div>所有今年观潮，并依常例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167869_comment'></div>其军人百姓辄敢弄潮，必行科罚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167869_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年8月24日</a>　蔡襄作《持书帖》致葛宫，邀其得便来杭一游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年9月</a>　蔡襄登有美堂，并书《有美堂记》碑本。<div id='poem_1168119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杭州清暑堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年九月十八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168119")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168119'>京师东南千里入吴越，杭于吴为一都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168119_comment'></div>其地倾而属海，又多陂池，以故善湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168119_comment'></div>方春夏时，梅雨蒸郁，础甓皆汗，披纤衣，覆大厦，犹鼻息奄奄，不得旷快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168119_comment'></div>非有高明之居，曷以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168119_comment'></div>于是清暑之堂作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168119_comment'></div>清暑者，负州廨之左，直海门之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168119_comment'></div>其风远来，洒然薄人，日以决事，佚而忘劳，至者莫不悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168119_comment'></div>或曰：「昔者召伯将营召以居，重爱民力，暴处远野，庐于甘棠之下而听断焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168119_comment'></div>百姓思之，作《甘棠》之诗以美其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168119_comment'></div>今斯堂也，度面势，揭崇宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168119_comment'></div>前有江海浩荡无穷之胜，潮涛早暮以时上下，奔腾汹涌，蔽映日月，雷震鼓骇，方舆动摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168119_comment'></div>浮商大舶往来聚散乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168119_comment'></div>朝霞夕景，不缋而彩翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168119_comment'></div>旁走群山，滨山而湖，崖溓㳽漫，并包钜泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168119_comment'></div>岩岫崒峍，圾乎河汉之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168119_comment'></div>苍烟白云，少顷万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168119_comment'></div>茂林香草，冬荣不彫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168119_comment'></div>此所以娱君之视听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168119_comment'></div>及夫夏日，比室烦燠，方且披轩闼，据高凉，放荡于无何，翱翔于至极，萧然而自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168119_comment'></div>或宾从环次，鸣管揳瑟，酾酒均饵，歌呼瞑醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168119_comment'></div>此所以怿君之心意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168119_comment'></div>于民乎何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168119_comment'></div>岂不与昔人庐乎远野者异哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168119_comment'></div>余谓之曰：「惟人之情，不得其适则慌然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168119_comment'></div>余于是堂也，愈吾疾，亦于是休吾心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168119_comment'></div>体康志宁，然后究民之不至而教之，度民之所有而用之，去其所不愿，就其所便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168119_comment'></div>如得其平，于为惠也亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168119_comment'></div>乘其閒也，燕宾友，接和好，是亦为政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168119_comment'></div>且召伯之治，或失其平，虽木栖露寝，民莫之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168119_comment'></div>甘棠之政，后世仰而慕之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168119_comment'></div>甘棠之茇，不可常也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168119_comment'></div>遂以其说为《清暑堂记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168119_comment'></div>治平三年九月十八日，端明殿大学士、尚书礼部侍郎、知军州事蔡襄撰。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1168119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1168119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年11月5日</a>　蔡襄致书“大隐何君”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《贺冬至表》<div id='poem_1167816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺冬至表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167816")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167816'>臣襄言：伏以七日来复，上应天心之和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167816_comment'></div>一阳始生，密符君道之长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167816_comment'></div>迩遐所底，动植均休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167816_comment'></div>臣襄诚欢诚忭，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167816_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下惠迪先猷，灵承骏命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167816_comment'></div>斡璇玑而观象，顺玉烛以调元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167816_comment'></div>茂对庆辰，诞膺景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167816_comment'></div>臣限临藩屏，阻远阙庭，不获进厕朝班，忭舞文陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167816_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄向两府大臣韩琦寄《贺昭文相公启》<div id='poem_1168012' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168012_comment'></div>坐调元化之工，力助圣时之祜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168012_comment'></div>履兹令序，密拥繁禧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168012_comment'></div>襄限守侯藩，阻趋铃阁，云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168012_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄向两府大臣曾公亮寄《贺集贤相公冬启》<div id='poem_1168013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1168013'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168013'>伏以推日于天，起牛宿之一度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168013_comment'></div>验气以律，生《复》卦之七分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168013_comment'></div>践兹令辰，丛厥休祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168013_comment'></div>襄限居藩守，阻造铃斋，云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168013_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄向两府大臣欧阳修寄《贺欧阳侍郎冬启》<div id='poem_1168014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168014' class='poemTitle /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄向两府大臣陈旭寄《贺陈副枢冬启》<div id='poem_1168019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168019' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_6_1168019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《册皇太后称贺表》<div id='poem_1167821' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167821' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167821?labeling=true' target='_blank'>册皇太后称贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167821")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167821_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167821'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167821'>臣襄言：得进奏院状报，十一月十六日皇太后受宝册者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167821_comment'></div>竭天下之养，虽恭报于厚慈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167821_comment'></div>尽朝廷之仪，在极崇于徽号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167821_comment'></div>神祇协应，夷夏同欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167821_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣闻夏、商以前，六宫之制邈焉而无纪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167821_comment'></div>姬、刘以降，五翟之法粲然而备存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167821_comment'></div>姜嫄、太姒之流音，明德、和思之继盛，载华礼典，允属昌辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167821_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下纯被九乾，绍恢四圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167821_comment'></div>成社稷之大计，母道有光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167821_comment'></div>酬天地之至仁，阴灵克顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167821_comment'></div>爰归功于慈训，遂推美于琼章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167821_comment'></div>家国庆安，孝恭交至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167821_comment'></div>臣忝尘法从，恪守藩封，无任瞻望抃蹈、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167821_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《册皇后称贺表》<div id='poem_1167822' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167822' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167822?labeling=true' target='_blank'>册皇后称贺表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167822")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167822_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167822'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167822'>臣襄言：得进奏院状报，十一月十六日皇后受册者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167822_comment'></div>俪尊皇极，宅正位于天闺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167822_comment'></div>配德紫宸，膺鸿名于宝册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167822_comment'></div>海内臣妾，抃蹈以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167822_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>臣闻文命造邦，涂山所以宣内助；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167822_comment'></div>重华嗣帝，皇英所以辅圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167822_comment'></div>宗庙歆其荐羞，穹壤因而垂祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167822_comment'></div>载光懿范，永属熙朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167822_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下缵服睿图，席休宝绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167822_comment'></div>两仪均大，含生荷亭育之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167822_comment'></div>二曜齐高，品物仰照临之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167822_comment'></div>是以淑誉流于区域，阴教序于宫闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167822_comment'></div>用赞王猷，必崇位号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167822_comment'></div>加丽袆衣之贵，增光彤管之华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167822_comment'></div>臣忝寄藩方，限遥天陛，无任瞻望欣跃、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1167822_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《贺赦表》<div id='poem_1167818' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167818' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167818?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赦表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167818")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167818_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167818'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167818'>臣襄言：今月二十三日马递到赦书一道，以南郊礼毕，大赦天下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167818_comment'></div>臣当时集本州官吏及僧道军民等宣布，并行下管属十县讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167818_comment'></div>圜丘致飨，讲修对越之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167818_comment'></div>大宥推仁，覃霈汪洋之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167818_comment'></div>含生至众，仰抃同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167818_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以因吉土曰郊，称大事者祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167818_comment'></div>粤自虞夏，迄于汉唐，有质有文，或沿或革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167818_comment'></div>诸儒参议，致谓六天而异名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167818_comment'></div>历代所行，止以三年而定礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167818_comment'></div>必于至者，取物成之大备；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167818_comment'></div>就乎阳者，法天道之资生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167818_comment'></div>然而千官备仪，百灵走职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167818_comment'></div>发挥往制，必属于昌辰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167818_comment'></div>宪法后王，允归于元圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167818_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下顺考古道，丕阐大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167818_comment'></div>怀翼翼之心，昭事上帝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167818_comment'></div>秉烝烝之孝，祗见祖宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167818_comment'></div>宿于清净之宫，致此精明之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167818_comment'></div>人神降格，海宇欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167818_comment'></div>回六玉之珍虬，御双云之华阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167818_comment'></div>与民更始，大覃雷雨之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167818_comment'></div>置国无穷，永享华夷之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167818_comment'></div>臣亲逢盛际，向忝近司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167818_comment'></div>方领寄于藩垣，但骛精于宸极。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1167818_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167818'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷七。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167818_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《谢加勋表》<div id='poem_1167819' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167819' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167819?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢加勋表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167819")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167819_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167819'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167819'>臣襄言：今月二十六日，进奏院递到敕牒各一道，以南郊礼毕，加臣护军、食邑五百户者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167819_comment'></div>大飨举修，方毕肇禋之礼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167819_comment'></div>徽章稠沓，均加在位之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167819_comment'></div>俯偻承荣，震惶知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167819_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢，）</span>伏念臣器质甚浅，学术非优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167819_comment'></div>徒遘休辰，遂跻清贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167819_comment'></div>内历禁林之邃，外专方面之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167819_comment'></div>非矫矫以出人，但渠渠而饬己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167819_comment'></div>当尧舜之在上，何以为功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167819_comment'></div>使龚黄之复生，仅能自守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167819_comment'></div>况臣衰拙，安在拟伦！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167819_comment'></div>护侍慈亲，幸叨便郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167819_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下讲明大典，备锡庆私，念持橐之旧臣，进宠勋之异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167819_comment'></div>虽葵藿之心尽吐，仰对大明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167819_comment'></div>然《蓼萧》之泽溥覃，岂遗一物！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167819_comment'></div>誓捐顶踵，以答乾坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167819_comment'></div>臣伏限守任在远，不获奔诣阙庭，臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1167819_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167819'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二一。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167819_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄进《谢赐历日表》<div id='poem_1167820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐历日表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167820")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167820'>臣襄言：今月二十六日，进奏院递到诏书一道，赐臣治平三年历日一道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167820_comment'></div>圣言温润，荣甚衮褒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167820_comment'></div>舜历昭明，宠于图瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167820_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>窃以惟王建国，颁朔治民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167820_comment'></div>奉时先一岁之端，藏庙谨诸侯之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167820_comment'></div>治古所载，熙朝益恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167820_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下勤念人时，允符乾造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167820_comment'></div>坐明堂而听政，命太史以谨元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167820_comment'></div>特重王春，首颁岁律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167820_comment'></div>度量寒暑，蓍龟咎祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167820_comment'></div>致阴阳之不愆，宜疾疠之毋作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167820_comment'></div>臣远分藩寄，祗奉诏恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167820_comment'></div>拜舞于庭，虽窃九天之赐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167820_comment'></div>卷舒在手，获知四序之迁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1167820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄撰书《司农少卿致仕王君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168197' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168197' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168197?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司农少卿致仕王君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年十一月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168197")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168197_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168197'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168197'>达夫讳益恭，姓王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168197_comment'></div>其先居太原，徙潞州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168197_comment'></div>曾祖讳崇，赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168197_comment'></div>曾祖妣周氏，齐国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168197_comment'></div>祖讳景纯，赠太师、中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168197_comment'></div>祖妣祁氏，鲁国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168197_comment'></div>父讳曙，枢密使、吏部侍郎、同中书门下平章事，赠太师、中书令兼尚书令、魏国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168197_comment'></div>妣石氏，追封永嘉郡太君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168197_comment'></div>寇氏，华原郡太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168197_comment'></div>自魏公始家河南，今为河南人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168197_comment'></div>君于大中祥符间以荫补右侍禁，天禧三年奏换卫尉寺丞，自卫尉六迁为尚书司封员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168197_comment'></div>康定二年，以司门致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168197_comment'></div>皇祐三年，大飨明堂，除库部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168197_comment'></div>以大祀恩，用子升朝，例叙封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168197_comment'></div>改水部，又改仓部、考功二郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168197_comment'></div>嘉祐八年，上即位，授司农少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168197_comment'></div>治平二年三月十二日，终于西省思顺里第，年七十四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168197_comment'></div>以其年十一月二十八日葬河南县魏封原先公之域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168197_comment'></div>娶李氏，封金城县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168197_comment'></div>子二人：谨言，尚书驾部郎中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168197_comment'></div>谨行，殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168197_comment'></div>女三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168197_comment'></div>君所历官：监昭应宫、法从库、开封府襄邑县税、西京面院、磨勘司，签书河南、河阳府节度判官公事，最后知河南县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168197_comment'></div>凡九任，行三十年，清修无过，必称其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168197_comment'></div>尝慕唐王龟之为人，务远权利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168197_comment'></div>魏公之治雍、孟、襄、汝也，皆去官侍养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168197_comment'></div>逮参知政事，于洛阳治新第成，君致书于魏公，陈老聃止足之戒，愿引年谢政，还居于家，辅药石，导和气，以延寿命，言词恳恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168197_comment'></div>公以诗答之曰：「疏家子叹挥金后，御寇妻悲遗粟回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168197_comment'></div>争似吾儿知止足，陶庐容膝早归来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168197_comment'></div>公以朝廷恩数，倚任之大，至于将相，终□□薨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168197_comment'></div>服除，君授河南，自伸夙志，遂还官事，日与高隐者游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168197_comment'></div>晚年喜释氏，笃好《华严经》，日翻一帙，深通体用止观之趣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168197_comment'></div>家所藏书，虽子弟求阅，必手自检授，出入甚谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168197_comment'></div>而于田产资利，随所厚薄，视亲疏急难赈济之，不复会校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168197_comment'></div>洛下多名园，时与其弟觞咏终日，陶然自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168197_comment'></div>居閒，古书真画，间或展阅，其外纷纶过前，不吾接也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168197_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168197_comment'></div>当少时，父为大官，乘势可进，辄以书规切，冀其引罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168197_comment'></div>仕及中年，后有显位可指而待，辄弃爵禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168197_comment'></div>人情莫不好荣观而厌卑处，君岂异于人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168197_comment'></div>顾其中所存者胜所为，故能安于所尚，非天机淡泊、动与道合者，恶能至是邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168197_comment'></div>某与君昆仲游最久，于葬之先，君之弟两浙转运使、尚书刑部郎中、集贤校理益柔状君之行，以铭见托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168197_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1168197'>大道之行，人隐于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168197_comment'></div>其德纯明，不居物先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168197_comment'></div>薄夫怀贪，生死利势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168197_comment'></div>扳跻勇前，罔或畏耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168197_comment'></div>嗟嗟夫君，中年退休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168197_comment'></div>超离造化，萧散林丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168197_comment'></div>高尚之节，可监于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168197_comment'></div>声名且远，于君何有！</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1168197_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年12月</a>　蔡襄撰书《尚书员外郎郭公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168198' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168198' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168198?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书屯田员外郎郭公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年十二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168198")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168198_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168198'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168198'>郭君讳之美，字君锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168198_comment'></div>世居庐陵，自其考始以文词举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168198_comment'></div>君锡少聪敏加人，从其父学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168198_comment'></div>景祐元年，年十八，与其父同日登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168198_comment'></div>仁宗皇帝临轩，赏其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1168198", 1168198, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>爽异</span>，为改今名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168198_comment'></div>初调蕲州蕲春，再授楚州淮阴，皆为主簿，以吏事不中法去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168198_comment'></div>庆历三年，为梧州司户参军□□□□年复注惠州，转运使闻其名，用之权韶州□□□□州有铸钱监，监卒怨其监官，是时侬智高叛，辄请于监军韦贵曰：「愿往邕州擒峒贼」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168198_comment'></div>贵叱去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168198_comment'></div>君策其必变，曰：「叱之所以激之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168198_comment'></div>阴为州备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168198_comment'></div>其夕，监卒杀监官，趋州门，斩关且进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168198_comment'></div>门有备兵，出其不意，格斗诛斩略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168198_comment'></div>侬智高入广州，肆兵外掠，又移权知南海、番禺二县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168198_comment'></div>募敢勇亡命之徒，遇贼必战，杀获甚多，所至贼为之缩敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168198_comment'></div>蒋偕被命专讨，军无法律，遣使召君计事，辞不往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168198_comment'></div>后数日，偕为贼擒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168198_comment'></div>皇祐五年，以功除大理寺丞、签书南雄州判官公事，以父丧不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168198_comment'></div>又丁母忧，服除，以大理丞知兖州莱芜监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168198_comment'></div>嘉祐五年，迁丞殿中，监在京丰济仓，赐绯鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168198_comment'></div>天子即位，恩迁太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168198_comment'></div>初作永昭陵，河南府素号穷空，所费仰给三司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168198_comment'></div>时余为三司使，荐君于永安，入中钱粮，善计纤悉，终以办事，时议称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168198_comment'></div>改尚书屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168198_comment'></div>治平元年，知开封府中牟县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168198_comment'></div>县居京西一舍，仍岁水灾，多盗贼，赋敛频数，民益贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168198_comment'></div>君视其部中沟洫不治，因上书乞治水，严盗禁，均赋役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168198_comment'></div>期月之间，使客称其毕给，百姓颂其均平而不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168198_comment'></div>未几，以命免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168198_comment'></div>仍坐举故人之为长吏者入官，长吏有罪，追君一官，罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168198_comment'></div>百姓条君善状诉于京尹，愿留，不得，即遮丞相马首，叩头嘘唏，幸少赐我，既又不得，泣涕而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168198_comment'></div>明年，归蕲州，未至，终于舒州桐城之传舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168198_comment'></div>其孥以丧归，十二月二十一日葬于蕲水龙潭山先人之茔，享年三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168198_comment'></div>曾祖讳谏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168198_comment'></div>祖玠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168198_comment'></div>考讳佺□□□□事推官，累赠太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168198_comment'></div>妣施氏，封安福县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168198_comment'></div>□□□娶程氏，再娶王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168198_comment'></div>男曰大时、大明，为进士，大昕、大□与三女皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168198_comment'></div>君好学，多通理势重轻之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168198_comment'></div>每官必有记述，皆世之要用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168198_comment'></div>有文数十百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168198_comment'></div>尤善论兵，数上书，言慷慨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168198_comment'></div>病且革，叹曰：「丈夫固当以病死耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168198_comment'></div>君之弟之翰以书自蕲至杭告余曰：「兄辱知于公，今失官而死，且葬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168198_comment'></div>公其哀悯其孤，而铭其圹，以慰存殁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168198_comment'></div>余为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1168198'>事而不试，惠而不施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168198_comment'></div>古人有言，世莫我知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168198_comment'></div>进焉而踬，寿上于斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168198_comment'></div>匪世之疾，又将咎谁？</div><div id='poem_sentence_48_1168198_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为韩缜饯别于山堂，作《韩玉汝山堂会别梅花已盛至苏州示谕水乡天寒未开》<div id='poem_249122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249122'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249122'>遥知画舫舣江隈，寒勒梅花未得开。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249122'>唯有山堂红烛下，至今繁艳傍尊罍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249122_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249122'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回秦州知府钱端明启》<div id='poem_1167976' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167976' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167976?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回秦州知府钱端明启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167976")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167976_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167976'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167976'>涖官东州，无日暇给；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167976_comment'></div>引领西屏，若天阻遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167976_comment'></div>勤企宴游，积深悰悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167976_comment'></div>久稽寒暑之问，惧黩高明之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167976_comment'></div>忽辱眷私，远烦礼讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167976_comment'></div>窃惟节制方面，奠安藩维，神明拥全，戬谷来相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167976_comment'></div>伏惟某官识通圣奥，德重坤元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167976_comment'></div>行业几于古人，经艺纯于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167976_comment'></div>光映朝列，简在宸衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167976_comment'></div>延登书殿之崇，总统麟符之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167976_comment'></div>敢冀副上之眷，御生以和，兹用感藏，岂胜谈悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1167976_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回瀛洲知府待制启》<div id='poem_1167981' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167981' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167981?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回知瀛州知府待制启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167981")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167981_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167981'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167981'>言念窃便藩之寄，越在天隅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167981_comment'></div>瞻帅阃之严，恍如霄极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167981_comment'></div>惟神交之留念，烦手记以相先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167981_comment'></div>宛然成章，永以为好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167981_comment'></div>伏以某人以道自镇，与时会亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167981_comment'></div>进更台阁之游，积有朝廷之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167981_comment'></div>维北之分，边防且严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167981_comment'></div>重天之威，兵制尽在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167981_comment'></div>况直云章之秘，方司武律之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167981_comment'></div>并授权纲，用清氛祲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167981_comment'></div>行促追锋之召，入持造物之钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167981_comment'></div>冀保兴居，庸符公望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167981_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167981_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回庆州经略观文孙侍郎启》<div id='poem_1167983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回庆州经略观文孙侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167983")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167983'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167983'>伏审就膺诏书，移奠侯服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167983_comment'></div>夙叨奖顾，不无欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167983_comment'></div>恭惟某官推诚在民，以道结主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167983_comment'></div>出处耸当世之耳目，议论系本朝之纪纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167983_comment'></div>故日月之光，得以明其义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167983_comment'></div>雷霆之下，不能移其忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167983_comment'></div>上以天下之雄，时惟关中之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167983_comment'></div>维周之翰，申伯偃藩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167983_comment'></div>自陕以西，召公作帅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167983_comment'></div>然考来今之制，此为元宰之基，纳愿兼常，治书见贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167983_comment'></div>意非词尽，感与抃俱。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1167983_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回卢龙图启》<div id='poem_1167989' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167989' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167989?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回卢龙图启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167989")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167989_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167989'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167989'>伏审得请宸廷，专制方面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167989_comment'></div>号称东海之表，仍宠驷车之荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167989_comment'></div>上眷素隆，欢颂交庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167989_comment'></div>伏以某官以道结主，推心及民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167989_comment'></div>议论系本朝之纪纲，出处耸士人之观听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167989_comment'></div>暂解经筵之务，遽分藩屏之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167989_comment'></div>齐鲁连疆，报政不须于期月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167989_comment'></div>勋华当宁，经邦即赖于谟明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167989_comment'></div>会承驿置之来，首枉笺修之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167989_comment'></div>兹用感服，岂胜究宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167989_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1167989'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1167989_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回定州傅密学启》<div id='poem_1167990' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167990' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167990?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回定州傅密学启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167990'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167990'>伏自进直斗枢，领符朔屏，谋帅之重，注意益隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167990_comment'></div>惟幕府之初开，保灵襟而加谧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167990_comment'></div>伏惟某官抱器闳远，逢辰靖嘉，内外展勤，文武惟宪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167990_comment'></div>中山屏翰，北道襟喉，常宿劲兵，号称<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1167990", 1167990, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>要壤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167990_comment'></div>聊护诸将，式遏一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167990_comment'></div>矧邻好之缔修，属戍防之罢警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167990_comment'></div>行膺迅召，别迟登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167990_comment'></div>猥荷眷私，远烦音讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167990_comment'></div>曲敦夙契，倍切感铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167990_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《回洪州施刑部启》<div id='poem_1167991' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167991' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167991?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回洪州施刑部启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167991")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167991_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_sentence_1_1167991_comment'></div>奉亲舆而至部，幸慰慈颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167991_comment'></div>承候置之远贻，辱珍縢之见贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167991_comment'></div>此盖某官之方繇器望，适统藩垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167991_comment'></div>早者奉朝，实托雅游之厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167991_comment'></div>今兹忝寄，又通邻道之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167991_comment'></div>尚阻披承，倍深感系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167991_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1167991_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄为来函问候之僚友作《建州运使曹郎中启》<div id='poem_1167997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167997?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建州运使曹郎中启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167997")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167997'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167997'>曩涖计廷，实托雅游之厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167997_comment'></div>洎分郡寄，复通邻道之欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167997_comment'></div>猥辱眷私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167997_comment'></div>远勤礼讯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167997_comment'></div>詹言清晤，弥切中藏。<div id='poem_content_1168038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168038'>比膺俞旨，出领便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168038_comment'></div>属总事之云劳，愧驰书之未逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168038_comment'></div>敢惟勤谊，特枉诲封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168038_comment'></div>讲好甚勤，玩词增感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168038_comment'></div>矧长才之济务，方美任以逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168038_comment'></div>宜航大和，前对光宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168038_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1168038_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_3_1167817_comment'></div>异俗来威，百昌荐贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167817_comment'></div>臣守郡于外，不获进庆阙庭，臣无任瞻天祝圣、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168007_comment'></div>上灵所佑，景贶如归，襄限守侯藩，阻趋材馆。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1168007_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_1_1167824_comment'></div>当赫隆于盛暑，俾明慎于常经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167824_comment'></div>正宁推恩，普天同抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167824_comment'></div>臣襄诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167824_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下文明御宇，法则在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167824_comment'></div>亲揽万几，休有一德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167824_comment'></div>化鸿钧而被物，道皇极以爱民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167824_comment'></div>画象衣冠，思循于往制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167824_comment'></div>省罪囹圄，曲畅于至慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167824_comment'></div>特布训辞，用清科禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167824_comment'></div>臣叨临藩服，绝远朝廷，臣无任瞻天荷恩、激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_content_1168119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168119'>京师东南千里入吴越，杭于吴为一都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168119_comment'></div>其地倾而属海，又多陂池，以故善湿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168119_comment'></div>方春夏时，梅雨蒸郁，础甓皆汗，披纤衣，覆大厦，犹鼻息奄奄，不得旷快。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168119_comment'></div>非有高明之居，曷以御之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168119_comment'></div>于是清暑之堂作焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168119_comment'></div>清暑者，负州廨之左，直海门之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168119_comment'></div>其风远来，洒然薄人，日以决事，佚而忘劳，至者莫不悦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168119_comment'></div>或曰：「昔者召伯将营召以居，重爱民力，暴处远野，庐于甘棠之下而听断焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168119_comment'></div>百姓思之，作《甘棠》之诗以美其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168119_comment'></div>今斯堂也，度面势，揭崇宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168119_comment'></div>前有江海浩荡无穷之胜，潮涛早暮以时上下，奔腾汹涌，蔽映日月，雷震鼓骇，方舆动摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168119_comment'></div>浮商大舶往来聚散乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168119_comment'></div>朝霞夕景，不缋而彩翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168119_comment'></div>旁走群山，滨山而湖，崖溓㳽漫，并包钜泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168119_comment'></div>岩岫崒峍，圾乎河汉之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168119_comment'></div>苍烟白云，少顷万变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168119_comment'></div>茂林香草，冬荣不彫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168119_comment'></div>此所以娱君之视听也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168119_comment'></div>及夫夏日，比室烦燠，方且披轩闼，据高凉，放荡于无何，翱翔于至极，萧然而自适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168119_comment'></div>或宾从环次，鸣管揳瑟，酾酒均饵，歌呼瞑醉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168119_comment'></div>此所以怿君之心意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168119_comment'></div>于民乎何有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168119_comment'></div>岂不与昔人庐乎远野者异哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168119_comment'></div>余谓之曰：「惟人之情，不得其适则慌然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168119_comment'></div>余于是堂也，愈吾疾，亦于是休吾心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168119_comment'></div>体康志宁，然后究民之不至而教之，度民之所有而用之，去其所不愿，就其所便安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168119_comment'></div>如得其平，于为惠也亦大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168119_comment'></div>乘其閒也，燕宾友，接和好，是亦为政也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168119_comment'></div>且召伯之治，或失其平，虽木栖露寝，民莫之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168119_comment'></div>甘棠之政，后世仰而慕之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168119_comment'></div>甘棠之茇，不可常也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168119_comment'></div>遂以其说为《清暑堂记》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168119_comment'></div>治平三年九月十八日，端明殿大学士、尚书礼部侍郎、知军州事蔡襄撰。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1168119'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1168119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年</a>　蔡襄作《尚书礼部侍郎郑君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书礼部侍郎郑君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168199")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168199_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168199'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168199'>郑君讳纾，字武仲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168199_comment'></div>先世居秦，曾祖讳保雍，始居安陆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168199_comment'></div>客有寓钱数百万而死，他日得其子，还之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168199_comment'></div>客子莫知所由，辞不受，遂施之浮屠氏，于是湖湘之人称其长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168199_comment'></div>祖讳屿，东头供奉官，尝总兵秦陇间，以数十骑入乘虏鄣，虏畏其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168199_comment'></div>考建中，举进士，积学而多材能，悉产以济人急难，故与游者多名人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168199_comment'></div>君承数世累义之美，资性明敏，所习过人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168199_comment'></div>初应明经，以为不足以自立，曰：「吾岂诵数者」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168199_comment'></div>又举进士，天圣八年登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168199_comment'></div>主安州之应城簿、越州司法参军，改大理寺丞，迁殿中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168199_comment'></div>历知婺之兰溪、越之馀姚，徙知益之新都，贫不能行，监楚之北神税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168199_comment'></div>湖南安抚使王丝荐君为签书桂阳监判官厅公事，权潭之长沙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168199_comment'></div>其县喜讼难治，君视其繁，为简其术，如无一事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168199_comment'></div>刘丞相号为明果，时知□□□□所为，大喜称叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168199_comment'></div>转运使时其事丛，临县观□□□□状非其要不问，问即自服，虽得罪者亦喜跃而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168199_comment'></div>郴州宜章民持伪券夺人之田，屡狱不直，委君决之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168199_comment'></div>君揽案曰：「义章以太宗旧名而更之，市田之岁在义章，其券乃今宜章印也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168199_comment'></div>狱遂决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168199_comment'></div>三迁为尚书都官员外郎、审刑院详议官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168199_comment'></div>峒蛮侬智高寇邕州，诏龙图阁直学士孙公沔往经制之，辟君与行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168199_comment'></div>从招讨使狄青破智高于邕州界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168199_comment'></div>是夜，军辄惊扰，孙公谓君曰：「行者数人，多以事避去，今独君在此，真义士也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168199_comment'></div>以劳授职方，权大理少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168199_comment'></div>君通《春秋》，及为法官，多引律傅经，酌理参谳，有可矜者，必为之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168199_comment'></div>殿直曹且监主自盗，应死，君曰：「其父英尝战殁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168199_comment'></div>仁宗闻之恻然，为减一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168199_comment'></div>仁宗恕宽哀矜，令天下大辟有疑或情可悯者，得以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168199_comment'></div>四方体朝廷好生之意，率以情法迁就，求为末减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168199_comment'></div>君曰：「法正情直，州郡当自决之，今乃诿上，以茍侥倖，类是者请致之法」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168199_comment'></div>于是朝廷著令以班天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168199_comment'></div>迁祠部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168199_comment'></div>嘉祐元年五月甲子卒于官，寿五十有六，累赠尚书礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168199_comment'></div>喜读书，记其大旨，以资职业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168199_comment'></div>比为审刑、大理，以中道论法，不为守文吏，故所济活甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168199_comment'></div>为诗有精思，入唐人风格，清峭可尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168199_comment'></div>尤善章奏书牍，诸公或请之，皆了其意，而文彩蔚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168199_comment'></div>祖妣傅氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168199_comment'></div>妣杨氏，天水县太君；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168199_comment'></div>刘氏，河间县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168199_comment'></div>娶李氏，汝南县太君，驾部郎中文蔚之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168199_comment'></div>今夫人鲍氏，乐安郡太君，其父□职方郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168199_comment'></div>男五人：狝，著作佐郎、知潭州攸县；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168199_comment'></div>獬，右司谏、知制诰、知荆南府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168199_comment'></div>猗，将作监主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168199_comment'></div>猛未□□□□士张蒙山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168199_comment'></div>以治平三年月日，葬于安州安陵县某乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168199_comment'></div>余与君为同年进士，少尝仕官往来，数相遇于淮浙间，每见饮酒，笑谑不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168199_comment'></div>皇祐中，司谏以文中科为天下第一，余尝庆君曰：「子为状元，而其父固可知已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168199_comment'></div>用是为适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168199_comment'></div>今援毫襞纸，遂铭君圹，遽至于是乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168199_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1168199'>材力之次，要必有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168199_comment'></div>文词之敏，炜烨敷荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168199_comment'></div>傅经裁谳，区处和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168199_comment'></div>世资以义，用永厥声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168199_comment'></div>屯于其躬，来者其亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168199_comment'></div>坎中之纪，后世之评。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1168199_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年10月</a>　蔡襄母卢太夫人病逝，致书欧阳修请撰《墓志铭》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='11f92be0ef92461c80ff6f9bf06f9bf6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("11f92be0ef92461c80ff6f9bf06f9bf6");'><span id='11f92be0ef92461c80ff6f9bf06f9bf6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='11f92be0ef92461c80ff6f9bf06f9bf6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年5月</a>　蔡襄至瓜州渡江，为风潮所阻，留宿扬州津馆，适次子旬周岁，作《宿扬州》、《广陵》、《马奴周晬思之因成》三首寄怀。<div id='poem_249094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿扬州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249094")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249094'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249094'>瓜洲堰埭阻行桡，更等江头后信潮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249094'>独背残灯数归路，风传寒柝夜迢迢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249094_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249094'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249094_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249159' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249159' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249159?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249159")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249159_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249159'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249159'>广陵归客叹飞蓬，怀古伤离向此中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249159'>前世翻波那复问，十年弹指已成空。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249159'>楼头画角催残日，城上寒鸦噪晚风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249159'>井径萧条人不见，又随潮信度江东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249159_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249159'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249159_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_249311' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249311' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249311?labeling=true' target='_blank'>马奴周晬思之因成</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249311")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249311_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249311'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249311'>马奴今日方周晬，昨夜迢遥梦到家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249311'>盘里应知心所爱，尊前唯祝寿无涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249311'>咿嚘弄语群儿学，踉跄初行乳母誇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249311'>独上扬州津馆望，江山摇落去鸿斜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249311_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249311'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249311_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　蔡襄渡江别杜殿丞，作《江头别杜殿丞》<div id='poem_249183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江头别杜殿丞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249183")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249183'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249183'>扬子江头南北路，木兰船上往来人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249183_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249183'>年华衮衮东流水，世事劳劳薄宦身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249183_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249183'>回首天涯成远别，忘怀物外自相亲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249183_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249183'>津亭共起忧时叹，重记津亭泪满巾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249183_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249183'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249183_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3d09c7207a12464fb9901cd4be9a3262_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3d09c7207a12464fb9901cd4be9a3262");'><span id='3d09c7207a12464fb9901cd4be9a3262_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='3d09c7207a12464fb9901cd4be9a3262' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　蔡襄游金山寺。作品：《题金山寺》<div id='poem_249138' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249138' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249138?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题金山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249138")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249138_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249138'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249138'>画梁诗板暗流尘，水石鱼龙万句新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249138'>谁识高僧最深意，慈航长护过江人<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《蔡忠惠集》卷四）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249138_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249138'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249138_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d4072a7b5d234907a6b1f596c604b26f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d4072a7b5d234907a6b1f596c604b26f");'><span id='d4072a7b5d234907a6b1f596c604b26f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='d4072a7b5d234907a6b1f596c604b26f' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄至镇江，会同年刘奕。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>刘奕忽病遽，蔡襄在床前接受托孤，作《祭刘屯田文》<div id='poem_1168215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭刘屯田文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168215")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168215'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168215'>襄谨以清酌庶羞之奠，致祭于亡友蒙伯屯田二兄之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168215_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168215_comment'></div>天地之大，其如传邮乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168215_comment'></div>人寓其间，若行旅之奔趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168215_comment'></div>相值而喜，相失而吁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168215_comment'></div>何数十年之游从，而不见于须臾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168215_comment'></div>我自闽来，子官江涘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168215_comment'></div>扁舟迓我，境上百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168215_comment'></div>我有宿疾，携医就治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168215_comment'></div>意有缓急，实为依倚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168215_comment'></div>我卧客舍，幸子来临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168215_comment'></div>笑言譬喻，调护之经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168215_comment'></div>间隔一朝，闻子被疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168215_comment'></div>曾不及旬，遂兹奄忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168215_comment'></div>奉书词之委曲，将永诀于幽明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168215_comment'></div>以爱子而见托，岂薄夫之可承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168215_comment'></div>哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168215_comment'></div>材可以通事变，而不施于政；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168215_comment'></div>智可以裁几𦕈，而不任于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168215_comment'></div>岂宰造之无意，抑志念之相违？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168215_comment'></div>前造子庭，宾主之仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168215_comment'></div>今也入门，阖棺繐帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168215_comment'></div>义虽朋友，爱均兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168215_comment'></div>哭奠一觞，词以达志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168215_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1168215_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9114cdfb82c6427fa0b785dcdfe2a122_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9114cdfb82c6427fa0b785dcdfe2a122");'><span id='9114cdfb82c6427fa0b785dcdfe2a122_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='9114cdfb82c6427fa0b785dcdfe2a122' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年4月</a>　四月末，蔡襄至京口，重游金山寺，作《游金山寺》<div id='poem_249270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249270?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游金山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249270")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249270'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249270'>平日压尘土，今游兴味长。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249270'>波涛围四际，台殿起中央。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249270'>鱼听晨餐鼓，云和夕炷香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249270'>薰风休递吹，襟袂不胜凉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249270'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249270_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

苏州

id='poem_sentence_12_249371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249371'>今而赐告归，计课免雠讨。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249371_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168121'>苏州吴江之滨，有亭曰如归者，隘坏不可居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168121_comment'></div>康定元年冬十月，知县事秘书丞张先治而大之，以称其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168121_comment'></div>既成，记工作之始以示于后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1168121_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ed717a293c1c47babf61784f1b0f2204_label'><a
