ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='ed717a293c1c47babf61784f1b0f2204' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄抵苏州，到苏舜钦灵前祭奠。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='24e05db15af4466ca531b240ba4a4341_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("24e05db15af4466ca531b240ba4a4341");'><span id='24e05db15af4466ca531b240ba4a4341_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，44岁</div><div id='24e05db15af4466ca531b240ba4a4341' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年8月</a>　八月中旬，蔡襄抵苏州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄过真慧上人院，作《过真慧上人院见红薇盛开因思西阁后轩数株遂成短章寄翰林原叔八丈禹玉阁长兼书真慧壁间以记所遇》诗寄王洙、王珪，并书院壁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄寄吴菱回赠杜衍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　蔡襄为葛氏夫人治病。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　蔡襄作《杭州新作双门记》<div id='poem_1168115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杭州新作双门记</a><span class='authorDate'>（至和二年九月二十日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168115")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168115'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168115'>杭州，二浙为大州，提支郡数十，而道通四方，海外诸国，物货丛居，行商往来，俗用不一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168115_comment'></div>自钱氏专有吴越，治兵蓄财，日为战守，政出临时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168115_comment'></div>朝廷除刺史以来，盖八十年，其风流治迹，有足称者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168115_comment'></div>要之起废弊、变繇习，斯亦难已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168115_comment'></div>至和元年，资政殿学士、给事中孙公自枢密副使来抚是邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168115_comment'></div>六月署事，曰：「此吾故乡也，敢易治之」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168115_comment'></div>廛里之税，岁糜中产馀二十家，为之籍其地而出其资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168115_comment'></div>市贾谩欺，取与不均，为之正量衡而一之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168115_comment'></div>富黠倚强，蚀贫诛利，为之索其党而逐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168115_comment'></div>盗侠闭藏，出没无常，为之根株而去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168115_comment'></div>俗尚浮屠，归施无节，严以约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168115_comment'></div>妇人女子，洁廉其行，宠以衣珥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168115_comment'></div>高年旧德，或复诹访。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168115_comment'></div>数月之间，所部远近，莫不竦动，迎向公训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168115_comment'></div>公知众之已悦也，随所譬论，勉之于善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168115_comment'></div>秋八月，语其僚曰：「诸侯台门以高为贵，盖以尊天子所命而示等威也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168115_comment'></div>昔钱氏于山阜为治所，而双门置县木、锢金铁，用为敌备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168115_comment'></div>今方内统平，吾为守臣，于以遵化而流泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168115_comment'></div>每大号令，从官属，陈兵校，会州之士民，即门首张次班列而布宣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168115_comment'></div>门圮而地狭，又非礼制，岂所以重方面之体乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168115_comment'></div>吾将易而新之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168115_comment'></div>即以其说谋之转运使，资以羡钱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168115_comment'></div>又询之于民，良家大姓愿以力助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168115_comment'></div>于是商其用而裁取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168115_comment'></div>凡金埴竹木之材，必可其直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168115_comment'></div>塈陶盖梓之功，必当其佣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168115_comment'></div>十一月甲戌兴作，明年五月讫工，十有五日壬申，合乐燕饮以落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168115_comment'></div>至于下邑旁郡，携扶老稚，阗溢郛郭，相与观听，指是巍然者曰：「上之命令由是而出，下之情伪由是而入，一有不诚，重为门羞，吾属戒焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168115_comment'></div>是年，襄出刺清源，州人遮余而言曰：「我公之为治，固有闻于执事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168115_comment'></div>始者革弊屏恶，人畏其明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168115_comment'></div>已而拊养鳏茕，教敕子弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168115_comment'></div>及其治成，井市童儿，不收落钱，田丰海熟，人得其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168115_comment'></div>公作双门，我实与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168115_comment'></div>公归有时，我思无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168115_comment'></div>愿为纪所作之始而刻之石，庶几传之子孙，益远不忘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168115_comment'></div>初，公定邕广大寇还，请莅杭，上以其能让而不伐，中道召升宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168115_comment'></div>未几，以直议不能与众合，遂伸前请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168115_comment'></div>至则励精，夙夜决事，不以宴息自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168115_comment'></div>其忠义进退之节与所施为，若千里之绩，固不足书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168115_comment'></div>然州人过余再三，称颂勤勤，不书无以慰其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168115_comment'></div>九月二十日，枢密直学士、起居舍人、新授知泉州军州事莆阳蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1168115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　蔡襄观赏颜真卿《告身帖》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年9月</a>　蔡襄访吉祥院老僧璘上人。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b3fd4e718271452489c1e8a6fb62100f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b3fd4e718271452489c1e8a6fb62100f");'><span id='b3fd4e718271452489c1e8a6fb62100f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>，50岁</div><div id='b3fd4e718271452489c1e8a6fb62100f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄行至苏州，作《与伯镇书》致章珉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ac694a87df51402591177ba378ba49d2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ac694a87df51402591177ba378ba49d2");'><span id='ac694a87df51402591177ba378ba49d2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='ac694a87df51402591177ba378ba49d2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年5月6日</a>　蔡襄至吴县，参观范仲淹故居，并题跋书画作品。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
延平
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7a384e4f8a0347f59e368b1eeb863d33_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7a384e4f8a0347f59e368b1eeb863d33");'><span id='7a384e4f8a0347f59e368b1eeb863d33_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='7a384e4f8a0347f59e368b1eeb863d33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>　蔡襄至南平，乘舟沿闽江顺流南下。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
福州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4aff90c1164040438df7ff4e048170ba_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4aff90c1164040438df7ff4e048170ba");'><span id='4aff90c1164040438df7ff4e048170ba_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年</a>，30岁</div><div id='4aff90c1164040438df7ff4e048170ba' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1041&endYear=1041')">1041年1月</a>　蔡襄抵福州，太守沈邈招待品丹荔，游乌山，遂为“幽幽亭”题榜，并书《福州修庙学记》<div id='poem_1168113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168113?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州修庙学记<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1041年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168113")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168113_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168113'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168113'>七闽滨海，其地险而壮，福州之治尤据其胜势，为东南一都会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168113_comment'></div>其风俗尊向儒术，唐之文盛，间有重人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168113_comment'></div>薰渍劘揉，日以滋众，然庠校之兴，前无著者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168113_comment'></div>自五代钱吴越王专制瓯冶，分子弟以莅之，乃作新宫，号为使学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168113_comment'></div>本朝太平兴国中，转运使杨公克让始立孔子庙，以奠春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168113_comment'></div>景祐四年，通判谢君居微权职郡治，遂表建州学，仍请赐田五顷，以久众处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168113_comment'></div>诏书报下，谢适罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168113_comment'></div>逮范公亢、许公宗寿更守此邦，参择曹掾之能者蔡黄中、方峤继任其事，商工度材，历五载而大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168113_comment'></div>公帑之泉，计费千万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168113_comment'></div>植宇之楹，总数六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168113_comment'></div>中设孔子与其徒高第者十人像，又绘六十子及先儒以业传于世者，皆傅之壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168113_comment'></div>曰九经阁，以藏旧所赐书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168113_comment'></div>曰三礼堂，以图舆服之制、祭享之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168113_comment'></div>黉舍斋庐，旁翼两序；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168113_comment'></div>庖次井饮，百用资给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168113_comment'></div>今尚书都官员外郎沈公之来，入而拜，出而叹曰：「学成，空不居，无以育贤才而起风化」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168113_comment'></div>乃与监郡太常博士陈君议增美田，充所赐数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168113_comment'></div>迎延旧儒，敷解经术，又立比业准程，群居约束，揭为众则，以侯官尉吴及兼总之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168113_comment'></div>于是远近学者靡然从慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168113_comment'></div>初，公至，精究疾毙，绳治强豪，人用震栗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168113_comment'></div>既而譬晓士民，教之六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168113_comment'></div>以是知公摧凶蘖而培善本，威惠并施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168113_comment'></div>有所归赖，更口腾道，厉戒幼小，无或失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168113_comment'></div>咸愿刻文于石，垂延久后，遂相与来请襄为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168113_comment'></div>已又作诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1168113'>于戏生民，角翼者群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168113_comment'></div>上圣有作，财治人文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168113_comment'></div>执道之中，立世之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168113_comment'></div>厥后迷谬，乖离本始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168113_comment'></div>躬服儒方，偶媲言词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168113_comment'></div>专用干禄，乃文之疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168113_comment'></div>入齿王官，习之法令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168113_comment'></div>不失有罪，乃政之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168113_comment'></div>然于当时，咸著能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168113_comment'></div>使二者失，由学弗明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168113_comment'></div>学斯谓何，忠义悌孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168113_comment'></div>政斯谓何，礼让风教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168113_comment'></div>譬如大鼎，量入千钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168113_comment'></div>龠石百数，罔不兼容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168113_comment'></div>在学于政，先其大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168113_comment'></div>言词法令，进治之假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168113_comment'></div>唯州有学，邦君实谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168113_comment'></div>驱汝闽民，来处来游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168113_comment'></div>象图严严，记书整整。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168113_comment'></div>衣冠肃雍，室庐閟静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168113_comment'></div>孰为人父，敕戒而子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168113_comment'></div>往焉问闻，弗往攸耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168113_comment'></div>孰为人师，启率其徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168113_comment'></div>开陈统要，罢诎巧诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168113_comment'></div>学后废兴，属于继承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168113_comment'></div>益完勿圮，惟贤者能。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1168113'></div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1168113_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8a25dd38730f4dc7995092f247582727_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a25dd38730f4dc7995092f247582727");'><span id='8a25dd38730f4dc7995092f247582727_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>，33岁</div><div id='8a25dd38730f4dc7995092f247582727' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　蔡襄返京途经福州，受太守王逵殷勤招待。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d6383dc8c9e843db9fc3edffcfd0b2da_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d6383dc8c9e843db9fc3edffcfd0b2da");'><span id='d6383dc8c9e843db9fc3edffcfd0b2da_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>，34岁</div><div id='d6383dc8c9e843db9fc3edffcfd0b2da' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年春</a>　蔡襄迎奉双亲，赴福州莅任。作《晚上碧蜂亭》诗抒怀。作品：《晚上碧峰亭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（66。）</span><div id='poem_249261' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249261' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249261?labeling=true' target='_blank'>晚上碧峰亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249261")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249261_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249261'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249261'>城头近晚忽开晴，有色皆鲜是物清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249261'>地势四来州午向，山围一罅水东行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249261'>乘风歌吹无时已，面日楼台触处明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249261'>不比儿曹誇衣锦，自缘恩与养亲荣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249261'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249261_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　蔡襄致书尹洙吊其兄尹源之卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年夏</a>　蔡襄作《海隅贴》致韩琦，殷勤问候。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年6月</a>　蔡襄作《兴化军曹殿丞寄荔支》诗，谢兴化军知军曹观寄赠乡荔。<div id='poem_249180' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249180' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249180?labeling=true' target='_blank'>兴化军曹殿丞寄<span class='inlineComment2'>（原缺，据蔡本补）</span>荔支</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249180")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249180_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249180'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249180'>厚叶先枝新绛囊，使君分寄驿人忙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249180'>彩毫封处曾留意，筠笼开时不见香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249180'>风色甚豪应少损，路程差近得分尝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249180'>闽州纵有千千树，未抵家园气味长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249180'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249180_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　苏舜元任福建监丞，蔡襄常与其切磋书法，过从密切。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b83bae260b2444dea1f5eb51b8385ce9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b83bae260b2444dea1f5eb51b8385ce9");'><span id='b83bae260b2444dea1f5eb51b8385ce9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1047')">1045-1047年</a>，34-36岁</div><div id='b83bae260b2444dea1f5eb51b8385ce9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　蔡襄书欧阳修所撰之《太子太师致仕赠司空兼侍中文惠陈公神道碑》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年12月29日</a>　蔡襄作大楷唐人绝句四首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年1月</a>　正月上元佳节间，蔡襄在福州号召郡民大摆灯会，后因陈烈以诗讽谏，遂为之罢。<br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_sentence_3_249259'>主恩未报头生白，羞见龙泉百鍊钢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249259_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年7月</a>　蔡襄偕邵去华、苏才翁、郭世济游鼓山灵源洞，作题名记及书“忘归石”擘窠字于崖石，并作《游鼓山灵源洞》。另有“国师岩”、“苔泉”等题刻，亦传为蔡襄书。<div id='poem_249410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>游鼓山灵源洞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249410")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249410'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249410'>郡楼瞻东方，岚光莹人目。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249410'>乘舟逐早潮，十里登南麓。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249410'>云深翳前路，树暗迷幽谷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249410'>朝鸡乱木鱼，晏日明金屋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249410'>灵泉注石窦，清吹出篁竹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249410'>飞毫划峭壁，势力勿惊触<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：题名石壁。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249410'>扪萝跻上峰，大空延眺瞩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249410'>孤青浮海山，长白挂天瀑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249410'>况逢肥遁人，性尚自幽独。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249410'>西景复向城，淹留未云足。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249410_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249410'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_249410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　蔡襄送故人柯庆文子归泉州应进士选拔考试，作《送柯秘书三子归泉应诏》<div id='poem_249388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送柯秘书三子归泉应诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249388")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249388'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249388'>秘书昔共官临漳，时呼三子侍侧傍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249388'>修瞳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_249388", 249388, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>阔颡</span>善应对，举措不类群儿行。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249388'>遥知成就在他日，尔时迄今十载强。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249388'>闽州太守无伎术，乞持符竹还故乡。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249388'>近观诏书下郡国，选访行实登俊良。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249388'>嶷然三子复过我，衣裾飘洒凝秋霜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249388'>各携编轴几百幅，互以理要充词章。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249388'>久之潜思叩幽眇，角牙腾触声礌硠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249388'>言归温陵入场屋，争奋笔舌论短长。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249388'>海鹰上云出瓜翼，天马历地无羁缰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249388'>秘书多才晚未遇，有如此子传义方。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249388'>吾徒沉升不须议，且看少者腾声光。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249388_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249388'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_249388_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年8月</a>　蔡襄为曹修睦作《尚书司封员外郎曹公墓志铭》》<div id='poem_1168182' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168182' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168182?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书司封员外郎曹公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168182")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168182_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168182'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168182'>公讳脩睦，字某，建安郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168182_comment'></div>为学通博，性介廉，喜自脩立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168182_comment'></div>大中祥符五年登进士第，调抚州军事推官、南雄州判官，改大理寺丞、知邵武军之邵武县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168182_comment'></div>迁殿中丞、知郁林州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168182_comment'></div>闻母太夫人疾，委州印于其佐，北走归道，未至，被丧，哀瘠过礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168182_comment'></div>服除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168182_comment'></div>以太常博士通判越州，再迁尚书屯田、都官二员外，通判泉州，知邵武军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168182_comment'></div>民有兄弟讼田者，公为陈兄兄弟弟之义，民弃让不争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168182_comment'></div>代还，前丞相杜公时为御史中丞，荐公材能，拜御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168182_comment'></div>踰年，改司封，出知寿州，又移泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168182_comment'></div>濒海有渠道迎潮波，溉浸旁田数十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168182_comment'></div>自渠水湮塞，田芜租逋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168182_comment'></div>公与疏渠，流人还业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168182_comment'></div>寻坐举者，夺司封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168182_comment'></div>去官岁馀，通判信州，知吉州，公皆不行，泰然有归止意，上书愿休官政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168182_comment'></div>以都官员外郎分司南京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168182_comment'></div>既而叹曰：「不事事而受禄，不可谓廉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168182_comment'></div>复申前自列于上，乃得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168182_comment'></div>久之，丞相章公言公退静可敦薄者，诏还所夺官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168182_comment'></div>居数年，声闻益达，朝廷以紫衣金鱼就第褒之，用悚动天下士大夫视听，以重进为高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168182_comment'></div>庆历六年春疾作，次所为文词四百馀篇，勒分三卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168182_comment'></div>疾益渍，戒其子薄葬，若世所向浮屠法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168182_comment'></div>输钱击钟，与计七日而去，斋者皆不得用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168182_comment'></div>二月乙卯终于家，年六十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168182_comment'></div>八月庚申，葬建安县万石村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168182_comment'></div>公之曾王父讳某，王父讳某，皆潜德延休，貤于后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168182_comment'></div>皇考讳某，累赠谏议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168182_comment'></div>皇妣某氏，赠某县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168182_comment'></div>公之配朱氏，封长安县君，治家有法，卒寿州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168182_comment'></div>男觌，建安主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168182_comment'></div>女四人：长适南剑州顺昌令丘与龄，次适进士丘规，次适太庙室长陈沂，次适常州司理参军何辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168182_comment'></div>男孙二人：曰颛，太庙斋郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168182_comment'></div>曰某，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168182_comment'></div>公兄二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168182_comment'></div>长讳某，举进士，早亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168182_comment'></div>次赠谏议大夫讳某，与公未仕时，同名右乡国，号为二曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168182_comment'></div>及谏议居朝，刚直好言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168182_comment'></div>明道中，以刑部员外郎为御史知杂事，论请复辟，触章宪明肃太后怒，左迁兴化军，终贬所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168182_comment'></div>其后天子追悼前忠，特以谏议大夫表之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168182_comment'></div>公年五十有四，即引身退，第舍园池，疏列泉石，置册书棋琴于其中，意之所适，则娱味终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168182_comment'></div>宾亲过从，或道时事，辄谢曰：「吾方与纸上圣贤语，差乐，勿溷吾听」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168182_comment'></div>以是兄弟皆有终誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168182_comment'></div>公之在官，不以法令绳驭下吏，刻己率之，而吏益畏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168182_comment'></div>不以威刑詟惮下民，平心治之，而民益信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168182_comment'></div>呜呼，终始之节，可谓善矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168182_comment'></div>将葬，其孤觌哭泣以书来乞铭，铭可辞乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168182_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1168182'>重势荣利，众所趋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168182_comment'></div>耄昏茍前，世所愉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168182_comment'></div>中年能休，矫妄愚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168182_comment'></div>惟公之存，励夸浮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168182_comment'></div>西人之法，志古无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168182_comment'></div>今民涵濡，费产输也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168182_comment'></div>遗戒勿用，遵礼儒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168182_comment'></div>惟公之没，祛怪诬也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1168182_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年秋</a>　蔡襄在州学饯送发解进士，与同僚拈韵赋诗，作《州学饯送发解进士》<div id='poem_249342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>州学饯送解发进士<span class='inlineComment2'>（坐中分得意字）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249342")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249342'>朝家岁取天下士，官守小大悉分治。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249342'>育材论荐苟失宜，德业英豪苦难致。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249342'>予尝备员内供奉，作书参议科场事。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249342'>乡举察廉未易复，责其节行在长吏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249342'>策之当世之大务，适时可以观周智。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249342'>问之六经之归趣，知言可以见精意。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249342'>众贤一划天子可，开设学校朔南被。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249342'>世儒苟欲便有司，诏令初传寻已置。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249342'>今年郡国选多士，糊名仍旧搜瑕颣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249342'>常忧玑贝随手遗，往往中夜起不寐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249342'>拆封辨号指姓名，十九冥合州人议。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249342'>耽耽黉舍秋景长，芳殽旨酒邀宾醉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249342'>惜哉今乐与古异，遣士礼数不能备。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249342'>霜天寥寥万象清，健风开送群飞翅。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249342'>大明帝居一气傍，春日照耀桐槐翠。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249342'>勉思奇策当天心，厚禄荣名时所贵。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249342'>时之所贵亦外物，君子存诚思远至。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249342'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_249342_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　秋冬之间，蔡襄作《寄题滁州丰乐亭》寄赠欧阳修。<div id='poem_249399' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249399' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249399?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题滁州丰乐亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249399")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249399_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249399'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249399'>君为滁上守，乘间务幽寻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249399'>群从留山阿，美望穷前林。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249399'>良宴追佳赏，高亭旷遐临。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249399'>烟云无定姿，水石唯清音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249399'>静见鱼鸟适，遥闻鸡犬深。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249399'>时节屡丰有，民里无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_249399", 249399, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>欺侵</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249399'>岂独延众物，因兹托冲襟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249399'>大笔每绝唱，芳樽宁孤斟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249399'>别日念已长，来期讵能今。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249399'>安得凌风翰，相从殚岁阴。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249399_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249399'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_249399_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年冬</a>　蔡襄在郡圃接待李觏，由陈烈作陪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年12月</a>　蔡襄为改变福州地区左医右巫之俗，作《太平圣惠方后序》书碑立石。<div id='poem_1168054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>圣惠方后序<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年十二月八日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168054")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168054'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168054'>生者天地之德，成者圣人之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168054_comment'></div>运化流物，随之不遗，生之之理至矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168054_comment'></div>推本兴治，安而有伦，成之之道著矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168054_comment'></div>是故作天下之美利者，其圣人之事乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168054_comment'></div>传称神农味百草，黄帝录《内经》，以除民疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168054_comment'></div>其术能死者生而夭者寿，以言乎功，虽大禹之疏洚水、驱龙蛇，汤武之用金革、戡祸乱，特救患于一时，孰与无穷之赖乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168054_comment'></div>故曰，作天下之美利者，皆圣人之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168054_comment'></div>宋当天命，出九州之人于火鼎之中，吹之濯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168054_comment'></div>太宗皇帝平一宇内，极所覆之广，又时其气息而大苏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168054_comment'></div>乃设官赏金缯之科，购集古今名方与药石诊视之法，国医诠次，类分百卷，号曰《太平圣惠方》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168054_comment'></div>诏颁州郡，传于吏民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168054_comment'></div>然州郡承之，大率严管钥、谨曝凉而已，吏民莫得与其利焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168054_comment'></div>闽俗左医右巫，疾家依巫索祟，而过医之门十才二三，故医之传益少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168054_comment'></div>余治州之明年，议录旧所赐书以示于众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168054_comment'></div>郡人何希彭者，通方伎之学，凡《圣惠方》有异域瑰怪难致之物，及食金石草木得不死之篇，一皆置之，酌其便于民用者得方六千九十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168054_comment'></div>希彭谨慎自守，为乡闾所信，因取其本誊载于版，列牙门之左右，所以导圣主无穷之泽沦究于下，又晓人以依巫之谬，使之归经常之道，亦刺史之要职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168054_comment'></div>庆历六年十二月八日，右正言、直史馆、知军州事蔡襄序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1168054_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　蔡襄延聘才学之士周希孟等在福州讲学，并亲至学舍听讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年春</a>　入春，蔡襄染病在郡斋休息调理，作《病中偶书二首》<div id='poem_249252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>病中偶书二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249252")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249252'>已感节候变，物态舒阳春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249252'>那复壮年意，如今多病身。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249252'>净室焚香久，烘炉煮药频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249252'>神欢百虑解，销尽眼前尘。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249251' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249251?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年春）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249251_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249251'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249251'>前看箫管辈，未免作埃尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249251'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249251_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年3月</a>　蔡襄罢知福州，改授福建路转运使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　蔡襄与新任太守交接毕，共同在碧峰亭宴请宾僚，蔡襄作《碧峰亭》<div id='poem_249423' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249423' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249423?labeling=true' target='_blank'>碧峰亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249423")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249423_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249423'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249423'>虚亭城西隅，开槛俯临北。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249423'>青山正相向，万状呈峭格。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249423'>落日涵紫翠，深春变颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249423'>云石抱幽致，猿鸟自娱适。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249423'>歌吹有杯酌，笔研角文墨。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249423_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249423'>从知闽州图，复记新名迹<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《蔡忠惠集》卷一）</span>。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年4月</a>　蔡襄移居转运司厩舍，作《移居转运宇别小栏花木》<div id='poem_249404' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249404' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249404")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249404_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249404'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249404'>三年对小栏，花蘤见颜色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249404'>红薇开已久，春风长先得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249404'>素馨出南海，万里来商舶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249404'>团团末利丛，繁香暑中拆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249404'>馀畦十数种，亦自尚风格。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249404'>念尔幽芳性，乞致多手植。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249404'>瑶草固微生，栽培子岂德。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249404_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　秋，蔡襄自闽北返福州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年9月</a>　九月初，蔡襄因病在告，梦游洛中，作《梦游洛中十首》<div id='poem_249112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_249111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249111?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span
