自注：赵韩王宅有藏酒百千器，范太尉宅花最多。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249107_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_249106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249106?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249106'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249106'>名花百种结春芳，天与秾华更与香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249106'>每忆月陂堤下路，便开图画觅姚黄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249106'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249106'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_249106_0'>⑴ 自注：月陂张家牡丹百多馀种，姚家黄为第一。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249106_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_249105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249105?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249105'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249105'>草白霜晴鹘眼开，原头游骑四边来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249105'>枯丛鸦鹊休惊噪，日暮分持走兔回<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249105'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249105'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_249105_0'>⑴ 自注：曾权洛阳县，屡陪诸君出猎。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249105_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_249104' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249104' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249104?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其九 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249104_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249104'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249104'>履道园池竹万竿，竹间池际笋斑斓。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249104'>当时酒所誇文战，今日谁登上将坛<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249104'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249104_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249104'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_249104_0'>⑴ 自注：普明寺乃白乐天履道第，水竹最佳，数为文字饮。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249104_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_249103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249103?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年9月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249103'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249103'>白马寺前冠盖盛，送行宾友尽英豪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249103'>耿丞血染边场草，留得声名日月高<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249103'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249103_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_249103'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_249103_0'>⑴ 自注：罢官时交游送饯白马寺，耿大监丞今死西事。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_249103_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　蔡襄梦忆与苏舜元会别之情景，作《昼寝宴坐轩忆与苏才翁会别》<div id='poem_249237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>昼寝宴坐轩忆与苏才翁会别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249237")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249237'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249237'>投凉下马卧僧家，绕簟清风卷绛纱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249237'>修竹满前微雨过，远山无际薄云遮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249237'>武侯旧隐人应到<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：京西提点刑狱厅宇在邓州。）</span>，闽粤孤城日自斜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249237'>解与尘心消百事，更开新焙煮灵芽。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249237'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　蔡襄发箧览亡友尹洙旧札，作《发箧得亡友书札》<div id='poem_249327' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249327' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249327?labeling=true' target='_blank'>发箧得亡友书札</a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249327")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249327'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249327'>宿昔重交义，零落今谁存。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249327'>旧情留纸札，永恨入丘坟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249327'>世味薄于水，生涯空似云。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249327'>抚孤无力及，流泪复何言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249327'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249327_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1047&endYear=1047')">1047年</a>　蔡襄作《尚书都官员外郎致仕叶府君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168183' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168183' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168183?labeling=true' target='_blank'>尚书都官员外郎致仕叶府君墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历六年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1047年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168183")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168183_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168183'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168183'>叶氏之先居丹阳，在唐、梁之际，有官于泉州者，属兵戈起，因留官下，子孙遂为今兴化军仙游人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168183_comment'></div>时方否鬲，连世晦遁，不克进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168183_comment'></div>府君讳宾，字虞卿，生当天下文治，乃始业词学，应进士贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168183_comment'></div>景德二年中第，注潮州海阳主簿，再调连州桂阳令、广州节度推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168183_comment'></div>商人陈从吉鬻铜钱，捕系，吏治急，自诬己铸，铸，法应弃市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168183_comment'></div>府君领案状，不署，曰：「是物非巧工不能为，从吉商也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168183_comment'></div>且铸必有范镕具，今无，请更核」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168183_comment'></div>果得真盗铸者，从吉坐买卖，得不死，一府称服，繇是有能名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168183_comment'></div>寻补建州节度掌书记，以保任材廉，改太子中允，累迁太常丞、博士、尚书屯田、都官二曹员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168183_comment'></div>历知泉州永春、南安、邛之临邛三县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168183_comment'></div>永春民有先恶嫌者，冒重辟，府君曰：「吾仇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168183_comment'></div>狱虽真，人亦乘以訾我」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168183_comment'></div>裁附轻比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168183_comment'></div>南安盗截牛舌，其主以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168183_comment'></div>府君阳为叱去，阴令屠之，即有告其自杀牛者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168183_comment'></div>府君谓告者曰：「截牛舌盗，汝也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168183_comment'></div>讯之，伏其罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168183_comment'></div>代归，除通判南剑州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168183_comment'></div>剑当闽冲，水行持贩茶盐禁物上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168183_comment'></div>山出铜银，冶场凡三十馀所，聚四方游黠，轻剽劫，击杀党与，牵连事日下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168183_comment'></div>吏惧滞系被罪，率不暇精覈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168183_comment'></div>府君专意诘决，民得尽其情，而狱无留焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168183_comment'></div>还朝，以年七十致官事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168183_comment'></div>家居九年，庆历五年正月九日终，寿七十九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168183_comment'></div>明年七月四日葬归德乡长安里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168183_comment'></div>王父讳擅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168183_comment'></div>皇考讳素，能以儒书训子，致遂大其门，累赠太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168183_comment'></div>皇妣陈氏，追封颍川县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168183_comment'></div>夫人陈氏，河南县君，厚淑恭谨，动有妇则，前府君卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168183_comment'></div>男二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168183_comment'></div>曰任，泉州司户参军，所临职，既去，人辄思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168183_comment'></div>曰传，登进士第，终泉州晋江尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168183_comment'></div>女五人，适郭尹、黄佐、郭日休、郭宪，皆进士，其季之婿泉州节度推官方慎德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168183_comment'></div>府君为政，能察民善伪与吏情隐，茍有蔽谩必立见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168183_comment'></div>然正其事则已，不深嫉而穷治之，故所至，吏民惮其明而不怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168183_comment'></div>躬自俭约，计奉以衣食，历官久，无锱铢过累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168183_comment'></div>既老閒居，课诸孙就学，时行田垄视农事，载酒肴，与旁邻阡巷耆旧往来，道说前事以为乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168183_comment'></div>晚年资用饶，叹曰：「吾其为利乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168183_comment'></div>于是籍亲戚富贫亲疏者，第而散之，人益知府君官有馀财而约不以资也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168183_comment'></div>葬之明年，司户君以书，并次其先君世族功治、卒葬月日，因其子婿漳州龙溪尉许稹以来乞铭于太史氏蔡襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168183_comment'></div>襄既以先达辈行视府君，又与其子游，遂为之序，且铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1168183'>叶先丹阳，官迁于闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168183_comment'></div>窒久而通，翰飞以振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168183_comment'></div>初盘邑治，爰佐南海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168183_comment'></div>直民冤死，声问弥大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168183_comment'></div>于泉之治，决断大明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168183_comment'></div>一语得盗，脱仇附轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168183_comment'></div>剑交衢途，猥集剽游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168183_comment'></div>事丛狱夥，乃恤乃孚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168183_comment'></div>还官卧家，协比里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168183_comment'></div>宴处遨游，岁月之逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168183_comment'></div>老而中礼，仕禄之仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168183_comment'></div>俭则克终，德厚之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168183_comment'></div>年岂不多，兹实其归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168183_comment'></div>载行于词，永世之诒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_53_1168183_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='484a631381264d70aa348e4f1a57b318_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("484a631381264d70aa348e4f1a57b318");'><span id='484a631381264d70aa348e4f1a57b318_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>，37岁</div><div id='484a631381264d70aa348e4f1a57b318' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄上《乞减放漳泉州兴化军人户身丁米札子》<div id='poem_1167850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞减放漳泉州兴化军人户身丁米劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167850")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167850'>臣伏见泉州、漳州、兴化军人户，每年输纳身丁米七斗五升，年二十至六十免放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167850_comment'></div>臣体问伪命日前诸州各有丁钱，惟漳、泉等州折变作米五斗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167850_comment'></div>至陈洪进纳疆土之后，以官斗校量，得七斗五升，每年送纳价钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167850_comment'></div>伏缘南方地狭人贫，终年佣作，仅能了得身丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167850_comment'></div>其间不能输纳者，父子流移，逃避他所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167850_comment'></div>又有甚者，往往生子不举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167850_comment'></div>人情至此，可为嗟痛！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167850_comment'></div>伏惟祖宗恢复天下，大去无名之敛，然诸州身丁，尚犹输纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167850_comment'></div>真宗皇帝哀怜百姓困穷之弊，祥符中特降御札，蠲除两浙、福建六路身丁钱四十五万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167850_comment'></div>其时漳、泉、兴三州亦是丁钱折变作米，无人论奏，因依科纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167850_comment'></div>遂至先朝大惠不及三郡，三郡之人引领北望，迄今又四十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167850_comment'></div>臣闻圣人以生为德，以孝为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167850_comment'></div>今陛下之民，至有父母不肯养子，不亦累于生生之德乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167850_comment'></div>先朝所行之事有所未尽，陛下推而行之，可谓至孝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167850_comment'></div>伏望陛下上成先帝之仁，下恤远民之苦，蠲放三州军丁米，只令依建州例岁纳口钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167850_comment'></div>在大国经费万分之一，于生民性命全活岂少也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167850_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1167850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄上《乞厢军屯驻广南只于比近军州节次那移对替札子》<div id='poem_1167851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞厢军屯驻广南只于比近军州节次那移对替劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167851")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167851'>臣前知福州日，窃见本州厢军，差在广南诸州屯驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167851_comment'></div>军回日，人数比去时大率死损一半，前后六七次尽皆如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167851_comment'></div>臣体问得诸处兵士差往广南，又分在巡检下，其间远处至有去本营八十程者，多为土风不同，沾染瘴毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167851_comment'></div>厢军屯驻，本为优轻，每至差发，便与父母妻子生死诀别，极可哀悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167851_comment'></div>臣窃谓若只于十数程内比近州军节次那移，乡里不遥，自然习熟风土，损失终少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167851_comment'></div>又缘屯驻，自来多寻旧窠年月对替，臣今欲乞诸州军屯驻广南，系奉宣差者，只乞于近比州军节次那移对替，年岁计之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167851_comment'></div>存救人命，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167851_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1167851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄上《请重定福州衙前额》奏折。<div id='poem_1167801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>请重定福州衙前额奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167801")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167801'>本路差使衙前不均，请行重定，以产多少均重难分数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167801_comment'></div>产钱五百者定入十九分重难，以上递加至三十三分止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167801_comment'></div>其乡户衙前岁以六十六人为额，以十二县产钱通排，共存留九百九十户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167801_comment'></div>仍请罢里正，以宽衙前歇役年限。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1167801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄号令严禁蓄蛊害人。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄号召众自福州大义渡至临漳沿途植松七百里。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='fed75bf8a2f54b8992ca58a1afded1d4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fed75bf8a2f54b8992ca58a1afded1d4");'><span id='fed75bf8a2f54b8992ca58a1afded1d4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>，39岁</div><div id='fed75bf8a2f54b8992ca58a1afded1d4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a>　蔡襄返京，途经福清渔溪，投宿黄檗寺，与主持彬长老谈禅，作《宿黄檗听彬长老谈禅》作品：《宿黄乐寺听彬长老谈禅》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9901715eb7bc4d7eae93d5eb981df764_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9901715eb7bc4d7eae93d5eb981df764");'><span id='9901715eb7bc4d7eae93d5eb981df764_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，45岁</div><div id='9901715eb7bc4d7eae93d5eb981df764' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄宿渔溪驿，见梅花感而作《题渔溪驿》<div id='poem_249139' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249139' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249139?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题渔溪驿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249139")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249139_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249139'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249139'>昔年同向腊中回，曾绕栏干折早梅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249139'>今日独来攀旧树，风翻黄叶下苍苔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249139_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249139'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249139_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a04ffc7130ee4a958f88709bbe8cd826_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a04ffc7130ee4a958f88709bbe8cd826");'><span id='a04ffc7130ee4a958f88709bbe8cd826_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1058')">1056-1058年</a>，45-47岁</div><div id='a04ffc7130ee4a958f88709bbe8cd826' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄再延聘周希孟等为教授，并亲临郡学执经讲问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄作《答赵内翰书》，致书赵概为石介辩诬。<div id='poem_1167878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答赵内翰书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167878")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167878'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167878'>襄再拜叔平内翰七丈足下：伏蒙示下众荐黄晞奏草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167878_comment'></div>晞闽人，与之游甚久，以书自喜，不茍于人，诚高世怀道之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167878_comment'></div>足下荐之于朝，庶乎盛时无有遗材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167878_comment'></div>足下之存心，不特为晞发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167878_comment'></div>然其奏曰：「石介在国子监时，请晞表率生徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167878_comment'></div>晞以介诈善不直，为事非是，遂拒之弗往，乃晞之先见知人、识虑高远也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167878_comment'></div>襄以谓斥介而引晞，意所未喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167878_comment'></div>介好论议当时人物，故众毁丛至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167878_comment'></div>原其所以为心，欲君侧无奸邪，人人为忠孝，百姓无疾苦，教化明白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167878_comment'></div>信周公孔子之言，谓太平可立致，而不度世务行之难易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167878_comment'></div>此介之所以修诚立节之大略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167878_comment'></div>所牴牾者，夏竦党辈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167878_comment'></div>一旦介去朝，奸人巧伪百端，构造谤毁，必欲赤其族然后快意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167878_comment'></div>赖天子圣明，辨是非，故介久而自白。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167878_comment'></div>嗟乎，谓介诈善何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167878_comment'></div>夫诈善者，将图富贵、取名誉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167878_comment'></div>介生不免寒饥，而死几斲棺，子孙流离，诈善者固如是耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167878_comment'></div>守己见，信道而不顾世俗者，伯夷、叔齐是也，死且数百年，孔子称之，其论遂定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167878_comment'></div>若介，信道而守死者也，其亦有待于后世乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167878_comment'></div>昔介之存，襄以同年进士，兄事而友之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167878_comment'></div>自介之亡，未见有如介之自信者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167878_comment'></div>介复生，当师事之，不敢以茍容无所自立为责，况敢毁之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167878_comment'></div>晞避介聘为学正，不肯为介下耳，此特小小者，岂足为晞高识远虑哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167878_comment'></div>足下与介疏，知之不至，然天下公议，固当有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167878_comment'></div>足下语论，众所瞻望，讵可雷同？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167878_comment'></div>今毁介之人满朝，使襄钳口，固不为少；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167878_comment'></div>虽开口明介，介岂遂明？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167878_comment'></div>然卖死友以合贵权，此襄所不为，而足下所见知之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167878_comment'></div>近为寒气薄中，日再食粥者七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167878_comment'></div>奉教不知疲惫，感叹颠倒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167878_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167878_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1167878_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄作《谢转礼部郎中表》<div id='poem_1167811' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167811' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167811?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢转礼部郎中表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167811")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167811_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167811'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167811'>臣襄言：今月十五日递到敕诰，伏蒙圣恩，授臣礼部郎中者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167811_comment'></div>函封芝检，特霈于殊私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167811_comment'></div>位列春官，骤加于宠命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167811_comment'></div>揣材甚薄，荷泽诚优，忝冒逾涯，兢惶罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167811_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣机露素浅，器术非深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167811_comment'></div>丁辰过时，历王途而寖久；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167811_comment'></div>承流宣教，著民政以无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167811_comment'></div>方怀惟谷之忧，积有瘝官之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167811_comment'></div>何霈恩而特厚，复增秩以敷荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167811_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下禹律均和，尧仁锡庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167811_comment'></div>诞推涣渥，施及蒙愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167811_comment'></div>敢不寅奉政条，恪图治绩，竭尽涓埃之力，仰酬覆育之私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167811_comment'></div>臣无任云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167811_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167811'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二二。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167811_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄上《乞相度开修城池》奏议。<div id='poem_1167775' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167775' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167775?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞相度开修城池奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167775")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167775_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167775'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167775'>臣于皇祐四年曾蒙朝廷除知福州，臣以私事辞免，续差天章阁待制曹颖叔知福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167775_comment'></div>臣其时得知朝廷有劄子指挥与曹颖叔，渐次开修城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167775_comment'></div>臣今来到任检阅不下司文字并诸案，并无宣命劄子，切虑只是曹颖叔附身文字，将带随行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167775_comment'></div>其城池不曾开修，只筑到数十丈高墙，又别无行遣计度工料，虑有误事，伏须举奏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167775_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1167775'>右，具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167775_comment'></div>福建一路州军，建、剑、汀州、邵武军连接两浙、江南路，乘船下水，三两日可至福州城下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167775_comment'></div>其东界连接温州，并南接兴化军、泉州、漳州，各在海畔，四向舟船可至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167775_comment'></div>闽中诸州皆福州为根本，以自太平兴国中归纳疆土后隳毁城池，至今四围城墙只高三五尺，可以遮闭牛羊，至于私商小儿皆可踰越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167775_comment'></div>臣又检得侬贼作过时，有劄子下本路修葺城垒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167775_comment'></div>不唯事至难办，兼福州外城周围约二十里，工料极大，若行修筑，须至科点丁夫、配约物料，收拾备足，一两月间便要了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167775_comment'></div>共候兵士功役，空延岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167775_comment'></div>臣今具上件因依，取候朝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167775_comment'></div>若令修筑，乞降指挥检计工料，点丁夫，木植、粮食，诸般擘画事件闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167775_comment'></div>若或重惜民力，未令修筑，亦系朝旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167775_comment'></div>切缘旧有开修指挥，今来并无文字照会，恐有缓急，朝廷不知未有城池，须有陈述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167775_comment'></div>谨具奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1167775_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄上《乞相度沿海防备盗贼》奏议。<div id='poem_1167776' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167776' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167776?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞相度沿海防备盗贼奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167776")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167776_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167776'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167776'>准中书劄子节文指挥：「枢密直学士、礼部郎中、知福州蔡襄奏：『臣于皇祐四年，曾蒙朝廷除知福州，臣以私事辞免，续差天章阁待制曹颖叔知福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167776_comment'></div>臣其时得知朝廷有劄子指挥与曹颖叔，渐次开修城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167776_comment'></div>臣今来到任，检阅不下司文字并诸案，并无宣命劄子，切虑只是曹颖叔附身文字，将带随行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167776_comment'></div>其城池不曾开修，只筑到数十丈高墙，又别无行遣计度工料，虑有误事，伏须举奏者』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167776_comment'></div>蒙朝廷检会：福建路沿海州军与外界水路通接，自来未曾别作防备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167776_comment'></div>于皇祐四年十二月奉圣旨，令新差知福州曹颖叔，候到任，专切用心经制，应系沿海地分外寇可来之处，立便擘画防扼设备，开析闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167776_comment'></div>又奉圣旨，宜令蔡襄详前项所降指挥，相度闻奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167776_comment'></div>劄送知福州蔡密学」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167776_comment'></div>今具相度因依下项：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1167776'>一、臣今相度福州、泉州、漳州、兴化军尽是边海，若是舟船要到城下，逐州各有海口小港，约近百里至七十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167776_comment'></div>其海口旧时各有镇寨把扼海路，后来无事，兵士渐次减少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167776_comment'></div>今来见作点检商税，量差兵级在彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167776_comment'></div>沿海路平静，难以宿兵，如有盗贼，逐州军可以随宜应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167776_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1167776'>一、泉州、福州、漳州、兴化军各是海边，今来逐州兵士并不会舟船，出入海路收捉茶盐，如遇贼人斗敌，多被贼船惯习水势，立见伤损。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167776_comment'></div>臣体问，福州闽安镇把港及钟门巡检一员，在海上封桩舶船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167776_comment'></div>泉州有同口巡检一员，去城七里，每年下海封桩舶船。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167776_comment'></div>漳州旧有黄淡头巡检一员，号为招舶，亦是夏间下海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167776_comment'></div>兴化军巡检一员，却在兴化县山中，去军城百里，海上别无巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167776_comment'></div>所有逐州逐县虽招舶船，每年或有或无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167776_comment'></div>原其创意，盖是沿海州军要得兵甲习会水战，以防急缓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167776_comment'></div>其漳州黄淡头巡检后因转运使高易简奏，移于龙岩县山中大池驿，去州七日，防备盗贼，因此废罢招舶一员。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167776_comment'></div>臣今相度，漳州管界巡检去城五里，却令兼带招舶，每年出海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167776_comment'></div>兴化军管界巡检移近军城，给与舟船，令往来海上巡警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167776_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1167776'>一、臣相度沿海州军兵士多是不习舟船出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167776_comment'></div>臣于去年奏，乞置澄海指挥，更不拣添宣毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167776_comment'></div>后来谓诸州已拣添宣毅，朝廷难更施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167776_comment'></div>臣今乞令福、泉、漳州、兴化军旧有刀鱼船及巡检司入海舟船，量与修整；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167776_comment'></div>旧有舟船亦乞量置五七只。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167776_comment'></div>其宣毅兵士差下巡检司，并令教习舟船，谙习水势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167776_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1167776'>右件具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167776_comment'></div>臣相度沿海水路防备盗贼，伏乞朝廷特赐指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167776_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1167776_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　蔡襄尝寄茶叶赠孙甫，作《和诗送茶寄孙之翰》<div id='poem_249214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和诗送茶寄孙之翰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249214")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249214'>北苑灵芽天下精，要须寒过入春生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249214'>故人偏爱云腴白，佳句遥传玉律清。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249214'>衰病万缘皆绝虑，甘香一味未忘情。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249214'>封题原是山家宝，尽日虚堂试品程。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249214'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年冬</a>　冬底，葛氏夫人和匀葬于木兰溪南岸之将军山，蔡襄派人携祭文到莆祭奠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年2月</a>　行春奠之礼于孔庙，蔡襄面请乡老诸生推荐人才。作品：《谕乡老诸生文》<div id='poem_1167868' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167868' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167868?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谕乡老诸生文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167868")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167868_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167868'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167868'>襄备位刺史，行春奠之礼于孔子庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167868_comment'></div>郡之人士，来相予职，爰及耆艾，亦集庭下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167868_comment'></div>既延之坐，谨问之曰：唯尔诸老，前观刺史之政多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167868_comment'></div>吾州数万族，人情善恶，亦唯万殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167868_comment'></div>刺史为治，孰不欲兴利去害，宣流风化，与古为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167868_comment'></div>逮及三年，民未之信，则又去矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167868_comment'></div>将良吏之难值耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167868_comment'></div>抑治道之难至耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167868_comment'></div>襄德业不能过人，智术不能济众，夙夜悉心，唯民实忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167868_comment'></div>察禁邪猾，扶善沮恶，使强弱各安其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167868_comment'></div>然未免于刑罚，岂足为治哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167868_comment'></div>至于孝慈友弟、敦厚信让之风，将有望于诸老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167868_comment'></div>老者之言，少者之法，父诏其子，兄命其弟，相率以从教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167868_comment'></div>一家修之，一国效之，能以兴礼让而止狱讼，亦诸老有助于刺史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167868_comment'></div>州郡之有学，所以励贤才而进德业，必有师友颛训导之方，为之治经术、习文章、讲道义，以称厥职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167868_comment'></div>设非其人而冒居之，学不用成，民罔攸信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167868_comment'></div>襄之治郡甫尔，士人之修德行与经术文章者莫知其谁，譬诸蒙雾，罔识处所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167868_comment'></div>诸公各以至公之心而称举能者，以备其阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167868_comment'></div>孔子曰：「十室之邑，必有忠信如丘者焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167868_comment'></div>诸生条陈其人，实密其封，予将择焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1167868_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年2月</a>　二月寒食日，蔡襄与同僚会饮池园，见梨花盛开，赋长诗《寒食梨花小饮》寄慨。<div id='poem_249406' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249406' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249406?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寒食梨花小饮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249406")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249406_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249406'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249406'>江南寒薄春尝早，花卉入春先自老。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249406'>嗟予衰病不及时，出见池园半青草。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249406'>纵有馀葩在叶间，行看落片随风扫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249406'>寻春已过索莫归，重忆欢娱耿怀抱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249406'>虽然妖艳难再得，但只逢花须醉倒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249406'>二月中央寒食朝，墙隈忽见梨花飘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249406'>开门四顾粲然白，传催翠帟宾朋招。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249406'>长吟环绕不知数，渐值明月临清霄。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249406'>谁剪轻云成碎蕊，天留密雪封枯条。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249406'>重重尽挂珠缨络，簌簌初呈簂步摇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249406'>傍花行酒发<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_249406", 249406, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>新唱</span>，满座例举黄金瓢。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249406'>西都姚黄高一尺，扬州宝髻分双翘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249406'>幽香绝艳信尤物，设欲置之千里遥。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249406'>壁门写生亦名画，未免五彩涂鲛绡。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249406'>莫如此君慰人意，相对一笑开无憀。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249406'>古来英豪多感激，坐使绿鬓朱颜雕。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249406'>劝君且作梨花饮，慎勿称量别流品。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249406_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249406'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_249406_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄闻杜衍讣告，作《祭杜祁公文》遥祭。<div id='poem_1168211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭杜祁公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168211")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168211'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168211'>庆历之初，边圉多事，生民被害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168211_comment'></div>天子思得贤辅相以脩庶政，于是擢公宥密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168211_comment'></div>公以暮年，当主知遇，与国谋论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168211_comment'></div>念其自效莫如荐引才能，乃条当世士可以为时用者数十人上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168211_comment'></div>会朝廷适已拔任，除目既下，而公疏中姓名往往契合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168211_comment'></div>有不悦公者乃訾曰：「上方用人，而辄荐引，是欲私自朋比也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168211_comment'></div>公不辨，而求士益切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168211_comment'></div>既而作宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168211_comment'></div>襄时为谏官，以亲求郡，得福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168211_comment'></div>将行，公又疏曰：「蔡襄愿少留之，不宜令远去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168211_comment'></div>公之同列曰：「彼求外补，而复留之，岂非朋比耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168211_comment'></div>未几，公罢相知兖州，遂请老以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168211_comment'></div>天子思之，遣使存问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168211_comment'></div>当时指以朋比者，不数年列台阁、参侍从，天下之论，益知公有大臣节，直己徇公，不恤于毁誉，不移于用舍也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168211_comment'></div>昔公之存，襄未尝以不才累公为谢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168211_comment'></div>今公之薨，可无言哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168211_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168211_comment'></div>襄于公门，无有雅旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168211_comment'></div>一见加礼，公实我厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168211_comment'></div>系官南闽，哀诚莫究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168211_comment'></div>侑奠以辞，永示于后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1168211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年春</a>　蔡襄观赏堂下自栽之花卉，有感作《福州堂下小栏花卉多是手栽今已繁盛因赏花有所感悼》<div id='poem_249275' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249275' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249275?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州堂下小栏花卉多是手栽今已繁盛因赏花有所感悼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249275")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249275_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249275'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249275'>爱花尽日傍花台，点检当年手自栽。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249275'>前事已随朝暮变，旧华空见浅深开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249275'>山禽忽下还飞去，溪雨才收又复来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249275'>只有春醪能遣恨，无人栏畔共持杯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249275_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249275'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249275_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　朝廷诏贡士，蔡襄上表推荐本州儒士周希孟。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年春</a>　蔡襄尝与同僚游宴于薛老亭，作《饮薛老亭晚归》<div id='poem_249199' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249199' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249199?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饮薛老亭晚归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年春）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年9月</a>　蔡襄闻王洙讣告，作《祭王侍读文》遥寄。<div id='poem_1168212' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168212' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168212?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭王侍读文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168212")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168212_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168212'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168212'>谨以清酌之奠，祭于侍读原叔八丈之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168212_comment'></div>惟灵学通贯变，文绍高古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168212_comment'></div>华林劝导，献明帝所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168212_comment'></div>禁密顾问，阙职斯补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168212_comment'></div>善与物同，世罔有拒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168212_comment'></div>当其议论，乃心自处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168212_comment'></div>智力未究，覂于夷路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168212_comment'></div>孰不永年，公何啬而不与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168212_comment'></div>孰不持秉，公何后而不举？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168212_comment'></div>念哲人之遐躅，岂外累之足数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168212_comment'></div>信问来门，官推守土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168212_comment'></div>怅天涯之吊酹，异西轩之笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168212_comment'></div>曷书牍之具存，终已焉其无睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168212_comment'></div>岩岩商丘，新阡其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168212_comment'></div>一奠伸哀，幽怀莫叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168212_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1168212_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄曾收到陈襄信札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄作《寄南海李龙图兑求素馨含笑花》<div id='poem_249098' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249098' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249098?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄南海李龙图<span class='inlineComment2'>（兑）</span>求素馨含笑花</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249098")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249098_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249098'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249098'>二草曾观岭外图，开时尝与暑风俱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249098'>使君已自怜清分，分得新条过海无。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249098_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249098'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249098_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄为治理官场和社会腐败，作《福州五戒文》<div id='poem_1167867' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167867' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167867?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州五戒文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167867")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167867_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167867'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167867'>观今之俗，为父母者视己之子犹有厚薄，迨至娶妇，多令异食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167867_comment'></div>贫者困于日给，其势不得不然，富者亦何为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167867_comment'></div>盖父母之心不能均于诸子以至此，不可不戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167867_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1167867'>人子之孝，本于养亲，以顺其志，死生不违于礼，是孝诚之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167867_comment'></div>观今之俗，贫富之家多于父母异财、兄弟分养，乃至纤悉，无有不校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167867_comment'></div>及其亡也，破产卖宅，盛为酒肴，以劳亲知，施与浮图，以求冥福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167867_comment'></div>原其为心，不在于亲，将以誇胜于人，是不知为孝之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167867_comment'></div>生则尽养，死不妄费，如此岂不善乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167867_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1167867'>兄弟之爱，出于天性，少小相从，其心欢欣，岂有间哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167867_comment'></div>迨因娶妇，或至临财，憎恶一开，即成怨隙，至于兴䜣讼，冒刑狱，至死而不息者，殊可哀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167867_comment'></div>盖由听妇言，贪财利，绝同胞之恩、友爱之情，遂及于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167867_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1167867'>娶妇何谓，欲以传嗣，岂为财也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167867_comment'></div>观今之俗，娶其妻不顾门户，直求资财，随其贫富，未有婚姻之家不为怨怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167867_comment'></div>原其由，盖婚礼之夕广縻费，已而校奁橐，朝索其一，暮索其二，姑辱其妇，夫虐其妻，求之不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167867_comment'></div>若不满意，至有割男女之爱，辄相弃背。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167867_comment'></div>习俗日久，不以为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167867_comment'></div>此生民之大弊，人行最恶者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167867_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1167867'>凡人情莫不欲富，至于农人、商贾、百工之家，莫不昼夜营度，以求其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167867_comment'></div>然农人兼并，商贾欺谩，大率刻剥贫民，罔昧神理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167867_comment'></div>譬如百虫聚居，强者食啖，曾不暂息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167867_comment'></div>求而得之，广为施与，冀灭罪恶，其愚甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167867_comment'></div>今欲为福，孰若减刻剥之心以宽贫民，去欺谩之行以畏神理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167867_comment'></div>为子孙之计则亦久远，居乡党之间则为良善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167867_comment'></div>其义至明，不可不知。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1167867_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄为治理官场和社会腐败，作《戒山头斋会碑》<div id='poem_1167870' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167870' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167870?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戒山头斋会碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（1057年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167870")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167870_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167870'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167870'>使州体问自来风俗，被丧之家言有靡用破卖产业，置办酒食斋筵，名为孝行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167870_comment'></div>至有亡殁之人，本家不敢哭临，先将田屋出帐典卖得人，就头商量，打了定钱，方敢举殓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167870_comment'></div>外殉人情，中抑哀毁，是不孝之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167870_comment'></div>出殡之夕，邻里识与不识，尽来即问，恣食酒肉，包携归家，至使丧家费用无极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167870_comment'></div>其于人情，邻里当有赠遗，以资丧家，慰吊之际，岂可恣食酒肉以为宴乐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167870_comment'></div>是无礼之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167870_comment'></div>山头斋筵，僧俗之中，本非知识，斋食不足，每人散钱二百文，如有少缺，便即忿怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167870_comment'></div>送葬之礼，虽出于古，岂有本无哀情，只趁斋食，丧家竭力不给，此与乞丐何异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167870_comment'></div>是无耻之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167870_comment'></div>若不断绝，民间转见不易礼义之日远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167870_comment'></div>右，仰丧葬之家，丧夜宴客不得置酒宴乐，山头不得广置斋筵聚会，并分散钱物，以充斋价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167870_comment'></div>如有辄敢，罪在家长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167870_comment'></div>并城外僧院不得与人办置山头斋，及坊虞候耆长常切觉察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1167870_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄为治理官场和社会腐败，作《教民十六事》<div id='poem_1167871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>教民十六事碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐二年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167871")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167871'>一、应有无□徒辈，诳是知州亲知，于州县打索关节，乞取财物，许人告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167871_comment'></div>二、市贾买物亏减价例，及不画时还钱，仰行人陈告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167871_comment'></div>三、行人于诸官厅干当厨库公人及市买等处，每月若有行用钱物，罪在行人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167871_comment'></div>四、巡拦告税，不得擅入人家搜检税物，须申州取候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167871_comment'></div>五、市行见行铜钱如有夹杂砂蜡新钱，许人告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167871_comment'></div>六、银行辄造吹银出卖，许人告捉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167871_comment'></div>七、人户居停赌钱，本罪科断外，必定折屋纳官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167871_comment'></div>八、僧人不得止宿俗家，妇女不得听讲及非时入僧院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167871_comment'></div>九、诸官除依条本厅并转辖处科决外，不得擅行决罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167871_comment'></div>十、巡检使臣非承使州指挥，不得带甲领兵搜围人家，捡索违禁服色；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167871_comment'></div>若窝藏强劫并杀人贼，明有踪迹，许收捉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167871_comment'></div>十一、诸县擅行科取修造，及诸色乡人歛掠人户钱物入己，许人陈理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167871_comment'></div>十二、在州坊虞候所由，并外县公人所受情弊放散公事不送州县，许人告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167871_comment'></div>十三、推司、当直司并外县公人因勘公事廉有所受，许人因事报覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167871_comment'></div>十四、诸坊只许管本地内争斗、火烛、奸盗、赌钱、杀牛公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167871_comment'></div>十五、在城里外丧葬之家，丧夜不得置酒肉宴乐，以亏孝道，山头不得广置斋筵，违者罪在家长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167871_comment'></div>十六、士庶家不肖子弟盗卖家产，并转肩出利买客人货，贵买贱卖，如本人无钱，勒牙保人卖业填还。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1167871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　在闽县、候官、怀安三县倡修水利，改善福州城内外的水环境。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　蔡襄为次子旬重申与刘家的婚约，代办妆奁、迎娶过门。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a>　岁末，蔡襄致书欧阳修，言人生聚散，相见之难。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年4月</a>　连江县令送灵芝到州，蔡襄作《芝草述》<div id='poem_1168127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>芝草述</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168127")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168127'>福州连江县宁善乡崇德里保福院产芝一本，四月八日癸未，令朱定得之，诣府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168127_comment'></div>质黑而坚，叶如侧荷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168127_comment'></div>其上又出一本，离为六茎，枝柯耸密，中有连理，末如燕尾而朱涅之，高可尺许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168127_comment'></div>世传古篆「芝」字皆枝叶扶疏，岂古人象形而作乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168127_comment'></div>而汉《齐房歌》曰：「九茎连叶，玄气之精」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168127_comment'></div>正谓玄芝而有九茎，与叶连也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168127_comment'></div>芝之为物，在处有之，大较形类苗檽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168127_comment'></div>近无是比，倘或有焉，而予未之见也，故特书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168127_comment'></div>枢密直学士、尚书礼部郎中、知军州事蔡襄题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1168127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年4月</a>　蔡襄上表请求知兴化军，以便治疾。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='740bef5df0da40aaa25fa29137534500_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("740bef5df0da40aaa25fa29137534500");'><span id='740bef5df0da40aaa25fa29137534500_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1061')">1060-1061年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='740bef5df0da40aaa25fa29137534500' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　岁末，抵福州，由知州燕度招待过年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年1月7日</a>　蔡襄自福州乘舟沿闽江北上，作《人日立春舟行寄福州燕二司封》寄燕度。<div id='poem_249146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>人日立春舟行寄福州燕二司封</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年1月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249146")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249146'>清溪潮上送行船，回望高城隔晓烟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249146'>景色似看名画展<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：前日君家尽出名画。）</span>，醉魂犹忆寿杯传<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：君家世传寿杯，行之侑酒。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249146'>春盘食菜思三九，人日书幡诵百千。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249146'>南国逢君唯道旧，后时何处笑今年。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249146'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249146_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年1月7日</a>　蔡襄自福州乘舟沿闽江北上，作《又寄兴化徐虞部》寄徐师闵。<div id='poem_249150' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249150' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249150?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又寄兴化徐虞部</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年1月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249150")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249150_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249150'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249150'>梅花狼籍拂轻舟，人日溪行动客愁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249150'>上昼去程初北首，故山归思满东流。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249150'>垂垂朝雨随双桨，草草春蔬送一瓯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249150'>不独怀乡便多感，看人难似府君侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249150_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249150'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249150_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='86a66d9818144316ab4f3f83f631c5f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("86a66d9818144316ab4f3f83f631c5f4");'><span id='86a66d9818144316ab4f3f83f631c5f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>，32岁</div><div id='86a66d9818144316ab4f3f83f631c5f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1043&endYear=1043')">1043年</a>　蔡襄至衢州，作《论东南事宜疏》，交驿递上朝。<div id='poem_1167793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论东南事宜疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（庆历三年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1043年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167793")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167793'>臣近者蒙恩赐告归觐父母，臣出宋都，历淮上，绝江而南，出东吴之域，萦委千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167793_comment'></div>臣潜度事势，周问民隐，可为寒心者，请试陈之，愿陛下少赐清閒之宴而垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167793_comment'></div>臣窃以天下治平之日已久，东南列郡，城池隳塞，士卒必少，府无完兵，廪无储粟，内无戒守之备，外无维制之具，道路人之所共知，此其尤可忧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167793_comment'></div>苏、秀、杭、越等数州，频年以来旱涝更作，稼穑不登，疠疫仍起，贫者流转沟壑，居者连病，丧亡相属，苦哀之声，痛贯人骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167793_comment'></div>虽朝廷屡行赈恤，然渥泽之施未能周及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167793_comment'></div>今岁春夏不雨，野田半芜，前秋之期，居可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167793_comment'></div>吴民偷侈，灾患之变，亦一极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167793_comment'></div>臣窃观前古兵革之兴，多缘饥旱，姑此茍生，相与为盗，及其势盛，制胁郡县，汉唐之世，终为邦梗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167793_comment'></div>而况奸雄豪杰，觇伺衅隙，须时而发，此不可不虞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167793_comment'></div>《易·萃卦》之大《象》曰：「泽上于地，萃，君子以除戎器，戒不虞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167793_comment'></div>说者曰：聚而无防，则生众心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167793_comment'></div>今有珠玉之货纳于府藏，敕主守吏严其扃鐍，常若寇至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167793_comment'></div>而地方数千里，生民数万族，乃忘保固之术，谨其细而遗其大，臣未见夫长画也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167793_comment'></div>借使浙东饥病之馀，凶突之人啸聚百数，草窃闾巷，臣未知以何郡兵卒而能制其死命乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167793_comment'></div>诚以东南之势为不足患，臣恐天下之患，正生于不足患矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167793_comment'></div>当今之策，莫若择郡守，宽民力，募兵卒，严盗法，四者最为急务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167793_comment'></div>一曰择郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167793_comment'></div>臣谨具录诸州军长吏姓名年齿、所为绩状，伏望陛下咨问宰臣，令议其材否而更易之，使材足以应变，而惠足以利民，然后可倚以为重也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167793_comment'></div>二曰宽民力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167793_comment'></div>莫若蠲赋税、均借贷、省配敛、赈流移，所谓发于国而藏于民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167793_comment'></div>三曰募兵卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167793_comment'></div>臣谓因此饥歉，颇易招置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167793_comment'></div>大凡吴民软弱，不便高寒，不知骑射，驱以备边，非可速用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167793_comment'></div>臣请权罢寄招禁军，于两浙重镇量多少之数，各令召募教习，以备寇盗，亦东南一胜势也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167793_comment'></div>四曰严盗法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167793_comment'></div>臣窃见顷年亦缘饥旱，强劫盗贼多蒙宽贷，实小惠而大害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167793_comment'></div>臣愿申敕两浙灾伤州军，应有贼盗，一准法令，无所矜宥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167793_comment'></div>密戒提点刑狱臣僚，如有因饥劫盗，应死而情有可矜者，即详度以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167793_comment'></div>刑罚不失厥中，亦以遏凶人之虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167793_comment'></div>夫未形之言难于信用，既形之言无逮于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1167793_comment'></div>臣之狂愚，非能造几而辨，徒以见闻，过为虑度，愿陛下采而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1167793_comment'></div>臣不胜惓惓恳恳之至，谨衢州附递以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1167793_comment'></div>臣襄昧死再拜，谨上。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1167793_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='b050aab7223c470b93d350e47d661fed_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b050aab7223c470b93d350e47d661fed");'><span id='b050aab7223c470b93d350e47d661fed_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='b050aab7223c470b93d350e47d661fed' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年1月</a>　元月，蔡襄从闽北冒大雪继续北上抵浙江衢州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c611bd37b62e4684b03f3bb2c2f44423_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c611bd37b62e4684b03f3bb2c2f44423");'><span id='c611bd37b62e4684b03f3bb2c2f44423_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，44岁</div><div id='c611bd37b62e4684b03f3bb2c2f44423' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年12月</a>　蔡襄妻葛氏夫人卒于衢州道中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年12月27日</a>　蔡襄作《上集贤相公书》致富弼。<div id='poem_1167879' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167879' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167879?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上集贤相公书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1055年12月27日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167879")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167879_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167879'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167879'>十二月十七日，襄再拜上书集贤相公阁下：伏自阁下入总台衡，天下慰庆，况素辱公知遇者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167879_comment'></div>然不得奏记左右，以导恳恳，盖私门多故，以至是耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167879_comment'></div>公之为相，伏计进说以助聪明，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167879_comment'></div>高论者不可为，为之无成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167879_comment'></div>卑论者不可用，用之败名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167879_comment'></div>惟是二者，称量世务，因事有作，正当今之急要者，伏惟留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167879_comment'></div>襄自六月去都，至南京，遽丧长子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167879_comment'></div>寻以妻室病患，道路就医，处处留滞，至衢州，比又丧亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167879_comment'></div>半年之间，再罹凶苦，生意几尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167879_comment'></div>上愿慈亲年馀八十，强安神情，以悦老者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167879_comment'></div>昨自开封府，以母老得请便郡，经岁犹未到官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167879_comment'></div>襄有所虑者，恐朝廷因有差除，而明公不遗姓名，或有移易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167879_comment'></div>襄母亲年高矣，乡土去京四五千里，侍亲而行则不可，委亲而行又不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167879_comment'></div>设有一旦之命，适足以趣襄退隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167879_comment'></div>又念食禄，理无自由，思欲归休以奉晨夕，生平不能为生，无田可耕，仰俸自给，以供甘旨，舍官而养，遂为穷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167879_comment'></div>傥台造为之守郡便安而不移，则重赐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167879_comment'></div>设或圣人尚记犬马，而公以此开说，当亦可解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167879_comment'></div>下诚区区，幸冀财悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167879_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167879_comment'></div>襄再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1167879_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泉州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='36ca0e02ebcf4ae1b5e447fb87c9ecbb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("36ca0e02ebcf4ae1b5e447fb87c9ecbb");'><span id='36ca0e02ebcf4ae1b5e447fb87c9ecbb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>，33岁</div><div id='36ca0e02ebcf4ae1b5e447fb87c9ecbb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年2月</a>　蔡襄应邀游泉州九日山遣怀。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='18a10d70c8dd4551b655581ad3c6f401_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("18a10d70c8dd4551b655581ad3c6f401");'><span id='18a10d70c8dd4551b655581ad3c6f401_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>，45岁</div><div id='18a10d70c8dd4551b655581ad3c6f401' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年2月7日</a>　蔡襄到泉州任，作《泉州谢上表》<div id='poem_1167809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泉州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年2月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167809")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167809'>臣襄言：臣奉敕知泉州军州事，已于今月初七日到官管勾讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167809_comment'></div>朝纶至渥，俯从臣子之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167809_comment'></div>海域虽遥，实便庭闱之养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167809_comment'></div>臣襄<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣生身遐远，逢辰休明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167809_comment'></div>独持愚直之心，早委圣神之照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167809_comment'></div>自参文馆，旋列谏垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167809_comment'></div>无嘉谋以奏上古之珍，无敏智以论当世之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167809_comment'></div>浸叨词掖，时迩威颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167809_comment'></div>被天语之丁宁，涖京都之繁浩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167809_comment'></div>初无才略，动忤贵权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167809_comment'></div>事必处于公平，要惟归于勤瘁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167809_comment'></div>每缘睿奖，仅免人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167809_comment'></div>念慈亲之高年，乞故乡而便养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167809_comment'></div>曲承厚泽，出守清源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167809_comment'></div>间关山川，历涉岁月，近临居署，寅布宽条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167809_comment'></div>讯问私门，不移于夕宿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167809_comment'></div>甘鲜庶品，足奉于晨羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167809_comment'></div>如臣侥荣，实少伦比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167809_comment'></div>此盖伏遇尊号皇帝陛下大仁覆物，广孝及民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167809_comment'></div>致兹犬马之诚，上获云天之施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167809_comment'></div>敢不励精邦治，殚尽夙夜之劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167809_comment'></div>宣谕帝慈，周通爱育之惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167809_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣、激切屏营之至，谨奉表陈谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167809_comment'></div>臣襄诚欢诚感，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167809_comment'></div>谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1167809_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167809'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167809_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年闰三月</a>　闰三月，蔡襄接诏命改知福州，因虑病体不堪重任而上表请求依旧知泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　晋江知县章拱之贪赃不法，蔡襄绳之以法，坐废。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6d6671230c4425a97072666f78eb256_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6d6671230c4425a97072666f78eb256");'><span id='a6d6671230c4425a97072666f78eb256_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1060')">1058-1060年</a>，47-49岁</div><div id='a6d6671230c4425a97072666f78eb256' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年6月</a>　蔡襄奉诏移知泉州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年7月1日</a>　蔡襄到知泉州任，作《移泉州谢上表》<div id='poem_1167812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移泉州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年7月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167812")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167812'>臣襄言：昨奉敕移知泉州军州事，已于初一日赴任讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167812_comment'></div>祗承温诏，已布宽条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167812_comment'></div>置身便安，蒙上轸恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167812_comment'></div>臣襄诚感诚惧，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167812_comment'></div>伏念臣自解京邑，出临清源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167812_comment'></div>违天日之清光，归江海之遐裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167812_comment'></div>过家上冢，在古之甚荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167812_comment'></div>守郡养亲，为子之至幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167812_comment'></div>曾未荐月，改付全闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167812_comment'></div>臣向缘爱苦之忧，遽致朘痟之病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167812_comment'></div>州称都会，居有版籍之繁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167812_comment'></div>俗不尚医，难求药石之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167812_comment'></div>气力羸虚，不可以治穰剧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167812_comment'></div>智识顽钝，不可以应急难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167812_comment'></div>辄露微诚，觊得便地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167812_comment'></div>军壁虽小，曾是故乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167812_comment'></div>狱讼差閒，足宽外虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167812_comment'></div>敢期朝渥，更与泉麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167812_comment'></div>再见吏民，仰宣威惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167812_comment'></div>因其无事，得以养和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167812_comment'></div>此盖伏遇体天法道钦文聪武圣神孝德皇帝陛下，曲念孤贫，俯矜衰悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167812_comment'></div>不穷驽力，而使之自适；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167812_comment'></div>仍有官俸，而代其为生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167812_comment'></div>况臣年齿方中，干祈之切者盖由疾故；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167812_comment'></div>傥臣筋骸复壮，报效之际者敢以家为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167812_comment'></div>上衔仁施之深，若负丘山之重。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1167812_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167812'><span class='label'>按：</span>《蔡忠惠集》卷二○。又见清抄一百五十卷本《圣宋名贤五百家播芳大全文粹》卷二八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167812_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年7月20日</a>　蔡襄祈雨飞阳庙，先后作《祭神文》四篇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年7月</a>　因蔡襄举荐，周希孟被授为国子监四门助教兼福州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月</a>　蔡襄《教民十六事》被刻碑立于福州虎节门下。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年12月</a>　蔡襄为叶任撰书《泉州司户参军叶君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168190' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168190' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168190?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泉州司户参军叶君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168190")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168190_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168190'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168190'>叶君任，字仲堪，兴化军仙游人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168190_comment'></div>父讳宾，尚书都官员外郎致仕，恩补一子官，君以是为江州德化县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168190_comment'></div>岁馀，乞便家事亲，得泉州司户参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168190_comment'></div>时监司有不喜君所为不茍者，因自牒去职，归侍都官府君，至殁不去左右，遂无意仕进，以终其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168190_comment'></div>君于为吏，临众必先绳其尤强猾者，治民必先怜其尤贫弱者，故所至必辨，而去则思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168190_comment'></div>上官以势夺其是，如以砾食，吾不从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168190_comment'></div>其馀家居，廪有馀粟，遇岁凶荒，薄其直而出，州党赖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168190_comment'></div>民有丧与疾，时其急难，以济其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168190_comment'></div>游旧之好，益困愈亲，若寒而就燠，吾不去也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168190_comment'></div>故其生也人誉之，而亡也哀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168190_comment'></div>迹其所从来，盖有以得之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168190_comment'></div>初，弃官归，年方壮强，颇穷山水，娱诗酒以自放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168190_comment'></div>或说君起仕，君谓之曰：「达者人之表，而议之招也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168190_comment'></div>享其利而不胜其任，得所欲而违于义，君子不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168190_comment'></div>古之人所以约而自全者，其心岂异乎人哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168190_comment'></div>盖知其所以然而安于分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168190_comment'></div>且怵惕穷年，孰与茫洋无间以自适乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168190_comment'></div>君生五十四年，而终于嘉祐三年十一月三十日，葬于归德乡化善里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168190_comment'></div>其世次，予尝志都官之墓，可从而考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168190_comment'></div>初娶王氏，再娶吕氏，皆有贤行，而早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168190_comment'></div>长子曰祐，以文词为名进士，卒年三十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168190_comment'></div>曰裕，十有五岁，持父丧如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168190_comment'></div>曰祫，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168190_comment'></div>女十一人，二人适太常博士许祯、郴州宜章令陈启期，六人为进士妻，三人未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168190_comment'></div>许君与予善，述其孤之意，从予请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168190_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1168190'>行修于乡而老少之怀，志安于分而荣悴不迁，此力于吾道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168190_comment'></div>若夫冥乎造有之端，托于适化之会，于我不居，乘时以行，抑老严之徒欤！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1168190_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　本年起，蔡襄致力于督造万安桥工程。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年</a>　本年，蔡襄曾上《奉举夏侯郎中状》保举夏侯锡。<div id='poem_1167831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奏举夏侯郎中状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167831")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167831_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167831'>右：襄伏睹尚书屯田郎中、知兴化军夏侯锡廉以持身，果于临事，未尝屈志以干誉，或乃省分而遗荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167831_comment'></div>久处仕途，素精吏干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167831_comment'></div>逮于晚节，仅领军麾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167831_comment'></div>心力强明，民俗畏爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167831_comment'></div>惜其才敏之邵，未参器使之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167831_comment'></div>今保举堪充刑狱钱谷重难任使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167831_comment'></div>如蒙朝廷擢用，后犯正入己赃，臣甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167831_comment'></div>其人在朝并无亲的骨肉食禄，与臣不<span class='inlineComment2'>（阙五字）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167831_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1167831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年1月1日</a>　蔡襄为次子旬举行弱冠礼。<br /><a href="javascript: /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　蔡襄上《举留柯述充州学教授状》<div id='poem_1167834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>举留柯述充州学教授状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1059年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167834'>具衔臣蔡某/右，具如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167834_comment'></div>伏以教育人材，先由学校；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167834_comment'></div>训导之职，实难其材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167834_comment'></div>臣本州进士岁趋贡举尝及七百馀人，州学生徒相聚讲议，日亦不减数十百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167834_comment'></div>昨以新授虔州赣县尉柯述在州待阙，权请教授，将及半年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167834_comment'></div>考校文词，动有程准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167834_comment'></div>诸生惜其罢去，诣臣乞留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167834_comment'></div>臣欲望朝廷特除本州州学教授，不理资考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167834_comment'></div>俾之在学训励生徒，兴明儒术，其于助治，亦可尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167834_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1167834_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年</a>　本年，蔡襄有《与陈秘书书》<span class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167889_comment'></div>子之文词日益新，道义亦随而有加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167889_comment'></div>其有未至者，当相见日评是非也。<div class='inline' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修驿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年五月二十八日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168117")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168117'>兴化军仙游县太平驿，在唐为风亭馆<span class='inlineComment2'>（事载《皇华四达记》。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168117_comment'></div>今门有新题，而乡俗犹名其旧，盖所繇来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168117_comment'></div>嘉祐元年，始作厅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168117_comment'></div>六月，襄自泉移福，诒书乡人，共完堂室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168117_comment'></div>二年，再临泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168117_comment'></div>时殿中丞、知县事阎君仲甫来见行舍，曰：「此吾所治也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168117_comment'></div>于是上盖旁立，不完与正者易之，闳庑隘狭，椽甓朽缺者去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168117_comment'></div>治材于公，民不知劳，旬月而大备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168117_comment'></div>使者行部、王人乘传之南者以舍息便安之美为言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168117_comment'></div>予嘉邑大夫能修其职，适事之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168117_comment'></div>又私自幸于东归也，与夫乡里有徘徊之顷，实被其利，斯可忘哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168117_comment'></div>因取诒乡人书，兼载所造，列之屏，著之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168117_comment'></div>昔人邮亭不修，见讥前史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168117_comment'></div>惟事毋小，乃政之纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168117_comment'></div>五年五月二十八日，莆阳蔡襄记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1168117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript:
