id='poem_sentence_2_249026_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年7月</a>　诏授翰林学士、权知开封府，蔡襄以母亲年老和自身久病为由，上《辞翰林学士知开封府表》恳辞，请求依旧知泉州。<div id='poem_1167813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞翰林学士知开封府表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167813")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167813'>臣襄言：今月初二日准中书劄子指挥，敕命除授依前礼部郎中、知制诰、充翰林学士、权知开封府者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167813_comment'></div>大明临下，无远裔而不均；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167813_comment'></div>零露坠霄，虽微物而必施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167813_comment'></div>俯承锡命，弥用震惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167813_comment'></div>臣襄诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167813_comment'></div>伏念臣向自掖垣，擢司京邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167813_comment'></div>上赖清光之烛，终依全庇之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167813_comment'></div>属私便于庭闱，遂求补于闽粤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167813_comment'></div>寻膺朝綍，出守泉山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167813_comment'></div>首尾五年，更移两郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167813_comment'></div>亲戚岁时之乐，足慰母心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167813_comment'></div>阡茔展省之勤，屡躬先祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167813_comment'></div>非由孝治之广，曷为天幸之多？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167813_comment'></div>惟臣贱微，感疾滋久，药石攻治之愈至，根本坚牢而未除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167813_comment'></div>日月因循，筋骸憔悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167813_comment'></div>深畏旷官之责，方潜退处之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167813_comment'></div>敢谓伏蒙尊号皇帝陛下曲贷素餐，复加恩数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1167813_comment'></div>禁林近职，儒者最荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1167813_comment'></div>都辇要权，吏之高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1167813_comment'></div>并疏宠渥，猥逮孱庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1167813_comment'></div>揣材干之非优，顾福基之甚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1167813_comment'></div>茍贻过溢之咎，实亏分量之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1167813_comment'></div>重念臣仰违法座之严，荐易周星之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1167813_comment'></div>思出入于省闼，意每在于本朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1167813_comment'></div>今此召还，适当趋进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1167813_comment'></div>然而慈亲垂老，于义不可以远行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1167813_comment'></div>病体至羸，于力不堪其剧任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1167813_comment'></div>愿特收于成命，俾再典于旧封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1167813_comment'></div>准是微诚，终期得请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1167813_comment'></div>干冒圣慈，臣无任激切屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1167813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年9月</a>　蔡襄再上《辞翰林学士知开封府状》，请求改知扬州或杭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　蔡襄作《龙游监寺硕德札》，叹仕路进退之难。<div id='poem_1167939' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167939' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167939?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙游监寺硕德札</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167939")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167939_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167939'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167939'>龙游监寺硕德：母亲安康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167939_comment'></div>襄昨表辞，以亲老兼襄久病衰悴，不堪繁剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167939_comment'></div>若不得，即乞扬、杭一郡，仰禄以养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167939_comment'></div>欲便还家，无衣食之给，转劳心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167939_comment'></div>若至京，以形骸之羸，亦当免府矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167939_comment'></div>仕路进退之难如此！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1167939_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1167939'><span class='label'>按：</span>《孙氏书画钞》卷上，涵芬楼秘笈本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1167939_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年10月4日</a>　蔡襄交印。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　蔡襄撰《太常博士胡君墓志铭》<div id='poem_1168170' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168170' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168170?labeling=true' target='_blank'>太常博士致仕胡君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168170")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168170_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168170'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168170'>胡氏世居长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168170_comment'></div>询为唐兵部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168170_comment'></div>其孙韬因乱留蜀，为伪蜀陵州刺史，蜀平，归京师，终卫尉卿，于君为曾祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168170_comment'></div>生泰州司寇参军讳脩己，卒葬海陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168170_comment'></div>司寇生宁海军节度推官讳讷，赠太子中允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168170_comment'></div>博学善属文，吕文靖公夷简尝荐其书，备修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168170_comment'></div>君其长子也，讳瑗，字翼之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168170_comment'></div>少有气节，颛意经学，兼通律吕之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168170_comment'></div>力贫以抚兄弟之孤，爱义良厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168170_comment'></div>景祐中，范文正公仲淹上言君知古乐，召见论乐，拜试秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168170_comment'></div>康定初，元昊寇边，陕西帅以辟为丹州推官，后移密州观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168170_comment'></div>丁父忧，举其族之亡于远者九丧归葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168170_comment'></div>服除，迁保宁军节度推官，治湖州州学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168170_comment'></div>又召教授诸王宫，病家，辞免，遂以太子中舍致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168170_comment'></div>泛恩改殿中丞，驿召会秘阁议乐，除大理评事，兼太常主簿，寻复解罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168170_comment'></div>岁馀，授光禄寺丞、国子监直讲，仍与议乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1168170_comment'></div>乐成，改大理寺丞，赐绯鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1168170_comment'></div>嘉祐元年迁太子中允，充天章阁侍讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1168170_comment'></div>既而疾，不能朝，拜太常博士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1168170_comment'></div>还官政，从其子志康杭州节度推官以就养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1168170_comment'></div>四年六月六日终于杭州，享年六十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1168170_comment'></div>明年十月五日，葬于湖州乌程何山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1168170_comment'></div>母随氏，赠京兆县太君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1168170_comment'></div>娶王氏，封长安县君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1168170_comment'></div>有子三人：志康进士及第，志宁、志正皆力学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1168170_comment'></div>长女婚大理寺丞滕希鲁，次进士王伯起，季女尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1168170_comment'></div>孙守约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1168170_comment'></div>君孤进所立，不恤权贵，义以自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1168170_comment'></div>本朝承周用乐，其声高，不合中和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1168170_comment'></div>太祖皇帝尝诏下一律，而未遑制作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1168170_comment'></div>天子知乐，命李照等修之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1168170_comment'></div>君初得对崇政，廷辨照等所修乐非是，诏令改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1168170_comment'></div>未几报罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1168170_comment'></div>及会秘阁议，按《周礼》以正钟律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1168170_comment'></div>用上党黍列为九等，累其中者为尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1168170_comment'></div>尺定而律成，验之比旧下一律，于是彻前乐而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1168170_comment'></div>天子临紫宸，钟磬在廷，天子曰：「学者能通典故而不能知声，工者习其声之传而不知制器之理，斯难能也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1168170_comment'></div>先有议镈钟当有大小，今与黄钟一之，非古制，乃用倍半之法作应钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1168170_comment'></div>至是钟成，特小小者不堪备宫县，诸儒侍从无异议者，天子可之，用于郊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1168170_comment'></div>又令作《皇祐新乐图记》，布之天下，盖积二十年而后成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1168170_comment'></div>其间同议论皆贵官老儒，相抵止者岂一二哉，然君未始恤之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1168170_comment'></div>尤患隋唐已来仕进尚文词而遗经业，茍趋禄利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1168170_comment'></div>及为苏、湖二州教授，严条约，以身先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1168170_comment'></div>虽大暑，必公服终日，以见诸生，设师弟子之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1168170_comment'></div>解经至有要义，恳恳为诸生言其所以治己而后治乎人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1168170_comment'></div>学徒千数，日月括劘，为文章皆傅经义，必以理胜，信其师说，敦尚行实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1168170_comment'></div>后为太学，四方归之，庠舍不能容，旁拓步军居署以广之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1168170_comment'></div>五经异论，弟子记之，目为「胡氏口义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1168170_comment'></div>侍迩英讲，不以讳忌为避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1168170_comment'></div>既疾，上数遣中贵人就问安否，盖亦有所待矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1168170_comment'></div>比去京，诸生诣阙下乞留者累日，公卿祖送都门甚盛，莫不惜其行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1168170_comment'></div>君虽老于训导，在丹州实与帅府事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1168170_comment'></div>建议更陈法，治兵器，开废地为营田，募土人为兵，给钱使自市劲马，渐以代东兵之不任战者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1168170_comment'></div>虽军校蕃酋、亭障厮役，以事见，辄饮之酒，访被边利害，以资帅府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1168170_comment'></div>府多武人，初谓君徒能知古书耳，既观君之所为不以异己，又翕然称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1168170_comment'></div>君隽材而行笃，卒艰勤以殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1168170_comment'></div>所著《资圣集》十五卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1168170_comment'></div>嗟乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1168170_comment'></div>士之有志于道，以身法世，莫不欲致之于用，推之于远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1168170_comment'></div>然才德之士多亦蹇轧难通，岂不有命乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1168170_comment'></div>君不鄙小官，进不及用，功于诲人，其施博矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1168170_comment'></div>晚乃得侍天子左右，若将有为，辄病以废，岂人事也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1168170_comment'></div>谨志。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1168170_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　蔡襄离泉前送驯鹿与东禅院长老，作《送驯鹿与东禅长老》<div id='poem_249079' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249079' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249079?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送驯鹿与东禅长老</a><span class='authorDate'>（1060年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249079")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249079_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249079'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249079'>二年驯扰傍山家，欲领东还道路赊。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249079'>送汝给孤园里去，此生长伴大牛车。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249079_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249079'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249079_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1060&endYear=1060')">1060年</a>　蔡襄复作大楷《万安桥记》大字以勒石。<div id='poem_1168118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>万安渡石桥记</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐五年秋）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1168118")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168118'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168118'>泉州万安渡石桥，始造于皇祐五年四月庚寅，以嘉祐四年二月辛未讫功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168118_comment'></div>累趾于渊，酾水为四十七道，梁空以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168118_comment'></div>其长三千六百尺，广丈有五尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168118_comment'></div>翼以扶栏，如其长之数而两之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168118_comment'></div>靡金钱一千四百万，求诸施者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168118_comment'></div>渡实支海，去舟而徒，易危而安，民莫不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168118_comment'></div>职其事者，卢锡、王寔、许忠、浮图义波、宗善等十有五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168118_comment'></div>既成，太守莆阳蔡襄为之合乐宴饮而落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168118_comment'></div>明年秋，蒙召还京，道繇是出，因纪所作，勒于岸左。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1168118_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
顺昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='29f0d5a5c5d84aad8ac8b0fdcc7a46d8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("29f0d5a5c5d84aad8ac8b0fdcc7a46d8");'><span id='29f0d5a5c5d84aad8ac8b0fdcc7a46d8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>，33岁</div><div id='29f0d5a5c5d84aad8ac8b0fdcc7a46d8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年4月20日</a>　蔡襄途次顺昌富屯溪，怀念亡弟，作《忆弟》诗，题诗馆驿屋梁。<div id='poem_249313' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249313' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249313?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忆弟</a><span class='authorDate'>（1044年4月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249313")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249313_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249313'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249313'>清溪曲曲抱山斜，绕溪十里蔷薇花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249313'>春风吹香袭人骨，乾红淡白相交加。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249313'>眼睛眩晃不能视，烂如赤日凌朝霞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249313'>时有扁舟向中下，共疑来处从仙家。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249313'>于时邀我临流饮，下踞大石盘犬牙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249313'>平生意气一快论，屈指世务还惊嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249313'>酒酣襞纸探强韵，胡涂醉字成乱鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249313'>侵更把火入官舍，下马犹吟诗各誇。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249313'>何言花落悲人世，只见溪流度岁华。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249313'>今年初夏我复至，深丛晚艳馀孤葩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249313'>山川故物依然在，惟子别路幽明赊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249313'>想象音容杳何许，桂旗猎猎随云车。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249313'>悲来独坐荫芳树，涕泪挥洒沾黄沙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249313'>行人怪我爱溪水，那知此恨无边涯。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249313_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249313'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_249313_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

建瓯

-----title
嘉兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cdc33271c05a4ad7ace5266e12c2d1e0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cdc33271c05a4ad7ace5266e12c2d1e0");'><span id='cdc33271c05a4ad7ace5266e12c2d1e0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='cdc33271c05a4ad7ace5266e12c2d1e0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年4月</a>　四月，蔡襄舟至嘉兴，作《自书诗帖.嘉禾郡偶书》作品：《嘉禾郡偶书》<div id='poem_249125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>嘉禾郡偶书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249125")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_249125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249125'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249125'>尽道瑶池琼树新，仙源寻到不逢人。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249125'>陈王也作惊鸿赋，未必当时见洛神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249125_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249125'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_249125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　四月，蔡襄作《思咏帖》致书冯京，并馈赠珍茶、茶具。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《年谱》只注明时间在四月，地点不详，推断在嘉兴或是苏州。）</span><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
无锡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6f7ed74153c043f4a7ce33f62cd8632e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6f7ed74153c043f4a7ce33f62cd8632e");'><span id='6f7ed74153c043f4a7ce33f62cd8632e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='6f7ed74153c043f4a7ce33f62cd8632e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年5月</a>　五月，蔡襄到达无锡，吊浮屠日开，作《自书诗帖·无锡县浮屠日开》作品：《自书诗帖.无锡县浮屠日开》；<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>　蔡襄作《即惠山泉煮茶》<div id='poem_249357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>即惠山煮茶</a><span class='authorDate'>（1051年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249357")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249357'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249357'>此泉何以珍，适与真茶遇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249357'>在物两称绝，于予独得趣。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249357'>鲜香箸下云，甘滑杯中露。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249357'>当能变俗骨，岂特湔尘虑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249357'>昼静清风生，飘萧入庭树。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249357'>中含古人意，来者庶冥悟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249357'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_249357_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
商丘
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fc1e07e75f7e49d6a37dfbc26009b055_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc1e07e75f7e49d6a37dfbc26009b055");'><span id='fc1e07e75f7e49d6a37dfbc26009b055_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年</a>，40岁</div><div id='fc1e07e75f7e49d6a37dfbc26009b055' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1051&endYear=1051')">1051年9月</a>　九月，蔡襄途经商丘，在商丘观汉碑，有题跋。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='600527909f8541e9a07b0778de3111e5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("600527909f8541e9a07b0778de3111e5");'><span id='600527909f8541e9a07b0778de3111e5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>，44岁</div><div id='600527909f8541e9a07b0778de3111e5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年6月22日</a>　蔡襄长子匀逝世。作品：《长子将作监主簿哀词》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　蔡襄致书葛密谢慰问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年7月13日</a>　蔡襄离宋都，致书杜君，表示谢忱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年7月27日</a>　蔡襄派州校持书札、祭礼驰往江阴参加葛宫妻孙氏葬礼。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d02df2750e33445c8d60c1a4650ba31b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d02df2750e33445c8d60c1a4650ba31b");'><span id='d02df2750e33445c8d60c1a4650ba31b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>，50岁</div><div id='d02df2750e33445c8d60c1a4650ba31b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄行抵商丘，再上《辞翰林学士知开封府又状》请“与免开封府，并罢翰林之职，依旧职名，许令在京兼判闲局”<div id='poem_1167837' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1167837' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1167837?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞翰林学士知开封府状<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_1167837")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1167837_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1167837'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1167837'>右，臣至和年中蒙差知开封府，臣是时久住京师，虑及母亲，思念乡里，乞知泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1167837_comment'></div>得任未几，便移福州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1167837_comment'></div>臣在福州病患，经年未愈，乞知兴化军，蒙朝廷再差知泉州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1167837_comment'></div>去年七月，准中书劄子，蒙恩除翰林学士、权知开封府，不得辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1167837_comment'></div>臣以老母不可远行，臣又久病不堪繁剧，奉表辞免，伏蒙降诏不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1167837_comment'></div>臣伏念近便乡土只有泉、福两郡，臣各两次知州，不敢再请，具状陈乞扬、杭一处，便于迎侍，兼臣可以访寻医药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1167837_comment'></div>十二月十一日准朝旨不允，臣遂奏乞从两浙乘船赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1167837_comment'></div>今来已至南京，渐次前进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1167837_comment'></div>重念臣禄仕之身，出处之际，上由君父，累奉圣旨，令臣赴阙，至于再三，臣所以不敢不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1167837_comment'></div>人子之志，惟亲所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1167837_comment'></div>臣若退居，贫无以为生，别有营图，是为亲累，臣所以不远数千里迎侍老母，以就禄食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1167837_comment'></div>然臣被疾日久，至今羸瘠，不堪劳苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1167837_comment'></div>昨因权知开封府事，迁翰林学士，恩例优厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1167837_comment'></div>臣伏望朝廷察臣诚恳，与免开封府，并罢翰林之职，依旧职名，许令在京兼判閒局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1167837_comment'></div>臣既得禄养，医治衰病，稍获安痊，朝廷驱使，不敢辞免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1167837_comment'></div>干冒圣慈，臣无任兢惶激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1167837_comment'></div>谨具状于应天府附递奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1167837_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='312f348ee29940c4a93d76287c62cc09_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("312f348ee29940c4a93d76287c62cc09");'><span id='312f348ee29940c4a93d76287c62cc09_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='312f348ee29940c4a93d76287c62cc09' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄过商丘，作《南都思杜祁公》<div id='poem_249376' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249376' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249376?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南都思杜祁公</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249376")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249376_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249376'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249376'>祁公清德老，在昔相先帝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249376'>青云吐论高，白璧持身锐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249376'>待俗无町畦，取人兼揭厉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249376'>甘贫安车后，直道洪钧际。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249376'>每闻天下士，行业若材艺。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249376'>未见比调饥，况乃挹襟袂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249376'>早尝登公门，顾睐叨末契。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249376'>谓有金石姿，良工心劘砺。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249376'>仰瞻通德衢，独立耆英第<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：所居名也。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249376'>评书草圣优，煮荈云腴细。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249376'>遗墨秘巾箧，感激君子惠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249376'>悲风吹白杨，佳城兹久闭。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249376'>声名与濉浼，东流无已岁。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249376_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249376'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_249376_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>蔡襄舟上遇孙沔，作《会亭遇资政孙公赴阙公致仕已七年时召归将有四鄙之任》古诗。<div id='poem_249340' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249340' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249340?labeling=true' target='_blank'>会亭遇<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup>资政孙公赴阙公致仕已七年时召归将有西鄙之任</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_249340_0'>① 原有孙子，据诗集删</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249340'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249340'>志节虽落落，不能无谤毁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249340'>壮年自雄豪，末路遽颠委。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249340'>众口方丛嘈，即欲置之死。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249340'>公尝为大臣，沈冤不辨理。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249340'>恭惟仁宗圣，散地而后已。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249340'>新治甬上居，閒逸安暮齿。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249340'>恭惟今天子，继照明鉴是。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249340'>问公何处在，勉哉为予起。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249340'>使者临其门，将驾不容俟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249340'>滔滔汴流急，行舟姑少止。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249340'>长堤榆柳深，夜凉襟带褫。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249340'>语终求其要，兹事殊可喜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249340'>朝廷英俊林，岂无人器使。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249340'>谓公先帝臣，擢任刷前耻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249340'>惟公体上意，毕力荷恩纪。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249340'>富贵安足论，清心寂如水。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249340'>古人老益壮，忠义在所指。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249340'>况复千载遇，功名迈良史。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249340_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249340'></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_249340_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5ca511a3d84a4de5964e7441461fd64d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5ca511a3d84a4de5964e7441461fd64d");'><span id='5ca511a3d84a4de5964e7441461fd64d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>，50岁</div><div id='5ca511a3d84a4de5964e7441461fd64d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1061&endYear=1061')">1061年</a>　蔡襄至常州，看望张景山，作《寄题张景山大卿园池》<div id='poem_249260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄题张景山大卿园池</a><span class='authorDate'>（1061年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249260")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249260'>人仰公才世吏师，更甘归老旧林池。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249260'>门阑清似当官处，心力强于少壮时。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249260'>物理自冥非寄酒，兵谋犹在却因棋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249260'>濠边风月如招隐，愿拂尘裾从所之<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《蔡忠惠集》卷六）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249260'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249260_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
南京
-----detail

-----title
永城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4e0b32352c9b4cd586704a4cd6f38488_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4e0b32352c9b4cd586704a4cd6f38488");'><span id='4e0b32352c9b4cd586704a4cd6f38488_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='4e0b32352c9b4cd586704a4cd6f38488' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄过酂阳，目睹灾区惨状，作《酂阳行》二十韵歌哭之。<div id='poem_249430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>酂阳行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249430")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249430'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249430'>春秋书大水，灾患古所评。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249430'>去年积行潦，田亩鱼蛙生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249430'>今岁谷翔贵，鼎饪无以烹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249430'>继亦掇原野，草莱不得萌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249430'>剥伐及桑枣，折发连檐甍。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249430'>谁家有仓囷，指此为兼并。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249430'>头会复箕敛，劝率以为名。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249430'>壮强先转徙，羸瘠何经营。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249430'>天子忧元元，四郊扬使旌。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249430'>朝暮给饘粥，军廪阙丰盈。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249430'>殍亡与疫死，颠倒投官坑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249430'>坑满弃道傍，腐肉犬豕争。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249430'>往往互食啖，欲语心魂惊。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249430'>荒村但寂寥，晚日多哭声。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249430'>哭哀声不续，饥病焉能哭。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249430'>止哭复吞声，清血暗双目。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249430'>陇上麦欲黄，寄命在一熟。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249430'>麦熟有几何，人稀麦应足。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249430'>纵得新麦尝，悲哉旧亲属。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249430'>我歌酂阳行，诗成宁忍读。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249430_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249430'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_249430_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
盱眙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='76cb2a312afb469f9e3998accaa2ae0b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("76cb2a312afb469f9e3998accaa2ae0b");'><span id='76cb2a312afb469f9e3998accaa2ae0b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='76cb2a312afb469f9e3998accaa2ae0b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄至泗州，登马子山观漕亭，作《泗州登马子山观漕亭》<div id='poem_249372' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249372' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249372?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泗州登马子山观漕亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249372")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_249372_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249372'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249372'>庙社奠东都，恃德非恃险。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249372'>聚兵三十万，待哺无容歉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249372'>西有砥柱峻，菽麦不踰陕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249372'>齐鲁粮食艰，灞水不潋滟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249372'>唯馀汴渠利，直贯长淮隒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_249372'>岁输六百万，江湖极收敛。<div id='poem_sentence_5_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_249372'>挽送入太仓，因陈失盖弇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_249372'>将漕苟不登，汝职兹为忝。<div id='poem_sentence_7_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_249372'>或谓取太多，六路有丰俭。<div id='poem_sentence_8_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_249372'>其间一不熟，饥殍谁能掩。<div id='poem_sentence_9_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_249372'>一旦俾之粟，是人意常慊。<div id='poem_sentence_10_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_249372'>区处失其宜，斯言反为玷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_249372'>尝欲请增减，革孚亦须渐。<div id='poem_sentence_12_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_249372'>连营今饭稻，香美若菱芡。<div id='poem_sentence_13_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_249372'>因循未易论，官曹畏书检。<div id='poem_sentence_14_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_249372'>虚亭一临眺，比比危樯飐。<div id='poem_sentence_15_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_249372'>来从数千里，岁时空苒苒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_249372'>雨馀山气净，黛色浅深染。<div id='poem_sentence_17_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_249372'>夜昏渔火出，倏忽电光闪。<div id='poem_sentence_18_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_249372'>须臾月色空，水面铺寒簟。<div id='poem_sentence_19_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_249372'>相逢喜道旧，城柝屡移点。<div id='poem_sentence_20_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_249372'>因语发长谣，谁能刊琬琰。<div id='poem_sentence_21_249372_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_249372'></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_249372_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宿迁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e8e812ff1e424c07bf6a170b2c197b09_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e8e812ff1e424c07bf6a170b2c197b09");'><span id='e8e812ff1e424c07bf6a170b2c197b09_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>，54岁</div><div id='e8e812ff1e424c07bf6a170b2c197b09' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　蔡襄将渡洪泽湖，为风所阻，蔡襄作《洪泽阻风》<div id='poem_249238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_249238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/249238?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洪泽阻风</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(29849, "北宋", "蔡襄", "poem_title_249238")'>蔡襄</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_249238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_249238'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_249238'>今日风期恶，迟回一水滨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_249238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_249238'>村旗呈酒圣，庙鼓赛河神。<div id='poem_sentence_1_249238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_249238'>跃鲤曾惊网，饥乌不避人。<div id='poem_sentence_2_249238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_249238'>商工时借问，何处即通津。<div id='poem_sentence_3_249238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_249238'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_249238_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
